# notes:                
42001001	Ŋic bocjaha jaŋe ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko wiac fârine fuawec irec binaŋ birickerâ qâreŋkembiŋ .
42001002	Jaŋe binaŋ i mitiŋiczi bapa fuŋfuŋ juhuc wiac fuŋgâtânehec hone manac eku banârembiŋ irec sâcko qâreŋkembiŋ .
42001003	Eme noni iŋuc jaha fuŋnaonecteaŋ wiac fua warewec irec aimuŋ mu ikisiŋ ehuc manaku mana-fârerâ Teofilo ŋicbomboŋ-nane gore ninic qâninic qâreŋkekopac .
42001004	Eme i wosehuc šiŋuc mana tarazemec : Dâŋ binaŋ egarekicne i fârine jâmbâŋ .
42001005	Herodezi Judia mâreŋte ŋicwofuŋ juwec , dameŋ ira taha bapa moc juwec šâŋene Zakaria , e Abia ere gie birionec . Ŋonâŋ-ticne Elisabete e Aroŋte tucne tofane .
42001006	Jahe Anuture maio bahac fâsâc juhuc sâcmutâc dâŋticne aiakic jaha reŋke-fârehuc jupic .
42001007	Eme Elisabete hufiŋ juwecte jahe ɋâric tâmiric juku ŋic ŋokac qizec epic .
42001008	Eme Zakaria juwec ŋic biri i jaŋe taha ufuŋko bâzi ririke gie baniŋte dameŋ-jeŋic maickeme
42001009	fisirâ gie-jeŋic ru sâc ehuc Zakaria hosâc bâzi rikeocte mucnepie taha ufuŋ maŋnao rašiwec .
42001010	Raširâ hosâc bâzi rikehame ŋic ŋokac omane jaŋe sapamaŋko Wofuŋ numecnehec jumbiŋ .
42001011	Ehame Wofuŋte aŋelozi fuarâ hosâc bâzi ririke alata ŋifecnao fâreopec domawec .
42001012	Domame Zakariazi honerâ fâfârerâ hemâtâckewec .
42001013	Iŋuc eme aŋelozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Zakaria , go mi hâwicguoc , Wofuŋzi nunumuge manawecte ŋonâŋge Elisabete motec kiweckerâ roocmu , ere šâŋe Johane muzemec .
42001014	Go šeri ehuc bubiaŋ manacmu , â ŋic bocjahazi fufua-ticnere aŋac-jopaocmu .
42001015	E Wofuŋte maio kâcɋene erâ juocmu ; â waiŋ me opâ momori irec sowa juocmu . Erâ e neŋgoc bumaŋko fohame Tiri Mârozi maŋticne bâfuseocmu .
42001016	Eme Israe ŋic boc jaha bârisiec-jopame Wofuŋ Anutu-jeŋic maickeniŋmu .
42001017	Elia maŋšoɋac â tâpiri focnewec sâc focneha Wofuŋte biŋedâŋ mumuŋic erâ juocmu . Ehuc kâcɋene jaŋere maŋ bârisieme ɋiene jaŋerao iticneocmu , â râŋgeŋne jaŋe ejareme tiŋne jaŋere mamana birire hazec râeniŋmu . Eme ŋic jaŋe mâmâc sâko Wofuŋte šawierâ juniŋmu . ”
42001018	Aŋelozi iŋuc mume manarâ Zakariazi dâŋ šiŋuc bârisiecnewec : “ No â ŋonâŋ-nane nâhe ŋic ŋokac qizec , irec dâŋge wemocko manape fârine eocmu ? ”
42001019	Mume aŋelozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Manakic , šâŋe-nane Gabirie , no Anuture maio domaekopac . Eki sorecnume waharâ biŋedâŋ biaŋ gazakopac .
42001020	Irec manac , dâŋnane mi mana šakiekomec irec okacne nâŋguŋ erâ dâŋ tâmiric juhaŋtec dâŋ gazakopac fârinehec eocmu . Dâŋ mukopac i racne mi eocmu . ”
42001021	Zakaria e ufuŋko boc jume ŋic ŋokac woŋec-ticne ŋeku manafecne manambiŋ .
42001022	Iŋuc ehapie šâhec jaŋerao waharâ dâŋ jazaocte eipiewec . Eipieme jaŋe šiŋuc manambiŋ : E taha ufuŋko wiac šâŋe furu moc honejec . Eme eki mezi sâsâc sawa ejarewec , dâŋ ine wemocko jazazac .
42001023	Iŋuczi iŋuc juhame gie bapa dameŋ-ticne tarame haeo risie rawec .
42001024	Eme šâhecko ŋonâŋ-ticne motec kiweckewec . Erâ mosa 5 soŋke soŋke juwec . Ehuc šiŋuc muwec :
42001025	“ Wofuŋ e dameŋ bawec i maickeme ehâmo-narerâ mimi bâsuec enarewec . ”
42001026	Mosa 6 tarame Wofuŋzi aŋelo Gabirie soreme Galilaia mâreŋko Nazarete haeo rawec .
42001027	Ira naru ŋokac moc juwec šâŋene Maria , e ŋic moc Dawidire oso gitecne , šâŋene Josefe , ere biŋe mukicne .
42001028	Eme aŋelo e Mariarao fuarâ muwec , “ Wofuŋte joroc biaŋ , go šeri ec , Wofuŋzi gohec jukac . ”
42001029	Aŋelozi dâŋ iŋuc mume maname quŋkeme maŋnezi šiŋuc manasuwec : Weniŋucte mu šeri enarekac ?
42001030	Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Maria go mi hâwicguoc , Anutuzi honecgume biaŋkekac .
42001031	Manakic , go motec kiweckerâ rocmu , ere šâŋe Jesu muzemec .
42001032	E kâcɋene jâmbâŋ jume Fekicne sâko ere Ŋokâ mucneniŋmu , â Wofuŋ Anutuzi apa-ticne Dawidi ere ŋeŋetacko râeocmu .
42001033	Eme Jakobore ɋâricfâc guriŋne bajarehuc jume ŋicwofuŋ juju-ticne forašihuc juocmu sanaŋ . ”
42001034	Mume Mariazi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No ŋic tâmiric jukopacko dâŋ mukic i weniŋuc erâ sanaŋkeocmu ? ”
42001035	Mume aŋelozi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec : “ Tiri Mârozi faigao wahaocmu â Fekicne sâko ere tâpirizi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ ŋegareocmu . Eme irec motec rocmu e tiri mucnezo , Anuture Ŋokâ hâcne .
42001036	Erâ moc gazape manac : Âgoge Elisabete e ŋokac qizeczi motec kiweckerâ juhame mosa 6 ekac , e hufiŋ ŋokac mucneeŋgopieŋzi iŋuc ekac hâcne .
42001037	Anutu e wiac moc ezomurâ mi eipieekac . ”
42001038	Mume Mariazi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ naru , irec dâŋ mukic iŋuc hâcne enarezejec . ” Iŋuc mume aŋelozi beherâ rawec .
42001039	Maria e jume mi šoraha biac šawierâ Judaia tiki mâreŋko hae moc ŋewec ira rawec .
42001040	Ra fisirâ Zakariare ficko ferâ Elisabete mu šeri ecnewec .
42001041	Mu šeri ecneme manahame izia bumaŋnao motec e kiwaewec . Eme Tiri Mârozi Elisabete ere maŋko hurâ fuseme
42001042	dâŋ bafehuc šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ŋokac âgo-nâŋec gore manape sâc moc eme mumbiaŋgukopac â bumaŋgao fuajec fokac e wâc iŋuc jaha mumbiaŋkekopac .
42001043	Go Wofuŋ-nanere neŋgoczi wemo biaŋ-nanere norao warekomec ?
42001044	Mu šeri enaretec hazec-naneo hume bumaŋ-naneo moteczi kiwaekac .
42001045	Go Wofuŋte biŋedâŋ gazakicne irec fârine fuaocmu manapaŋkemeŋte gore manape šerine ekac . ”
42001046	Eme Mariazi kecšiŋuc muwec : “ No maŋ qâqâtâc-nanezi Wofuŋ muafeckekopac ,
42001047	â maŋnanezi Anutu bâbâpiaŋ-nane šeri ecnekopac .
42001048	E kiŋaŋ naru-ticne waha qaqane no bafecnukacte ŋic gurune gurune nore manapie šerine eocmu .
42001049	E bapafârezi norao mâsi sâko bakac hâcne . Ʒâŋe biŋe-ticne tiri jaha fokac .
42001050	Araŋ bacneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋuruc-ticnere erâ mimiŋzi ɋâric ehâmo-jareekac .
42001051	E tâpiri-ticnere fuŋne bâfuahuc maŋfefe jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe bâtâtiec-jopaekac .
42001052	E ŋicbomboŋ sâko jaŋe popoonec tuŋjopame wahahapie hujukicne jaŋe bafec-joparâ toŋko râec-jopakac .
42001053	E roroc hapetac jaŋe wiac bâmâckehuc jare gumec ekac , â mafa sâkohec behec-jopame qarâ suriŋne juŋgopieŋ .
42001054	Erâ Israe kiŋaŋ ŋicfâc-ticne maŋuru-ticnere roroŋ fâre-nârekac .
42001055	Mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec , Abraham â ɋâricfâcne , jurahuc juniŋmu , jaŋe dâŋ jazawec irec fârine fuakac . ”
42001056	Eme Maria e mosa jahec â moc Elisabetehec juku hae-ticnao risie rawec .
42001057	Elisabete e dameŋ-ticne maickeme motec rowec .
42001058	Eme haefâc-ticne â mame sâkofâc-ticne jaŋe Wofuŋzi maŋuruc-ticnere fuŋne erao bataniŋkewecte manarâ ehec mâmâc bubiaŋ manambiŋ .
42001059	Izi šoaŋ gie bapa 8 tarame jaŋe tumaŋnerâ motec sahacnao Wofuŋte ma barâ mamac-ticne Zakaria ere wase bazo mumbiŋ .
42001060	Eme neŋgoc-ticnezi qatara-jarerâ muwec , “ Aricne , šâŋene Johane muzo . ”
42001061	Mume šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Hâc , mame sâkofâcge jaŋerao šâŋe wase iŋucne moc mi fokac . ”
42001062	Qaqatarac erâ Zakaria e motecte šâŋe muocte ecnepie
42001063	tafere ejareme râcnepie fainao šiŋuc qâreŋkewec : “ Ʒâŋe-ticne Johane . ” Iŋuc qâreŋkeme jaŋe manapie moc eha
42001064	izia nameŋne risieme dâŋ dâŋ ehuc Anutu muteŋkewec .
42001065	Eme hae rârec rârec ŋic jurambiŋ jaŋe dâŋ binaŋ i manapie hâhâwicne ewec . Eme Judaia tiki mâreŋko binaŋ miczi mic nazaŋ gazaŋ efârembiŋ .
42001066	Eme manambiŋ jaŋe dâŋ i maŋke juhuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Motec iŋucnezi sokarâ weniŋuc eocmu ? ” Eme Wofuŋzi dopecke sapec ecneha juwec .
42001067	Eme mamac-ticne Zakaria e Tiri Mârozi maŋne fusucmame findaŋdâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec :
42001068	“ Israe ŋic nâŋâc Wofuŋ-nâŋec Anutu muteŋkenaŋ . Eki hâcne ŋicfâc-ticne iqic-nâporâ kitâc-nâpokac .
42001069	Ehuc kiŋaŋŋic-ticne Dawidi ere ɋâricfâc nâŋâcnao bâbâpiaŋte wâtuŋ moc âkendâŋnekac .
42001070	Mârâc jaha porofetefâc-ticne ejareme findaŋdâŋ mujumbieŋ sâc iŋuc hâcne fuakac .
42001071	Eki kisâ enârehuc qaisoc-nâpoeŋgopieŋ jaŋeraonec hâcne batarac-nâpoocmu .
42001072	Mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋehec tiri šâšâfic sanaŋ ewecte manasuc-jopahuc maŋuruc-ticnere iŋuc enâreocmu .
42001073	Apa-nâŋec Abraham mupaŋkecnewecte
42001074	râsifâc-nâŋec jaŋeraonec batarac-nâpoocmu hâcne . Iŋuc enâreme âke mâteŋ-nâpoha
42001075	maŋfuru â bahac fâsâc juhuc kiŋaŋ qacnehuc juku hâmonšepeneŋ .
42001076	Erâ motec go hâcne Femicne sâko ere porofete erâ jucmu . ehuc Wofuŋte biŋe muhuc hata bâšâwecnecmu .
42001077	Erâ ŋicfâc-ticne bâbâpiaŋte dâŋ jaza qazuc etecne mana šakiepie sâqocne-jeŋic tâmireocmu .
42001078	Anutu-nâŋec e maŋuruc-ticne kâcɋene sâko fokacte mume faickonec furic râehuc
42001079	dapâcko â hâmoc uupicko ŋeŋene nâŋâc bataniŋ-nâpokac . Ehame wamare hata fuame honehuc sâcne âtenaŋmu . ”
42001080	Eme motec e sahaczi â maŋzi soka sanaŋ ewec . Erâ mâreŋ tuhuo juhame gie dameŋ-ticne maickeme Israe ŋic janerao fua tâcnewec .
42002001	Dameŋ ira Roma ŋicwofuŋ sâko Augusto ere micdâŋ kecšiŋuc fuawec : ŋic mâreŋ sâc wose qâreŋ ejarezo .
42002002	Gie iŋucne mârâc mi bakicne , i Qirinio e Siria mâreŋko kia sâko juhame furune fuŋkekicne .
42002003	Eme ŋic mâmâc sasawa wose qâreŋ ejareniŋte haefuŋ-jeŋic sâc rafârembiŋ .
42002004	Rahapie Josefe e Dawidire ɋâric Galilaia mâreŋko Nasarete haeo juweczi iŋuc jaha Judaia mâreŋko Dawidire haefuŋ Betelehem ira rawec .
42002005	Ehuc ŋokac biŋe-ticne Maria ehec mâmâc qâreŋ-jofaniŋte kiwechec jowame rapic .
42002006	Fisirâ juhapire Maria motec roro dameŋ-ticne maickewec .
42002007	Eme mârâc motec-ticne rorâ qoruczi foŋkerâ bulimakao otoo râeme hurâ fowec . Ŋic jaŋe tomafic fusucmambiŋte ŋeŋe fofo basarâ bulimakao ficko ferâ ŋepic hâcne .
42002008	Eme hae mâreŋ ijaha ŋic tucne jaŋe ŋafe ira kecɋaŋ gieo lama jaŋere soŋaŋ ŋembiŋ .
42002009	Ŋehapie Wofuŋte aŋelo moczi jaŋerao fuame Wofuŋte oŋararaczi batamaec-jopame mâretec hâwic-jopawec .
42002010	Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe mi hâwic-ŋopaoc , manaŋgopieŋ , no aŋac šeridâŋ bajukopac , irec fârine ŋic mâmâc sasawa fua-ŋareocmu .
42002011	Miŋecgac Bâbâpiaŋ rune Wofuŋ Kristo hâcne , Dawidire haefuŋko fua-ŋarekac .
42002012	Eme mutâcne-ŋarepe mananiŋ : Ŋoŋe motec geune jâmbâŋ qoruczi foŋkekicne bulimakao otoo foha ra bâfuaniŋmu . ”
42002013	Dâŋ iŋuc muhame izia sambâŋ momori gurune fufusuc jaha ututuŋ aŋelo âgo-jeŋictao tumaŋnerâ šiŋuc muhuc Anutu muteŋkembiŋ :
42002014	“ Ʒeri mumuteŋ Anutu faic sambâŋko , mâreŋko ŋic âgo jauŋ ejarekac jaŋerao wama fuakac . ”
42002015	Aŋelo jaŋe sambâŋko risie fepie soŋaŋŋic jaŋe šiŋuc muhuc nazaŋ gazaŋ embiŋ : “ Nâŋâc Betelehem haeo ferâ Wofuŋzi dâŋ nâzâkac irec fârine honenaŋ . ”
42002016	Iŋuc murâ bâruŋ jaha ferâ Maria â Josefe bâfuac-jofarâ motec geune bulimakao otoo fohame honembiŋ .
42002017	Honerâ motecte dâŋ biŋe manambiŋ i mufuambiŋ .
42002018	Eme soŋaŋ jaŋere mickonec binaŋ manambiŋ jaŋe warecke-fârembiŋ .
42002019	Maria eki ine dâŋ i maŋkerâ manatâc qâtâc ehuc juwec .
42002020	Eme soŋaŋ jaŋe risierâ wiac hone manac embiŋ sâc manasurâ Anutu daŋge mumuteŋ ecnembiŋ .
42002021	Jesu motec fuarâ fohame šoaŋ gie bapa 8 eme motec sahacnao Wofuŋte ma bahuc šâŋene Jesu mumbiŋ . Ʒâŋe i motec e mi fuahame aŋelozi qanaŋ mufuawec .
42002022	Eme Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ fowec , i reŋkehuc Mariazi bâtâcko juku sahac herâ Josefehec motec Jerusalem haeo baferâ Wofuŋte biŋe qapic .
42002023	Wofuŋte sâcmutâc dâŋ kecšiŋuc fowec i hâcne sâsehuc epic : “ Mârâc motec fuapie i Wofuŋte biŋe qafârezo . ”
42002024	Erâ Wofuŋte sâcmutâc dâŋko hapâ jajahec me buni jajahec bâzi ririkere mukicne i wâc barâ rapic .
42002025	Jerusalem haeo ŋic moc juwec šâŋene Simeoŋ . E tiŋne â mitihec juhuc Israe ŋic jaŋerao bâbâmiriŋ fuaocte woŋec juwec . Ehame Tiri Mârozi maŋticnao ŋeŋe juju ehuc
42002026	dâŋ šiŋuc mufuacnewec : “ Go mi hâmohaŋtecne Wofuŋ Kristo fuame honecmu . ”
42002027	Ŋic e Mârozi ecneme taha ufuŋko fewec . Eme Maria â Josefe jahe sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc Jesu motec ijaha bafepire
42002028	Simeoŋzi motec hâporâ šiŋuc muhuc Anutu muafeckewec :
42002029	“ O Wofuŋ sâko , šine hâcne šâŋe fâri-nanezi goraonec bâbâpiaŋ honekopacte
42002030	go kiŋaŋŋicge no micdâŋgere sâcko râecnutec bumâteŋ fuaha rakopac .
42002031	Go bâbâpiaŋ i mâreŋ sâc ŋicne ŋicne jaŋe honeniŋte bâfuakomec .
42002032	Izi qâpuc jaŋere maŋ âke tamaekac â Israe ŋicfâcge jaŋere šâŋe biŋe bafaharekac . ”
42002033	Motecte dâŋ iŋuc mume neŋgoc mamac jahecne manapire bipinehec ewec .
42002034	Eme Simeoŋzi jambuŋ-jopahuc motec neŋgoc-ticne Maria šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Manakic , motec kecši erao Israe ŋic fâuckeniŋte mukicne , gâcne jaŋe erao hetakirerâ rândiŋke qa eniŋmu â gâcne jaŋe erao hesiŋnerâ fahareniŋmu , erâ aka-jeŋic râekicnere ro waha âte boc ecneniŋmu .
42002035	Erâ gahacne wâc šikare busâqoc hâtânezi buheric bâfua-garezokac . Waic iŋucne fuame ŋic bocjaha maŋjeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeocmu . ”
42002036	Eme miti ŋokac moc juwec šâŋene Hana . E Fanuere otâ , Ase ere tucne tofane . Naru-ticnao ŋic barâ ehec juhame jara 7 eme hâmome
42002037	hozec erâ jufeku jara 84 bazurâ ŋokac qizec jâmbâŋ ewec . Ŋokac eki hâcne taha ufuŋko hati jurâ ju ehuc Anuture erâ sowa â nunumu gie bajujec .
42002038	Eme eki hâcne dameŋ ijaha taha ufuŋko fisirâ Anutu mumbiaŋkewec , â Jerusalem rune jaŋere fifirue dameŋte woŋec jumbiŋ , jaŋe Jesu motecte biŋedâŋ jazawec .
42002039	Maria â Josefe jahe Wofuŋte sâcmutâc dâŋ mukicne i efârerâ Galilaia mâreŋko Nazarete haeo risie rapic .
42002040	Ira juhapire motec e Anutuzi hone jauŋ ecneha soka sanaŋ ehuc mamana sâkohec ewec .
42002041	Maria â Josefe jahe jara sâc aakic hombaŋte Jerusalem haeo fejupirec .
42002042	Ehame Jesu motec jara-ticne 12 bazume hombaŋte fefe dameŋ-jeŋic maickeme jowapire mâmâc fembiŋ .
42002043	Ferâ juhapie hombaŋ tarame Maria â Josefe jahe Jesu motec hetarapire Jerusalem haeo juhame buc risiepic .
42002044	Risiehuc guru sâko jaŋehec biac bâniejec murâ hatao âgo wiacfâc-jekic jaŋerao basa rahuc juhapire ŋafewec .
42002045	Jaŋerao basa-bipierâ hae fureme mocwâc Jerusalem haeo risierâ ira basapic .
42002046	Basahapire gie bapa jahec â moc eme taha ufuŋko bâfuapic . Ira miti qaqazu jaŋere ŋondeŋko ŋehuc dâŋjeŋic manahuc fuŋnere mu wioc ejarewec .
42002047	Eme ŋembiŋ jaŋe mâmâc sasawa mamana-ticnere â dâŋticnere wareckembiŋ .

42005035	Juku ŋicwofuŋ jowac ropie basahuc dameŋ ira sowa juniŋmu . ”
42005036	Iŋuc murâ dâŋ herâricne moc šiŋuc jazawec : “ Mozi ŋaqi ɋâricnaonec qoruc susuc moc bâtâcnerâ ŋaqi raŋɋanao ɋâtâocmu ? Moc e iŋuc erâ muzac ŋaqi ɋâricne maŋgâŋ sipirickezac â qoruc susuc ɋâricnezi ŋaqi raŋɋanao sâctiri jaha ezac .

42006001	Sabata hombaŋ mocko Jesu â motecfâc-ticne jaŋe padi gie ŋondeŋko rambiŋ . Rahuc motec jaŋe fârine moc moc bâtâcnerâ mezi šâmurâ nâmbiŋ .

42006004	Dawidi e Anuture ufuŋko ferâ poroŋ Anuture biŋe râekicne i rorâ nâhuc ŋicfâcne jareme mâmâc nâmbiŋ . Poroŋ i ŋic omane bâtâc bajarekicne , bâzi ririke ŋic micbuc-jeŋic . Eme i sifu nâmbiŋ . ”

42011031	Juwic mâreŋkonec ŋokac wofuŋ eki mumu tara dameŋko ŋicguru ši ŋoŋehec faharerâ fuŋne-ŋeŋic ritume katucne roniŋmu . Erâ i mâc mâcne , ŋokac e Salomoraonec mamana fârine roocte mâreŋ qaŋeŋnaonec warewec ” eme mananiŋ , ši fuakac e Salomore sâc sirickekac .

42011033	“ Ŋoŋe lambe qazerâ mi soŋkeeŋgopieŋ , me kušizi mi hetutuckeeŋgopieŋ , aricne , lambe ŋeŋe-ticnao hepie fic âke tamaeme ŋic ŋoŋe honehuc feeŋgopieŋ .

42011035	Eme maŋgao tatamac fokac izi dapâc ezacte aimuŋ soŋaŋkehuc juzemec .

42011037	Dâŋ i mutararâ juhame farisaio ŋic moczi Jesu nânâre ficticnao hefârewec . Hefâreme ficticnao ferâ izia nânâ teboo waha ŋewec .
42011038	I me sahac-ticne qanaŋ mi šurehuc iŋuc ewecte farisaiozi maname mi sâckewec .
42011039	Eme irec Wofuŋzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Oi , farisaio ŋoŋe , oto râqâc-ŋeŋic šure ɋaɋackeeŋgopieŋ , maŋŋeŋicko ine nânâ mafare sasec â bâbâsifuczi fusucmakicne .
42011040	O ŋic mutucne ŋoŋe , wiac sasawa irec sahacne bâfuaweczi maŋne mi bâfuawec me ?

42011042	Oi farisaio , ŋoŋe hâwic-ŋopazac me , ŋoŋe wiac racne , romboc , wifu , qase â iŋucne gâcne i tucne Wofuŋte biŋe qahuc râeeŋgopieŋ , ehuc ŋifecne wiac fârine , mitio mubâtiŋ â Anutu sâsâse ine mi eeŋgopieŋ . Moc reŋkehuc moc reŋkezo .
42011043	Oi farisaio ŋoŋe , mitificko ŋicbomboŋ ŋeŋeoa micne ŋeniŋte mueŋgopieŋ â hatao ŋic ŋokac omanezi bâfuac-ŋoparâ mu šeri eŋareniŋte irec maŋŋeŋic domaekac .

42011047	Jei , mimiŋnefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋe porofete jopa sipiric embiŋ i jaŋere šâŋeruŋ ericke emasaŋ eeŋgopieŋ .

43002019	Eme micjeŋicko rorâ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe taha ufuŋ kecši heropiepie noni šoaŋ jahec â moc eha mocwâc bâzickepemu . ”
43002020	Iŋuc muhuc jazame mumbiŋ , “ Kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec jaŋe taha ufuŋ ši jara 46 baku bâzickembiŋ , eme goki šoaŋ jahec â moc sawa ira bâzickezo mukomec me ? ”
43002021	Jesu eki ine sahac-ticnere ufuŋko ɋetickehuc muwec .
43002022	Juku hâmockonec ɋârerâ fahareme motecfâcne jaŋe dâŋ i manasumbiŋ . Ehuc ufuŋte muwec , â miti papiao ere dâŋ gâcne mukicne , irec mâmâc manapie fârine eha mana šakiembiŋ .
43002023	Jesu e aakic hombaŋko Jerusalem haeo juhuc fuŋne qaqa mâsi bame ŋic bocjahazi honerâ šâŋe-ticne mana sakac embiŋ .
43002024	Jesu e jahac ine ŋic hone tarac-jopa-fârewecte jaŋerao mi fohorewec .
43002025	E ŋic mocte fuŋne manaocte gâcne mu indiŋ mi ejarewec , e jahaczia ŋic maŋjeŋic hone šâŋitac ejare-fârewec .
43003001	Farisaio ŋic jaŋere âgo moc juwec šâŋene Nikodemo . E Judaŋic jaŋere micne sâko wâc juwec .
43003002	Ŋic eki hâcne Jesu ŋafeo iqickerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Qaqazu , nâŋe fuŋnege manaeŋgopeneŋ , go qaqazu fârinezi Anuturaonec wahameŋ , go mâsi baekic i ŋic moczi Anutu tâmiric juhuc bapane mi ekac . ”
43003003	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape : Moc e harierâ fufua ɋâricne mi fuaocmuzi Anuture uucmaŋ sâcne mi bâfuaocmu . ”
43003004	Eme Nikodemozi muwec , “ Hâc , moc e kâcɋeŋkekicnezi fufua ɋâricne weniŋuc fuaocmu , wemocko neŋgoc bumaŋko mocwâc hume hâsine roocmu ? ”
43003005	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape : Moc e Opâ â Mârore kiwecko ɋâricne mi fuakicnezi Anuture uucmaŋko sâcne mi rašiocmu .
43003006	Ŋickiwecko fuakicnezi ŋic hawari jaha , Mârore kiwecko fuakicnezi Mârore hawari jaha .
43003007	Ŋoŋe fufua ɋâricne fuaniŋte mupe go manatec mi quŋkeoc .
43003008	Mâŋâŋ e kosa qaekac , eme go fânâŋ-ticne i manaekic , â fuŋne wenirec fuŋkerâ wareekac , â wena rataraekac , ine mi manaekic . Eme moc e Mârore kiwecko fuakicne , e fuŋne-ticne iŋucnea fokac . ”
43003009	Mume Nikodemozi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec : “ I weniŋuc erâ iŋuc ezo ? ”
43003010	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go Israe ŋic jaŋere qaqazuzi irec kâuc bakomec me ?
43003011	No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape : Nâŋe wiac hone manac eeŋgopeneŋ ijaha ŋaza mutâc eeŋgopeneŋ , eme ŋoŋe ine dâŋnâŋec qikiŋneeŋgopieŋ .
43003012	Wiac mâreŋko fufuane irec mac ŋazape sifu mi mana šakieeŋgopieŋ , eme wiac sambâŋko fufuane irec ŋazape wemo-ŋeŋiczi mana šakieniŋmu ?
43003013	Ŋic moczi sambâŋko moc mi fewec , Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne , sambâŋkonec wahawec , e mocjahazi sambâŋko wâc juekac .
43003014	“ Mose e mârâc jaha mâreŋ sawao homa bâfeŋnewec , iŋuc jaha Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e bâfeŋnezo mukicne .
43003015	Eme e manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe juju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu .
43003016	Anutu e ŋic ŋoŋere mo iŋucne ecnewecte Ŋokâ jâmbâŋ-ticne mocjaha e râe qikiŋ ecnewec . Eme e manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe moc mi sipirickehuc ju ju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu .
43003017	Ŋokâ e ŋic jaŋere kiŋ bataraocte mâcne , ŋic bâpiaŋ-jopaocte Anutuzi soreme wahawec .
43003018	Moc e Ŋokâ manasiŋkekaczi okacnere biŋe mi ekac . Á moc e Ŋokâ mi manasiŋkekaczi ine biac okacnere biŋe ekac . Wemocte ? E Anuture ŋokâ jâmbâŋ mocjaha ere šâŋe mana maŋ mi ekac irec .
43003019	Okacnere fuŋne šiŋuc fokac : Tatamaczi ŋic maic-jopame jaŋe tatamac bâsuerâ dapâcte wosâembiŋ , juju bapa-jeŋic sâqocnere iŋuc hâcne embiŋ .
43003020	Moc e sindaŋ eocmuzi tatamac râpeckeocmu , juju bapa-ticnere fuŋne jaŋgeŋkezacte wemocko tatamacko fua taniŋ eocmu .
43003021	Moc e dâŋ fâri qizecne reŋkeocmuzi ine tatamac maickeocmu , eme eebapa-ticne Anuture micdâŋte sâcko ekicne irec fuŋne taniŋkeocmu . ”
43003022	Eme juku Jesu e motecfâcne rocjopame Jerusalem hae beherâ Judaia qaŋeŋnaopec ra jumbiŋ . Ira jaŋehec juhuc ŋic opâ rua-jarewec .
43003023	Johane e mâreŋ moc šâŋene Ainoŋ , Salim haeopec juhuc iŋuc jaha Miti Opâ gie bawec , ira opâ bocjaha fowecte ŋic jaŋe fisipie rua-jarewec .
43003024	Johane e dameŋ ira kâpâcwâru ficko mi ŋekicne .
43003025	Eme Judaŋic moczi Johane motecfâc-ticne jaŋehec opâ ruruare mu qaqatarac embiŋ .
43003026	Eme motec jaŋe Johanerao rarâ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Qaqazu , go Jordaŋ ocniŋucnao juhaŋtecne ŋic moc bâfuacgume fuŋne-ticne mujaŋgeŋkerâ nâzâmeŋ , eki dameŋ šiŋuczia ŋic opâ rua-jareme erao rafâreŋgopieŋ . ”
43003027	Mupie Johanezi šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋic moc e sambâŋ runezi wiac râcne tahac mi ehame e jahac wemocko kâŋgâc roocmu .
43003028	No kecšiŋuc muhuc ŋazapo i wemocko mickeniŋmu , ` No Kristo aricne , no biŋe mumu-ticne sawa . Ž
43003029	Ŋokac biŋe mucnekicne eki hâcne ŋokac rune . Eme ŋokac bahuc šeri kâcɋene šeri eme âgo-ticnezi manarâ bafickehuc bubiaŋ sâko bâfuaocmu wâc . Bubiaŋ i hâcne manapemurâ dameŋne maickekac ši .
43003030	Eki fua fehame noni pitiwazepac .
43003031	Faicnec wahaweczi qâhuc-nâpo-fârekac . Moc e mâreŋkonec fuakicnezi mâreŋte biŋe ekac â mâreŋkopec dâŋ muekac . Á sambâŋkonec wahaweczi ine qâhuc-nâpo-fârekac .

43003034	Anutuzi ŋic sorewec eki Anuture dâŋ jaha muekac . Ŋic iŋucne e Anutuzi Mâro sâc tâmiric qikiŋnecneekac .

43003036	Moc e Ŋokâ manasiŋkeocmu e juju sanaŋ šiŋuczia fuacnekac , â moc e Ŋokâre dâŋ bâsuehuc juocmuzi juju sanaŋ mi bâfuaocmu . Iŋucnere faio Anuture kimbeŋ feweczi foocmu . ”
43004001	Farisaio jaŋe Jesure šiŋuc manambiŋ : “ Eki motec rocjoparâ opâ rua-jareekac , i Johanere gurufâc jowaruŋgopieŋ . ”

43004004	Rahuc Samaria mâreŋ fotâcnewec .
43004005	Fotâcnehuc Samariare hae moc šâŋene Sika ira fisiwec . Hae i Jakobozi ŋokâ-ticne Josefe mâreŋ qikiŋnecnewec irec mendâŋko ŋewec .
43004006	Eme ijaha Jakobore opâ nombâŋ fowec wâc . Eme Jesu e ira guŋpiticko fisirâ betaŋkerâ nombâŋmecko waha ŋemanawec .
43004007	Ŋehame Samaria ŋokac moczi opâ fiaocte fisiwec . Fisime Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go opâ moc gumecnuc . ”

43004009	Âzâcneme ŋokac e muwec , “ Go Judaŋiczi weniŋuc erâ Samaria ŋokac norao opâre mukic ? ” Judaŋic â Samaria ŋic jaŋe bâtâcko jujumbieŋte ŋokac e iŋuc muwec .
43004010	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go Anutu jauŋ-ticnere fuŋne â opâre gazakopac nore fuŋne mâmâc kâuc bakic . Mana tararâ muzac numu-naretec opâ fifisine garezapo . ”
43004011	Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Bomboŋ , opâ nombâŋ i šoricne , erâ go opâ fifiage aricnere opâ fifisine wenirec fiacmu ?
43004012	Mimiŋne-nâŋec Jakobo e opâ nombâŋ ši rowec . Erâ e jahacne â ŋokâfâcne â lama bulimakaofâc-ticne jaŋe opâ ši jaha nâhuc jumbiŋ . Goki Jakobore sâc i jâuruhuc opâ moc bâfuacmu ? ”

43004015	Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc muwec : “ Bomboŋ , go opâ i naretec nârâ opâre mocwâc mi hâmozepac , ehuc šira gâbâ ware fiahuc domaekopac i behezepac . ”
43004016	Iŋuc mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ra ŋowege jowatec warenic . ”

43004021	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc muwec : “ Ŋokac , no gazape manac : Dameŋ moc bembeŋkekac , i maickeme ŋoŋe Mamac mai ecneniŋmu i tiki kecšira mâcne â Jerusalem haeo wâc mi eniŋmu .
43004022	Ŋoŋe kâuc bahuc mai ecneeŋgopieŋ , nâŋe ine mana tarahuc mai ecneeŋgopeneŋ . Bâbâpiaŋ i Judaŋic nâŋeraonec .
43004023	Dameŋ moc maickeocmu erâ ši biac maickekac hâcne , ira kikefuŋfâc-ticne fârine jaŋe maŋzi â dâŋ fâri qizecnere sâcko Mamac mai ecneniŋmu . Mamac e ŋic iŋucne jaŋere ecneekac .
43004024	Anutu e Mâro fuŋgâtâne , irec e mai ecneeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe Mâro â dâŋ fâri qizec jahere ŋesiŋko mai ecnenšepieŋ . ”
43004025	Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No manakopac , Mesia fuaocte mukicne , šâŋene moc Kristo , eki fuarâ wiac sasawa mu bataniŋ enâreocmu . ”
43004026	Eme Jesuzi âzâcnewec : “ Dâŋ gazakopac , no hâcne ši . ”
43004027	Iŋuc muhame motecfâcne fisimbiŋ . Fisirâ ŋokachec muc manac ewec irec wareckembiŋ . Erâ wemo wiacte dâŋ âzâcnekomec , me weniŋucte âzâcnekomec , iŋuc muhuc wiocneniŋte manapie quŋkeme behembiŋ .
43004028	Eme ŋokac e opâ râqâc-ticne beherâ haeo gasacke rarâ ŋic šiŋuc jazawec :
43004029	“ Ŋoŋe warerâ ŋic moc honeniŋ , eki epo bapo irec dâŋ mutaniŋke-nare-fârekac . E Kristo wiac moc ? ”

43004035	Ŋaŋac šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ : ` Mosa 4 tarame nânâ fârine fuaocmu . Ž Á noni ine ŋazape mananiŋ : Ŋoŋe qâhâŋnerâ šâŋe fihuc gie honeniŋ , nânâ fârine fufua dameŋ šine hâcne maickekac .
43004036	Ro qânusuc gie baocmuzi furine roocmu , â fârinezi ju ju sanaŋte biŋe eocmu . Eme he sarac ewec â fârine rome fewec jahe mâmâc babafic erâ šeri enicmu .
43004037	Ehame dâŋ kecši sanaŋkeocmu : ` Moczi he sarac eekac , â moczi fârine rome feekac . Ž

43004040	Irec Jesurao fisirâ jaŋehec juocte hefârembiŋ . Eme Jesuzi mana-jarerâ šoaŋ gie bapa jajahec jaŋere haeo juwec .

43004042	Ehuc ŋokac šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Qanaŋ gore dâŋ binaŋte erâ manasiŋkembeneŋ , ši ine nâŋe nâŋâc micticnaonec dâŋ manarâ šiŋuc manapaŋkeŋgopeneŋ : Eki jâmbomac mâreŋ sâc ŋic nâŋâcne Bâbâpiaŋ . ”
43004043	Eme Jesu e jaŋehec gie bapa jajahec jurâ Galilaia mâreŋko rawec .

43004047	Eme Jesu e Judaia mâreŋkonec risierâ Galilaia mâreŋko mocwâc ware fisikac , iŋuc mupie manarâ kia e Kana haeo Jesurao rarâ ŋokâ-ticne hâmozo ehuc fowec irec jowame ranicte numucnewec .

43004051	Ehame motec jaŋe kiŋaŋ warerâ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Ŋokâge ɋiɋic qajec jukac . ”

43004053	Iŋuc mupie ŋiczi fuŋne kecšiŋuc manawec : Dameŋ ira hâcne Wofuŋzi sorecnuhuc mujec , “ Ŋokâge ɋiɋic qakac . ” Eme e jahacne â garikiŋfâc-ticne Jesu manasiŋke-fârembiŋ .

43005010	Irec Judaŋic jaŋe ŋic ɋiɋic qawec e šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Miŋecgac hombaŋko fofoge hâpokomec i mi eene . ”

43005013	Mupie ŋic biaŋkeweczi kâuc bawec . Jesu e ŋicguru ira domambiŋ jaŋere ŋondeŋko kamierâ rawec .
43005014	Izi šâhec Jesuzi ŋic e taha ufuŋko bâfuarâ uŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go sahacge biaŋkejec , eme wiac ŋemâc bâmâcne jâmbâŋ fua-garezacte sâqocne mocwâc mi bazemec . ”
43005015	Eme ŋic e Jesu hone tararâ ra Judaŋic šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋic bâpiaŋnukac šâŋene Jesu . ”

43010001	Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ , moc e lama jaŋere sapao feocte motâcko mi rašihuc mocko sac huckerâ huocmu , ere fiuc roro â soroŋ qaqa muzo .
43010002	Moc e motâcko raširâ feocmu , ere ine lama soŋaŋ-jeŋic muzo .
43010003	E fisime motâc soŋaŋzi honerâ motâc rocneocmu â lama jaŋe dâŋ hawari-ticne mananiŋmu . Eme lamafâc-ticne jaŋere šâŋe wirahuc sapaonec jowac-jopa wahaocmu .
43010004	E jahacne biŋefâc jowac-jopa-fâreme waharâ , dâŋ hawari-ticne manaeŋgopieŋte bâjâpeniŋmu .
43010005	Ŋic furune moc e ine mi bâjâpeniŋmu , e dâŋ hawari-ticne kâuc bahuc hâhâwic bacnerâ wiseniŋmu . ”
43010006	Jesu e dâŋ suŋsuŋne iŋuc mume jaŋe weniŋucte iŋuc mukac muhuc kâuc bambiŋ .
43010007	Eme Jesu e harierâ jazawec , “ Jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ , lama jaŋerao fefe irec motâc no .
43010008	No mi fuahape fuambiŋ jaŋe ine fiuc roro â soroŋ qaqa . Irec lama jaŋe dâŋjeŋic mi manambiŋ .
43010009	Motâc no hâcne . Moc e fotâcnurâ rašiocmu , e mi sipirickeocmu . E rašic wefuc ehuc nânâ mâriri bâfuaocmu .
43010010	Fiuc roro e lama qa sipiric erâ fiuc bawiseocte sawa fisiekac . No ine lama jaŋe juhâc qâhâmoniŋte nânâ bâfuape ɋaŋɋaŋ ɋâriaŋ fojareocte fisipo .
43010011	“ No soŋaŋ biaŋne . Soŋaŋ biaŋnezi lama jaŋere erâ juju-ticne qikiŋneocmu .
43010012	Soŋaŋ jabane , lama ru jeŋic mi juekaczi ine kâte qâto fisime honerâ lama behec-joparâ wiseocmu . Ehame kâte qâtozi lama ki bâtâtiec ejareocmu .
43010013	E soŋaŋ jabanere lama jaŋere manabâc mi eocmu .
43010014	No ine soŋaŋ biaŋne juekopac , eme Mamac â no hohonec mamanac eekoperec ,
43010015	irec sâcko no â gurufâc-nane hohonec mamanac eeŋgopeneŋ . Irec no lama jaŋere erâ juju-nane qikiŋnepemu .

43010018	Juju-nane moczi mi nowac roocmu , i no nahacne maŋte qikiŋnepemu . No juju-nane qikiŋnepemurâ â ropemurâ irec tâpiri mâmâc fonarekac . Iŋuc epemurâ Mamac-nanezi munarewec . ”
43010019	Jesu e dâŋ iŋuc mume Judaŋic jaŋe manarâ mocwâc mu qaqatarac embiŋ .
43010020	Ehuc bocjahazi šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ E demoŋzi ecneme maŋne sifuckekac , dâŋ mume wemocte manahuc juŋgopieŋ . ”

43010025	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec : “ No ŋazape mi mana šakieeŋgopieŋ . Mamac-nanere micte gie baekopac izi mutaniŋnuekac .

43010028	Eme juju sanaŋ bâfua-jarepe sisipiric tâmiric jurašihuc juniŋmu . Jaŋe nore meonec moczi babatarac-jopane mi fokac .

43011016	Eme Toma , šâŋene moc Didimo , eki motec âgofâcne šiŋuc jazawec : “ Nâŋâc mâmâc rarâ ehec hâmonšepeneŋ . ”

43011021	Bâfuarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Wofuŋ , go šira jutec muzac ɋanane mi hâmozac .

43011056	Eme taha ufuŋko Jesu basarâ šiŋuc muhuc nazaŋ gazaŋ embiŋ : “ Ŋoŋe weniŋuc muŋgopieŋ , e hombaŋte wareocmu me mâcne ? ”

43012001	Aakic hombaŋ juwicnao šoaŋ gie bapa 6 fohame Jesuzi Betania haeo ra fisiwec . E hae ira hâcne Lazaro hâmockonec bâɋârewec .

43012003	Ŋehapie Mariazi kiruŋ moc opâ âsu biaŋ furi sâko jâmbâŋ i rorâ Jesu kikene ruacnerâ qizec susuc-ticnezi bâkereŋkewec . Eme fic âsu biaŋ fifârewec .
43012004	Eme motec jaŋere âgo moc Juda Karioto haeonec docbapa ŋic , eki šiŋuc muwec :
43012005	“ Opâ âsu izi 30 kina kitâcneme ŋic hapetac jarepene sâckezac me ! ”
43012006	E dâŋ i hapetac jaŋere manasuhuc mi muwec , e moneŋ kânoŋ wirec-jeŋic bajuhuc moneŋ hume ro soŋsoŋ ejujec , irec muwec .
43012007	Eme Jesuzi muwec , “ Ŋoŋe ŋokac dâŋ mi mucneniŋ , e opâ âsu i sahac-nane ruacneme hâmope ducnuniŋte irec biŋe hâcne bajuwec .
43012008	Ŋic hapetac dameŋ sâc ŋoŋerao juhuc juniŋmu , no ine ŋoŋerao boc mi jupemu . ”
43012009	Eme Judaŋic bocjaha jaŋe hae ira jume manarâ ijaha fisimbiŋ . Erâ Jesure sawa mâcne , Lazaro hâmockonec bâɋârewec e mâmâc honeniŋte fisimbiŋ .
43012010	Eme irec taha bapa micne jaŋe Lazaro mâmâc qaniŋte dâŋgie bambiŋ .
43012011	Judaŋic bocjahazi ere erâ rarâ Jesurao qohotambiŋte iŋuc embiŋ .
43012012	Hae fureme ŋic guru sâko hombaŋte biac Jerusalem haeo fisimbiŋ jaŋe dâŋ biŋe šiŋuc manambiŋ : “ Jesu warehuc jukac . ”
43012013	Dâŋ i manarâ šariŋ bazu amec erâ hatao bâfuaniŋte rambiŋ . Erâ bâfuarâ ofac hecnehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Ohec , Wofuŋte micte ware-nârekac e mumbiaŋkenaŋ , Israe ŋicwofuŋ ohec ! ”
43012014	Jesu e doŋgi motecne bâfuacnepie fainao ŋehuc rawec . I findaŋdâŋ kecšiŋuc fokac irec sâcko ewec :
43012015	“ Zioŋte otâ , go mi hâwicguoc ; manakic , ŋicwofuŋgezi fakac , doŋgi motecnere âsio fakac . ”
43012016	Dâŋ i motecfâc-ticne jaŋe mârâc mi mana-hâmombiŋ . Juku Jesu sambâŋ tatamac-ticnao risie feme dâŋ irec manasurâ šiŋuc mana tarambiŋ : I ere qâreŋkekicnere sâc ijaha ecnembiŋ .
43012017	Jesu e Lazaro wiracneme šâŋeruŋkonec wahame honembiŋ ŋic guru sâko i jaŋe gâcne dâŋ binaŋ ejarembiŋ .
43012018	Eme mâsi irec biŋe manambiŋte bocjahazi hatao ra bâfuambiŋ hâcne .
43012019	Eme farisaio ŋic jaŋe jaŋackoaŋ šiŋuc muhuc muc manac embiŋ : “ Manaŋgopieŋ . ŋoŋe dâŋgie bâipiehapie ŋic mâmâc sasawa erao qohota-fâreŋgopieŋ ine ! ”
43012020	Judaŋic hombaŋte Jerusalem haeo fisimbiŋ jaŋere ŋondeŋko Grikŋic qâpuc moc moc mâmâc juhuc Anutu mai ecnembiŋ .
43012021	Eme jaŋe Filipo Besaida haeonec Galilaia mâreŋkonec erao rarâ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Ŋicbomboŋ , nâŋe Jesu honezo muŋgopeneŋ . ”
43012022	Mupie Filipozi Anderea âzâcneme mâmâc Jesurao rarâ dâŋ i âzâcnepic .
43012023	Âzâcnepire šiŋuc muwec : “ Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne huriri qâreŋ-ticne fua tâcneocte šâfo maickekac hâcne .
43012024	Jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ , jacgoŋ hândâŋ e mâreŋko mi hurâ mâc foku foocmu , mâreŋte nânâ eme ine fârine bocjaha fuaocmu .
43012025	Moc e juju-ticne âgo ecneme sifuckecneocmu , moc e mâreŋko juhuc juju-ticne râsi ecneme juju sanaŋte biŋe focneocmu .
43012026	Moc e nore kiŋaŋ qaqa ezo murâ bâjâpecnuzejec , eme no jupemuoa kiŋaŋ qaqa-nanezi juocmu . Moc e no kiŋaŋ qanareocmu , e Mamac-nanezi erickeocmu .
43012027	Ʒi maŋnane fâfârerâ ɋarac ɋarac qakac . Ehame weniŋuc mupemu ? ` Mamac go dameŋ maicnukac i bâsuecƷ iŋuc mupe ? Misac , iŋuc aricne , dameŋ i hâcne maicnuocte mukicne .
43012028	Irec Mamac go mutec šâŋe biŋegere huriri qâreŋ fua tâcnezejec . ” Mume sambâŋkonec dâŋ šiŋuc wahawec : “ I huriri qâreŋ-ticne fuawec erâ huriri qâreŋ jaha fua raocmu . ”
43012029	Eme ŋicguru domambiŋ jaŋe manarâ mumbiŋ , “ Ɋuŋ hejec . ” Á gâcnezi mumbiŋ , “ Aŋelo moczi dâŋ âzâcnejec . ”
43012030	Mupie Jesuzi micjeŋicko rorâ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Dâŋ i nahacnere mâcne ŋoŋere erâ fuajec .
43012031	Ʒi mâreŋko ââke râwiŋ dameŋ maickekacte mâreŋ širec ŋicbomboŋ e hetuŋkezo .
43012032	Mâreŋkonec bâfeŋnupie mâreŋ sâc ŋic fârec-jopape norao fisiniŋmu . ”
43012033	I hâmoc weniŋucne hâmoocmu irec dâŋ suŋsuŋne iŋuc muwec .
43012034	Mume ŋicguru domambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Nâŋe mitio dâŋ kecšiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : Kristo e mi hâmohuc jurašihuc juocmu . Eme goki wemocte šiŋuc mukic : ` Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e bâfeŋneniŋmu ' ? Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e mo ? ”
43012035	Eme Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikie-jarewec : “ Ʒoctamac e ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko dameŋ bembeŋne mac tamaeocmu . Irec dapâczi foŋŋopazacte šoctamac foŋarehame e maickerâ junšepieŋ . Moc e dapâcko rahuc hata mi hone taraocmu .
43012036	Irec šoctamac foŋarehame maŋzi sakarehuc kikefuŋfâc-ticne enšepieŋ . ” Jesu e dâŋ iŋuc murâ ra soŋsoŋko juwec .
43012037	Jesu e mâsi fuŋne fuŋne šâŋe fai-jeŋicko bame hone-bipiehuc sifu erao mi roweckembiŋ .
43012038	I porofete Jesajare dâŋ sanaŋkeocte iŋuc embiŋ . E dâŋ šiŋuc qâreŋkewec : “ Wofuŋ , biŋedâŋge mupene mozi mana šakieekac ? Á Wofuŋte me i morao fua taniŋkeekac ? ”
43012039	Erâ Jesure dâŋ mi mana šakiembiŋ i Jesajare dâŋqâreŋ moc fokacte embiŋ ine kecšiŋuc :
43012040	“ E šâŋe-jeŋic tiŋtuŋ barâ maŋjeŋic bâzickewec , jaŋe šâŋezi wiac hone taranšipiŋte , â maŋzi wiac mana taranšipiŋte , ehuc maŋjeŋic bârisiepie bâpiaŋ-jopazipore . ”
43012041	Jesaja dâŋ muwec , i Jesu sambâŋ tatamac-ticne honerâ muwec .
43012042	Eme micne bapa jaŋeraonec gâcne jaŋe Jesu manasiŋkembiŋ wâc . Erâ mufuapie farisaio jaŋe miti sakare-jarenšipiŋte hâwic-jopame hesoŋkembiŋ .
43012043	Jaŋe šâŋe biŋe-jeŋic ŋic jaŋerao waha qaqane ezacte manapie ŋemâckewec , â Anuturao waha qaqane ezacte manapie afeckewec .
43012044	Jesu e hahaŋne bahuc dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Moc e no manasiŋnuocmu , e no sawa mâcne , sorecnuwec e mâmâc manasiŋkeocmu .
43012045	Á moc e no honecnuocmuzi sorecnuwec e mâmâc honeocmu .
43012046	No šoc tatamaczi mâreŋko wahapo , eme moc e no manasiŋnuocmuzi dapâckonec wefuocmu .
43012047	Moc e dâŋnane manarâ beheme okacne mi râcnepemu , no ŋic okacne jarepemurâ mâcne , bâpiaŋ-jopapemurâ wahapo .
43012048	Moc e no qikiŋnuhuc dâŋnane beheocmu , e mumutara fuacneocmu , dâŋ muekopac izi juku dameŋ sâkoo mumutara ecneocmu .
43012049	No dâŋ i no nahacne maŋte mi muekopac , Mamac sorecnuwec e jahac dâŋ mufuapemurâ sâcmutâc enarewec .
43012050	Erâ no manakopac , micdâŋ-ticnezi juju sanaŋ bâfuaekac . Dâŋ muekopac i Mamaczi mutâcne-narewec sâc muekopac . ”
43013001	Aakic hombaŋ maickehame Jesuzi e jahacnere šiŋuc manawec : No mâreŋ beherâ Mamactao risie fepemurâ dameŋ bembeŋkekac . Iŋuc manarâ mâreŋko wiacfâc-ticne maŋjauŋ ejarewec , i ejare tarahuc hâmoocte muwec .
43013002	Eme ŋafere nânâ nâniŋte tumaŋnehapie wiac kecšiŋuc fuawec : Simoŋ ŋokâ-ticne Juda , Karioto haeonec , e Jesu doc baocte Sataŋzi maŋticnao qafeŋ râewec .
43013003	Á Jesu e šiŋuc manawec : Mamac e wiac sasawa furu qârârie-narekac , eme no Anuturaonec wahapozi mocwâc Anuturao risie fepemu .
43013004	Fuŋne iŋuc manahuc nânâ nâhuc ŋembiŋkonec faharerâ ŋaqi šora faine i hetararâ gie qoruc jomawec .
43013005	Erâ opâ râqâcko qame hume fuŋkerâ motecfâcne kike šure-jarewec . Ehuc gie qoruczi bâkereŋke-jarewec .
43013006	Ejare raku Simoŋ Petororao fisime šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go Wofuŋzi kike-nane šurezo mukic me ? ”
43013007	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Wiac ekopac irec fuŋne šiŋuczia mi manakomec , juku šâhecko manacmu . ”
43013008	Eme Petorozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Aricne , go kike-nane mi šure-jâmbâŋkecmu . ” Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Noni mi šurecgupe nohec maŋ šušuhuc mi jucmu . ”
43013009	Eme Petorozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Wofuŋ , murâ kike-nane sawa mâcne , me qizec-nane mâmâc šurec . ”
43013010	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Moc e opâ ruarâ šâhec kike-ticne sawa šureme sahacne ɋaɋacne fofâreocmu , eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ɋaɋackembiŋ , erâ ɋaɋacnea mi jufâreŋgopieŋ . ”
43013011	E doc bapa-ticne mana tarahuc šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe ɋaɋacnea mi jufâreŋgopieŋ . ”
43013012	Kike-jeŋic šure-fârerâ ŋaqi šora-ticne mocwâc heme hume waha ŋehuc šiŋuc jazawec : “ No wiac eŋarepac irec fuŋne manaŋgopieŋ me ?
43013013	Ŋoŋe Qaqazu â Wofuŋ munareeŋgopieŋ , erâ iŋeŋic jukopacte sâcne munareeŋgopieŋ .
43013014	Eme no Wofuŋ â Qaqazu-ŋeŋiczi kike-ŋeŋic šure-ŋarepacte ŋaŋaczia iŋuc jaha kike šušurec erahuc jupie sâckezejec .
43013015	Mâsi eŋarepac izi juju bapare ma qâreŋ-ŋeŋic eme i honehuc , eŋarepac irec sâc ehuc junšepieŋ .
43013016	No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mupe mananiŋ : Kiŋaŋ moteczi bomboŋ-ticnere sâc sirickerâ jujune i mi fokac , â sorekicnezi sorewec ere sâc sirickerâ jujune i wâc mi fokac .
43013017	Eme dâŋ i manapaŋkerâ irec sâcko jupie no ŋoŋere manape šerine eocmu .
43013018	No dâŋ mupe mâmâc sasawa mi rocŋopakac . No wenimoi rowosâec-ŋopapo i manakopac . Dâŋqâreŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac , i sanaŋkeocmu hâcne : Nânâ bâfâuc ecneekopac eki wâc bunaneo bakac .
43013019	Wiac i mi fuahame qanaŋ ŋazakopac , eme šâhec fuame , e Wofuŋzi qanaŋ manahuc muwec , nore iŋuc munšepieŋ .
43013020	No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape , moc e gie muŋarekicne ŋoŋe hezu hewâneŋ eŋareocmuzi gie rune no hezu hewâneŋ enareocmu , â moc e no enareocmuzi sorecnuwec e hezu hewâneŋ ecneocmu . ”
43013021	Jesu e dâŋ iŋuc murâ bu šašamaŋne fâuckezo eme mutaniŋkerâ šiŋuc jazawec : “ No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mupe mananiŋ , ŋoŋeraonec moczi no doc bacnuocmu . ”
43013022	Iŋuc mume motec jaŋe hohonec efârerâ , i more mukac , muhuc kâuc bambiŋ .
43013023	Eme motec moc Jesure maŋfuŋko ŋewec , e bufuŋ jâmbâŋ-ticne ,
43013024	e hâcne Simoŋ Petorozi mezi sâsâc ecnerâ muwec , “ Wiocnetec gazaoc , more mukac ? ”
43013025	Eme motec eki hâcne qizec-ticne Jesure amecko fohorerâ muwec , “ Wofuŋ go more mukic ? ”
43013026	Eme Jesuzi muwec , “ Poroŋ sicko âke uruckerâ râcnepe nâocmu ere hâcne mukopac . ” Iŋuc murâ poroŋ sicko âke uruckerâ Simoŋ ŋokâ-ticne Juda , Karioto haeonec , e râcneme nâwec .
43013027	Nâme Sataŋzi maŋne sakioŋkewec . Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Wiac ezo mukomec , i biac jaha ezemec . ”
43013028	Dâŋ iŋuc âzâcneme gâcne mâmâc ŋembiŋzi mi mana-hâmombiŋ .
43013029	Ehuc tucnezi šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Juda e moneŋ kânoŋ wirec-nâŋec bajukacte hombaŋte wiac moc furine baocte sorekac , me ŋic hapetac moneŋ jareocte mukac . ”
43013030	Eme Juda e poroŋ nârâ izia ŋafe fuaha rawec .
43013031	Juda rame Jesuzi motec gâcne šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ʒi Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e huriri qâreŋ-ticne fuakac , eme ere erâ Anuture huriri qâreŋ mâmâc fuakac .
43013032	Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋnezi Anuture huriri qâreŋ bâfuawecte Anutu e jahac Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne ere huriri qâreŋ iŋuc jaha bâfuaocmu , dameŋ mi šorahame biac bâfuaocmu .
43013033	Motecfâc-nane , no dameŋ bembeŋne mac moc ŋoŋehec jupemu . Eme šâhec basacnuniŋmu . Eme Judaŋic jazapo ijaha ŋoŋe ŋazape : No rapemu ijaha sâcne mi fâniŋmu .
43013034	Eme ši sâcmutâc dâŋ ɋâricne ŋazape : Maŋjauŋ eec enšepieŋ , noni maŋjauŋ eŋare warehuc jupo iŋuc jaha ŋaŋackoaŋ maŋjauŋ eec enšepieŋ .
43013035	Maŋjauŋ eec epie ŋic jaŋe honec-ŋopapie motecfâc-nane juŋgopieŋ ezejec . ”
43013036	Eme Simoŋ Petorozi wiocnerâ muwec , “ Wofuŋ , go wena racmu ? ” Eme Jesuzi muwec , “ No rapemu ijaha šiŋuczia sâcne mi fâcmu , juku šâhec ine fâzemec . ”
43013037	Eme Petorozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Wofuŋ , no wemocte šiŋuczia sâcne mi fâpemu ? No gore erâ juju-nane sâcne qikiŋnepemu . ”
43013038	Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go nore erâ jujuge qikiŋnezo mukomec me ? No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape : Qâqâczi mi dâŋehame goki jahec â moc mic bacnucmu .
43014001	“ Ŋoŋe fâfârerâ maŋŋeŋic mi gâckezejec . Anutu manasiŋkehuc no mâmâc manasiŋnunšepieŋ .
43014002	Mamac-nanere hae qizecko fic bocjaha ŋerakac . Iŋuc mi fome muzac , ŋeŋe hewâneŋke-ŋarezo rapemu , i moc ŋazazapo me ?
43014003	Eme ra ŋeŋe hewâneŋke-ŋarerâ mocwâc risie warerâ jowac-ŋopape rarâ no jupemuoa junšepieŋ .
43014004	Rapemu hata i honeeŋgopieŋ . ”
43014005	Mume Tomazi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go wena racmu , i nâŋe mi manaŋgopeneŋ , irec wemocko hata honenaŋmu . ”
43014006	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Hata â dâŋ fâri qizec â juju irec rune no . No nowarurâ Mamactao fifisi i mi fokac .
43014007	Ŋoŋe juwicnao no šâŋitacnurâ muzac Mamac-nane iŋuc jaha šâŋitanšapiŋ . Ʒi ine Mamac-nane šâŋitarâ mana taraŋgopieŋ . ”
43014008	Iŋuc mume Filipozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Go Mamac nâwotutec honerâ manapene taraocmu . ”
43014009	Eme Jesuzi muwec : “ Filipo , no dameŋ šora ŋoŋehec juhape go mi hone tarac-nukomec ? Moc e no honecnuekaczi Mamac honeekac . Eme go wemocte šiŋuc mukomec : ` Go Mamac nâwotutec honenaŋ ' ?
43014010	Mamaczi no maŋnuekac â noni Mamac maŋkeekopac i mi mana šakiekic me ? Dâŋ ŋazaekopac i nahacne maŋte mi ŋazaekopac , Mamaczi nore maŋko juhuc gie-ticne baekac .
43014011	Mamaczi no maŋnuekac â noni Mamac maŋkeekopac , dâŋ i manapie fârine ezejec . Me miczi mupe mi sâcŋopakacko wiac bapa-nanere erâ dâŋ i mana šakieniŋ .
43014012	“ No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mupe mananiŋ : No manasiŋnuocmuzi gie baekopac ijaha baocmu . Erâ i sawa mâcne , sâcnane jâuruhuc baocmu . No Mamactao fepemure iŋuc hâcne fuaocmu .
43014013	Eme ŋoŋe nore šâŋe bajuhuc numupie sâc mana-ŋarehuc epemu . I Mamacte mumuteŋ Ŋokâre erâ fuaocte iŋuc epemu .
43014014	Ʒâŋe-nane bajuhuc numu-narepie mana-ŋarehuc epemu .
43014015	Maŋŋeŋic nore qikiŋneeŋgopieŋko micnane reŋkeniŋmu .
43014016	Eme noni Mamac numucnepe neŋgoc ŋesiŋ-ŋeŋic moc soreme waharâ ŋoŋehec juhuc juocmu sanaŋ .
43014017	Dâŋ fâri qizecnere Mâro hâcne . I miti tâmiriczi rorone mi fokac . Jaŋe e mi hone taraeŋgopieŋ â e mi mana taraeŋgopieŋ . E ŋoŋehec juekaczi maŋŋeŋicko hurâ juocmu , irec ŋoŋe e kâuc mi baeŋgopieŋ .
43014018	No behec-ŋopape bekâ mâsiŋ erâ mi juniŋmu . No ŋoŋerao risie warepemu .
43014019	Dameŋ bembeŋne mac moc fokac , i tarame miti tâmiriczi mocwâc mi honecnuniŋmu . Ŋoŋe ine honecnuniŋmu . No juju sanaŋ jukopac , irec ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ɋâricne juraniŋmu .
43014020	Dameŋ ira , Mamaczi no maŋnuekac â noni ŋoŋe maŋŋopaekopac , â ŋoŋe no maŋnueŋgopieŋ i mana taraniŋmu .
43014021	“ Moc e micdâŋ-nane bajuhuc sâseocmu , eki maŋjauŋ enareocmu . Eme moc e no maŋjauŋ enareme Mamac-nanezi e iŋuc jaha maŋjauŋ ecneocmu , â no nahac wâc maŋjauŋ ecnehuc fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkecnepemu . ”
43014022	Iŋuc mume Juda Karioto haeonec ere wasezi wiocnerâ muwec : “ Wofuŋ , go weniŋuc erâ fuŋnege nâŋerao sawa bataniŋkehuc ŋic gâcne sâko jaŋe hesoŋke-jarezo mukic ? ”
43014023	Mume Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec : “ Moc e maŋjauŋ enareocmuzi dâŋnane mana rereŋ eocmu . Eme Mamac-nanezi e iŋuc jaha maŋjauŋ ecneocmu . Eme nâhe mâmâc erao fisirâ ŋeŋe juju enacmu .
43014024	Moc e maŋjauŋ mi enareocmuzi dâŋnane wemocko mana rereŋ eocmu . Erâ dâŋ ŋazaekopac i no nahacnaonec mâcne , i Mamac sorecnuwec eraonec .
43014025	“ No nahac ŋoŋehec juhuc dâŋ iŋucne ŋaza qazuc eekopac .
43014026	Eme neŋgoc ŋesiŋ Tiri Mâro hâcne e Mamaczi nore micte soreme waharâ dâŋ sasawa ŋaza qazuc eŋareocmu , â noni ŋazaekopac i heɋâre-ŋare-fâreocmu .
43014027	No merâfâc-nane wama ŋarekopac , ŋic wama mâcne , no nahacne wama jâmbâŋ ŋarekopac . Irec maŋŋeŋic mi fâfârerâ gâckezejec .
43014028	No kecšiŋuc ŋazape manambieŋ : ` No rarâ juku ŋoŋerao mocwâc risiepemu . Ž Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic nore qikiŋnerâ muzac , ine Mamactao fepemu i manarâ bubiaŋ bâfuanšapiŋ . Mamac e nore femicne jukacte manasuhuc iŋuc enšapiŋ .
43014029	Ʒi fârine mi fuaha qanaŋ ŋazakopac , irec fuame honerâ mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic sanaŋkezejec .
43014030	No ši dâŋ bocjaha mi šuhuckerâ ŋazapemu . Mâreŋ širec ŋicbomboŋ wareocte šawiekac , warerâ norao hetakireocmu .
43014031	Eme Mamac maŋjauŋ ecnehuc gie munarewec baekopac i miti tâmiriczi hone taraniŋte faharepie ranaŋ .
43015001	“ No waiŋjâc fuŋqizecne jâmbâŋ , â Mamac-nanezi waiŋ gie rune .
43015002	Tieŋne moc norao foipiehuc fârinehec mi eme qâtâcne behec eocmu , â tieŋne moc fârinehec fome gie bacneme soka biaŋ eocte soŋaŋkeocmu .
43015003	Ŋoŋe ine miti ŋazape manahuc biac ɋaɋackembiŋ juŋgopieŋ hâcne .
43015004	Eme ŋoŋe no maŋnupie noni ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha maŋŋopapemu . Waiŋ tieŋnezi jâcnehec šušuhuc mi fohuc e jahackoaŋ sawa fârinehec mi eocmu . Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha no mi maŋnuhuc wemocko fârinehec eniŋmu .
43015005	Waiŋjâc fuŋqizecne no , tieŋ taeŋne ŋoŋe . Moc e no maŋnuhame noni e maŋkepemu , eme iŋucnezi fârine sâkohec eocmu . Ŋoŋe no tâmiric juhuc wiac eene i mi fokac .
43015006	Moc e no mi maŋnume e behezo , eme waiŋ tieŋne behepie ɋaŋame qâzuckerâ behepie šocko šaekac , sâc ijaha ecnezo .
43015007	Ŋoŋe no maŋnuhuc dâŋnane maŋkeniŋmu , eme wiac irec me irec numupie fua-ŋareocmu .
43015008	Ŋoŋe fârine sâkohec ehuc motec jâmbâŋfâc-nane erâ jupie Mamac-nanere mumuteŋ fuaocmu .
43015009	“ Mamaczi no maŋjauŋ enareekac , iŋuc jaha noni ŋoŋe maŋjauŋ eŋareekopac . Eme ŋoŋe nore maŋjauŋkoa junšepieŋ .
43015010	Micdâŋ-nane reŋkehuc ine nore maŋjauŋko juniŋmu , no iŋuc jaha Mamac-nanere micdâŋ reŋkehuc ere maŋjauŋko juekopac .
43015011	Nore bubiaŋzi ŋoŋerao fotâcneme ŋoŋerezi fufusuc foocte dâŋ ši ŋaza-fârekopac . Erâ ŋoŋerao fohuc fua sawec ezejec .
43015012	Micdâŋ-nane kecšiŋuc ŋazakopac : Noni maŋjauŋ eŋareekopac , iŋuc jaha ŋaŋaczia maŋjauŋ eec enšepieŋ .
43015013	Moc e âgofâcne jaŋere riŋ rohuc juju-ticne qaisockeocmu , irec maŋjauŋ fekicne sâko muzo .
43015014	Gie muŋareekopac i bapie honec-ŋopape âgofâc-nane eniŋmu .
43015015	No dameŋ ši kiŋaŋ qaqa mocwâc mi muŋarekopac , mana-ŋarepe âgofâc-nane eŋgopieŋ . Kiŋaŋ qaqazi bomboŋ-ticnere maŋko dâŋ foekac i mi manaekac . Noni ine Mamac-naneraonec dâŋ manapo sâc mufuarâ ŋaza-fârepore honec-ŋopape âgofâc-nane eŋgopieŋ .
43015016	ŋoŋe no mi rowosâecnumbiŋ , noni ŋoŋe rowosâec-ŋopapo , erâ ra juhuc fârine bâfuaniŋte muŋarepo . Eme fârine bâfuapie fofonehec ezejec . Iŋuc erâ nore šâŋe bajuhuc Mamac numucnepie sâc ŋareocmu .
43015017	Maŋjauŋ eec enšepieŋ , micdâŋ ine hâcne ŋazakopac .
43015018	“ Miti tâmiriczi qaisoc-ŋopapie šiŋuc munšepieŋ : ` Wofuŋ e mârâcko iŋuc hâcne fuŋkerâ qaisockembiŋ . Ž
43015019	Miti tâmiric jaŋere guruo rašipie muzac âgo eŋarenšapiŋ . No ine jaŋere guruonec rowosâec-ŋopape eebapa-jeŋic râpeckembiŋte qaisoc-ŋopaeŋgopieŋ .
43015020	No dâŋ moc kecšiŋuc ŋazapo irec manasunšepieŋ : Kiŋaŋ qaqazi bomboŋ-ticnere sâc sirickerâ jujune mi fokac . Jaŋe no râsi enarembiŋko ŋoŋe râsi jaha eŋareniŋmu , jaŋe nore dâŋ mana maŋ embiŋko ŋoŋere dâŋ iŋuc jaha mana maŋ eniŋmu .
43015021	Sorecnuwec e mi šâŋitaeŋgopieŋte nore erâ iŋuc hâcne eŋareniŋmu .
43015022	No jaŋerao mi waharâ fuŋne mi jazape muzac kiŋ tâmiric junšapiŋ . ši ine kiŋjeŋic wemocko murârâŋneniŋmu .
43015023	Moc e no qaisocnuekaczi Mamac-nane iŋuc jaha qaisockeekac .
43015024	No ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko mâsi sâko , ŋiczi mi bapane , i mi bazapo muzac kiŋ tâmiric junšapiŋ . ši ine bape hone-fâre-bipiehuc no qaisocnuhuc Mamac-nane iŋuc jaha qaisockeeŋgopieŋ .
43015025	Iŋuc epie mitio dâŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac , i sanaŋkekac hâcne : ` Jaŋe oma jâmbâŋ qaisocnumbiŋ . Ž
43015026	Neŋgoc ŋesiŋ , dâŋ fâri qizecnere Mâro hâcne , Mamactao jukac , e sorepe Mamactaonec waharâ fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkeocmu .
43015027	Erâ ŋoŋe gie fuŋkepoonec nohec juwarembiŋte iŋuc jaha fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkenšepieŋ .
43016001	“ Juku wiac eŋarepie manapie ririsi ezacte dâŋ i qanaŋ ŋazakopac .
43016002	Jaŋe mitific sakare-ŋareniŋmu . Erâ wâc dameŋ moc maickeocmu , ira Anuture gie baŋgopeneŋ muhuc qâhâmoc-ŋopaniŋmu .
43016003	Jaŋe Mamac mecne no mecne mi šâŋitac-nâfoeŋgopieŋte iŋuc eniŋmu .
43016004	No dâŋ qanaŋ ŋazakopac , i sanaŋkeme munšepieŋ : Eki mârâc jaha nâzâwec hâcne . Dâŋ i dameŋ-nane šoricne fohame mârâc biac mi ŋazapo .
43016005	“ Ʒi ine sorecnuwec erao fezo ehape ŋoŋeraonec moczi moc šiŋuc mi wio-narekac : ` Go wena racmu ? Ž
43016006	Dâŋ iŋucne ŋazakopacte mâc busâqoczi maŋŋeŋic fusucmakac .
43016007	No dâŋ jâmbomac mupe mananiŋ : Risie fepemu i ŋoŋerao fârine fuaocte fepemu . Mi fezapo muzac , neŋgoc ŋesiŋzi mi wahazac . Ferâ ine sorepe wahaocmu .
43016008	Waharâ ŋic fuŋne bataniŋke-jareme šiŋuc mananiŋmu : Kiŋ fokac â tiŋke biaŋ fokac â okacne dâŋ mumutara fokac .
43016009	Kiŋte fuŋne šiŋucko mananiŋmu : Jaŋe no mi manasiŋnueŋgopieŋ .
43016010	Tiŋke biaŋte fuŋne šiŋucko mananiŋmu : No Mamactao risie fepe mocwâc mi honecnuniŋmu .
43016011	Okacne dâŋ mumutara irec fuŋne šiŋucko mananiŋmu : Mâreŋ širec ŋicbomboŋ okacne dâŋ biac mutaracnekicne .
43016012	“ Dâŋ ŋaŋazane bocjaha fokac , erâ dameŋ šiŋuczia ŋazape wemocko amecke-fâreniŋmu .
43016013	Dâŋ fâri qizecnere Mâro eki ine waharâ dâŋ fâri qizecnere šâkâŋko bâutuc-ŋopaocmu . E jahacne maŋte dâŋ mi ŋazaocmu , mutâcnecnekicne sâc ŋazaocmu , erâ juku wiac fuaocmu i wâc mufua-ŋareocmu .
43016014	Dâŋ i no nahacne rowaŋkonec rorâ mujaŋgeŋke-ŋareme nore huriri qâreŋ fuaocmu .
43016015	Mamactao wiac fokac Irec rune no . Irec hâcne mupac , ` Nore rowaŋkonec rorâ mujaŋgeŋke-ŋareocmu . '
43016016	“ Dameŋ bembeŋne fokac , i tarame rape basacnuniŋmu . Erâ irec faicnao dameŋ bembeŋne jaha wâc fokac , i tarame warepe honecnuniŋmu . ”
43016017	Iŋuc mume motec jaŋe nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Weniŋucte dâŋ kecšiŋuc mukac ? ` Dameŋ bembeŋne fokac , i tarame rape basacnuniŋmu , erâ irec faicnao dameŋ bembeŋne jaha wâc fokac , i tarame warepe honecnuniŋmu . Ž Á moc šiŋuc mukac : ` Mamactao fepemu . Ž ”
43016018	Iŋuc murâ harierâ mumbiŋ : ` à ` Dameŋ bembeŋne fokac , Ʒ iŋuc wemocte mukac , nâŋe kâuc baŋgopeneŋ . ”
43016019	Wiocnezo epie Jesuzi hone tarac-joparâ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Dâŋ kecšiŋuc ŋazapacte muc manac eŋgopieŋ , ` Dameŋ bembeŋne fokac , i tarame rape basacnuniŋmu , erâ irec faicnao dameŋ bembeŋne fokac , i tarame warepe honecnuniŋmu . Ž
43016020	No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape : Ŋoŋe ki mamakuc ehapie miti tâmiriczi šeri eniŋmu . Ŋoŋe busâqocko juniŋmu , ehame busâqoc-ŋeŋiczi ŋerisieme bubiaŋ fuaocmu .
43016021	Ŋokac moc e motec roocte dameŋne maickeme šâic manaocmu . Izi motec rome šâic omaeme , ɋâric fuajec irec bubiaŋ manaocmu .
43016022	Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha dameŋ šiŋuczia bušâichec juniŋmu . Juhapie mocwâc risierâ honec-ŋopape bubiaŋ bâfuaniŋmu . Eme bubiaŋ i moczi mi qâsua-ŋareocmu .
43016023	Eme dameŋ ira wiac mocte mi kâuc barâ wio-nareniŋmu . No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape : Ŋoŋe Mamac wiac mocte numucnepie šâŋe-nanere erâ ŋareocmu .
43016024	Juwarembiŋ ira nore šâŋe bajuhuc mi numu jumbieŋ . ši ine numurâ ropie bubiaŋ-ŋeŋiczi fua sawec erâ fufuse fozejec .
43016025	“ Dâŋ ŋaza warehuc jupo i suŋsuŋne qahuc ŋazapo . Juku dameŋ moc maickeocmu ira ine dâŋ suŋsuŋne mi muhuc , Mamacte fuŋne mâc mutaniŋkerâ ŋazapemu .
43016026	Dameŋ ira šâŋe-nane bajuhuc numupie noni ŋoŋe bâsâoc-ŋopahuc Mamac ââzâcne i mi epemu .
43016027	No Mamactaonec wahapo , dâŋ i mana šakiehuc maŋjauŋ enareeŋgopieŋte Mamac e jahac wâc iŋuc jaha maŋjauŋ eŋareekac .
43016028	No Mamac beherâ mâreŋko wahapo , eme ši mâreŋ beherâ Mamactao mocwâc fekopac . ”
43016029	Iŋuc mume motec jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Ʒi dâŋ suŋsuŋne mi muhuc mâc mutaniŋkerâ nâzâkomec hâcne .
43016030	Irec gore šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Ŋic jaŋe mu wioc mi egarehapie go gahaczia wiac sasawa mana-fâreekic , go Anuturaonec wahameŋ i mana šakieeŋgopeneŋ . ”
43016031	Mupie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe miŋecne mana šakieŋgopieŋ me ?
43016032	Dameŋ moc fokac , i biac maickeme no behecnurâ siŋsaŋ qarâ ficŋeŋic sâc rafâreniŋmu . Erâ behecnupie buc mi jupemu , Mamaczi nohec jukacte buc jâmbâŋ mi jupemu .
43016033	Nore wamazi ŋoŋerao foocte dâŋ iŋucne ŋazakopac . Ŋoŋe mâreŋko šârâ hâriŋ faio jueŋgopieŋ , eme noni mâreŋte micne momori fozukopacte ŋoŋe hâbi-ŋeŋichec junšepieŋ . ”
43017001	Jesu e dâŋ i mutararâ sambâŋko fime feha šiŋuc muhuc numuwec : “ Mamac , dameŋ maickekac . Go Ŋokâgere huriri qâreŋ bâfuatec Ŋokâzi iŋuc jaha gore huriri qâreŋ bâfuazejec .
43017002	Go e mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere rusâko râemeŋ , ehuc ŋic erao ŋec-jopameŋ sâc jaŋe juju sanaŋ bâfua-jareocte mucnemeŋ .
43017003	Juju sanaŋte fuŋne ine šiŋuc fokac : Go Anutu fârine mocjaha â soremeŋ , Jesu Kristo hâcne , ŋic jaŋe iŋuc mana tarac-nâfopie juju sanaŋ fua-jareocmu .
43017004	Gie munaremeŋ i baku batarape mâreŋko huriri qâreŋge fuakac .
43017005	O Mamac , mâreŋ mi fuahame gohec sambâŋ tatamac-nanehec jupo , ijaha ši mocwâc bârisie-naretec rojuzepac .
43017006	“ Guru sâkoonec ŋic nore bâwosâec-jopameŋ jaŋe biŋedâŋge mujaŋgeŋke-jarepo . I gore biŋe juhapie nore qikiŋ-jopameŋ , eme jaŋe gore dâŋ ropie maŋjeŋic ewec .
43017007	Wiac fonarekac i goraonec sasawa , jaŋe i mana taraŋgopieŋ .
43017008	Go dâŋ naremeŋ i jarepe ro sakarec embiŋ . Ehuc goraonec wahapo i manapaŋkembiŋ , â go gahac gie munaremeŋ i mana šakiembiŋ .
43017009	“ No jaŋere erâ numu-garekopac . Miti tâmiric jaŋere erâ mi numu-garekopac , naremeŋ jaŋere sawa erâ numu-garekopac , jaŋe gore biŋe hâcne .
43017010	Nore biŋezi gore biŋe â gore biŋezi nore biŋe . Eme maŋjeŋicko huriri qâreŋ-nane fuawec fokac .
43017011	No mâreŋko juju-nane tarakac , jaŋe ine mâreŋko šuhuckerâ juhapie no gorao fâzo ekopac . Tiri Mamac , biŋedâŋge naretec jazapo , eme go hemiriŋ-jopatec dâŋ irec maŋnao junšepieŋ . Eme nâhâc maŋ mocjaha juekoperec , iŋuc jaha jaŋe maŋ mocjaha junšepieŋ .
43017012	Jaŋehec jupo sâc biŋedâŋge naremeŋ izi hemiriŋ-jopape irec maŋnao jumbiŋ . Ehuc soŋaŋ-jopape moc mi sifuckembiŋ . Dâŋqâreŋ sanaŋkeocte hârâcte biŋe mocjahazi sipirickewec .
43017013	Ʒi gorao fâzo ehuc šira mâreŋko dâŋ iŋuc gazape nore bubiaŋzi jaŋerao fotâcnerâ ɋârâŋkeme bajunšepieŋ .
43017014	No dâŋge jarepe bajupie mâreŋte biŋe jaŋe qaisoc-jopaeŋgopieŋ . No nahac mâreŋte biŋe mi juekopac , iŋuc jaha jaŋe mâreŋte biŋe mi jueŋgopieŋte iŋuc hâcne ejareeŋgopieŋ .
43017015	Go mâreŋkonec rocjopacmurâ mâcne , sâqocnere ŋezic-jopacmurâ gazakopac .
43017016	No gâtâ-nane mâreŋko mi bawec , iŋuc jaha jaŋe gâtâ-jeŋic mâreŋko mi bawec .
43017017	Gore dâŋ fâri qizecnezi maŋjeŋic furu batec fozejec . Gore mitizi dâŋ fâri qizecne hâcne .
43017018	Goki no mâreŋko gie munaremeŋ , iŋuc jaha noni jaŋe mâreŋko gie mujarepo .
43017019	Jaŋe dâŋ fâri qizecnezi maŋjeŋic furu bame juniŋte no nahac wâc jaŋere erâ maŋsahac-nane bâtirirâ râekopac .
43017020	“ Erâ no jaŋere sawa mi numu-garekopac , miti jazapie manasiŋnuniŋmu jaŋere mâmâc numu-garekopac .
43017021	Jaŋe maŋwirec erâ juniŋte gazakopac . Mamac , go no maŋnuekic â noni go maŋguekopac , iŋuc jaha jaŋe nâhâc maŋnâfonšepieŋ . Iŋuc epie miti tâmiric jaŋe gahac sorecnutec wahapo i manapaŋkenšepieŋ .
43017022	Nâhâc maŋ mocjaha juekoperec , iŋuc jaha jaŋe maŋ mocjaha erâ junšepieŋ . Iŋuc juniŋte hâcne huriri qâreŋ naremeŋ ijaha jarepo .
43017023	No maŋjopahape go maŋnutec jaŋe maŋzi šâšâfic ehuc hâcbuc erâ junšepieŋ . Iŋuc jupie miti tâmiriczi goki sorecnutec wahapo i mana šakienšepieŋ , â no maŋzi šâficnuhuc jaŋe mâmâc šâfic-jopaekic , i wâc manapaŋkenšepieŋ .
43017024	Mamac , naremeŋ ŋic i jaŋe no jupemuoa juniŋte mukopac . Eme mâreŋ hobeteŋne mi fuahame maŋjauŋ enarehuc sambâŋ tatamac tahacnumeŋ , i hâcne nohec juhuc hone aŋac enšepieŋ .
43017025	Mamac , tiŋne rune , ŋic jaŋe mi mana taracgumbiŋ , noni ine mana taracguekopac , erâ kikefuŋfâc-nane jaŋe gahac sorecnutec wahapo i manapaŋkeeŋgopieŋ .
43017026	No biŋedâŋge mutaniŋke-jarepo erâ mutaniŋke-jarehuc jupemu . Eme maŋjauŋ no enaremeŋ ijaha jaŋerao fome maŋjopahuc jupemu . ”
43018001	Jesu e nunumu dâŋ i muku mufârerâ motecfâcne rocjopame haeonec hurâ Kidoroŋ opâ herâ , mâreŋ mocko jufu gie fowec , ira rambiŋ .
43018002	Jesu â motecfâcne ira gâbâ tumaŋne jumbieŋte Juda docbapa ŋic e jufu i honewec wâc .
43018003	Eme ira hâcne juhapie Judazi kiaraonec momori erâ taha bapa micne â farisaio ŋic jaŋeraonec motec rocjopame waha lambe â šika barâ rambiŋ .
43018004	Eme Jesu e wiac ecneniŋmu i mana-fârehuc jufu tofanao ra bâfuac-joparâ wio-jarewec : “ Ŋoŋe mo basaŋgopieŋ ? ”
43018005	Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ , “ Jesu Nazarete rune . ” Mupie muwec , “ No hâcne ši . ” Ehame Juda docbapa ŋic e ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko domawec .
43018006	Eme “ no hâcne ši ” Jesuzi iŋuc jazame jaŋe rârâpe rahuc rândiŋke qambiŋ .
43018007	Iŋuc epie hâsine wio-jarerâ muwec : “ ŋoŋe mo basaŋgopieŋ ? ” Eme mumbiŋ , “ Jesu Nazarete rune . ”
43018008	Mupie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec : “ No ŋazapac i , no hâcne ši . No basacnuŋgopieŋko keci jaŋe behec-jopaniŋ . ”
43018009	Iŋuc eme dâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec i sanaŋkewec : “ Naremeŋ jaŋe soŋaŋ-jopape moc mi sifuckembiŋ . ”
43018010	Eme Simoŋ Petoro e sâqe bajuwec i becsahackonec unuckerâ taha bapa sâko kiŋaŋ motec-ticne hazecne fâreopec i qatarawec . Motec šâŋene Maiko .
43018011	Iŋuc eme Jesuzi Petoro šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Sâqege becsahacko râec huoc . Me šâic guru Mamac-nanezi râe-narekac , i qikiŋnepemurâ mukic ? ”
43018012	Eme soŋaŋ-jeŋiczi mume momori â Judaŋic motecfâc-jeŋic jaŋe Jesu rorâ mene qarâ
43018013	Hanasire ficko barambiŋ . Eme dameŋ ira Judaŋic taha bapa sâko-jeŋic juwec , šâŋene Kaifa , eki Hanasire otâ bawec .
43018014	Kaifa eki hâcne Judaŋic šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋicguru nâŋâc sipiricke-fârenšipeŋte mocjahazi âkehoc-nâporâ hâmome tarazejec . ”
43018015	Simoŋ Petoro â motec âgo-ticne moc jahe Jesu barahapie šâhec rapic . Eme âgo-ticne e ine taha bapa sâkozi hone jujecte Jesu bâjâperâ ficmaŋko mâmâc rašimbiŋ .
43018016	Petoro eki ine sacrâpeo domawec . Eme âgo-ticnezi taha bapa sâkore ficko jujujecte hurâ sacmotâc soŋaŋ naru e âzâcneme Petoro motâc rocneme sacmaŋko rašiwec .
43018017	Eme motâc soŋaŋ naru eki Petoro honerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ŋic kecocnirec motecfâc jaŋere guruonec go moc ine hâcne . ” Eme eki muwec , “ No aricne . ”
43018018	Eme kiŋaŋ motec â momori jaŋe mâmâteŋte šoc ruqerâ ruahuc domahapie Petoro e ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko rarâ iŋuc jaha šoc ruawec .
43018019	Eme taha bapa sâkozi Jesu motec rocjopawec â miti muwec , irec mu indiŋ ecnewec .
43018020	Ecneme Jesuzi dâŋ kecšiŋuc bâtikiecnewec : “ No dâŋ hofao tâtâc muekopac , Judaŋic mitificko â taha ufuŋko tumaŋnehapie dâŋ jaza qazuc eekopac , soŋsoŋ mi muekopac .
43018021	Irec wemocte no wio-narekic ? Dâŋ jazape manaeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ejaretec muekopac sâc gazapie manac . ”
43018022	Iŋuc mume kiŋaŋ motec doma rambiŋ jaŋeraonec moczi Jesu maucnao qahuc muwec , “ Go taha bapa sâko dâŋ iŋucne wemocte âzâcnekomec ? ”
43018023	Eme Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Dâŋ hehesic mukopacko fuŋne mutec manape , â tiŋne mukopacko wemocte nukomec ? ”
43018024	Eme Hanasizi mume Jesu mene qarâ taha bapa sâko Kaifa erao barambiŋ .
43018025	Eme Simoŋ Petoro e ine šoc ruahuc domahame wiocnerâ mumbiŋ , “ Motecfâc-ticne jaŋere guruonec go moc ine hâcne mecne ? ” Eme mic barâ muwec , “ No aricne . ”
43018026	Mume taha bapa sâkore kiŋaŋ motec moc , Petorozi hazecne qatarawec ere qomâ , eki šiŋuc muwec : “ Á go jufuo ehec mâmâc jupie honecgupac . ”
43018027	Eme Petoro e mic bame izia qâqâczi dâŋewec .
43018028	Hae fureme Jesu Kaifare fickonec bawaharâ kiarao barambiŋ . Judaŋic jaŋe ine wâwânâŋ erâ aakic hombaŋko bâtâcko junšipiŋte kiare ficko mi fembiŋ .
43018029	Ehuc hae šoŋao domapie Pilatozi šaeo waharâ wio-jarerâ muwec : “ Ŋic keci wemo kiŋte bawareŋgopieŋ ? ”

43018031	Mupie Pilatozi šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋaŋacne sâcmutâc dâŋ sâcko dâŋticne mutaracneniŋ me . ” Eme Judaŋic jaŋe mumbiŋ , “ Nâŋe ŋic hâmocko rârâec-jopare aka henârekicne . ”
43018032	Judaŋic jaŋe iŋuc epie Jesu e jahac hâmoc-ticnere dâŋ muwec , hata i âke fuawec .
43018033	Eme Pilatozi ficmaŋko ferâ Jesu hefârerâ muwec : “ Go jâmbomac Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ me ? ”
43018034	Eme Jesuzi muwec , “ Dâŋ i gahacne maŋte mukic me gâcnezi micgao râepie mukic ? ”
43018035	Mume Pilatozi muwec , “ Wiac no Judaŋic me ? Go gahacne ŋicfâc â taha bapa micne jaŋe norao râecguŋgopieŋ . Go wemo emeŋ ? ”
43018036	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc muwec : “ No mâreŋ ŋicwofuŋ aricne , mâreŋ ŋicwofuŋ juzapo muzac momorifâc-nane jaŋe šikazi ŋezicnuhapie Judaŋic jaŋe wemocko rocnunšapiŋ . No ine mâreŋ ŋicwofuŋ aricne . ”
43018037	Eme Pilatozi muwec : “ Eme go ŋicwofuŋ fuŋmoc ? ” Mume Jesuzi muwec , “ Ine hâcne mukomec , no ŋicwofuŋ fuŋmoc . No dâŋ fâri qizecne mutaniŋkepemurâ mâreŋko waharâ fuapo . Eme moc e dâŋ fâri qizecne jauŋkeocmuzi dâŋnane âgo ecneocmu . ”
43018038	Eme Pilatozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Dâŋ fâri qizecne i wemo wiac moc ? ” Iŋuc murâ šaeo mocwâc hurâ Judaŋic šiŋuc jazawec : “ No ŋic kecširec kiŋ basakopac .
43018039	Hata-ŋeŋic moc fokac . Ŋoŋe aakic hombaŋko mupie no kâpâcwâru ŋic moc akicke-ŋareekopac . Eme ši manapie sâckeme Judaŋic ŋicwofuŋ-ŋeŋic akickepe juŋarezejec . ”
43018040	Eme jaŋe harierâ owackehuc mumbiŋ : “ Aricne , e mâcne , Baraba akicke-nârec . ” Baraba e ine šikaŋic .
43019001	Eme Pilatozi mume momori jaŋe Jesu becsahac biriŋneheczi qambiŋ .
43019002	Qarâ muc šârâneheczi hendiŋ ba akic erâ qizecnao hecnepie huwec â ŋaqi bâbâroŋ mâmâc hecnepie huwec .

43019004	Eme Pilatozi Judaŋic jaŋerao mocwâc hurâ muwec , “ Honeniŋ , no ŋoŋerao jowa wahakopac , no kiŋticne basakopacte ŋaŋac fuŋne-ticne honeniŋ . ”
43019005	Eme Jesu e muchendiŋ â ŋaqi bâbâroŋ , wiac iŋucnehec waha domame Pilatozi jowaturâ muwec : “ Ŋic mac ši honeniŋ . ”

43019010	Iŋuc eme Pilatozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go dâŋ mi nazakomec me ? Noni mupe jucmu me mupe maripoŋko hâmocmu irec tâpiri râe-narekicne , i mi manakic me ? ”
43019011	Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Mâc muzac go nore dâŋ wemocko munšaŋ , nore dâŋ mumure faicnec tâpiri qikiŋne-ŋarekicnere mukomec hâcne . Irec gorao râecnukac ŋic ere kiŋzi gore jâurukac . ”
43019012	Dâŋ i manarâ Pilatozi Jesu akickezo mume Judaŋic jaŋe owa ruruckerâ mumbiŋ : “ Go ŋic e akickerâ Sisare ª âgo mocwâc mi jucmu . Moc e jahacnere ŋicwofuŋ muhuc Sisa âkehockeocmu . ”
43019013	Pilatozi dâŋ i manarâ mume Jesu jowa wahapie dâŋ mumutara ŋeŋe-ticnao waha ŋewec . Ŋeŋe i qânâ šaeo râekicne , eme šae irec šâŋe Judaŋic jaŋe Gabata mujumbieŋ .
43019014	Eme Judaŋic jaŋe hae fureme aakic hombaŋ ŋeniŋte teuŋko rašimbiŋ . Ehame qâqâtâc bembeŋkeha Pilato e ŋeŋe-ticnao ŋehuc Judaŋic šiŋuc jazawec : “ Honeniŋ , ŋicwofuŋ-ŋeŋic ši . ”
43019015	Mume jaŋe owa ruruckerâ mumbiŋ : “ E arictac eoc , e arictac eoc , maripoŋko feoc . ” Eme Pilatozi muwec : “ Hâc , eme ŋicwofuŋ-ŋeŋic mupe maripoŋko hâmoocte muŋgopieŋ me ? ” Mume taha bapa micne jaŋe dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnembiŋ : “ Nâŋe ŋicwofuŋ-nâŋec moc aricne , Sisa mocjahazi junarekac . ”
43019016	Eme Pilatozi mana urue-jarerâ Jesu maripoŋko hâmoocte qikiŋne-jarewec .
43019017	Eme momori jaŋe Jesu rorâ maripoŋ râcnepie hâpome mâreŋ moc šâŋene Utusiec , Judadâŋko Goligata , ira barambiŋ .
43019018	Bararâ maripoŋko qambiŋ . Erâ sâqocne bapa jajahec mâmâc jofarâ moc ŋifec , moc ŋifec , â Jesu šâšâŋiŋko , iŋuc biric-jopambiŋ .
43019019	Eme Pilatozi mume Jesure qizec botâŋko maripoŋko qâreŋ kecšiŋuc râembiŋ : “ Jesu Nazarete haeonec Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ . ”
43019020	Jesu qambiŋ mâreŋ i hae bembeŋko fowecte Judaŋic bocjahazi ira rac warec ehuc qâreŋ i wosembiŋ . Eme qâreŋ i Judadâŋko â Romadâŋko â Grikdâŋko râekicne .
43019021	Eme Judaŋic jaŋere taha bapa micne jaŋe Pilato šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Go Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ iŋuc mi qâreŋkec E jahacne muwec , no Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ , iŋuc qâreŋkec . ”

43019023	Eme momori jaŋe Jesu maripoŋko qarâ ŋaqi-ticne faine bâtâcnepie jahec â jahec eme ru sâc embiŋ . Á ŋaqi-ticne maŋne hâfâ iŋucne oorâŋ fukicnere

43019025	Momori jaŋe iŋuc hâcne embiŋ . Jesure maripoŋ fuŋko ine šiŋuc domambiŋ : Neŋgoc-ticne â neŋgoc-ticnere qo , erâ Maria Kelopa ere ŋonâŋ , â Maria Madala haeonec .
43019026	Eme Jesu e neŋgoc-ticne â motec bufuŋ-ticne domapire honec-jofarâ neŋgoc-ticne šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ŋokac , motecge keci hâcne . ”
43019027	Iŋuc murâ motec-ticne šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Neŋgocge keci hâcne . ” Eme dameŋ ira Jesure neŋgoc jowame motec jahacne ficko ferâ ŋec juc ewec .
43019028	Eme Jesu e gie-ticne tarame manarâ , miti papiao findaŋdâŋ moc fokac i deŋkeocte , šiŋuc muwec : “ No opâre enarekac . ”
43019029	Eme râqâc moc maŋnao waiŋ opâ šašacne ŋewec , ira hâwec sâmbiŋ âke uruckerâ qeŋqeŋko âke kindeŋnerâ micnao iticnepie nâwec .
43019030	Waiŋ opâ nârâ wirahuc muwec : “ Batarakopac . ” Iŋuc mume qizecne forârieme mâro-ticne wefuwec .
43019031	Eme Judaŋic jaŋe teuŋko rašimbiŋte šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Tomâcko sabata hombaŋ sâkoo ŋic jopakicne jaŋere qâŋɋâŋ maripoŋko mi domazejec . ” Iŋuc murâ Pilato âzâcnepie momori jaŋe ŋic siec-jeŋic qazurâ qâŋɋâŋ-jeŋic bataraniŋte Judaŋic mana-jarewec .

43019036	Miti papiao findaŋdâŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac i sanaŋkeocte wiac i fuawec : “ Ŋoŋe siecne mi qazunšepieŋ . ”
43019037	Erâ wâc miti papiao dâŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac : “ Jaŋe âke mârâŋkembiŋ erao šâŋe finšepieŋ . ”
43019038	Josefe Arimataia haeonec e Jesure motec juwec , erâ Judaŋic jaŋere hâwickeme fufua mi juwec , soŋsoŋ juwec . Eki hâcne Pilatorao rarâ Jesu qâŋɋâŋ-ticne bataraocte mufuacnewec . Eme Pilatozi manacneme ra batarawec .

43019041	Eme Jesu qambiŋ mâreŋ irec ŋifecnao Jufu gie moc fowec , ira hawec moc šâŋeruŋte biŋe gufukicne fowec . Ira ŋic moc mi ducjopakicne , furu fowec .
43019042	Eme Judaŋic hombaŋte teuŋko rašimbiŋte bembeŋko ira hâcne Jesure qâŋɋâŋ râepic .
43020001	Eme Sonda hae mi fure taniŋkeha Maria Madala haeoneczi šâŋeruŋko rawec . Ra fisirâ honewec : Qânâ e šâŋeruŋkonec bârâriekicne .
43020002	Iŋuc honerâ gasacke rarâ Simoŋ Petoro â Jesu motec bufuŋ-ticne jasarâ muwec : “ Wofuŋ qâŋɋâŋ-ticne bawisembieŋ , eme wena râembieŋ i nâŋe kâuc baŋgopeneŋ . ”
43020003	Iŋuc mume Petoro â motec âgo-ticne jahe šâŋeruŋko rapic .

43020013	Eme jahe mupic : “ Ŋokac , go wemocte kiokomec ? ” Eme eki muwec : “ Wofuŋ-nanere qâŋɋâŋ mocko bawisepie basakopac . ”

43020030	Mâsi gâcne bocjaha Jesuzi motecfâcne jaŋere šâŋe faio bawec , i papia šira mi qâreŋke-fârekicne .
43020031	Qâreŋkekicne mac kecši ine šiŋucte qâreŋkekicne : Ŋoŋe wose manac erâ Jesu e Kristo , Anuture ŋokâ , dâŋ i mana šakienšepieŋ , erâ e jahacne manasiŋkehuc šâŋe biŋe-ticnere erâ juju sanaŋhec enšepieŋ .
43021001	Juku motec jaŋe Tiberia riqicko juhapie fua-jarewec . Kecšiŋuc ehapie fua-jarewec :
43021002	Jumbiŋ ine Simoŋ Petoro , Toma , šâŋene moc Didimo , Natanae e Galilaia mâreŋko Kana hae ŋewec irecnec , erâ Ʒebedaio ŋokâ jahec-ticne â motecfâcne jaŋeraonec jajahec mocwâc , ŋic iŋuczi jumbiŋ .
43021003	Ehuc Simoŋ Petorozi šiŋuc jazawec : “ No qowi rozo rakopac . ” Mume mumbiŋ , “ Nâŋe gohec mâmâc ranaŋ . ” Iŋuc murâ wokeo ferâ rambiŋ . Ra juhuc ŋafe ira qowi mi rombiŋ .

44003011	Eme Petoro â Johane jaherao qohotame ŋic mâmâc sasawa taha ufuŋ maŋne moc šâŋene Salomo ira jaherao tumaŋne-fârehuc me kirâ domambiŋ .
44003012	Iŋuc epie Petorozi honec-joparâ ŋic dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Israe ŋicbureŋ , ŋoŋe wemocte ŋic širec hone warec boc enâctehuc domaŋgopieŋ ? Wiac nâhe nâhâcne mitire me tâpirire e hata juju-ticne bâfuacnekoperec me ?
44003013	Aricne , Abraham â Isaka â Jakobo jaŋere Anutu , mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere Anutu , eki hâcne kiŋaŋŋic-ticne Jesu ere Wofuŋ qâreŋ ŋic kecširec faio bâfuame honeŋgopieŋ . Ŋoŋe ine e qaisockerâ qâpuc jaŋerao râembiŋ . Ehame Pilatozi firuezo mume ŋoŋe qikiŋnembiŋ .
44003014	Ine hâcne Maŋɋaɋac â Tiŋne rune e qikiŋnehuc šika qaqaŋic akicke-ŋareocte mu bâuruec ecnembiŋ .
44003015	Ehuc jujure Micne bapa qambiŋ . Qapie Anutuzi bâɋâreme hâmockonec fahareme šâŋe fâri-nâŋeczi qame honembeŋ .
44003016	Eme hone manac ecneeŋgopieŋ ŋic kecši e Jesu šâŋe-ticne manasiŋkepene šâŋe-ticnere tâpirizi bâpiaŋkeme sahac ɋiɋic eme hone-fâreŋgopieŋ .
44003017	Erâ qomâfâc-nane , no manakopac , ŋoŋe â micne bapafâc-ŋeŋic ŋoŋe kâuc bahuc iŋuc embiŋ .
44003018	Iŋuc epie Anutu e Kristo šâic manaku hâmoocte irec dâŋ porofete sasawa jaŋere micko râeme mu qâreŋ embiŋ i hâcne sanaŋkewec .
44003019	Irec ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic bârisierâ juju raŋɋa-ŋeŋic râpeckepie kiŋŋeŋic tâmirezejec . Eme Wofuŋte maio nanaŋ šurec šurec juju irec dameŋ maicke-ŋarezejec .
44003020	Erâ wâc Kristo-ŋeŋic bašawie-ŋarewec , Jesu hâcne , sore-ŋarezejec .
44003021	Ʒi ine Jesu e sambâŋzi foŋkeme jukuhame wiac sasawa Anutuzi mârâc jaha jâmbâŋ porofetefâc-ticne micjeŋicko râeme mumbiŋ i fâri fideteŋ eocte dameŋne maickeocmu .
44003022	Mose e dâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec : ` Wofuŋ Anutu e qomâfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere ŋondeŋkonec porofete moc no iŋucne bâfua-ŋareme dâŋ ŋazame sâc mananšepieŋ .
44003023	Eme moc e dâŋticne qikiŋneme e qarâ qârârâŋnenšepieŋ . Ž
44003024	Erâ porofete gâcne Samue jume juwarembiŋ jaŋe iŋuc jaha dameŋ širec dâŋ mu qâreŋ efârembiŋ .
44003025	Porofete jumbiŋ jaŋere ɋâricfâc ŋoŋe , erâ Anutuzi mimiŋnefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋehec šâšâfic ewec , šâšâfic irec rune ŋoŋe jaha wâc . Ʒâšâfic i Abraham šiŋuc âzâcnehuc bâfuawec : No ɋâricfâcge jambuŋ-jopape jambuŋ izi mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic sâcjopa-fârezejec . Ž
44003026	Ŋoŋere hâcne Anutuzi qanaŋ manasurâ Ŋokâ-ticne soreme waha fuawec , i ŋoŋe sasawa sindaŋ hata-ŋeŋickonec bârisiec-ŋopahuc jambuŋ-ŋopaocte iŋuc hâcne ewec . ”
44004001	Petoro â Johane jahe ŋic dâŋ iŋuc jazahuc domahapire taha bapa â ufuŋte polismaî micne â sadukaio ŋic jaŋe mâmâc jaherao fisimbiŋ .
44004002	Jahe ŋic miti jazahuc , Jesu e hâmockonec ɋârewec , biŋedâŋ i muiŋnepire manapie sâqoreme
44004003	rocjofarâ hae biac owâewecte kâpâcwâru ficko râec-jofapie fohapire hae furewec .
44004004	Eme Petorozi miti mume manambiŋ jaŋeraonec bocjahazi i mana šakierâ Jesure kikefuŋfâc jaŋerao šuhuckepie ŋic sasawa šare-jeŋic 5 tauseŋ ewec .
44004005	Hae fureme micne bapa â soŋaŋ â miti qaqazu jaŋe Jerusalem haeo
44004006	taha bapa sâko Hanasi â Kaifa â Johane â Alesande â kikefuŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋehec tumaŋnembiŋ .
44004007	Erâ mupie aposolo jahe tutumaŋ-jeŋicko bacjofa fembiŋ . Eme mai-jeŋicko domapire esâic-jofarâ mumbiŋ , “ Mozi mamac eŋactehuc mu qafeŋ eŋacteme mâsi i bapirec ? ”
44004008	Eme Petoro e Tiri Mârozi maŋnao fusucmame dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Micne bapa â soŋaŋfâc-nâŋec , mupe mananiŋ :
44004009	Nâhe ŋicpuriŋ jauŋkeperec , irec ŋoŋe , mozi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ eŋacteha ŋic bâpiaŋkepirec , muhuc miŋecgac mu gufuc enâcteŋgopieŋko
44004010	mutaniŋkepe ŋoŋe â Israe ŋic mâmâc sasawa mananiŋ : Jesu Kristo Nazarete haeonec , ŋoŋe maripoŋko qapie hâmome Anutuzi hâmockonec bâɋâreme faharewec jukac , ere tâpirire ŋic keci sahac ɋiɋic ejec mai-ŋeŋicko domakac hâcne .
44004011	Ficbapa ŋic ŋoŋe Jesu e wâtuŋ sâqocne muhuc behepie izi hâcne jâmâ wâtuŋ sâko ewec domakac .
44004012	Bâbâpiaŋ i ŋic moctao moc mi fokac , â ŋic mocte šâŋe riwaseckehuc bibiaŋkene i wâc mâreŋko mi fokac . ”
44004013	Eme Petoro â Johane jahe ŋic omane , mamana ficko mi jukicnezi hâhâwic tâmiric micafec jaha dâŋ mupire manarâ wareckembiŋ . Erâ jahe Jesuhec jupic i hone tarac-jofambiŋ ,
44004014	â ŋic sahac ɋiɋic eweczi jaherao domame e wâc honehuc irec dâŋ bâtikie-jacteniŋte basambiŋ .
44004015	Basarâ ejactepie hae šoŋao hurâ domahapire jaŋackoaŋ šiŋuc muhuc nazaŋ gazaŋ embiŋ :
44004016	“ Nâŋâc ŋic jahe weniŋuc ejactenaŋ ? Jahe mâsi bapire fua tâcneme Jerusalem haeoneczi biŋene biac mana-fârembieŋ , irec wemocko hemackezo ?
44004017	Eme dâŋ i hae sâc haŋ bame mana-fârenšipiŋte mu hâhâwic ejactepene ŋic hâcne šâŋe biŋe-ticne mocwâc mi jaza-jâmbâŋkezepirec . ”
44004018	Iŋuc murâ hefârec-jofarâ šiŋuc jasambiŋ : “ Ŋohe Jesure šâŋe ŋic mocwâc mi jaza qazuc ejâmbâŋkezepirec . ”
44004019	Mupie Petoro â Johane jahe dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikie-jarepic : “ Ŋoŋe ŋaŋac mana honeniŋ , ŋoŋere dâŋ reŋkehuc Anuture dâŋ qiqikiŋ , irec Anutuzi maname sâckeocmu me ?
44004020	Wiac hone manac ehuc jumbeŋ i sâcne mi hesoŋkerâ junaŋmu . ”
44004021	Iŋuc mupire jaŋe mu hâhâwic dâŋ mocwâc jasahuc râec-jofapie rapic . Haeŋic ŋokac omane jaŋe mâsi i hone manac erâ Anutu mucne bacnembiŋte jaŋerao quŋkehuc aposolo jahe wiac mi ejactembiŋ .
44004022	Ŋic sahac ɋiɋic bakicne e puriŋ fohuc juha jara 40 ewec i mana-fârembiŋ hâcne .
44004023	Petoro â Johane jahe ŋic tutumaŋkonec waharâ âgo wiacfâc-jekic jaŋerao rarâ taha bapa micne â soŋaŋ jaŋe dâŋ jasambiŋ irec mu binaŋ ehuc jaza-fârepic .
44004024	Eme jaŋe i manarâ maŋjeŋic qâzuckerâ Anuturao sâsepie fehame šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Wofuŋ sâko Wofuŋ , go sambâŋ â mâreŋ â hâwec i wiac fuŋne fuŋne-jeŋichec râemeŋzi
44004025	Tiri Mâro ecnetec eki mimiŋne-nâŋec Dawidi , kiŋaŋŋicge hâcne , micne baafeckeme dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : ` Oapuc jaŋe wemocte ju fâfânâŋ eeŋgopieŋ , â ŋicne ŋicne dâŋ racne birickeeŋgopieŋ ?
44004026	Wofuŋ â Kristo-ticne râsi ejacteniŋte mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe meo roroc eeŋgopieŋ , â ŋicbomboŋ jaŋe ââte sanaŋ eeŋgopieŋ . '
44004027	“ Hae kecšira ine jâmbomac tiri Ŋokâge Jesu , Kristo âkendâŋnemeŋ , e râsi ecneniŋte Herode â Pilato jahe ŋic qâpuc jaŋehec â Israe ŋic jaŋehec dâŋ ŋiŋihec embiŋ .
44004028	Erâ gahacne mezi â miczi mu bâmoc emeŋ irec sâcmac embiŋ .
44004029	Eme Wofuŋ , ši ine mu hâhâwic dâŋjeŋic hone manac ehuc kiŋaŋŋicfâcge hâbi hejaretec mitige hâhâwicmâc munšepieŋ .
44004030	Ehapie mege sicnetec sahac ɋiɋic â mâsi fuŋne fuŋne tiri kiŋaŋŋicge Jesu ere erâ fua razejec . ”
44004031	Iŋuc numupie fic , tumaŋnerâ ŋembiŋ , qiriŋ qiriŋ qawec . Ehame Tiri Mârozi maŋjeŋicko fusucmame Anuture dâŋ micafec jaha ŋic jazambiŋ .
44004032	Opâ ruac guru jaŋe maŋ mocjaha ehuc šâšâfic erâ jumbiŋ . Ehuc wiac fojarewec irec nore gore mi muhuc qâqâhâc mocjaha fojarewec .
44004033	Eme aposolo jaŋe Wofuŋ Jesu hâmockonec faharewec irec biŋedâŋ tâpiri jaha muhuc jumbiŋ . Eme aki anonoc sâkozi sâcjopa-fârerâ fowec .
44004034	Erâ ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko moczi tac qararacne mi juwec . Jufu gie â mafa wiac-jeŋichec jumbiŋ jaŋe i qikiŋnepie moneŋ kitâcne-jareme
44004035	aposolo jaŋerao râembiŋ . Eme jaŋe ŋic wiac basapie sâc bârâwiŋnerâ jare jumbieŋ .
44004036	Eme ŋic moc juwec šâŋene Josefe , aposolo jaŋe šâŋene moc Banaba mumbiŋ , nâŋâcne dâŋko Bâmiriŋmotec , e Lewire ɋâric , Kipiro nucko fuawec .
44004037	Ŋic eki jufu-ticne qikiŋneme moneŋ fuame aposolo jaŋerao furu jaha râe-fârewec .
44005001	Eme ŋic moc juwec šâŋene Anania , e ŋonâŋ-ticne Safira ehec muc manac ehuc hae mâreŋ-ticne qikiŋneme moneŋ fua-jacteme
44005002	mamanac erâ tucne hefackepire fojactewec â tucne sawa ŋiczi aposolo jaŋerao râewec .
44005003	Râeme Petorozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Anania , go wemocte Sataŋzi maŋge bâsifuckeme Tiri Mâro eatuckehuc hae mâreŋgere furi tucne hefackekomec ?
44005004	Hae mâreŋge fogarezo murâ fogarezac , me qikiŋnerâ furine moneŋ rorâ izi iŋuc me iŋuc ezo murâ enšaŋ . Go weniŋuc erâ maŋgezi surucgume iŋuc emec ? Go ŋic nâŋe mâcne , go Anutu eatuckekomec . ”
44005005	Iŋuc mume Anania e dâŋ mana manahuc rândiŋke qarâ hâmowec . Eme hone manac embiŋ jaŋe hâhâwic sâko fua-jarewec .
44005006	Eme ŋicmotec domambiŋ jaŋe qâŋɋâŋ-ticne qoruczi râpâckerâ bara duckembiŋ .
44005007	Eme aua 3 tarame ŋonâŋ-ticne biŋe mi mamana , mâc fokac muhuc fisiwec .
44005008	Fisime Petorozi šiŋuc wiocnewec : “ Hae mâreŋte furine ine mac hâcne warejec ? ” Eme eki muwec , “ Ine mac sawa hâcne . ”
44005009	Mume Petorozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : Ŋohe wemocte Wofuŋte Mâro eatuckenicte mamanac epirec ? Manakic , ŋowege duckembieŋ motâc râpeo domaŋgopieŋ , jaŋe go iŋuc jaha bacgu ra ducguniŋmu . ”
44005010	Iŋuc mume izia kikefuŋnao rândiŋke qarâ hâmowec . Eme ŋicmotec jaŋe ficmaŋko ferâ qâŋɋâŋ-ticne honerâ bara ŋowe-ticne duckembiŋko ijaha duckembiŋ .
44005011	Eme opâ ruac guru â ŋic gâcne biŋe-jekic manambiŋ jaŋerao hâhâwic sâko fuawec .
44005012	Aposolo jaŋe mâsi fuŋne fuŋne bocjaha ŋic jaŋerao bambiŋ . Eme Jesure kikefuŋ jaŋe taha ufuŋ maŋne moc šâŋene Salomo ira maŋ mocjaha erâ tumaŋne jumbieŋ .
44005013	Tumaŋnehapie ŋic gâcnezi araŋ bajarehuc enšaŋauc kosa mi ejare jumbieŋ . Jaŋe opâ ruac jaŋere manapie bipinehec ewec .
44005014	Erâ ŋic â ŋokac gurune gurune miti mana šakiehuc Wofuŋtao šuhucke jumbieŋ .
44005015	Erâ wâc âgofâc-jeŋic huc šâichec hatao fofo â kanše faio kecšiŋuc muhuc râec-jopambiŋ : Petorozi rac warec eme nâkumuc-ticnezi foninipec-jopazejec .
44005016	Erâ Jerusalem hae rârec rârec ŋic jurambiŋ jaŋe orâŋ bârâŋ fisihuc jumbiŋ . Ehuc huchec â demoŋhecfâc-jeŋic mâmâc amec-jopa fisipie biaŋke-fârembiŋ .
44005017	Eme wiac iŋucne fuame taha bapa sâko e â qaŋeŋfâc-ticne , sadukaio ŋic hâcne , jaŋe maŋzi ruc bahuc
44005018	aposolo mana sâqore-jarerâ rocjoparâ kâpâcwâru fic sâkoo râec-jopambiŋ .
44005019	Eme ira fohapie ŋafeo Wofuŋte aŋelozi motâc rojarerâ jowac-jopa hurâ šiŋuc jazawec :
44005020	“ Ŋoŋe taha ufuŋko ferâ ŋic sasawa juju hata kecširec biŋedâŋ jazahuc domanšepieŋ . ”
44005021	Iŋuc jazame jaŋe manarâ furicte taha ufuŋko ferâ miti mumbiŋ . Ehame taha bapa sâko e â qaŋeŋfâcne jaŋe qâturerâ ŋic fekicne â Israe ŋic micne guru-jeŋic hefârec-jopapie furu fisimbiŋ . Erâ polismaî jaŋe kâpâcwâru ficko ra aposolo rocjopapie fisiniŋte mumbiŋ .
44005022	Eme polismaî jaŋe ra kâpâcwâru ficko basac-joparâ risierâ mumbiŋ ,
44005023	“ Nâŋe ra fisirâ motâc kine sanaŋne bakicne honembeneŋ , erâ soŋaŋ jaŋe motâcko domambieŋ wâc . Erâ motâc rorâ ferâ ŋic ine basac-jopambeneŋ . ”
44005024	Dâŋ i mupie ufuŋte polismaî micne â taha bapa micne jaŋe manapie quŋkewec .
44005025	Ehapie ŋic moczi fisirâ muwec , “ Manaŋgopieŋ , kâpâcwâru ficko râec-jopambieŋ jaŋe ufuŋko ŋic miti jazahuc domaŋgopieŋ . ”
44005026	Mume polismaî micne eki soŋaŋfâcne rocjopame ra aposolo urucko jowac-jopa warembiŋ . Ŋic jaŋe qânâzi hecjopanšipiŋte hâwic-jopame wânšâŋnehec šame kirac mi ejarembiŋ .
44005027	Eme micne bapa tutumaŋko râec-jopapie domahapie taha bapa sâkozi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec :
44005028	“ Nâŋe ŋic hâcne šâŋe biŋe-ticne mi mupie haŋ baocte mic muac mi eŋarembeŋ me ? Eme ŋoŋe sifu dâŋ i Jerusalem haeo mocwâc muiŋneŋgopieŋ , ehuc ŋic hâcne ere kiŋ nâŋere faio râezo muŋgopieŋ . ”
44005029	Mume Petoro â aposolo gâcne jaŋe dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnembiŋ : “ Ŋicdâŋ reŋkehuc Anuture dâŋ qiqikiŋ i mi fokac .
44005030	Ŋoŋe Jesu maripoŋko qarâ qâhâmopie mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere Anutuzi bâɋâreme faharewec .
44005031	Fahareme Anutuzi e jahacne mefâreo râerâ micne sâko â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec âkendâŋnewec . Eme ši Israe ŋic ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic bârisiepie sâqocne-ŋeŋic šureocte muekac .
44005032	Eme irec biŋe hâcne Tiri Mâro â nâŋe mueŋgopeneŋ . Tiri Mâro e Anutuzi micrereŋfâc-ticne jareekac . ”
44005033	Dâŋ iŋuc jazame bujeŋic henšaŋneme mana hâtâwerâ aposolo jopaniŋte mumbiŋ .
44005034	Eme tutumaŋ-jeŋicko farisaio ŋic moc ŋewec , šâŋene Gamalie , e sâcmutâc dâŋ qaqazu-jeŋic fekicne . Eki hâcne mume aposolo jaŋe hae šoŋao hurâ juhapie
44005035	micne bapa âgofâcne šiŋuc jazawec : “ Israe ŋicbureŋ , ŋoŋe ŋic i wiac mana wosâehuc ejarenšepieŋ .
44005036	Mârâc ŋic moc šâŋene Teuda eki , no ŋicbomboŋ micne-ŋeŋic , iŋuc mume ŋic 400 erao qohotambiŋ . Eme e jahacne šika kime ŋicfâc-ticne tâtiepie gie-jeŋic omatac fuawec .
44005037	Erâ šâhec Galilaia mâreŋko ŋic moc šâŋene Juda , e wose qâreŋ enârembiŋ dameŋ ira ŋic gâcne qafeŋ-jopame bâjâpembiŋ . Eme e jahacne qahuc ŋicfâc-ticne jopa qâtâtiec ejarembiŋ .
44005038	Irec ši dâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ : ŋoŋe ŋic ši behec-jopapie juniŋ . Jaŋe dâŋ â gie i maŋjeŋicte mu bac eeŋgopieŋko sifuckerâ arictac eocmu .
44005039	Me Anutuzi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ ejarehame mu bac eeŋgopieŋko bâipiec-jopaniŋmu . Ŋoŋe gie-jeŋic ima bahuc Anutu e jahacne râsi ecnenšipiŋkohec . ”
44005040	Iŋuc jazame jaŋe manapie sâckeme aposolo ejarepie tutumaŋko fepie kâcbiŋzi jopambiŋ . Joparâ ŋic Jesure šâŋe biŋe mi jazaniŋte muac-joparâ sorec-jopambiŋ .
44005041	Sorec-jopapie Wofuŋ e jaŋere maname sâckeha šâŋe-ticnere erâ šika kimbiŋte bubiaŋ manahuc ŋic tutumaŋkonec waharâ rambiŋ .
44005042	Erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne taha ufuŋko â ŋicficko Jesu Kristo ere Biŋebiaŋ jaza qazuc erâ mi behembiŋ .
44006001	Dameŋ ira opâ ruac guru sâko embiŋte nânâ bârâwiŋne-jarehuc Grië opâ ruac jaŋere hozec bâtiric-jopapie Juda opâ ruac jaŋere manapie mi sâckeme dâŋ bâfuambiŋ .
44006002	Iŋuc epie aposolo 12 jaŋe opâ ruac hetumaŋ-jopa-fârerâ šiŋuc jazambiŋ : “ Nâŋe sahackopec gie i dopeckehuc Anuture dâŋ mumu irec gie behepene wahame mi sâckeocmu .
44006003	Irec ŋic âgofâc , ŋoŋe ŋic 7 ŋaŋacne ŋondeŋko Mâro â mamanahec jupie honec-jopapie sâckeme rowosâec-jopanšepieŋ . Eme nâŋe gie i mujarepene banšepieŋ .
44006004	Nâŋe ine nunumu â miti mumu irec gie paŋšâic jaha banšepeneŋ . ”
44006005	Dâŋ iŋuc mupie opâ ruac jaŋe manapie sâcke-fârewec . Ehuc ŋic šiŋuc bâwosâec-jopambiŋ : Stefano , e maŋnao mamanasiŋ â Tiri Mâro fufusuc fowec , erâ Filipo â Porokoro â Nikano â Timoŋ â Pamena â Nikolao , e Antiokia haeonec ŋic qâpuczi Judaŋic jaŋerao šuhuckewec .
44006006	Eme ŋic i hâcne jaŋe aposolo jaŋere maŋfuŋko birickerâ domapie mejeŋic qizec-jeŋicko râehuc numu jambuŋ ejarembiŋ .

44014018	Ŋicjahec jahe dâŋ iŋuc muhuc mu bâmâteŋ ejarehuc qatara-jarekupire bâzi ririke-jacte i behembiŋ .

44015002	Iŋuc muhuc Paulo â Banaba jahehec mufec muwahac ehuc qaqatarac sâko embiŋ . Eku šiŋuc mumockembiŋ : “ Paulo â Banaba erâ opâ ruac jaŋeraonec ŋic tucne jaŋe dâŋ i aposolo â mitire micne Jerusalem haeo juŋgopieŋ jaŋerao baranšepieŋ . ”
44015003	Iŋuc murâ kikefuŋzi sorec-jopahuc mâzoc-jopapie rambiŋ . Rahuc Foinike â Samaria mâreŋ fotâcnehuctecne opâ ruac šiŋuc jaza rambiŋ : “ Qâpuc bocjahazi mitio rašiŋgopieŋ . ” Jazapie manarâ jaŋerao bubiaŋ kâcɋene fuawec .
