44015019	Irec no mana wosâerâ šiŋuc mukopac : Qâpuc guruoneczi Anutu maickeŋgopieŋ jaŋe tagi sâko mi râe-jarenšepeneŋ .
44015020	Jaŋe nemuɋâŋte wiac mamakâcne â sasec boe sau â qowi bituakicne â qowisoc , wiac i bâec baniŋte mupaŋkerâ papia qâreŋke-jarenšepeneŋ .
44015021	I šiŋucte enšepeneŋ : Mosere dâŋ i mimiŋzi ɋâric mârâc jaha fuŋkerâ hae sâc wose warehuc jukicne , â šiŋuczia wâc iŋuc jaha sabata hombaŋ sâc mitificne ficne wose manac eeŋgopeneŋ .
44015022	Eme aposolo â micne jaŋe kikefuŋte ŋic sasawa jazapie manapie sâckeme jaŋeraonec ŋic jajahec bâwosâec-jofambiŋ . Moc šâŋene Juda , šâŋe-ticne moc Basaba , erâ Sila , mitire micne bapa jahe hâcne bâwosâec-jofarâ Paulo â Banaba jahehec mâmâc Antiokia haeo raniŋte sorec-jopambiŋ .

44015024	Nâŋe mi manahapene širec ŋic gâcne ŋoŋerao fârâ dâŋ ŋazahuc maŋ bâsifuc eŋarepie ŋoŋerao dâŋ fâfâuc fuawec .
44015025	Eme nâŋe i manarâ tumaŋne-fârehuc ŋic jajahec bâwosâec-jofarâ qomâ jahec-nâŋec Banaba â Paulo jahehec sorec-jopapene fâŋgopieŋ .

44016016	Dameŋ mocko nunumure tomao huhapene kiŋaŋ naru moczi bâfuac-nâpowec . Naru e faŋfaŋ demoŋ-ticnehec juhuc ŋic jaŋere fuŋne mufua jujec , ehuc rufâc-ticne moneŋ mafa bocjaha hure-jare jujec .
44016017	Eme eki hâcne bâfuac-nâporâ Paulo â nâŋe bâjâpec-nâpohuc dâŋ wiwira kecšiŋuc ewec : “ Ŋic kecšizi Anutu femicne sâko ere kiŋaŋ qaqa juhuc biaŋkeniŋte hata mušâwe-ŋareeŋgopieŋ . ”

44017024	Anutu e mâreŋ bâfuarâ fainao wiac sasawa râe-fârewec , eki hâcne sambâŋ â mâreŋ irec rune .

44020002	Mâreŋ i fotâcnehuc opâ ruac jurambiŋ jaŋe mu keteŋ bocjaha ejare rawec . Raku Grië mâreŋko fisiwec .
44020003	Ira mosa jahec â moc juku hâwecko hurâ wokeo ferâ Siria mâreŋko razo mume Judaŋic jaŋe somâ râecnepie manarâ Makedonia mâreŋko rawec .
44020004	Eme ŋic šiŋuczi hatao bâjâpembiŋ : Berea haeonec Sopate , e Pirore ŋokâ , Tesalonike haeonec Aristako â Sekundo , Derebenec Gaio , erâ Timoteo , â Asia masunaonec Tikiko â Trofimo .
44020005	Ŋic izi bânierâ Troa haeo woŋec-nâŋec jumbiŋ .
44020006	Nâŋe ine goreŋ sowa hombaŋ tarame Filipi haeo wokeo ferâ šoaŋ 5 raku Troa haeo fisimbeŋ . Ira fisirâ šoaŋ gie bapa 7 jumbeŋ .
44020007	Eme nâŋe Sondao Ŋafe Tiwâ nanaŋte tumaŋnembeŋ . Ehuc Paulo e hae fureme raocte murâ miti muhuc juhame ŋafe šâŋiŋke-jâmbâŋkewec .
44020008	Fic maŋne ŋembeŋ ira lambe bocjaha šawec .
44020009	Ehame motec moc šâŋene Eutiko , e Paulozi miti mume šorame qâqâtâc kataŋko ŋeku guŋ qâmâckewec . Erâ guŋko qâqâtâc kataŋkonec hurâ mâreŋko qarâ fohame bafaharepie hâmocne ewec . Fic maŋne jahec â moc hâŋ bafehuc âke tâcne fekicne irecnec hâcne hurâ qawec .
44020010	Eme Paulozi hurâ motec fofackerâ hâporâ ŋic šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe ki ojowa mi eniŋ , e mâro-ticne fuakac . ”
44020011	Iŋuc murâ ficmaŋko ferâ ŋafe Tiwâ gumec-joparâ nânâ piticne nâwec . Nânâ nârâ jaŋehec mitire muc manac ehuc juhapie hae furewec . Hae fureme behec-joparâ rawec .
44020012	Ŋic jaŋe ine motec ɋâreme ficticnao jowa rarâ bujeŋic boc urue biaŋ ewec .

44020015	Irecnec raku hae fureme Ʒintacko Kio nucko fisirâ jâurumbeŋ . Izi raku Mituoc Samo nucko fisimbeŋ . Eme irecnec raku Sekiqanâcko Milete haeo fisimbeŋ .
44020016	Paulo e Mâro hombaŋko Jerusalem haeo ra fisiocte muwec . Irec Efeso haeo wokeonec waharâ Asia masunao juhame dameŋ qâtirizacte fofotâc raku Milete haeo fisiwec .

44020018	Fisipie Paulozi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec : “ No Asia mâreŋko fisirâ izia ŋoŋerao gie-nane fuŋkerâ wiac ehuc jupo , i fuŋnaonecteaŋ mana wareeŋgopieŋ .
44020019	No hone suŋgiŋnezi ki busâqochec Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qahuc jupo , ehuc Judaŋic jaŋe keke suec suec enarehapie râsi faio jupo .
44020020	Erâ dâŋ ŋoŋe ŋaŋazane moc mi bâtiripe fowec , ŋoŋe biaŋkeniŋte mitidâŋ bocjaha hofao â ficne ficne ŋaza qazuc ehuc jupo .

44020025	Erâ ši moc mupe mananiŋ , no uucmaŋte biŋedâŋ ŋazahuc ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju epe honecnueŋgopieŋ izi šâhec šâŋe mai-nane mocwâc mi honeniŋmu .

44022024	soŋaŋ sâkozi mume momori jaŋe Paulo ficjeŋicko bafembiŋ . Erâ ŋic jaŋe wemo wiacte boc owackecnembieŋ irec fuŋne mufuame manazore kâcbiŋzi qaniŋte mujarewec .
44022025	Eme jaŋe kâcbiŋzi qaniŋte fâretiŋkerâ becsahaczi bândeŋnezo epie Paulozi micne-jeŋic šiŋuc muhuc wiocnewec : “ Ŋoŋe Romaŋic fârine dâŋticne mi mutarahuc kâcbiŋzi qapie sâckeocmu me ? ”
44022026	Iŋuc mume micne-jeŋiczi soŋaŋ sâkorao rarâ âzâcnerâ muwec , “ Weniŋuc ezo ? Ŋic e Romaŋic fârine . ”
44022027	Mume soŋaŋ sâkozi Paulorao rarâ wiocnerâ muwec , “ Go muc , go jâmbomac Romaŋic fârine ? ” Eme Paulozi muwec , “ I jâmbomac . ”
44022028	Mume soŋaŋ sâkozi šiŋuc muwec : “ No ŋic jabanezi moneŋ bocjaha rope kitâcnume Romaŋic jâmbâŋ epo . ” Eme Paulozi muwec , “ No ine fufua-nane Romaŋic fuapo . ”
44022029	Eme izia Paulo wiac ecnezo mumbiŋ i behembiŋ . Momori soŋaŋ e ine , Paulo e Romaŋic , iŋuc manarâ , no wemocte ŋic iŋucne kâpâcwâru bapac muhuc fâfârewec .
44022030	Hae fureme momori soŋaŋ sâko e Judaŋic jaŋe Paulo wemo wiacte mana sâqorecnembiŋ irec fuŋne jâmbâŋ manaocte taha bapa micne â micne guru furu jaha ejareme tumaŋnembiŋ . Ehame Paulo jowa hurâ tutumaŋ-jeŋicko râewec .
44023001	Paulo e micne bapa hone dendeŋ-jopahuc dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋic âgofâc-nane , no sâcmutâc dâŋ qaqatarare maŋnanezi mumu hehec moc mi enareha Anuture maio juwefuhuc jupozi jukopac . ”
44023002	Iŋuc mume taha bapa sâko Anania eki ŋic Paulore maŋfuŋko domambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe masunao qaniŋ . ”
44023003	Mume Paulozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Maŋge tâŋzi qakicne go Anutuzi guocmu . Go sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko norao mumutiŋ gie bazo mukiczi wemocte sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuahuc nuniŋte jazakic ? ”
44023004	Iŋuc mume ŋic doma rambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ : “ Go Anuture taha bapa sâko wemocte musoriŋkekic ? ”
44023005	Mupie Paulozi šiŋuc muwec : “ Âgo bureŋ , e taha bapa sâko jukac i mi manahuc dâŋepac . Mitio dâŋ kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : ` Go micne bapa mi musâqorec-jopazemec . Ž No dâŋ i manaekopac . ”
44023006	Eme micne guru ŋic tucne sadukaio â tucne farisaio ŋic jumbiŋ , Paulozi i manahuc dâŋ baferâ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋicbureŋ , no farisaio ŋic â apa ŋosafâc-nane jaŋe farisaio ŋic jaha jumbiŋ . Hâmockonec fafahare fokac dâŋ i dopeckeekopacte dâŋko râecnuŋgopieŋ . ”
44023007	Dâŋ iŋuc mume farisaio ŋic â sadukaio ŋic jaŋe qaqatarac epie micne bapa jaŋerao fâfâuc fuawec .
44023008	Sadukaio ŋic jaŋe hâmockonec fafahare â aŋelo â sawa qâqâtâc , wiac iŋucne micke-fâreeŋgopieŋ . Farisaio ŋic jaŋe ine irec fârine mueŋgopieŋ .
44023009	Eme irec tutumaŋ-jeŋicko ojowa sâko bambiŋ . Eku farisaio ŋic jaŋere guruonec miti qaqazu gâcne faharerâ dâŋ fârone kecšiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Nâŋe ŋic kecširec kiŋ manapene aricne ekac ” aŋelo me sawa qâqâtâc moczi dâŋ âzâcnewecko weniŋuc moc munaŋmu ? ”
44023010	Eme fecko fefec mâretec epie momori soŋaŋ sâko e Paulo qâsuckenšipiŋte hâwickeme mume momori jaŋe fisirâ Paulo ŋicŋondeŋkonec fâre waharâ ficjeŋicko barambiŋ .
44023011	Eme ŋafe ira Wofuŋzi Paulo fuacnerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go hâbige roc , šira Jerusalem haeo mutaniŋnukomec iŋuc jaha Roma haeo mutaniŋnuzemec . ”
44023012	Hae fureme Judaŋic gâcne šâšâfic erâ nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ nânâ opâ nâniŋte mumundeŋ embiŋ .
44023013	Ŋic šâšâfic erâ iŋuc mumbiŋ šare-jeŋic 40 jâuruwec .
44023014	Ŋic jaŋe hâcne taha bapa micne â soŋaŋ jaŋerao rarâ mufua-jarerâ šiŋuc jazambiŋ : “ Nâŋe nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ wiac nanaŋte mumundeŋ embeneŋ ”
44023015	irec micne bapa ŋoŋe momori soŋaŋ sâkorao dâŋ šiŋuc râepie razejec : ` Go Paulo nâŋere tutumaŋko soretec wareme dâŋticne mocwâc muhâmonšepeneŋ . Ž Eme dâŋŋeŋic manarâ iŋuc eme nâŋe Paulo hatao qanaŋmu . ”
44023016	Eme Paulo baŋec-ticnezi šikadâŋ i manawec . Manarâ momori ficko rarâ wawa-ticne âzâcnewec .
44023017	Âzâcneme Paulozi momori jaŋere micne moc wiracnerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Go motec ši momori soŋaŋ sâkorao jowa ratec dâŋ moc âzâcneoc . ”
44023018	Mume ŋic eki motec soŋaŋ sâkorao jowa rarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Kâpâcwâru ŋic Paulo eki wira-narerâ nazame motec ši dâŋ gazaocte jowape warekoperec . ”
44023019	Iŋuc muhuc âzâcneme soŋaŋ sâkozi motec menao rorâ herâricnao bararâ wiocnerâ muwec , “ Dâŋ weniŋuc nazacmu ? ”
44023020	Eme moteczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Judaŋic jaŋe gorao dâŋ râepie wareocte muc manac embieŋ , jaŋe go Paulo tutumaŋ-jeŋicko jowa rarâ fuŋne-ticne bataniŋke-hâmocmurâ gazaniŋmu .
44023021	Gazapie dâŋjeŋic mi manazemec . Ŋic šare-jeŋic 40 jâurukac , iŋuczi Paulo qâhâmoniŋte muŋgopieŋ . Jaŋe nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ wiac nâniŋte mumundeŋ embieŋ , erâ biac šawierâ gore dâŋte woŋec juŋgopieŋ . ”
44023022	Motec e dâŋ iŋuc mume soŋaŋ sâkozi šiŋuc muhuc sorewec : “ Go dâŋ mufuarâ nazakomec i ŋic moc mi jazazemec . ”
44023023	Eme soŋaŋ sâkozi momori jaŋere micne jajahec hefârec-jofarâ šiŋuc jasawec : “ Ŋohe mupire momori kikezi hata rara 200 â becâsicko rara 70 â damu bapa 200 izi šawierâ ŋafere 9 kiloë ehame Kaisarea haeo ranšepieŋ .
44023024	Erâ Paulore becâsic moc sate hecnenšepieŋ . Eme aimuŋ soŋaŋkehuc kia Feliki erao baranšepieŋ . ”
44023025	Iŋuc murâ kiare papia moc šiŋuc muhuc qâreŋkewec :
44023026	“ Klaudio Lisia noni kia biaŋ-nane Feliki gore papia ši qâreŋkekopac .
44023027	Momori jaŋe ŋic moc bafâŋgopieŋ e Judaŋic jaŋe qazo embiŋ . Eme noni e Romaŋic jâmbâŋ ere iŋuc manahuc momori jaŋehec rarâ mejeŋickonec batarambeŋ .
44023028	Eme dâŋko râembiŋ irec fuŋne manapemurâ micne bapa tutumaŋ-jeŋicko barapo .
44023029	Bararâ sâcmutâc dâŋjeŋicte qorickepie šiŋuc manapo : Wiac ewec izi ferâ šika kâpâcwâru bâbâfuane mi ekac .
44023030	Eme ŋic gâcne jaŋe somâ barâ Paulo qaniŋte mupie manarâ gorao sorepe fakac hâcne . Á qorickeeŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe iŋuc jaha ejarepe gorao fârâ dâŋticne gazanšepieŋ . ”
44023031	Eme momori jaŋe soŋaŋ-jeŋicte mic reŋkehuc Paulo ŋafeoa jowa raku Antipatri haeo fisimbiŋ .
44023032	Hae fureme momori gâcne jaŋe ficjeŋicko risiehapie becâsicko ŋeŋe jaŋe buc Paulo jowa raku Kaisarea haeo fisimbiŋ .
44023033	Fisirâ kia papia râcnehuc Paulo iŋuc jaha ere meo râembiŋ .
44023034	Eme kiazi papia woserâ Paulo mâreŋ qizec-ticnere wiocneme muwec , “ No Kilikia mâreŋkonec . ”
44023035	Eme kiazi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Dâŋko râecguŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe ware fisipie gore dâŋ muzo . ” Iŋuc murâ momori jazame Herodere ficko râerâ soŋaŋkembiŋ .
44024001	Ʒoaŋ gie bapa 5 tarame taha bapa sâko Anania e â soŋaŋ gâcne â dâŋŋic moc šâŋene Teatulo jaŋe Kaisarea haeo hurâ kiarao Paulore dâŋ muniŋte fuambiŋ .
44024002	Eme kiazi mume Paulo fisime Teatulozi e qorickehuc kia dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Kia biaŋ-nâŋec Feliki , go sâcne soŋaŋ-nâpotec wamaoa jueŋgopeneŋ , erâ ŋicguru ši nâŋere manabâc ehuc bafic-nâpotec
44024003	nâŋerao hae sâc wiac sasawa biaŋkeekacte gore manapene sâcke-hâmoekac .
44024004	Erâ dâŋ mupe šorazacte go uruerâ mana-nâretec dâŋ bembeŋne mac gazape .
44024005	Ŋic kecirec manapene boc sâqorekac , e sopa sâwec-ticnehec , Judaŋic mâreŋ sâc juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋbâiŋ ejareekac , erâ Nazarete rune repicnefâc-ticne jaŋere qizec eki hâcne .
44024006	Eme taha ufuŋ-nâŋec gâc hecnezo ehame rombeŋ , [ erâ nâŋe sâcmutâc dâŋnâŋecte sâcko wiac ecnenšapeŋ .
44024007	Ehame ine kapiteŋ sâko Lisia eki fisi šocnehec nâwoc rowec .
44024008	Ehuc dâŋko râembiŋ ŋic i jaŋe gorao fisi fuaniŋte mujarewec . Ý Eme nâŋe dâŋ gazaŋgopeneŋ i go gahac mu esâic ecnehuc fuŋne sâcne bataniŋkecmu . ”
44024009	Dâŋ iŋuc mume Judaŋic jaŋe e bafickehuc dâŋticne dopeckembiŋ .
44024010	Eme kiazi Paulo mezi sâsâc ecneme dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Go mâreŋ šira jara bocjaha kia juekic i manasuhuc dâŋnane manabâc tâmiric mupemu .
44024011	No Jerusalem haeo Anutu mai ecnepemurâ ferâ juwarekupe šoaŋ gie bapa 12 sawa ekac , go dâŋ irec maŋjahec erâ ŋic esâic-jopatec gazaniŋmu .
44024012	No taha ufuŋko me mitific gâcnao me miti haeo ŋic jaŋehec mitire mu qaqatarac me ŋic maŋbâiŋ eejare i moc mi epe honecnumbiŋ .
44024013	Ŋic šizi qoricnuhuc dâŋ gazaŋgopieŋ , irec fârine wemocko gowatuniŋmu .
44024014	Erâ moc mufua-garepe manac : Hata ɋâri sureeŋgopieŋ i âteekopac mueŋgopieŋ , ine jâmbomac eekopac . Erâ jaŋere dâŋmiti bajuhuc sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko miti qâreŋkekicne fokac â porofete mu qâreŋ embiŋ i manape fârine ehame mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere Anutu kiŋaŋ qacneekopac .
44024015	Erâ juku ŋic biaŋne â sâqocne hâmockonec fafahare maickeocmu , irec ŋic keci jaŋe â no mâmâc mamanac jueŋgopeneŋ .
44024016	Iŋuc ehuc Anuture maio â ŋicmaio bahacmâc jupemurâ rucnane bahuc jaha juekopac .
44024017	“ Eme no jara bocjaha mâreŋ wiwicko juhuc mitire moneŋ qânusuckeku Jerusalem haeo ŋic âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋerao warepo .
44024018	Erâ bâzi ririkere bašawierâ taha ufuŋko ferâ juhape bâfuacnumbiŋ . Ira ŋicguruo juju me dâŋfânâŋ sâkohec juju ine arictac .
44024019	Asia mâreŋkonec Judaŋic gâcne jaŋe ine iŋuc embiŋ . Jaŋe hâcne nore bahac moc manaŋgopieŋko gorao fisirâ mutaniŋkenšapiŋ .
44024020	Me micne bapa tutumaŋko domahape nore bahac moc bâfuambiŋko ŋic domaŋgopieŋ šizi gazaniŋ .
44024021	Jaŋe no dâŋ mocjaha sawa ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko domahuc mupe manapie mi mecne sâckewec , ine hahaŋne bahuc kecšiŋuc jazapo : ` Hâmockonec fafahare fokac , dâŋ i dopeckeekopacte gâcnezi dâŋko râecnupie mai-ŋeŋicko domakopac ši . Ž ”
44024022	Kia Feliki e Paulore dâŋ i mi mutarahuc mâc râeme fowec . E miti ɋâricnere biŋe mana-hâmowecte šiŋuc sawa jazawec : “ Momori soŋaŋ Lisiazi Jerusalem haeonec wahame dâŋŋeŋic mutarapemu . ”
44024023	Iŋuc murâ momori micne šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ŋoŋe Paulo soŋaŋkehuc râsi šâŋe mi ecnenšepieŋ , â âgofâcne fisirâ jauŋ bazo mupie mi qatara-jarenšepieŋ . ”
44024024	Ʒoaŋ gie bapa tucne jurâ Feliki e Juda guruonec ŋonâŋ-ticne Drusila ehec mâmâc ŋehuc Paulo ecneme hefârâ Kristo Jesu manasiŋkembiŋ irec fuŋne jasawec .
44024025	Ehuc tiŋke biaŋ eere â sasecte sowa jujure â okac dameŋte mume Felikizi weaŋkerâ Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Sâcne rac , juku nacnere dameŋ sawane moc fua-nareme mocwâc hefârecgupemu . ”
44024026	Kia e Paulozi moneŋ narezejec muhuc dameŋ sâc hefârerâ ehec dâŋ muc manac ejujec .
44024027	Ehame jara jajahec tarame kia moc šâŋene Porkio Festo eki Feliki âkehockewec . Eme Feliki e Judaŋic bubiaŋ qajarehuc Paulo kâpâcwâru ficko ŋehame beherâ rawec .
44025001	Festozi kia erâ šoaŋ jahec â moc Jurâ Kaisarea haeonec Jerusalem haeo fewec .
44025002	Fe fisime taha bapa micne â Judaŋic fekicne erao fisirâ Paulore dâŋ âzâcnembiŋ .
44025003	Ehuc mana urue-jarerâ mume Paulo Jerusalem haeo fisiocte âzâcnembiŋ . Jaŋe hatao Paulo somâckerâ qaniŋte manasuhuc kia iŋuc âzâcnembiŋ .
44025004	Mupie Festozi šiŋuc jazawec : “ Paulo e Kaisarea haeo kâpâcwâru ficko ŋekac ” eme no ijaha biac mocwâc risie hupemu .
44025005	Paulo bahacdâŋ-ticne muzo murâ ŋoŋeraonec micne bapa nohec mâmâc hurâ munšepieŋ . ”
44025006	Iŋuc murâ šoaŋ 8 me 10 Jerusalem haeo jurâ Kaisarea haeo rahuwec . Izi hae fureme dâŋficko ferâ mume Paulo bafembiŋ .
44025007	Ficko feme Jerusalem haeonec Judaŋic jaŋe orâŋkerâ samarierâ qorickehuc domambiŋ . Erâ qoqoricte fârine mi fuawec .
44025008	Mupie Paulozi dâŋjeŋic bawahahuc šiŋuc muwec : “ No Judaŋic sâcmutâc dâŋjeŋic me taha ufuŋ me Roma ŋicwofuŋ moc mi musuaekopac . ”
44025009	Eme Festozi Judaŋic bubiaŋ qajareocte Paulo indiŋkerâ muwec , “ Go Jerusalem haeo jowacgu ferâ ira dâŋge mutarape me ? ”
44025010	Indiŋkeme Paulozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Roma ŋicwofuŋte dâŋfic šine hâcne ” nore dâŋ šira mutarazo ” go gahac fuŋne-nane manakic , no Judaŋic wiac hehesic moc mi ejarepo .
44025011	No bahac me kiŋsâko moc bâfuarâ muzac , nuzo mutec sahac-nane mi sakarezapo . Jaŋe ine burecko qoricnuŋgopieŋte moczi moc bubiaŋ qajarehuc jaŋere meo sâcne mi râecnu-jâmbâŋkeocmu . Irec ši Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋnane mutaraocte mukopac . ”
44025012	Iŋuc mume Festo e ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋehec muc manac erâ Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Ŋicwofuŋ sâkore mukomec , irec ŋicwofuŋ sâkorao razemec . ”
44025013	Ʒoaŋ gie bapa tucne tarame ŋicwofuŋ Agripa â seŋticne Beanike jahe Kaisarea haeo hurâ Festo âgo bapic .
44025014	Eme jahe šoaŋ gâcne ehec ŋeŋe juju ehapire Festozi Paulore dâŋ binaŋ ecnehuc ŋicwofuŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Felikizi kâpâcwâru ŋic moc beherâ rame ŋehuc jukac .
44025015	Eme no fisirâ Jerusalem haeo fepe taha bapa micne â Judaŋic jaŋere soŋaŋ jaŋe norao tumaŋnehuc ŋic e qape hâmoocte munarembiŋ .
44025016	Munarepie no dâŋ ŋifecne šiŋuc jazapo : ` Romaŋic nâŋe qoqoricte sawa ŋic moc šikare mi qikiŋneeŋgopeneŋ . Nâŋe ŋic dâŋko râekicne e mecne â dâŋrune mecne mâmâc hetumaŋ-jopapene ŋifec â ŋifec dâŋ sâckoa mueŋgopieŋ . Ž
44025017	Iŋuc jazape Judaŋic norao warepie izia hae fureme jaŋe â e dâŋficko bâturec-jopapo .
44025018	Eme jaŋe ere sâqocne qizecne moc mufuaniŋmu muhape
44025019	jaŋe miti-jeŋicte hehefaric dâŋ â ŋic hâmokicne moc šâŋene Jesu ere dâŋ bajumbiŋ ” ŋic ere hâcne Paulozi šiŋuc muekac : ` E faharewec jukac . Ž
44025020	Eme no dâŋ iŋucnere kâuc barâ Paulo Jerusalem haeo feme ira dâŋticne mutarapemurâ âzâcnepo .
44025021	Âzâcnepe Paulo e Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋticne mutaraocte muwec . Eme Paulo e rara dameŋ maickeme mupe Roma ŋicwofuŋtao raocte kâpâcwâru ficko woŋec jukac . ”
44025022	Festozi iŋuc muhuc âzâcneme Agripazi muwec : “ No ŋic e hâcne dâŋ moc mume manapemurâ enarekac . ” Eme Festozi muwec , “ Sâcne , tomâcko manazemec . ”
44025023	Hae fureme Agripa â Beanike jahe eri qaraweŋ-jekichec tutumaŋ ficko fepire momori soŋaŋ kâcɋene â hae irec ŋic fekicne mâmâc bâjâpec-jofarâ fembiŋ . Fefârepie Festozi mume Paulo bafembiŋ .
44025024	Bafepie Festozi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋicwofuŋ Agripa â ŋicfâc-nane gâcne dâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ . Ŋic domakac ši ere erâ Judaŋic wemo afecnezi Jerusalem haeo fotarie-narehuc wira owac erâ mumbiŋ , ` E mi jujâmbâŋkezejec . Ž
44025025	No ine bahac-ticnere manape šika kiocte irec sâc mi ewec . Eme Roma ŋicwofuŋte muwecte erao sorepe raocmu .
44025026	Erâ dâŋ fârine basahuc ŋicbomboŋ sâkore papia qâreŋkepemurâ fâcke turuŋ ekopac . Eme irec hâcne ŋic kecši e ŋoŋerao â ŋicwofuŋ Agripa gorao râepe domakac . Eme ŋoŋe fuŋne-ticne bataniŋkepie dâŋticne qâreŋkepe razejec .
44025027	No kâpâcwâru ŋic moc kiŋticnere dâŋ mi qâreŋkehuc Roma haeo mâc sorepe raocte manape quŋkekac . ”
44026001	Eme Agripazi Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Gahac fuŋnege mutec mananaŋ . ” Eme Paulozi meticne sicnerâ dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec :
44026002	“ Judaŋic dâŋzi dâŋ enarehuc jueŋgopieŋ irec ŋifecne ŋicwofuŋ Agripa miŋecgac gore maio mupemurâ bunane biaŋkekac .
44026003	Go hâcne Judaŋic mitire hehefaric-nâŋecte â wiac eenâŋecte fuŋne manaekic . Irec go mana uruehaŋtec dâŋnane mupe .
44026004	“ No motec ɋie-naneoa Jerusalem haeo ŋic âgofâc-nane jaŋere ŋondeŋko juku sokapo .

45001004	erâ e maŋɋaɋac bâbâfua Mârohec jujuzi Anuture Ŋokâ jukac , irec fuŋne hâmokonec faharewecko fua taniŋke-jâmbâŋkewec .
45001005	Jesu Kristo e Wofuŋ-nâŋeczi aki anonoc enarehuc aposolo gie tahacnuwec . Ehuc mâreŋ sâc ŋic miti jazepe mana rereŋ epie Jesure šâŋe biŋe raocte munarewec .
45001006	Eme ŋoŋe jaŋere âgofâc jaha , Jesu Kristore ŋicfâc eniŋte hefârec-ŋopakicne , irec gie i ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha bapere munarewec .
45001007	Roma haeonec Anuture jorofâc , tiriŋic mucŋopakicne , ŋoŋere hâcne papia ši qâreŋkekopac . Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
45001008	Miti babaju-ŋeŋicte mâreŋ sâc manapie biaŋkekacte qanaŋ ŋoŋere erâ daŋge mupe Jesu Kristorao qarâ Anutu-nanerao fotâcnekac .
45001009	No Ŋokâ-ticnere Biŋebiaŋ muhuc maŋnanezi Anutu kiŋaŋ qacnepe fuŋne-nane manakacte ere maio dâŋ ši mupe mananiŋ :
45001010	No numucneekopac sâc ŋoŋere mâmâc hati manasuekopac , ehuc Anutu maname sâckeme hata bâfua-nareme ŋoŋerao fâpemurâ âzâcneekopac .
45001011	No ŋoŋe honec-ŋopapere enareekac . Ehuc fârâ maŋte bâmec moc baŋarepe qiŋ herâ juniŋte muekopac .
45001012	Me kecšiŋuc mupe : No ŋoŋerao fâpe mamanasiŋte fârine nowac gowatuŋ ehuc keketeŋ enšepeneŋ .
45001013	Erâ âgofâc-nane , fuŋne-nane kâuc banšipiŋte šiŋuc ŋazape : No ŋicguru gâcne jaŋerao eeckopac iŋuc jaha ŋoŋerao fârâ miti giere fârine piticne bâfuapemurâ hati muekopac . Erâ fâzo mupe sâc wiac gâcnezi niŋgiŋnume juekopac .
45001014	Noni ŋic kosa . Grikŋic â kâte sanaŋ , mamanahec â mutucne mâmâc mitizi tofa bazu-jarepemurâ munarekicne .
45001015	Irec Romaŋic ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapemurâ maŋnanezi afeckeekopac .
45001016	No Biŋebiaŋte manape mimi gaŋgaŋnehec mi eekac , i Anuture tâpirihec , irec mana sakac eniŋmu sâc bâpiaŋ-jopaocmu , Judaŋic hâcne , erâ Grikŋic mâmâc .
45001017	Biŋebiaŋko hâcne Anuture tiŋne fua taniŋkeekac , i hâcne eki mamanasiŋhec jaŋe tahac-jopaekac , ehame mamanasiŋko utuckeniŋmu . Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Biaŋkekicnezi mamanasiŋte erâ juju hotâckeocmu . ”
45001018	Ŋiczi ine Anutu qamaserâ sindaŋ ehuc kike hata-ticne hesifuckeeŋgopieŋte kimbeŋ ticnezi sambâŋkonec fua taniŋkeekac .
45001019	Anuture fuŋne gâcne ŋiczi mamanane i manaeŋgopieŋ , Anutu jahac bataniŋke-jarewec .
45001020	Anutu e ŋiczi mi hohonene , â mâreŋ bâfuahuc ine wiac fuŋne fuŋne râewec izi tâpiri sanaŋ-ticne â qâreŋ-ticne bataniŋkeme sâcne hone mana tarac eeŋgopieŋ . Irec ŋic gâcne jaŋe wemocko kâuc bahuc sahac ŋeŋezic dâŋ muniŋmu .
45001021	Jaŋe ine Anutu jukac i mana-bipiehuc mi jukac-tinac eha araŋ mi bacnembiŋ â mucne bacne mi ecnembiŋ , aricne . Jaŋe mumusifuc fuŋne fuŋne bâfuahuc maŋmutuc epie dapâczi foŋjopawec .
45001022	Ehuc nâŋe mamanahec juŋgopeneŋ muhuc sâke bâbâc eku maŋmutuc embiŋ .
45001023	Iŋuc ejareme jaŋe Anutu juju hati e araŋ mi bacnehuc ŋic â wipe â qowi â homa , wiac sisirowene hâcne irec ɋâŋ qâqâtâc barâ araŋ bacnembiŋ .
45001024	Iŋuc epie Anutuzi hone suŋgiŋ ejareme maŋzi sasec kosa hurerâ mamakâc ehuc maŋ sahac-jeŋic bâsâqorembiŋ .
45001025	Jaŋe Anutu jâmbomac rune râpeckerâ burec maickembiŋ . Ehuc ru bâbâfua-Jeŋic qikiŋnerâ wiac bâfuakicne araŋ bacnehuc kiŋaŋ qacnembiŋ . Wiac bâfua-fârewec e mumuteŋheczi mumuteŋhec jurašihuc jume sâckeocmu . Jâmbomac .
45001026	Ŋic jaŋe e hâcne râpeckembiŋte suŋgiŋ-jopame sasec sâqocne jâmbâŋ bâfuambiŋ . Ehuc ŋokac jaŋe Anutuzi hata muwec i qâsorierâ mi jujuo rambiŋ .
45001027	Á ŋic jaŋe iŋuc jaha ŋowe ŋonâŋ juju qikiŋnerâ maŋjeŋicko sasecte šocsâko šame jaŋe jaŋackoaŋ mamakâc fuŋmoc bâfuambiŋ . Erâ bâbâsifuc-jeŋicte okacne maŋ sahac sisipiric rombiŋ .
45001028	Jaŋe Anuture fuŋne mana-bipiehuc enšaŋauc ecnepie suŋgiŋ-jopame maŋjeŋic bâzickeme wiac mi eene i hâcne embiŋ .
45001029	Ehuc wiac hehesicne fuŋne fuŋne hurepie fewec , sindaŋ , andac , râŋgeŋne , erâ maŋjeŋicko iiŋguuŋ â šika â rârâsi â eeatuc , erâ gibioc izi fusucmakicne .
45001030	Jaŋe gupe bapa , micko âkec ŋic , Anutu kisâ eecne , šaubacne , pepecne , sahac mumuteŋ , sâqocnere hata bâbâfua , neŋgoc mamac dâŋ qaqatara ,
45001031	maŋ mamanasu tâmiric juju , doc bapa , uruc jauŋ tâmiric juju .
45001032	Wiac iŋucne ehuc sipirickezo , Anuture micdâŋ iŋuc fokac i mana-bipiehuc sifu eeŋgopieŋ , erâ i sawa mâcne , gâcnezi epie hume keteŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ wâc .
45002001	Irec ŋic go wemocko fuŋnege murârâŋnecmu ? Ŋic gâcnezi bahac bâfuapie mana sâqore-jarehuc gahacne fuŋne bataniŋkeekic hâcne . Mana sâqore-jareekomec , go ijaha hâcne eekomec i ¡
45002002	Eme Anutuzi ŋic iŋuc eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne bazu-jareme sâcke-hâmoekac iŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ .
45002003	Ŋic go gâcne jaŋere dâŋbahac muhuc ijaha eekic , ehuc “ no Anutuzi akicnuocmu ” iŋuc mu wiac moc ezic ine ¡
45002004	Me Wofuŋzi buuruc â wama ruaine sâc fekicne egarehuc akicguhuc jume go wemocte manatâc qatakic ehuc juekic ? Go maŋge bârisiecmurâ Anutuzi buuruc egareekac i mi mana taraekic me ?
45002005	Go maŋsanaŋ erâ maŋge mi bârisiehuc šocfiki bafeku seroŋ batec šoc šaza dameŋko Anuture mumutara dâŋ fârine fua taniŋkeme šâhâmocguocmu .
45002006	Anutuzi ŋic eebapa-nâŋecte sâc furine nârezokac hâcne .
45002007	Ŋic eehâmo gie paŋšâic bahuc eri tatamac â juju saric bâfuaniŋte samarieniŋmu jaŋe juju sanaŋ jarezokac .
45002008	Ŋic râŋgeŋne dâŋ fâri qizecne bâsuehuc wiac hehesicne bajuniŋmu jaŋerao ine wiac šâšâicne â mimicne bâfuaocmu .
45002009	Sâqocne bapa sasawa , Judaŋic hâcne â Grikŋic mâmâc , jaŋe šâic serereŋ â hâhâwic sâko fua-jareocmu .
45002010	Tiŋne Juniŋmu sasawa , Judaŋic hâcne â Grikŋic mâmâc , jaŋe eri tatamac â wama fua-jareocmu .
45002011	Anutu e ra rowec ware rowec mi focnekac .
45002012	Ŋic sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric juhuc sâqocne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric jaha sipirickeniŋmu . Á sâcmutâc dâŋhec juhuc sâqocne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa Anutuzi sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko dâŋjeŋic mutara-jareocmu .
45002013	Sâcmutâc dâŋ mâc hazeczi mananiŋmu jaŋe Anutuzi honec-jopame tiŋne mi eŋgopieŋ , manarâ reŋkeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine tiŋne mujareocmu .
45002014	Ŋic qâpuc sâcmutâc dâŋ mi mufua-jarekicne jaŋe maŋjeŋicte sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc ine sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiriczi sâcmutâc dâŋhec tinac eeŋgopieŋ .
45002015	Iŋuc epie sâcmutâc dâŋ i maŋjeŋicko qâreŋkekicne , irec fuŋne jaŋgeŋkeekac . Sâcmutâc dâŋ maŋjeŋicko qâreŋkekicnere maŋjeŋiczi tutuc qajareekac , erâ wâc maŋ mamanasu-jeŋiczi foc forisic ehuc ŋifec mu qatarac eekac â ŋifec mu bâmiriŋ eekac .
45002016	I dameŋ sâkore iŋuc eekac . Ira Anutuzi Jesu Kristo ecneme maŋnâŋecko wiac soŋsoŋ fokac irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu . No Biŋebiaŋ muekopac irec sâcko bataniŋkeocmu hâcne .
45002017	Go šâŋege Judaŋic muhuc sâcmutâc dâŋzi roŋgâŋ egareme herâ foekic . Erâ no Anuture fuŋne manakopac muhuc sahac fefe juekic .
45002018	Go Anuture micdâŋ manaekic , erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ qazu-garekicnere keci ezo , keci mi ezo i mana wosâeekic .
45002019	Ehuc gahacnere šiŋuc muekic : “ No tiŋtuŋ sâcne jowa qataŋ ejarepemu , â dapâcko juŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne batamae-jarepemu ,
45002020	â ŋic maŋpuriŋhec jaŋe sâcne jaza bâtiŋ ejarepemu , â ɋiemaŋ jaŋe wiac sâcne qazu-jarepemu . No sâcmutâc dâŋhecte mamana â dâŋfâri irec wamboŋne rauckerâ jukopac i . ”
45002021	Go iŋuc muekiczi ŋic gâcne miti qazu-jarehuc gahacne maŋ mi qazucneekic . Go ŋic fiuc mi ronšepieŋ jazahuc gahac fiuc roekic .
45002022	Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋohe bebehec mi ezepirec jazahuc gahac ŋonâŋge beheekic . Go nemuɋâŋ sureekiczi nemu ufuŋte wiac fiuc roekic .
45002023	Go sâcmutâc dâŋte manasuhuc maŋfefe eekiczi sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuahuc Anutu gâc hecneekic .
45002024	Irec hâcne kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : “ Qâpuc jaŋe ŋoŋere kiŋte erâ Anuture šâŋe musoriŋkeeŋgopieŋ . ”
45002025	Go sahacgao Anuture ma bakicne i sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋketec fârinehec eocmu . Me sâcmutâc dâŋ qataratec sahacgao ma izi fârimâc eocmu .
45002026	Erâ dâŋ irec ŋifecne qac qârisic fokac wâc . Ŋic moc ma tâmiriczi sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkeocmuo mahec tinac eocmu .
45002027	Ehuc ma tâmiric fuarâ juekaczi sâcmutâc dâŋte gie baocmu eki ine fuŋnege rituocmu , miti papia â mahec juhuc sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuaekic gore fuŋne hâcne rituocmu .
45002028	Moc e mâc sahaczi Judaŋic hawari eocmu â sahacko sawa mahec juocmu , iŋucnezi Judaŋic fârine mi eocmu .
45002029	Maŋzi Judaŋic izi fârine . Á sahacko sâcmutâc dâŋte ma rojuju i mâcne , maŋko Mârore ma rojuju izi fârine . Ŋic iŋucnere ŋiczi mâcne , Anutuzi maname biaŋkeocmu .
45003001	Hâc , eme Judaŋic jaŋe qâpuc jaŋehec sâc mocjaha eŋgopieŋ , â sahacko ma i wiac racne me ?
45003002	Iŋuc aricne . Judaŋic jaŋe wiac bocjaha tahac-jopakicne . Jaŋe hâcne Anutuzi biŋedâŋ fuŋne fuŋne jazame irec rune embiŋ .
45003003	Eme weniŋuc ? Judaŋic gâcne jaŋe dâŋte woŋec juku pârâckembiŋte šiŋuc muzo me ? “ Dodocke-jeŋiczi Anutu mume sasanaŋ-ticne bawahaocmu . ”
45003004	I aric kereŋne ¡ Anutu e buc mume sasanaŋ â ŋic ine mumu dodocne , iŋuc muzo . Miti qâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Go mumutiŋgezi dâŋfâri eocmu , â mumutaragezi ɋaɋacne eocmu . ”
45003005	Eme hehesic-nâŋeczi Anutu tiŋne-ticnere fuŋne bajaŋgeŋkekacte weniŋuc muzo ? šiŋuc muzo me ? “ Fuŋne iŋuc fokacte Anutuzi irec okacne nâreme mi sâckeocmu . ” ( Dâŋ i ŋic mamanare sâcko mukopac . ( c )
45003006	I aric kereŋne ¡ Anutu e hehesic-nâŋecte okacne nâreme sâckeocmu . Mâc muzac wemocko mâreŋŋic šeŋgoma dâŋnâŋec sâcne mutarazac .
45003007	Eme ŋifec ine burecdâŋ-nanezi Anuture dâŋfâri dopeckeme šâŋe biŋe-ticne irec erâ fekacko wemocte sifu no wâc sâqocne bapa munarehuc okacne nareekac ?
45003008	Erâ wemocte šiŋuc mi mueŋgopeneŋ : “ Sâqocne bapene ŋerisierâ fârine biaŋne fuaoc me . ” Nâŋe iŋuc mueŋgopeneŋ munârehuc micko âkec enâreeŋgopieŋ hâcne . Dâŋ iŋucne muhuc hata i âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne fua-jareme sâckeocmu .
45003009	Eme weniŋuc ? Judaŋiczi ŋic gâcne jowarurâ sâc moc juŋgopeneŋ me ? I aricne jâmbâŋ . Biac mumbeneŋ , Judaŋic â Grikŋic nânâc mâmâc sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaeŋgopeneŋ .
45003010	Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Ŋic moczi tiŋne moc mi jukac , aric ɋaɋacne ;
45003011	moczi mamanahec moc mi jukac , moczi Anutu wira basac mi ecneekac .
45003012	Jaŋe qâsoriekicne sasawa , šeŋgoma repirembiŋ ; moczi moc wiac biaŋne mi eekac , arictac jâmbâŋ .
45003013	Marac-jeŋic i hâmoc qâŋɋâŋ bâbâfua , nameŋ-jeŋic forisieme eatuc dâŋ wefuekac , qotâ marasiŋ kisoŋnerâ jueŋgopieŋ .
45003014	Bipic-jeŋic sâwec â aaric dâŋte gegerockeekac .
45003015	Ʒikare kike afec jueŋgopieŋ .
45003016	Ima samaki bahuc tuhu bâfuaeŋgopieŋ .
45003017	Wamare hata ine kâuc baeŋgopieŋ .
45003018	Á šâŋe mai-jeŋicko Anuture hâhâwic mi fokac . ”
45003019	Nâŋâc šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : Sâcmutâc dâŋ i dâŋ rune nâŋe nazakicne . I ŋic sasawa fuŋne-nâŋec rituhuc micnâŋec ɋâtâocte ekicne . Eme ŋic mâmâc sasawa kiŋnâŋec Anuturao fua-fârekac .
45003020	Sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ kiŋ nânâwoc ro i Anuturao moc mi fokac . Sâcmutâc dâŋzi sindaŋ-nâŋec bataniŋkeekac hâcne .
45003021	Eme irec sâcmutâc dâŋ fohame Anutuzi tiŋne-ticne fua taniŋkeocte hatane moc bâfuawec fokac , hata i sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko â porofete jaŋerao wâc biŋedâŋ-ticne mu qâreŋ ekicne .
45003022	Jesu Kristo manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc erâ juju , hata i hâcne mamanasiŋhec sasawa jaŋere biŋe ekac . Fuŋne-nâŋec bârâwiŋ mi fokac ,
45003023	Nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa sâqorembeŋte Anuture eri tatamacko fifisinere sâc mi eŋgopeneŋ .
45003024	Ehame Kristo Jesu e kiwiric-nâŋec rowecte Anutuzi aki anonoc-ticnere erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpoekac .
45003025	Eki mume Jesu e socticnezi sâqocne-nâŋecte erâ taha bawec , eme e manasiŋkeniŋmuzi taha i biŋeckeniŋmu . Sâqocne ewarehuc jukicne irec kiŋ i Anutuzi buuruc-ticnere râeme fowarehuc juwecte Jesu hâmocko râewecko tiŋnere fuŋne bataniŋkewec .
45003026	E tiŋnere rune juekac , â Jesu manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe kiŋfâsâc bacjopaekac , irec fuŋne dameŋ šiŋuczia taniŋkeocte iŋuc hâcne ewec .
45003027	Eme mumuteŋ-nâŋec moc fokac me ? Aricne , mumuteŋ-nâŋec hetâtiekicne . Wemozi hetâtiewec ? Eehâmo giere hatazi me ? Aricne , mamanasiŋte hatazi .
45003028	Irec dâŋ šiŋuc manapene fozejec : Ŋic nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋkere mâcne , mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc fuaeŋgopeneŋ .
45003029	Me Anutu e Judaŋic nâŋere Anutu sawa , qâpuc jaŋere aricne ? Iŋuc mâcne , e qâpuc jaŋere Anutu jaha wâc .
45003030	E Anutu-nâŋec mocjaha jukaczi hâcne Judaŋic â qâpuc mâmâc mamanasiŋ-nâŋecte erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpoekac .
45003031	Eme iŋuc muhuc mamanasiŋte erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ hetâtieŋgopeneŋ me ? Aric kereŋne , sâcmutâc dâŋ hešakieŋgopeneŋ .
45004001	Eme sahackopec mimiŋne-nâŋec Abraham e wemo bâfuawec munaŋmu ?
45004002	E jahacne eehâmo giere erâ kiŋticne hefâsâewecko ropaŋ sâcne focnezac . Erâ Anuture maio ine arictâc .
45004003	Miti papiao dâŋ šiŋuc fokac i : “ Abraham e Anutu manasiŋkeme irec erâ maname kiŋticne tarawec . ”
45004004	Moc e gie bame furime râcnepene izi katucmâc rârâcne mi ekac , tofa babazucne ekac .
45004005	Á moc e ine eehâmo gie mi bapa , sâqocne bapa kiŋjeŋic beheekac e manasiŋkeocmu , eme Anutuzi ere hâcne mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ maname kiŋfâsâc eocmu .
45004006	Dawidi e iŋuc jaha Anutuzi ŋic moc eehamo gie mi baha , akickehuc kiŋ behecneocmu ere mu šeri ehuc kecšiŋuc qâreŋkewec :
45004007	“ Bahac-jeŋic behekicne , â sâqocne-jeŋic bâtâmirekicne , jaŋere manape šerine ekac ;
45004008	ŋic moc Wofuŋzi manacneme kiŋhec mi eekac , ere manape šerine ekac . ”
45004009	Mušeri dâŋ kecši i mahec nâŋere biŋe sawa ekac me ma tâmiric jaŋere mâmâc ekac ? Abrahamte šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : E Anutuzi mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ kiŋ behecnewec .
45004010	Mo dameŋko behecnewec , mahec juhame me ma tâmitric juhame behecnewec ? Mahec mâcne , ma tâmiric juhame behecnewec .
45004011	E ma tâmiric juhuc Anutu manasiŋkeme kiŋticne behecnewec irec maqâreŋ šâhec râecnewec . Eme Abraham e iŋuc ehuc ine ma tâmiric jaŋe Anutu manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere micne ewec .
45004012	Erâ mahec nâŋere micne bapa wâc ewec , erâ mahecte sawa mâcne , e ma tâmiric juhuc mamanasiŋte kike hata âtewec , hata ijaha mimiŋ qâjâpec âtehuc Abraham micne bapa-nâŋec mucnepene sâckeocmu .
45004013	Anutuzi Abraham â ɋâricfâc-ticne mâreŋ sâko mâreŋ biŋe qajarewec , i sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋte erâ mâcne , mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ kiŋticne behehuc iŋuc ecnewec .
45004014	Eme biŋe qajarekicne hâcne i sâcmutâc dâŋ rune jaŋere ezac muzac , ine mamanasiŋzi wiac jawane ezac â mitio biŋedâŋ feŋec-nâpokicne i fârimâc ezac .
45004015	Sâcmutâc dâŋzi kiŋte okacne fai-nâŋecko râeekac . Sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiricko ine qaqatara mi fuaekac .
45004016	Irec hâcne wiac biŋe qanarekicne i mamanasiŋte erâ fuaocmu . Wemocte ? I aki anonoczi feŋeŋ râecneme Abrahamte ɋâricfâc sasawa nâŋâcnao sanaŋkeocte . Sâcmutâc dâŋko roweckembiŋ jaŋe sawa mâcne , Abrahamzi mamanasiŋ hata âtewec ijaha âteeŋgopeneŋ nâŋâcnao mâmâc . Eki hâcne Anuture maio apa wirec-nâŋec ekac .
45004017	Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Noni go ŋic gurune gurune jaŋere mamac ecmurâ mugarepo . ” Abraham e ine Anutu manasiŋkehuc šiŋuc manapaŋkewec : “ E hâmoc qâŋɋâŋ bâɋârezo murâ bâɋâreocmu â wiac mi fokac i mume fuaocmu . ”
45004018	E ŋicguru bocjaha jaŋere mamac ezokac , dâŋ i mana hameŋke-bipiehuc sifu irec mamanac juwec , šiŋuc âzâcnekicnere : “ Ɋâricfâcge iŋuc fuanšoŋgopieŋ . ”
45004019	Erâ wâc e jara-ticne 100 bazukicnezi e jahacne sahac bâmuzuckekicne â Sarare sahac kereŋkekicne i hone-bipiehuc mamanasiŋ-ticne sifu mi ŋeŋgoroŋkewec .
45004020	Anutuzi biŋedâŋ âzâcnewec i maname fârimâc mi ewec , ehuc mamanasiŋte sanaŋkerâ Anuture maname fekicne sâko ehame šiŋuc muhuc mana utuckewec :
45004021	Anutu e wiac mocte biŋe qaocmu i fârine sâcne bâfuaocmu .
45004022	Irec Abraham e mamanasiŋ focnewecte Anutuzi ere maname kiŋfâsâc ewec .
45004023	Anutuzi maname kiŋfâsâc ewec , dâŋ i Abrahamte sawa mi qâreŋkekicne , nâŋâcnere wâc mâmâc .
45004024	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârewec Anutu hâcne e manasiŋkepene nâŋâcnere iŋuc jaha maname kiŋfâsâc enaŋmu .
45004025	Jesu hâcne kiŋbahac-nâŋecte erâ hâmocko râekicne , erâ wâc kiŋfâsâc enaŋte hâmockonec bâɋârekicne .
45005001	Nâŋâc mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc embeŋte Jesu Kristorao qohotahuc Anuture wamao juŋgopeneŋ .
45005002	Jesu ekizia motâc ronârewecte akio juŋgopeneŋ wâc . Erâ juku Anuture huriri qâreŋ fua tâcneme hone šiziwenaŋmu irec mamanac juhuc mu šeri eeŋgopeneŋ .
45005003	Erâ i sawa mâcne , hume serereŋ jujure wâc mu šeri eeŋgopeneŋ , ehuc šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : Hume serereŋ jujuzi maŋuruc bâfuaekac ,
45005004	maŋuruczi sasanaŋ bâfuaekac , sasanaŋzi sambâŋte woworic bâfuaekac .
45005005	Sambâŋte woworic juocmuzi ine mi qurutuaocmu . Tiri Mâro nârekicne eki Anuture maŋjauŋ maŋnâŋecko qoŋgiŋkewecte mi qurutuanaŋmu .
45005006	Kristo e ŋic nâŋâc hâŋ qa otec qa ehuc juhapene dameŋ-ticne maickeme sâqocne bapa nâŋâcne okacne hâmowec .
45005007	Ŋic tiŋne mocte erâ hâhâmo i ŋic nâŋâcnao mi mecne fokac , mâc ŋic biaŋne mocte erâ hâhâmo ine fufuane mecne .
45005008	Anutu eki ine , sâqocne bâfuahuc bunao bahuc juhapene maŋjauŋ-ticne bâfuahuc mume Kristozi okac-nâŋec hâmowec .
45005009	Eme ši socticnere erâ kiŋfâsâc embeŋte okac dameŋko roroŋ sasapec sâcne enâre-jâmbâŋkeocmu .
45005010	Nâŋâc Anutu râsi ecnehuc juhapene ŋokâ-ticnere hâmocte erâ miriŋ bacnâpowec . Eme ši miriŋ bacnâpowecko juju-ticnere erâ sâcne juju saricko râec-nâpo-jâmbâŋkeocmu .
45005011	Erâ i sawa mâcne , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristozi aki bâfuahuc Anutuhec bâturec-nâpowecte Anutu hâcne mu šeri ecneeŋgopeneŋ .
45005012	Irec šiŋuc mananaŋ : Ŋic mocjahare erâ sâqocne mâreŋko fuawec , â sâqocnere erâ hâmoc fuawec , ehuc ŋic sasawa jaŋerao fotâcnewec . Iŋuc fuame ŋic sasawa sâqore-fârembiŋ .
45005013	Sâcmutâc dâŋ mi fuahame sâqocnezi qanaŋ fuarâ fowec . Erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ arictacte mâc forâ fowefuwec .
45005014	Ehame hâmoczi Adamtao fuŋkerâ ŋic juwefumbiŋ jaŋe ŋicbomboŋ ejare warehuc juhame Mose fuawec , ine dâŋ qâhuckehuc Adamte sâc mi bâfuambiŋ jaŋerao wâc sifu fotâcnewec . Adam e hâcne hâmocte micne bapa ehuctecne , šâhecko jujure micne bapa fuaocte mukicne ere sâsâcne ewec .
45005015	Aki anonoczi ine dâŋ qaqare sâc mi ekac . Ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere bocjahazi hâmo sipiric embiŋ . Ehame Anuture uruc jauŋ i ine ŋic mocjaha Jesu Kristo ere aki anonocte erâ , Adamte dâŋ qaqa sirickehuc , ŋic bocjaha tahac-nâpokicne
45005016	Ŋifec aki anonoc â ŋifec ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere fârine jahe sâcjekic bârâwiŋ . Ŋic mocjahare bahaczi hârâcte mumutara bâfuawec , aki anonoczi ine bahac bocjaha qofackehuc kiŋfâsâc bâfuawec .
45005017	Ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere erâ hâmoczi ŋicbomboŋ ewec , ehame ine aki anonoc fofo dunduŋ â kiŋfâsâc katucmâc fufua i ro maŋ eeŋgopeneŋzi ine ŋic mocjaha Jesu Kristo ere erâ juju sanaŋko ŋicbomboŋ ejâmbâŋkerâ junaŋmu .
45005018	Irec šiŋuc : Ŋic mocjahazi dâŋ qaqa bâfuame ŋic mâmâc sasawa hârâcte biŋe embeŋ , iŋuc jaha ŋic mocjaha tiŋne jume kiŋfâsâc ehuc juju biŋecke-fârembeŋ .
45005019	Ŋic mocjahare qaqatarare bocjahazi sâqorembeŋ , iŋuc jaha ŋic mocjahare dâŋrereŋte bocjahazi biaŋkenaŋmu .
45005020	Sâcmutâc dâŋ e ine sâqocnezi ɋârâŋkeocte ŋondeŋnao rašiwec . Eme sâqocnezi fua fehame aki anonoczi sirickehuc meckecnewec .
45005021	Fârine šiŋuc fuaocte : Sâqocnezi hâmocte uucmaŋko ŋicbomboŋ ewec jukac , iŋuc jaha aki anonoczi ŋicbomboŋ erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpohuc juju sanaŋko râec-nâpozejec . I Jesu Kristo Wofuŋ-nâŋec ere erâ iŋuc fuazejec .
45006001	Eme weniŋuc muzo ? Sâqocnere gie bahuc jaha jupene aki anonoczi fua ɋârâŋkehuc sirickezejec , iŋuc muzo me ?
45006002	Iŋuc misac ¡ Sâqocne hâmocnembeŋzi wemocko irec maŋnao šuhuckerâ junaŋmu ?
45006003	Me kecšiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ ? Miti Opâ ruahuc Jesu Kristorao šuhuckembeŋzi hâmoc-ticnao ŋeutuckembeŋ .
45006004	Ine hâcne , nâŋâc Miti Opâ ruahuc Kristohec mâmâc hâmo duduc ekicne , eme Mamac eri tatamac-ticnezi Kristo bâɋâreme hâmockonec faharewec jukac , iŋuc jaha nâŋâc ɋârerâ juju ɋâri moc junšepeneŋ .
45006005	Nâŋâc hâmoc-ticnere hawari ehuc erao šuhuckembeŋte fafahare-ticnao sâc i jaha ehuc šuhuckenaŋmu .
45006006	Ʒiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Maŋraŋɋa-nâŋec Jesuhec mâmâc maripoŋko qakicne , i maŋsahac-nâŋecko sâqocnere tâpiri ŋeŋgoroŋkeocte â sâqocnere kiŋaŋ mocwâc mi qanaŋte .
45006007	Moc e hâmome sâqocnere niŋgiŋ ŋetaracneocmu .
45006008	Kristohec hâmombeŋko ine ehuc wâc junaŋmu , iŋuc manapaŋkenaŋmu .
45006009	Kristore manaŋgopeneŋ , e hâmockonec fahareweczi mocwâc mi hâmoocmu , hâmoczi ŋicbomboŋ mocwâc mi ecneocmu .
45006010	Hâmowec i sâqocnere arec mocjaha hâmome tarawec eme ši jukac i Anuture erâ jukac .
45006011	Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ŋaŋacnere manapie sâqocne hâmocnembiŋ ehuc Jesu Kristo ehec Anutu jucneŋgopieŋ ezejec .
45006012	Sâqocnezi sahac-ŋeŋic sisirowenao ŋicbomboŋ eŋarezo mume mi manacnenšepieŋ , â sahac-ŋeŋiczi sasecte suruc-ŋopame i wâc mi manacnenšepieŋ .
45006013	Erâ wâc me sahac-ŋeŋic i hehesicte mi qikiŋnepie sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qazejec . Aricne , ŋoŋe hâmockonec bâɋârec-ŋopakicnezi Anuture gieo rašinšepieŋ , ehuc mesahac-ŋeŋic Anuture qikiŋnepie tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qazejec .
45006014	Ŋoŋe sâcmutâc dâŋko mâcne , Anuture aki anonocko jueŋgopieŋte sâqocnezi ŋicbomboŋ mi eŋareocmu .
45006015	Eme ši wenac ezo ? Anuture aki anonocko rašihapene sâcmutâc dâŋte aka râriewecte sâqocne bazo me ? Iŋuc aricne ¡
45006016	Me ŋoŋe šiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Ŋicbomboŋ moc maŋ sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnecnehuc micne reŋkeniŋmuzi ere kiŋaŋ qaqafâc erâ gie-ticne baniŋmu . Sâqocnezi ŋicbomboŋ-ŋeŋic eme ere kiŋaŋ qahuc juku hâmo sipiric eniŋmu me micrereŋzi ŋicbomboŋ-ŋeŋic eme ere kiŋaŋ qahuc tiŋkeniŋmu .
45006017	Ŋoŋe sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaqa juwarembiŋ i tarawec , eme ši mitire hata qazu-ŋarekicne irec sâcko maŋzi manahuc reŋkeeŋgopieŋ irec Anutu muteŋkezo .
45006018	Ŋoŋe sâqocnaonec batarac-ŋopakicnezi tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ juŋgopieŋ .
45006019	Maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic gegec dodocnere ŋicko wiac fokac ira sâc hehuc dâŋ ŋazakopac . Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha me sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnepie sasec â sindaŋ irec kiŋaŋ qaqa ehame kosa jujumbieŋ , eme dameŋ šiŋuczia me sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnepie tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa ehame maŋfuru erâ junšepieŋ .
45006020	Sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaqa jumbiŋko tiŋnere niŋgiŋ mi foŋarewec .
45006021	Eme dameŋ ira wemo fârine bâfuambiŋ ? Fârine hotâckembiŋ irec šiŋuczia manapie miminehec eekac ” eme irec faicnao hâmoc bâbâfuane fokac .
45006022	Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine sâqocnere niŋgiŋ ŋeŋgoroŋkeme Anuture kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ juŋgopieŋ , ehuc fârine maŋfuru rombiŋ â šâhec juju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu .
45006023	Sâqocnere furine hâmoc rozo , â Anutu aki anonoc-ticnere fârine ine Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo erao šuhuckehuc juju sanaŋ rozo .
45007001	Âgo bureŋ , sâcmutâc dâŋ mamana ŋoŋere mukopac ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋke i hâmocko taraekac .
45007002	Irec hâcne ŋokac moc e ŋowene ɋâricne juhame bebehene mi fokac . sâcmutâc dâŋko iŋuc mukicne . Ŋowe-ticne hâmome ine sâcmutâc dâŋko ŋowe ŋonâŋ jahere mukicne i tarakac .
45007003	Ŋokac moc e ŋowe-ticne ɋâricne juhame beherâ ŋic moctao qohotame šuhuc bâtâcte kiŋ hurekac muzo . Ŋowe-ticne hâmome ine sâcmutâczi niŋgiŋ-jofawec niŋgiŋ i tâcneocmu : ehame ŋic moc baocmuo šuhuc bâtâcte kiŋ mi hureocmu .
45007004	Âgo bureŋ , ŋoŋere fuŋne ijaha fokac . Kristo e sahac-ticne hâmocte qikiŋnewec , erao šuhuckehuc sâcmutâc dâŋ hâmocnembiŋ . Ʒi ine ru mocte embiŋ . Hâmockonec faharewec jukac ere hâcne embiŋ . Irec nâŋâc Anutu fârine bâfuacnenšepeneŋ ¡
45007005	Juju raŋɋa jujumbeneŋ dameŋ ira sâqocnere sasec i sâcmutâc dâŋzi šocticne ficneme me sahac-nâŋecko gie-ticne bajujec . Iŋuc enâreme hâmo sipiricte fârine bâfuambeŋ .
45007006	Ʒi ine sâcmutâc dâŋ hâmocnepene niŋgiŋ-ticne tarawecko dâŋqâreŋte hata raŋɋane mi âtehuc Mârore hata ɋâricne âteŋgopeneŋ .
45007007	Eme ši weniŋuc muzo ? Sâcmutâc dâŋ i sâqocne me ? I aricne i ¡ Mâc sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric muzac , no sâqocnere fuŋne mi mana tarazapo . Sâcmutâc dâŋzi šiŋuc mufua-nâreekac : “ Go andac mi ezemec . ” Dâŋ i mi fome muzac andacte kâuc bazapo .
45007008	Sâqocne e ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋesiŋ ecnehame maŋnane suruckeme andac fuŋne fuŋne fuawec . Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc mi fome muzac sâqocnezi mâc mâteŋkerâ fozac .
45007009	No mârâc jaha sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc tâmiricko sâcne juhâmopo . Izi šâhec sâcmutâc dâŋzi bâfuacnume sâqocnezi maŋnaneo ɋâreme hâmopo .
45007010	Sâcmutâc dâŋzi enareme juhâmopemurâ mukicne izi hâcne ŋerisierâ šikanehec ewec .
45007011	Ine hâcne sâqocnezi hobeteŋko ŋesiŋnehuc sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ eatucnuhuc qâhâmocnuwec .
45007012	Erâ ine šiŋuc : Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc e bahacmâc , â bâfâuckehuc moc moc mutâcnekicne i wâc bahacmâc â tiŋne â biaŋne .
45007013	Hâc , eme dâŋ biaŋnezi hâmoc bâfua-narewec ? Iŋuc mâcne , sâqocnezi nuwec . Sâqocne fuŋne-ticne taniŋke-jâmbâŋkeocte dâŋ biaŋnezi âki heha hâmocne nuwec . Sâqocnere manapene gâgâpâcne jâmbâŋ eocte sâcmutâc dâŋzi âki heha nuwec .
45007014	Nâŋâc šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Sâcmutâc dâŋ e Mârore tofa , no ine mâreŋte tofa , sâqocnere hozine .
45007015	No eebapa-nanere manape ririsi eekac . No wiac moc ezo enare-bipieme mi eekopac , â wiac sureekopac ine eekopac .
45007016	Erâ wiac sureekopac i ehuc ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi biaŋne irec fuŋne bataniŋkeekopac .
45007017	Eme hehesic eekopac i no nahacne maŋte mâcne , sâqocnezi maŋnaneo fohuc surucnume eekopac .
45007018	No fuŋne šiŋuc manakopac : Maŋnaneo , sahac biuc-nanere maŋko hâcne , biaŋnezi fic hae mi ewec jukac , wiac biaŋnere mumu I muekopac , â fârine bâbâfua ine arictac .
45007019	No wiac biaŋne ezepac muhuc mi eekopac , â wiac sâqocne mi ezepac muhuc ine eekopac .
45007020	Sâqocne mi ezo muhuc sifu eekopac ine šiŋucte , i no nahac mâcne , sâqocnezi maŋnaneo fic hae ewecte jâiŋko eekopac .
45007021	Norao sâcmutâc kecšiŋuc fuaekac : Wiac biaŋne ezo muhape sâqocnezi maicnuekac .
45007022	No maŋwâmbuŋ-nanezi Anutu sâcmutâc dâŋticnere mana aŋac eekopac .
45007023	Ehame me sahac-naneo sâcmutâc moc fokac izi maŋ mamanasu-nanere dâŋhec rârâsi eekopirec , ehuc niŋgiŋnume sâqocnere sâcmutâc dâŋ me sahac-naneo fic hae ewec ere kâpâcwâru ŋic eekopac
45007024	Ŋic huacbucne no mozi sahac-nane hâmocte biŋe ekicne hetara-nareocmu ?
45007025	Anutu e Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ muteŋkekopac . Eme šiŋuc hâcne : No nahac maŋ mamanasu-nanezi Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ kiŋaŋ qacneekopac , sahac-nanezi ine sâqocnere sâcmutâc dâŋ kiŋaŋ qacneekopac .
45008001	Eme Jesu Kristohec jueŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋerao sâqocnere okacne mumutara-jare moc mi fufuane .
45008002	Kristo Jesure erâ juju bâfua-nâreekac Mâro hâcne , ere sâcmutâc dâŋzi sâqocne â hâmoc irec sâcmutâc dâŋ bârârie-nârewec .
45008003	Sâcmutâc dâŋ e maŋraŋɋa-nâŋeczi tâpirine bawahame nâŋâcnao gie bâipiewec . Irec Anutu e šiŋuc ehuc maŋraŋɋa sâqocne-ticnere tâpiri qame wahawec : Ŋokâ-ticne soreme sâqocne bapa nâŋâcne sahac hawari rorâ sâqocnere due bawec .
45008004	Ine maŋraŋɋare hata mâcne , Mârore hata âteeŋgopeneŋ nâŋâcnao sâcmutâc dâŋrereŋ biaŋ fua-fâreocte iŋuc ekicne .
45008005	Juju raŋɋare hata âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic juju raŋɋare wiacte foekac , â Mârore hata âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic Mârore wiacte foekac .
45008006	Maŋraŋɋare wiacte manasuhuc sisipiric bâfuazo , â Mârore wiacte manasuhuc juju â wama bâfuazo .
45008007	Maŋraŋɋare wiacte mamanasu izi Anutu kisâ ecneekac . Ehuc sâcmutâc dâŋticne mi dapecneekac , i wemo-ticnezi sâcne ezac ¡
45008008	Maŋraŋɋahec jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere Anutuzi takickeekac .
45008009	Anuture Mârozi maŋŋeŋicko fic hae ewecko ine maŋraŋɋaopec mâcne , Mâroraopec utuckerâ jueŋgopieŋ . Moc e Kristore Mâro tâmiric juocmuzi ere ŋicbiŋe mi juocmu .
45008010	Kristozi maŋŋeŋicko jukacko sahac-ŋeŋiczi sâqocnere erâ hâmoc ruckekac , â maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋiczi ine kiŋfâsâc bacŋopakicnere juju ruckekac .
45008011	Eme Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârewec Anutu hâcne , ere Mârozi maŋŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ekacko , Kristo Jesu hâmockonec bâɋâreweczi maŋŋeŋicko Mâro-ticne jukac ere erâ sahac-ŋeŋic hâmocne i iŋuc jaha bâɋâreocmu .
45008012	Âgo bureŋ , irec hâcne maŋraŋɋazi wemo nâre tahac eekacte nâŋâc tofa bazucnehuc ere wiacko qohotanaŋmu ?
45008013	Ŋoŋe maŋraŋɋare wiacko qohotaniŋmuo sipirickeniŋmu . Á Mârore tâpirio sahacte dâŋ qaniŋmuo ine juju sâcne jurašihuc juniŋmu .
45008014	Anuture Mârozi de âsic ejareha jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne Anuture naru motecfâc .
45008015	Anutu e Mâro ŋarewec i kiŋaŋ qaqafâcne juhuc harierâ hâhâwic bacneniŋte mâcne , naru motecfâcne erâ juniŋte ŋarewec . Irec hâcne “ Mamac biaŋ-nâŋec ” muhuc wasickeeŋgopeneŋ .
45008016	Nâŋâc Anuture naru motecfâc jueŋgopeneŋ , dâŋ i Mârozi maŋnâŋecko musokame manaeŋgopeneŋ .
45008017	Naru motecfâcne juŋgopeneŋzi Anuture huhure wâc rauckenaŋmu , Kristohec mâmâc wirec rauckenaŋmu . Ʒira mâreŋko ehec šârâ hâriŋ faio junaŋmuo ehec eri tatamac biaŋko mâmâc jaha junaŋmu .
45008018	Sambâŋko Anutuzi eri aŋac bâfua-nâreocmu , i mâreŋko šâic busâqoc fokac ira sâc hepe mamakâc eocmu .
45008019	Anuture naru motecfâc eri aŋac-nâŋec fua tâcneocte , wiac bâfuac-jopakicne jaŋe irec woŋec juhuc maŋ hâhâŋ ejareekac .
45008020	Wiac omane jaŋe wâc bie gufec hâmo qanšaraŋte maŋnao râec-jopakicne , erâ jaŋacne maŋte mâcne , ŋiczi sahacko râec ejarewec . Erâ jaŋe iŋuc hati fohuc juniŋte mi mujarekicne .
45008021	Wiac omane jaŋe wâc hâmo qanšaraŋte niŋgiŋ hetararâ firiehuc Anuture naru motecfâc nâŋâcne eri aŋacko šuhuckeniŋmu hâcne .
45008022	Nâŋâc manaŋgopeneŋ , dameŋ i hâcne maickeocte wiac omane jaŋe harac huacbuc ehuc gozi kicjopame šâic manaeŋgopieŋ .
45008023	Erâ wiac omane jaŋe sawa iŋuc mi eeŋgopieŋ , sambâŋkonec qaqasune Mâro hâcne nârekicne nâŋâc iŋuc jaha , naru motecfâc-ticne juŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne Anutuzi , sahac-nâŋec bâfiriehuc , bataniŋkeocte woŋec juhuc maŋzi harac huacbuc eeŋgopeneŋ .
45008024	Nâŋâc bâpiaŋ-nâpokicne irec fârine tapamaŋko fokâc . Fârine tâtâc fuame muzac harac huacbuc mi enšapeŋ . Wiac i basahuc ine harac huacbuc ezo .
45008025	Fârine tâtâc mi fuame honeeŋgopeneŋte maŋzi worickehuc woŋec jueŋgopeneŋ hâcne .
45008026	Mâro e wâc gegec dodoc-nâŋecte erâ bafic-nâpoekac . Nâŋâc iŋuc me iŋuc numupene sâckeocmu , i mi mana-hâmoeŋgopeneŋte Mârozi âkehoc-nâporâ saŋuc ŋiczi mi mamanane i qaekac .
45008027	Ehame Anutu e maŋ hohonezi Mârore dâŋ manaekac . Mâro e mitiŋic jaŋere okacne Anutu dâŋsâc-ticnao numuekac .
45008028	Nâŋâc manaŋgopeneŋ , Anutu maŋzi jauŋkeniŋmu jaŋe wiac izi me izi fua-jarehuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋic dopecke-fâreocmu , ine eki hefârec-jopaocte maname fowecte hefârec-jopawec jaŋe hâcne .
45008029	Ŋic qanaŋ honec-jopame sâckewec jaŋe ŋokâ-ticnere hawari eniŋte mucjopawec . Eme ɋafâc-ticne bocjaha ehapene e jahac ine mârâc hahac-nâŋec erâ juocmu .
45008030	Anutu e ŋic qanaŋ hone wosâec-jopawec sâc hefârec-jopawec . Hefârec-jopawec sâc kiŋfâsâc bacjopawec . Kiŋfâsâc bacjopawec sâc eric-jopawec .
45008031	Dâŋ irec fuŋne weniŋuc fokac ? Anutuzi âgo enârehame mozi râsi enâreocmu ?
45008032	E ŋokâ-ticne mi sakarehuc nâŋâcnere erâ qaisockeweczi ere erâ wiac sasawa mi sesi qeqeric jaha tahac-nâpoocmu me ?
45008033	Anutu bâwosâecfâc-ticne jaŋe mozi dâŋko râec-jopaocmu ? Anutu e jahac kiŋfâsâc bacjopakac .
45008034	Me mozi tuŋjopaocmu ? Kristo Jesu e jahac hâmowec , erâ hâmowec sawa mâcne , e hâmockonec wâc faharerâ Anuture mefâreo feweczi nâŋâcne riŋ rohuc juekac .
45008035	Kristore uruc jauŋkonec wemozi moc batarac-nâpoocmu ? Ʒâic busâqoczi me hume serereŋzi me fific guguriŋzi me roroczi me qarâ suriŋnezi me šârâ šâpâzi me šika kâpâcwâruzi ?
45008036	Dâŋqâreŋ kecšiŋuc fokac irec sâcko wiac enâreeŋgopieŋ : “ Gore erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne qa imac enâreeŋgopieŋ , lama qa hezuc eejarene jaŋere sâcko râec-nâpoŋgopieŋ . ”
45008037	Erâ wiac iŋucnezi mi bâdoc-nâpoocmu , aricne , Jesure uruc jauŋko âtesiŋnehuc sasanaŋ fekicne bâfuarâ domaeŋgopeneŋ .
45008038	Irec no šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac : Hâmoczi me jujuzi , aŋelozi me ŋicbomboŋzi , wiac šiŋucne fofonezi me šâhec fufuanezi , me wiac tâpirineheczi ,
45008039	wiac faicne wawahanezi me juwicnec wewefunezi , wiac izi me izi Anuture uruc jauŋkonec moc mi batarac-nâpo-jâmbâŋkeocmu . Uruc jauŋ i Wofuŋnâŋec Kristo Jesu ere erâ ɋoroc-nâpoekac .
45009001	No Kristore ŋiczi burec mi ehuc dâŋ jâmbomac mupe mananiŋ . Tiri Mârozi maŋnane batamaehame mana-jâmbâŋkehuc ŋazape :
45009002	No busâqoc fârine manahuc maŋnane wemo afecne fârorockeekac .
45009003	Judaŋic âgofâc-nane , soctofafâc-nane hâcne , jaŋere erâ no nahac Kristore sacmaŋkonec wawahare sâcne afeckezapo .
45009004	Jaŋe hâcne Israe ŋic , eme Anutuzi fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne bacjopawec , ehuc tâpiri tatamac-ticne jowatuwec . Erâ jaŋehec šâšâfic erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ mufua-jarewec â mai ecnehuc juniŋte hatane jowatuwec . Erâ wâc biŋedâŋ jazawec .
45009005	Á mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic jaŋe mitire fuŋqizecne jumbiŋ . Eme Kristozi ŋicsahac rohuc fuawec i jaŋere guruo fuawec . Wiac sasawa irec Wofuŋ jukac , Anutu hâcne , e mumuteŋheczi mumuteŋhec jurašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
45009006	Wiac iŋuc fuawec irec Anuture dâŋ dodocne ewec mi muzo . Israeraonec fuambiŋ jaŋe Israe ŋic fârine ninic mi efârembiŋ .
45009007	Á Abrahamte tofafâc jaŋe ɋâricfâc-ticne fârine wâc mi efârembiŋ . Eme irec hâcne dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnekicne : “ Isakare ɋâricfâc jaŋe sawa gore biŋe eniŋmu . ”
45009008	Dâŋ irec fuŋne šiŋuc fokac : Sahaczi Abrahamtao fuambiŋ sâc Anuture ŋicfâc mi efârembiŋ , biŋedâŋko fuakicne jaŋe sawa Abrahamte ɋâricfâc fârine embiŋ .
45009009	Biŋedâŋ kecšiŋuc mukicne : “ Jara moc tarame Sarazi motec rorâ bajuhame mocwâc warepemu . ”
45009010	Erâ i sawa mâcne , Rebekarao sâc ijaha fuawec . E mimiŋne-nâŋec Isaka ehec juhuc motec jajahec kiwec-jofawec .
45009011	Eme motec jahe mi fuahuc wiac biaŋne me sâqocne mi ehapire Anutuzi jahere šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Hahaczi ɋare kiŋaŋ qazejec . ”
45009012	Ine Anutu mumupaŋ-ticne sanaŋkeocte manasuhuc motec juju-jekicte mâcne , e jahacne maŋte ro bârâwiŋ ejactehuc dâŋ i muwec .
45009013	Irec dâŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ No Jakobore enarewec â Esaure takicnuwec . ”
45009014	Eme irec weniŋuc muzo ? Anutu erao guriŋ bapa hehesicne moc fokac me ? I aric kereŋne .
45009015	E Mose dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ No ŋic moc akickezo murâ akickepemu â ŋic moc buuruc ecnezo murâ ecnepemu . ”
45009016	Irec ŋicmaŋte me ŋic eebapare mi muzo , Anutu buuruc-ticnere sawa muzo .
45009017	Anutuzi Farao dâŋ âzâcnewec , irec miti papiao šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : “ No gorao tâpiri-nane bataniŋkepe šâŋe biŋe-nane mâreŋ sâc raocte muhuc âkendâŋgupo hâcne . ”
45009018	Eme irec Anuture šiŋuc manazo : E ŋic moc akickezo murâ akickeocmu â moc e maŋne bâzickezo murâ bâzickeocmu .
45009019	Eme ŋifecne šiŋuc mecne nazacmu : “ Anutu e ŋic nâŋâcne wemocte maname sâqoreekac ? E wiac moc ezo mume ŋiczi aka hehecne i mi fokac . ”
45009020	Ŋic go wemogere Anuture dâŋ mucmu ? Kušizi wemocko kuzi bapa šiŋuc âzâcneocmu : “ Go wemocte sâc iŋucne bacnumeŋ ? ”
45009021	Me kuši bapa e afe izia kuši gâcne ŋic jaŋere biŋe â gâcne bec qâto jaŋere biŋe bame sâqoreocmu me ?
45009022	Eme Anutu e kuši kimbeŋ-ticnere biŋe , šâhecko qanšaŋ-joparâ behec-jopaocte maname fokac , kuši i jaŋerao šika bâfuahuc tâpiri-ticne bataniŋkeocte sifu bumâteŋ-ticnere erâ jâbu ejare warehuc juekac .
45009023	Erâ ŋifecne kuši buuruc-ticnere biŋe , juku eri tatamac-ticnao biric-jopaocte maname fokac , kuši i jaŋerao eri aŋac mâriri hejareocte bacjopa juekac .
45009024	Eme Judaŋic sawa mâcne , qâpuc mâmâc kuši buuruc-ticnere biŋe enaŋte hefârec-nâpoekac .
45009025	Eme irec porofete Hoseare papiao dâŋticne šiŋuc fokac : “ Ŋicguru mi rucjopapo jaŋe ` nore ŋicfâcƷ mucjopapemu , â biŋemâc juwec e šâŋene ` joroc-naneƷ mucnepemu . ”
45009026	“ Eme ` ŋoŋe nore ŋicfâc aricneƷ ŋazakicne , mâreŋ ira wâc šâŋe-jeŋic ` Anutu jujunere naru motecfâcƷ fuaocmu . ”
45009027	Erâ Jesajazi hahaŋne bahuc Israe ŋic jaŋere šiŋuc muwec wâc : “ Israe ɋâricfâcne jaŋe hâwecmecko moŋgeŋ fokac irec sâc bâfuazo murâ bâfuaniŋmu , eme sifu uuc šanšaŋne sawazi biaŋkeniŋmu . ”
45009028	Wofuŋ e mâreŋko dâŋticnere fârine ɋeŋnea bâfuame fideteŋ efâreocmu .
45009029	Jesajazi findaŋdâŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne muwec : “ Sambaŋ momori jaŋere Wofuŋ e ŋicukic moc mi getâc-jopa-nâreme muzac , ine Sodom jaŋere sâc bâfuanšapeŋ , â Gomora jaŋe iŋucne enšapeŋ . ”
45009030	Eme ši weniŋuc muzo ? Kecšiŋuc : ŋic qâpuc tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte mi fotariembiŋzi tiŋke biaŋ embiŋ , mamanasiŋte tiŋke biaŋ embiŋ hâcne .
45009031	Á Israe ŋic sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte fotariembiŋzi sâcmutâc dâŋ bâmâmâckembiŋ .
45009032	Wemocte ? šiŋucte : Jaŋe mamanasiŋte mâcne , mâc juju bapa-jeŋicte tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte mumbiŋ . Ehuc hatao qânâ fowec ira kike-jeŋic hezumbiŋ .
45009033	Kecšiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Manakic , no Zioŋ haeo qânâ moc râekopac ira kike-jeŋic hepirickeniŋmu , â buse ŋeŋene moc hekopac ira heariweniŋmu . Eme moczi e manasiŋkeocmu ine mi qurutuaocmu . ”
45010001	Qomâfâc-nane , Judaŋic âgofâc-nane biaŋkeniŋte maŋnanezi boc enareme Anutu irec numucneekopac .
45010002	Jaŋe Anutu kiŋaŋ qacneniŋte šoɋac ehuc jueŋgopieŋ i honeekopaczi mukopac . Erâ i hatane kâuc bahuc eeŋgopieŋ .
45010003	Jaŋe Anuturaonec kiŋfâsâc eere hata fokac i kâuc baeŋgopieŋte jaŋac tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte giene baeŋgopieŋ . Irec Anutu tiŋne rune mi dapecnembiŋ .
45010004	Ŋiczi mamanasiŋhec erâ kiŋfâsâc bâfuanaŋte Kristozi sâcmutâc dâŋte hata hebâzicke-nârewec .
45010005	Mose e dâŋ šiŋuc qâreŋkewec : “ Ŋic moc e sâcmutâc dâŋte tiŋke biaŋ hata âteocmuzi juju bâfuaocmu . ”
45010006	Á mamanasiŋte tiŋke biaŋ eere dâŋ ine kecšiŋuc fokac : “ Go maŋgezi šiŋuc mi muzemec : Mozi sambâŋko ferâ Kristo bawahaocmu ,
45010007	me mozi hârâcko hurâ Kristo hâmokicne jaŋeraonec jowa wefuocmu ? ”
45010008	Iŋuc mâcne , tiri papiao kecšiŋuc mukicne : “ Miti i šoricko mi fokac , i mumugao â mamanagao râekicne . ” I mamanasiŋte dâŋ ŋaza qazuc eeŋgopeneŋ irec mukicne .
45010009	Jesu e Wofuŋ-nane i mumugao foocmu â Anutuzi Jesu hâmockonec bâɋâre-narewec i mamanagao foocmu eme biaŋkerâ jucmu .
45010010	Maŋzi Jesu manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc ezo , â miczi e mutaniŋkehuc biaŋkezo .
45010011	Eme irec hâcne miti papiao kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : “ E manasiŋkeocmuzi mi qurutuaocmu . ”
45010012	Judaŋic â Grikŋic bârâwiŋ mi eŋgopeneŋ , e mocjahazi Wofuŋ junâre-fâreekac , erâ wiac fuŋne fuŋne hezu henâreekac .
45010013	Irec hâcne šiŋuc mukicne : “ Wofuŋte šâŋe riwaseckeocmuzi biaŋkerâ juocmu . ”
45010014	Ririwasecke i e mi manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋzi wemocko eniŋmu ? Anutu mamanasiŋke i dâŋticne mi manaeŋgopieŋzi wemocko eniŋmu ? Anutu dâŋticne mamana i biŋe mumu tâmiric wemocko eniŋmu ?
45010015	Á biŋe mumu i moczi jaza sorec mi ejarehame wemocko fuaniŋmu ? Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Biŋebiaŋ mumuŋic jaŋere kike fânâŋzi maŋ baafec bâfuaekac . ”
45010016	Biŋebiaŋ ine ŋic gâcnezi mana rereŋ mi embiŋ . Jesajazi wâc šiŋuc muwec : “ Wofuŋ , biŋedâŋ muhaŋnekicne i mozi mana šakiewec ? ”
45010017	Irec šiŋuc manazo : Mamanasiŋ i miti mu manacte fârine , â miti mu manac i Kristore micte fuaekac .
45010018	Hâc , eme šiŋuc muhuc wiokopac : Jaŋe miti mi manambiŋ me ? Iŋuc mâcne , “ Micfânâŋ-jeŋiczi mâreŋ sâcke-fârewec â dâŋjeŋiczi mâreŋ qaŋeŋnao fisiwec . ”
45010019	Eme mocwâc wiohuc mukopac : Israe ŋic jaŋe mi mecne mana-hâmombiŋ ? Iŋuc mâcne , qanaŋ Mosezi šiŋuc qâreŋkewec i mupe : “ No ŋic omane rocjopape siric-ŋopapie iiŋguuŋ ejarenšepieŋ ; ŋicguru mutucne hefârec-jopape buŋeŋic gâpârezejec . ”
45010020	Eme šâhec Jesajazi dâŋ bâutuckehuc kecšiŋuc muwec : “ Mi basacnuhuc jumbiŋzi bâfuacnumbiŋ , nore mi muhuc jumbiŋ jaŋe maic-jopapo . ”
45010021	Erâ Israe ŋic jaŋere ine šiŋuc mu qâreŋ ewec : “ No ŋicguru mana qâomane â mickobacne dameŋ šora meoric qajarehuc jupo . ”
45011001	Eme wiokopac : Anutuzi ŋicfâc-ticne behec-jopawec me ? Aricne , iŋuc mi ewec . Noni Israe ŋic jaha wâc , Abrahamte ɋâric , Benjamiŋte guruonec
45011002	Anutuzi qanaŋ manac-jopawec ŋic i mi behec­jopawec . Me ŋoŋe Eliare binaŋ miti papiao i wose manac mi eeŋgopieŋ me ?
45011003	E Israe ŋic jaŋere dâŋ muhuc Anutu šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Wofuŋ , jaŋe porofetefâcge jopa-fârehuc alatage henšaŋnembiŋ , eme ši buc juhape no wâc nuniŋte muŋgopieŋ . ”
45011004	Iŋuc mume Anutuzi dâŋ weniŋuc bâtikiecnewec ? “ No ŋic 7000 sakarec-jopape Baali nemu mi dapecnembiŋ . ”
45011005	Eme dameŋ ši iŋuc jaha Anutuzi aki anonoc-ticnere erâ ŋic tiwâne rowosâec-jopawec juŋgopieŋ .
45011006	I aki anonoc-ticnere iŋuc ejarewecko juju bapa-jeŋicte mi ejarewec . Iŋuc mi eme muzac , ine aki anonoc fârine mi ezac .
45011007	Eme weniŋuc ? Israe ŋic jaŋe wiac fârine bâfuazo mumbiŋ i mi bâfuambiŋ ” rowosâec-jopakicne jaŋe sawa bâfuambiŋ , gâcne sâko ine maŋsanaŋ embiŋ .
45011008	Irec šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Anutu e maŋjeŋic bâsifuckewec , šâŋe-jeŋic bâhâpowec â hazec-jeŋic qâzic qawec . Iŋuc ejareha jumbiŋzi jueŋgopieŋ . ”
45011009	Á Dawidizi mu qâreŋ ewec : “ Jaŋe nânâ nahapie râsi fisipie fâfâc-jopazejec , Mâreŋko jopaha okacne fisi-jarezejec .
45011010	Go šâŋe-jeŋic bâhâpotec tiŋtuŋ qanšepieŋ , â râpe-jeŋic bahasicketec miŋgeŋ miŋgeŋ junšepieŋ sanaŋ . ”
45011011	Eme wiokopac : Israe ŋic jaŋe fâfâc-jopawec i waha qâhâmoc-jopaocte iŋuc fuawec me ? Iŋuc aricne , jaŋe bâbâpiaŋ râpeckepie qâpuc jaŋere biŋe ewec , ine qâpuc jaŋe manapie Israe ŋic jaŋe honec-joparâ iiŋguuŋ ejareniŋte iŋuc fuawec .
45011012	Eme miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋiczi mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋerao miti mâriri bâfuawecko , â dodocke-jeŋiczi ŋic qâpuc jaŋerao miti šâkâŋ bâfuawecko , opoŋ , juku furu jaha maŋjeŋic bârisiepie fârine mo iŋucne fuazokac !
45011013	Qâpuckonec opâ ruac ŋoŋe dâŋ ši ŋazape mananiŋ : No qâpuc ŋoŋere aposolo juekopaczi gie-nane baericko bašihuc baekopac ,
45011014	i soctofafâc-nane âkeriŋ-jopape gâcnezi bâjâpecnuhuc biaŋkeniŋte .
45011015	Anutuzi Israe ŋic behec-jopame mâreŋ sâc miti fuawec , izi juku rocjopame mi hâmockonec ɋâɋârezi fuazokac me ?
45011016	Nânâ hata qaqasune jambuŋkepene nânâ mâmâc sâcke-fâreekac , â jâc gâtânezi furu fome tieŋne iŋuc jaha furu foocmu .
45011017	Eme Anutuzi tieŋne gâcne hetâcne behec ehuc irec dodoma tacko oliwa kâteo fuakicne irec tieŋne go râe šuhuc egarewec . Eme oliwa gâtânere ŋiŋic wokemaŋzi gume hesiwiŋ egarehame ,
45011018	go tieŋne raŋɋane mi mana pitiwac-jopahuc maŋfefe mi ezemec . Iŋuc ezicte šiŋuc manac : Go gâtâ gume hesiwiŋ mi ecnekomec , gâtâzi go egareekac .
45011019	Mupe go ŋifecne šiŋuc mecne mucmu : “ Anutuzi no hâcne râe šuhuc enareocte tieŋne raŋɋane hetâcne behec ejarewec . ”
45011020	I mukic mac . Jaŋe miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋicte hetâcne behec ejarekicne â go ine mamanasiŋgere dodomatac-jeŋicko domakomec . Irec go sahacge mi bafehuc rumerâ juzemec .
45011021	Anutu e oliwa e jahacne tieŋne mi akickewecko go iŋuc jaha mi akicguocmu .
45011022	Irec go buuruc-ticnere mecne â fâro-ticnere mecne mi nikecguzejec . Fâro-ticnere fârine i miti râpeckembiŋ jaŋerao fuawec , â buuruc-ticnere fârine i gorao fuawec . Eme go erao qohotahuc jutec fârine i sâcne fogareocmu . Iŋuc mi etec ine go wâc hetâcne behec egareocmu .
45011023	Erâ wâc tieŋne raŋɋane jaŋe maŋsanaŋ-jeŋic beheniŋmuo Anutuzi mocwâc râe šuhuc ejarezo murâ sâcne ejareocmu .
45011024	Eme kâteonec oliwa rocgurâ hae oliwa jâcnao râe šuhuc egareweczi hae oliwa e jahacne tieŋfâc mocwâc šuhuc-jopazo murâ mi quŋkeocmu , i onšoŋ jaha šuhuc-jopaocmu .
45011025	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe , kâuc bahuc ŋaŋacne mamanao roweckerâ mana sifuckenšipiŋte dâŋ soŋne ši mufua-ŋarepe . Israe ŋic tucne jaŋe maŋsanaŋ erâ juhapie qâpuc sâko jaŋe mitire maŋko rašiniŋmu .
45011026	Rašihapie šâhec Israe ŋicguru qâqâhâc biaŋke-fâreniŋmu . Ʒiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Zioŋ haeonec Bâbâpiaŋ moc fuarâ Jakoborao jawa âsu gârec ofaŋneme raocmu .
45011027	Iŋuc eme no sâqocne-jeŋic šurerâ jaŋehec mocwâc šâšâfic epemu . ”
45011028	Israe ŋic jaŋe qâpuc ŋoŋere erâ Biŋebiaŋte râsi juŋgopieŋ â rowosâec-jopakicnere ine mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic jaŋere erâ Anuture jorocfâc juŋgopieŋ .
45011029	Anutu e âgo šâšâfic dâŋsaric-ticne â hehefâre dâŋticne mi dockeocmu .
45011030	Qâpuc ŋoŋe mârâc jaha maŋsanaŋ erâ jumbiŋ , eme šâhec Israe ŋic jaŋe maŋsanaŋ ehapie Anutuzi buuruc-ticnao râec-ŋopawec .
45011031	Iŋuc jaha jaŋe maŋsanaŋ juhapie Anutuzi buuruc-ticnao ŋec-ŋopawec , i jaŋe wâc buuruc ejareocte iŋuc ewec .
45011032	Anutu e ŋic sasawa bâturec-jopahuc qaqatarao basanaŋ-jopawec , i mâmâc sasawa buuruc-ticnao ŋec-jopaocte iŋuc ewec .
45011033	Opoŋ , Anutu e mitire mâriri â maŋɋârâŋ â mamana saric-ticne irec šâkâŋne mo iŋucne fokac ¡ Mumutara-ticnere fuŋne i ŋiczi mi mamanane gie bapa-ticnere hata i ŋiczi mi hohonene .
45011034	“ Wofuŋte maŋko dâŋ fokac i mo ŋiczi manawec , me dâŋ muhame mozi bafickerâ muwec ? ”
45011035	“ Me mo ŋiczi e qanaŋ wiac moc qikiŋnecnewecko tofane bazucneocmu ? ”
45011036	Wiac sasawa eraonec wareekac â erao siŋkerâ foekac â erao rafâreekac . Mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ i erao šuhuckeme šuhuc forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
45012001	Âgofâc-nane , no Anutu buuruc-ticnere erâ dâŋ hazec qâuŋ ŋazape mananiŋ . Ŋoŋe sahac-ŋeŋic Anutu qikiŋnecnepie taha bâzi ɋaɋacne â tirine eme honeme biaŋkezejec . Iŋuc ehuc Anutu kiŋaŋ fârine qacnenšepieŋ .
45012002	Erâ juju bapa-ŋeŋiczi miti tâmiric jaŋere sâc mi ezejec . Ŋoŋe maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic bâtikiepie hawarine moc eme Anutu micdâŋ-ticnere sâcko gie biaŋne â hohone šiziwene â tirine irec wosâenšepieŋ .
45012003	Aki anonoc tahacnukicnere mâmâc sasawa ŋazape mananiŋ : Moc e jahacnere maname fefene boc mi ezejec , Anutuzi miti râcnewec sâc i sawa ezejec , sâc jâuruhuc ine mi ezejec .
45012004	Ʒiŋuc mananiŋ : Fâri ombâŋ-nâŋec mocjaha e kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ticne bocjahazi gie fuŋne fuŋne baeŋgopieŋ .
45012005	Eme ŋifec Kristorao iŋuc jaha bocjahazi qâfâsâepene fâri ombâŋ mocjaha ekac , erâ me kikefâcne juhuc dodopec eeŋgopeneŋ .
45012006	Mitire tâpire fuŋne fuŋne i aki anonoc nâre tahac ekicne sâc fonâre rakac . Eme irec sâcko gie banšepeneŋ . Irec moc e Anuture micdâŋ mumufuare tâpiri focnekacko mamanasiŋ-ticnere sâcko muzejec .
45012007	Moc e kiŋaŋ qaqa giere tâpiri focnekaczi gie i bazejec , â moc e qaqazu gie baocmu e irec tâpiri focnekac sâc bazejec .
45012008	Uŋsawaŋ dâŋ muekac e irec tâpiri focnekacko muzejec , bâmec gie baekac e maŋticne bawahahuc bazejec , moc e micne juocte mucnekicko šoɋachec juzejec , â moc e jauŋ gie baocmuzi buafec jaha bazajec .
45012009	Jauŋ babac i sahaczi sawa mi enšepieŋ . Wiac sâqocnere mamakâc-ŋopazejec â wiac biaŋnao qohotanšepieŋ .
45012010	Ŋoŋe ââgo fârine junšepieŋ , erâ sâsâsec eniŋte sisiric efârenšepieŋ .
45012011	Rokac bârokac tâmiric ɋicwânšâŋhec erâ junšepieŋ . Mârore buŋeŋic bâruŋkezejec , ehuc Wofuŋ kiŋaŋ qacnenšepieŋ .
45012012	Sambaŋ worickehuc bubiaŋ junšepieŋ , â šâic busâqocko maŋuruc junšepieŋ . Erâ nunumu gie i uruc šuhuc jaha banšepieŋ .
45012013	Anuture mitiŋicfâc hume serereŋ jupie hone bafic ejarenšepieŋ . Ŋic fisipie afeckerâ hezu hewâneŋ ejarenšepieŋ .
45012014	Ŋopa jâpec eŋareniŋmu jaŋe jambuŋ-jopanšepieŋ . Micŋeŋickonec sâwecdâŋ mâcne , jambuŋdâŋ sawa wahazejec .
45012015	Bubiaŋ eniŋmu jaŋe qâtec-joparâ bubiaŋ enšepieŋ , kioniŋmu jaŋe qâtec-joparâ kionšepieŋ .
45012016	Maŋŋeŋic bâturehuc wiac mocjahare henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ . Ŋaŋacnere boc mi manapie sâckezejec .
45012017	Sâqocnere okac babazuc mi enšepieŋ . Ŋic âgo ejareekac ijaha enšepieŋ .
45012018	Ŋicne Ŋicne jaŋehec wamao juju i eene eme ŋoŋe hâcne irec hatane âtenšepieŋ .
45012019	Âgofâc , kiŋŋeŋic ŋaŋac mi batarahuc Wofuŋ kimbeŋ-ticnere biŋe râepie fozejec . Dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Kiŋ babatara i nore gie , â okacne babazu i no nahac epemu , Wofuŋ e iŋuc mukac . ”
45012020	Ŋoŋe ine šiŋuc enšepieŋ : Râsige nânâre hâmome nânâ gumezemec , opâre hâmome opâ gumezemec . Go iŋuc etecne mimiehuc šara marane eocmu .
45012021	Sâqocnezi go mi bawahacguzejec . Aricne , go wiac biaŋne ehuc sâqocne bawahazemec .
45013001	Ŋic mâmâc sasawa kia gawamaî jaŋere dâŋ reŋkenšepieŋ . Kia gawamaî gie i Anuturaonec . Juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anuture micte juraŋgopieŋ hâcne .
45013002	Irec moc e kia gawamaî jaŋere dâŋ qâsuahuc Anuture dâŋ qâsuaocmu . Erâ qâsuaniŋmu jaŋe okacne roniŋmu .
45013003	Ebapa-jeŋic biaŋne jaŋe kia gawamaî jaŋere mi hâwic-jopaekac , sâqocne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine hâwic-jopaekac . Irec go hâhâwic tâmiric juzo murâ wiac biaŋne ezemec . Wiac biaŋne etec gore manapie sâckeocmu .
45013004	Kia gawamaî jaŋe Anuture kiŋaŋ qaqa hâcne , ŋezicgupie juhâmocmurâ mujarekicne . Go sâqocne bacmuo ine hâwicguzejec , jaŋe šika maŋgâŋ mi bajueŋgopieŋ . Jaŋe Anuture kiŋaŋ qaqazi sâqocne bapa jaŋerao bâbâtiŋ gie bahuc okacne jareniŋmu .
45013005	Irec dâŋjeŋic reŋke-jâmbâŋkezo , erâ i okacnere hâhâwicte sawa mâcne , gahacne maŋzi tutuc qagarezacte wâc dâŋjeŋic reŋkezemec .
45013006	Jaŋe Anutuzi soŋaŋ gie mujarewec i baeŋgopieŋte hâcne ŋoŋe takesi moneŋ râeeŋgopieŋ .
45013007	Eme ŋoŋe wiac mukicne sâc ejarenšepieŋ : Takesi jajarere mukicne jaŋe takesi jarenšepieŋ , kiŋaŋ qaqajarere mukicne jaŋe kiŋaŋ qajarenšepieŋ , araŋ babajarere mukicne jaŋe araŋ bajarenšepieŋ , sâsâsec-jopare mukicne jaŋe sâsec-jopanšepieŋ .
45013008	Wiac omanere tofa bazupie tarazejec , maŋjauŋte tofa mocjaha babazuc epie tatarane ine mi fokac . Maŋjauŋhec juekaczi sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkekac muzo .
45013009	Sâcmutâc dâŋ šiŋuc mukicne : Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋohe bebehec mi ezepirec , go šika mi qazemec , go fiuc mi rozemec , go andac mi ezemec , sâcmutâc dâŋ i erâ gâcne i mâmâc sasawa qâhâckerâ qizecne šiŋuc mukicne : Gahacnere egareekac sâc ijaha âgogere egarezejec .
45013010	Maŋjauŋhec juocmuzi âgo-ticne sâqocne mi ecneocmu . Irec maŋjauŋzi sâcmutâc dâŋrereŋ fârine ekac .
45013011	Iŋuc eniŋte muŋarekicne ŋoŋe dameŋ širec fuŋne manaŋgopieŋ , guŋkonec ɋârerâ faharezo irec šâfo maickekac hâcne . Miti fuŋkerâ manambeŋ ira bâbâpiaŋte dameŋ šošoricne fowec , ši ine dameŋ qândâŋkekac .
45013012	Ŋafe tarazo ekacte hae fureocte furic râekac . Irec dapâcte wiac hetararâ tatamackonec sându maro menâŋecko rašizejec .
45013013	Ʒoaŋ ɋaɋacko jujune pectâc junšepeneŋ , nâ areŋ â tiwâ kadahe me gae wowo â sasec mamakâc me rârâsi â iiriac i mi ezo , aricne .
45013014	Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo e ŋaqi-ŋeŋic eme rojunšepieŋ Erâ sahac-ŋeŋiczi sasec bâfuazacte mana manahuc jauŋ bacnenšepieŋ .
45014001	Mitio gegec bititicne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe âgo miriŋ ejarenšepieŋ , ehuc wiac omanere memeŋgaru epie mu qâsuac mi ejarenšepieŋ .
45014002	Moc e manabâc tâmiric wiac kosa nâekac , moc e ine memeŋgaru ehuc monšaŋ sawa nâekac .
45014003	Irec wiac kosa nâocmuzi âgo-ticne nâ bâtâc eekac ere maname wawahane mi ezejec , â nâ bâtâc eocmuzi âgo-ticne wiac kosa nâekac ere maname mi sâqorezejec . E Anuture ŋic jaha wâc .
45014004	Irec go wemogezi mocte kiŋaŋ qaqa miti babaju-ticnere fuŋne mutec sâckeocmu ? E sanaŋkeocmu me dockeocmu , i Wofuŋ-ticnere wiac . Erâ e mi dockeocmu , Wofuŋ e sâcne hume keteŋ ecneme qiŋ herâ domaocmu .
45014005	Á šoaŋ gie bapare iŋuc jaha , moc e wose bâtâc eocmu , â moc e maname qâfâsâeocmu . Moczi me moczi iŋuc me iŋuc ezo murâ mana sanaŋkehuc ezejec .
45014006	Ʒoaŋ gie bapa wose bâtâc eekaczi Wofuŋte erâ eekac , â nânâ kosa nâekaczi Wofuŋte erâ eekac wâc , ehuc Anutu nânâre daŋge âzâcneekac . Á nâ bâtâc eekaczi iŋuc jaha Wofuŋte erâ eekac , ehuc Anutu daŋge âzâcneekac wâc .
45014007	Nâŋâcnaonec moczi moc e jahacnere mi juekac â e jahacnere mi hâmoekac .
45014008	Juju i Wofuŋte jueŋgopeneŋ , hâhâmo i Wofuŋte hâmoeŋgopeneŋ . Irec junaŋmu me hâmonaŋmu i Wofuŋtea enaŋmu .
45014009	Irec hâcne Kristozi hâmokicne â ɋâricne mâmâc Wofuŋ enâreocte hâmorâ wâc ɋârewec .
45014010	Eme go wemogezi âgogere dâŋ mutaracmu ? Me go wemogezi âgogere manatec wawahane eocmu ? Nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa Anuture maio fuapene dâŋnâŋec mutara-nâreocmu .
45014011	Ʒiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Wofuŋzi mukac , no jujâmbâŋkekopacte ŋic šeŋgoma dieŋzi henare-fârenšepieŋ â šeŋgoma micjeŋiczi muafecnunšepieŋ . ”
45014012	Irec nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa Anuturao fuŋne-nâŋec munaŋte munârekicne hâcne .
45014013	Irec nâŋâc dâŋ mumutarac mi enšepeneŋ . Kecšiŋuc ine ezo : Ŋoŋe âgo gâcne maŋ bâsifuc ejarehuc mamana sâqoc bâfua-jarenšipiŋte manabâcko junšepieŋ .
45014014	No Wofuŋ Jesuhec juekopaczi šiŋuc mana sanaŋkekopac : Nânâ i me i nâhuc wâwânâŋhec eene mi fokac . Á moc e , wiac kosa nârâ wâwânâŋhec ezo , iŋuc muhuc sifu nâocmu , e ine jâmbomac wâwânâŋhec eocmu .
45014015	Go ine âgoge nânâre busâqoc bâfuacnetec maŋjauŋ micke-garezo . Âgoge biaŋkeocte Kristozi ere wâc hâmowec , go irec manasuhuc âgoge nânâre erâ ba imac mi ecnezemec .
45014016	Ŋoŋe wiac fârine bajuŋgopieŋ i ŋic gâcnezi musoriŋkenšipiŋte soŋaŋkehuc bajunšepieŋ .
45014017	Nânâ qowizi Anuture uucmaŋte fârine mi ekac , kiŋfâsâc fufua â wama â Tiri Mâroraonec šeri bubiaŋ izi wiac fârine .
45014018	Moc e hata i âtehuc Kristo kiŋaŋ qacneme e Anutuzi honeme biaŋkeocmu â ŋic jaŋe ere manapie sâckeocmu .
45014019	Irec hâcne nâŋâc wama foocte â miti maŋ sâc fua bâbâriŋ eocte hehesanaŋ enšepeneŋ .
45014020	Go nânâre erâ Anuture gie ima mi qazemec . Nânâ qowi i biaŋne sasawa , moc e ine , nârâ maŋbâiŋ gie bapemu , iŋuc manahuc sifu nâme sâqorecneocmu .
45014021	Go âgoge maŋbâiŋ ecnezicte ere erâ qowi â waiŋ opâ qikiŋnetec sâckeocmu .
45014022	Go wiac iŋucnere maŋfâsâcge fokac , i Anuture maio bajutec gahacnao sawa fozejec . Mo e wiac mocte maname sâckeha maŋbahac fâfâsâc eme biaŋkeocmu .
45014023	Á moc e mana maŋjahec eipiehuc sifu nâme sâqorecneocmu , e mamanasiŋ faio me ekac irec . Wiac i me i mamanasiŋ faio mi epene bahacnehec eocmu .
45015001	Sanaŋheczi gegec dodocne âsi qataŋ ejarenšepeneŋ , nâŋec nâŋâcnere mamanac mi junšepeneŋ .
45015002	Nâŋâc âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋere mamanac juhuc biaŋkeniŋte â mitio sanaŋkeniŋte bafic-jopanšepeneŋ .
45015003	Kristo e iŋuc jaha e jahacnere mamanac mi juwec . Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Go musoriŋgumbiŋ jaŋere mumusoriŋzi nore faio fekac . ”
45015004	Mârâc jaha dâŋ mu qâreŋ embiŋ , i nâŋâc mitire fuŋne mana-hâmonaŋte embiŋ , dâŋqâreŋ izi hâcne basanaŋ-nâpohuc baafec-nâpome wiac biŋe qanarekicne irec mamanac junaŋte qâreŋkekicne .
45015005	Anutu e babasanaŋ â bâbaafec runezi eŋareme Jesu Kristore sâko maŋ mamanasu mocjaha erâ junšepieŋ .
45015006	Ehuc maŋŋeŋic â micŋeŋic tureme Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere Anutu â Mamac muteŋkenšepieŋ .
45015007	Irec hâcne Anuture eri qâreŋ fuaocte Kristozi rocŋopawec iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe maŋzi roroc efârenšepieŋ .
45015008	No kecšiŋucte ŋazakopac : Anutu e mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec biŋedâŋ mujâmbâŋkehuc jazawec i fârinehec eocte Kristozi mahec nâŋere kiŋaŋ qaqa ewec .
45015009	Erâ wâc ŋic qâpuc jaŋe Anutu buuruc-ticnere erâ muteŋkeniŋte iŋuc ewec . Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ No qâpuc jaŋerao muteŋguhuc šâŋege mumbiaŋkepemu . ”
45015010	Erâ dâŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac : “ Ŋic qâpuc ŋoŋe Anuture fuŋfuŋfâc jaŋehec mu šeri enšepieŋ . ”
45015011	Erâ moc šiŋuc : “ Qâpuc ŋoŋe šeŋgoma Wofuŋ mucne bacnenšepieŋ , â ŋicne ŋicne jaŋe e muac baafec ecnenšepieŋ . ”
45015012	Erâ Jesajazi dâŋ moc šiŋuc mu qâreŋ ewec : “ Jâctuc Isai gitecne fuarâ eki qâpuc Wofuŋ ejareocmu ; eme qâpuczi ere mamanac juniŋmu . ”
45015013	Ʒeŋaŋ rune Anutu e mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte bubiaŋ â wama bâfua-ŋareme Tiri Mârore tâpirio ŋesiŋnepie sambâŋ šeŋaŋ-ŋeŋicte manariŋ qâriŋ ŋoŋerao fua ŋeiŋ ezejec .
45015014	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe uruc jauŋ-ŋeŋic fokac â mitire fuŋne i wâc sâcne mana-hâmoŋgopieŋ , irec ŋaŋaczia faŋ qaqac ezo murâ mi bititieniŋmu , i no fuŋne-ŋeŋic iŋuc hâcne mana sanaŋkekopac .
45015015	Erâ sifu no Anutuzi miti gie tahacnuwecte dâŋ gâcne i mai qanšaŋ Jaha qâreŋke-ŋarehuc mitire manasu-ŋarekopac .
45015016	Jesu Kristo e qâpuc ŋoŋere miti kiŋaŋŋic râecnuwecte no Anutu Biŋebiaŋ-ticnere taha bapa gie bape Tiri Mârozi maŋfuru bacŋopame Wofuŋte taha biaŋ enšepieŋ .
45015017	No Anuture gie baekopac i Jesu Kristore erâ manape fefene eekac .
45015018	Gie i nahackoaŋ wemo-nanezi bazapo , aricne , Jesu Kristozi neŋgoc ŋenareha qâpuc jaŋe miti mana rereŋ eniŋte miczi â mezi gie bapo .
45015019	No tâpiri â mâsihec juhuc Tiri Mâroraonec hâbi rorâ Jerusalem haeonec fuŋkerâ Kristore Biŋebiaŋ mâreŋ râreckehuc muiŋne rakupe Iliriko ŋ mâreŋko mickewec .
45015020	Ehuc gâcne jaŋere hâsinao bazipore Kristore šâŋe biŋe mi ra fisiwecko furunao šocne qapemurâ herâ wâwânšâŋneekopac .
45015021	Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac irec sâcko eekopac : “ Dâŋ binaŋ-ticne mi ejarekicne jaŋe e honeniŋmu , â biŋe-ticne mi manambiŋ jaŋe mamanahec eniŋmu . ”
45015022	No fuŋne iŋucte hâcne ŋoŋerao fâpemurâ dameŋ sâc quŋkeekopac .
45015023	Juwarepo i ŋoŋerao fâpemurâ maŋzi sawa manahuc jupo , ši ine mâreŋ gâcnao gie-nane tarakacte
45015024	Sipeî mâreŋko razo ehuc ŋoŋerao fisipemurâ manasukopac . Fisipe ŋoŋehec sahac hâroŋ qaqac erâ ŋoŋeraonec moc moczi qâtecnupie mâmâc Sipeî mâreŋko ranšepeneŋ .
45015025	Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine mitiŋic kiŋaŋ qajarehuc Jerusalem haeo razo ekopac .
45015026	Makedonia â Akaia kikefuŋ jaŋe Jerusalem haeonec mitiŋic hapetac dopec-jopaniŋte afeckerâ mupaŋkembiŋ .
45015027	Jaŋe buafec-jeŋicte iŋuc epie sâckewec . Qâpuckonec miti mamana jaŋe Jerusalem haeonec mitiŋic jaŋeraonec miti boreŋ rombiŋte tofa jaŋerao fokac . Eme tofa i hâcne bazu-jareniŋte sahackopec wiac jarepie sâckeocmu .
45015028	Eme mumupaŋ-jeŋicte fârine fuawec i no nahac bararâ jarepe tarame ŋoŋerao fotâcnehuc Sipeî mâreŋko rapemu .
45015029	Erâ no manakopac , ŋoŋerao metariŋ mi fâpemu , Kristoraonec jambuŋ kadahe bafâpemu .
45015030	Âgofâc-nane , no Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere erâ â Mârore Jauŋte erâ hazec qâuŋ ŋazakopac , ŋoŋe nore erâ Anutu numucnehuc juju gie-nanere baficnunšepieŋ .
45015031	Baficnupie Anutuzi Judaia mâreŋko ŋic jaŋere meonec bataracnuzejec , â Jerusalem haeonec mitiŋic bubiaŋ wiac jarepe aŋac-jopazejec .
45015032	Izi šâhec Anutuzi manahame bubiaŋko fârâ ŋoŋerao jumanahuc âke mâteŋnuzejec .
45015033	Anutu wama rune eki ine ŋoŋehec jufârezejec . Jâmbomac .
45016001	Ŋokac âgo-nâŋec Foibe , Keŋkereai kikefuŋ bafic-jopahuc juekac , e fâ fisime
45016002	ŋoŋe mitio munârekicne irec sâcko Wofuŋte erâ hezu hewâneŋ ecnenšepieŋ . Erâ e irec me irec ecneme bafickenšepieŋ . Ŋokac e no nahacne â gâcne mâmâc kiŋaŋ qanârehuc juwec .
45016003	Erâ Prisika â Aqila , Kristo Jesu gie-ticnere babafic jahec-nane jahe jasaniŋ , mamanac-nane jaherao fokac .
45016004	Jahe hâcne nore erâ sahac-jekic qaisockezo epicte no sawa mâcne , hae sâc kikefuŋ nâŋe jahere bubiaŋ bajueŋgopeneŋ .
45016005	Jahere ficko mitire tumaŋneeŋgopieŋ ŋic ŋokac i jaŋe wâc mu šeri ejarekopac . Âgo-nane Epaineto , Asia mâreŋ masunao micne barâ Kristoŋic ewec , e wâc mu šeri ecnekopac .
45016006	Maria e wâc mu šeri ecnekopac âzâcneniŋ , e ŋoŋere erâ gie bocjaha bawec .
45016007	Androniko â Junia , Judaŋic âgo jahec-nane , kâpâcwâru mâmâc bacnâpokicne , jaherao mamanac-nane fokac i jasaniŋ . Jahe ŋic šâŋe biŋeheczi aposolo jaŋere guruo juhuc , no mâc juhape Kristore miti bânierâ manapic .
45016008	Mitio âgo-nane Ampiliato e wâc mu šeri ecnekopac .
45016009	Urbano , Kristore giere babafic embeŋ , â Sitaki âgo-nane jahe wâc mu šeri ejactekopac i jasaniŋ .
45016010	Apele , Kristore ŋic fârine , â Aristobulo ere wiacfâc jaŋe mu šeri ejarekopac .
45016011	Judaŋic âgo-nane Herodioŋ erâ Narikiso wiacfâcne gâcne mitio jueŋgopieŋ , jaŋerao mamanac-nane fokac .
45016012	Ŋokac jahec Tirifaina â Tirifosa , Wofuŋte erâ gie sâko bapic , â Peasi e iŋuc jaha Wofuŋte erâ gie paŋšâic bawec , jaŋe mu šeri ejarekopac wâc .
45016013	Wofuŋte bufuŋ Rufu â neŋgoc-ticne , e no wâc neŋgoc enarewec , jaherao mamanac-nane fokac .
45016014	Asiŋkrito , Filegoŋ , Hereme , Patoroba , Herema â âgofâc-jeŋic jaŋe mu šeri ejare-fârekopac .
45016015	Filologo â ŋokac Julia erâ Nereo â seŋticne â Olumpa â miti ŋic ŋokac jaŋehec jueŋgopieŋ , jaŋe mâmâc mu šeri ejare-fârekopac .
45016016	Ŋaŋac wâc mitio meo babac enšepieŋ . Hae sâc Kristore kikefuŋ jaŋe ŋoŋere mamanac wâc juŋgopieŋ .
45016017	Âgofâc , ŋoŋerao fâfâuc bâfuahuc , miti qazu-ŋarekicne i bâsifuckezo eeŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋere ruc bahuc dic bajarenšepieŋ .
45016018	Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe Wofuŋ Kristo mâcne , jaŋe jaŋacne hobu kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopieŋ . Ehuc mumumbiaŋ dâŋ muhuc ŋic ŋokac omane mu bâmiriŋ ejarehuc eatuc-jopaeŋgopieŋ .
45016019	Miti mana rereŋ-ŋeŋicte biŋe i hae sâc rafârewec . Eme no irec ŋoŋere bubiaŋ manahuc kecšiŋuc eniŋte ŋazape : Wiac biaŋnere maŋafec junšepieŋ â wiac sâqocnere ine maŋ ŋeŋemâc enšepieŋ .
45016020	Anutu wama rune eki mi šoraha Sataŋ ro bawaha âte ecneocmu . Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec .
45016021	Babafic-nane Timoteo â Judaŋic âgofâc-nane Lukio â Jasoŋ â Sosipate jaŋe ŋoŋere mamanac juŋgopieŋ .
45016022	Teatio no papia ši ( Paulore mickonec ) qâreŋkehuc iŋuc jaha Wofuŋte maio ŋoŋere manasukopac .
45016023	Gaio e no â kikefuŋ mâmâc sasawa hezu hewâneŋ enâreekaczi iŋuc jaha ŋoŋere manasukac Erâ hae soŋaŋ Erasto â âgo-nâŋec Qâto jahe iŋuc jaha eŋarekopirec , [
45016024	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec . Jâmbomac . ]
45016025	Anutu e Biŋebiaŋ muekopac â Jesu Kristore dâŋ muromackeekopac irec sâcko mamanasiŋko keteŋ-ŋopaocte tâpiri focnekac . Anutu juju sanaŋ dâŋticne hâcne soŋne fowarehuc jukume
45016026	dameŋ šiŋuczia ere micte muropiekicne â ŋicne ŋicne mana rereŋ eniŋte miti papiao bajaŋgeŋkekicne .
45016027	Eme Anutu hâcne , buc maŋɋârâŋ juekac , erao Jesu Kristore erâ mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ hati forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
46001001	Anuture micte Jesu Kristore aposolo epo Paulo no hâcne â âgo-nâŋec Sostene
46001002	nâhe Korinti haeonec Anuture kikefuŋ ŋoŋere papia ši râekoperec . Ŋoŋe Jesu Kristozi jambuŋ-ŋoparâ tirimoc juniŋte hefârec-ŋopawec . Iŋuc eŋareme ine hae sâc opâ ruac šira â gâcnao Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo šâŋe-ticne riwaseckehuc jueŋgopieŋ jaŋehec mocjaha embiŋ .
46001003	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
46001004	Anutu e Jesu Kristore erâ aki anonoc sesic-ŋopawecte no ŋoŋere manasuhuc daŋge berec jaha âzâcneekopac .
46001005	E miti mumure aafec â mamana fuŋne fuŋne aameo tahac-ŋopawec .
46001006	I Kristore mumutaniŋ dâŋzi ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko gâtâ bawecte iŋuc fuawec .
46001007	Eme mitire wiac moc mi basaeŋgopieŋ . Mâc Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo fua taniŋkeocte woŋec mocjaha jueŋgopeneŋ .
46001008	Eki hâcne Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore fifisi dameŋko kiŋfâsâc domaniŋte hefârec-ŋopame juhapie dameŋ-ŋeŋic taraocmu .
46001009	Anutu e Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu Kristo , Wofuŋ-nâŋec hâcne , erao šuhuckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopaweczi mocmu mocmu-ticne mi fokac .
46001010	Âgofâc-nane , no Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo šâŋe-ticnere erâ uŋdâŋ ši mupe mananiŋ : Ŋoŋe dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne â fâfâuc mi bâfuanšepieŋ , aricne . Maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic bâturepie mocjaha eha junšepieŋ .
46001011	Âgo bureŋ , no ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko dâŋ fuawec fokac i Koloe ere wiacfâc mupie manapo .
