46001012	Dâŋ kecšiŋucte mukopac : Ŋoŋeraonec moczi muekac ` no Paulore ŋic ' , â moczi muekac “ no Apolore ŋic ” , â moczi muekac “ no Kefare ŋic ” , â moczi muekac “ no Kristore ŋic . ”
46001013	Hâc , i weniŋuc , Kristozi fâuckewec me ? Me Paulo noni ŋoŋere erâ , maripoŋko hâmopo ? Me Paulo nore šâŋezi hucŋopaha Miti Opâ ruambiŋ ?
46001014	Sowine no nahac Miti Opâ mi rua-ŋarepo , Krisipo â Gaio jahe sawa rua-jactepo .
46001015	Ŋoŋe šiŋuc munšipiŋte : “ Ere šâŋezi hucnâpoha Miti Opâ ruambeŋ . ”
46001016	Mâcne , ši moc manasukopac , Stefana ere wiacfâc jaŋe wâc rua-jarepo , gâcne jaŋere ine mi manakopac .
46001017	Kristozi ŋic Miti Opâ rua-jarepemurâ mâcne , Biŋebiaŋ jaza qazuc epemurâ munarewec . Erâ Kristo maripoŋ-ticnere dâŋ tâpirimâc ezacte maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ ericke bâpiaŋ ehuc mi muekopac .
46001018	Maripoŋte dâŋ i sisipiric hata âteeŋgopieŋzi manapie racne eekac , â bâbâpiaŋ hatao jueŋgopeneŋzi ine manapene Anuturaonec tâpirihec eekac .
46001019	Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ No maŋɋârâŋhec jaŋere dâŋ qape wahaocmu â mamana-jeŋichec jaŋere mamana batackepemu . ”
46001020	Eme maŋɋârâŋhec jaŋe weni ? Á mana gufu koparic ŋic jaŋe weni ? Á dameŋ širec fuŋne mamana jaŋe weni ? Anutu e maŋ mamana-jeŋic bahameŋkewec hâcne .
46001021	Eme Anuture maŋɋârâŋ dâŋbiri fua-bipieha ŋic jaŋe jaŋacne mamanazi Anuture fuŋne šâŋitaniŋte emâmâŋkembiŋ , irec Anutuzi maname sâckeme mitidâŋ mutucne i manarâ biaŋkenaŋte muwec .
46001022	Judaŋic jaŋe fuŋne qaqa mâsire qizec qaeŋgopieŋ â Grikŋic jaŋe maŋɋârâŋhec eniŋte fotarieeŋqopieŋ ,
46001023	nâŋe ine Kristo maripoŋko qakicne irec dâŋ mupene Judaŋic jaŋe manapie quŋke sâqoreekac â qâpuc jaŋe manapie dâŋ mutucne eekac ,
46001024	ehame hefârec-jopakicne , Judaŋic mecne Grikŋic mecne , jaŋe ine Kristore manapie Anutu tâpiri-ticnere â maŋɋârâŋ-ticnere hozine eekac .
46001025	Ŋic jaŋe Anuture mutucne muhapie mutuc-ticnezi ŋic jaŋere mamana jâuruekac â Anuture dodocne muhapie dodocne-ticnezi ŋic jaŋere tâpiri sirickeekac .
46001026	Âgofâc-nane . ŋic weniŋucne hefârec-ŋopakicne i mana honeniŋ : Sahackopec wiacte maŋɋârâŋhec bocjaha mâcne , tâpirihec bocjaha mâcne , ŋicbomboŋ guruonec bocjaha mâcne .
46001027	Ŋic maio mutucne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anutuzi hefârec-jopahuc maŋɋârâŋhec mimi qaqa ejareekac , â ŋic maio gegec dodocne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anutuzi hefârec-jopahuc tâpirihec mimi qaqa ejareekac ,
46001028	â ŋic maio omane â hujukicne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anutuzi hefârec-jopaekac , â ŋic maio bebekâne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anutuzi hefârec-jopahuc šai šonšoŋ-jeŋichec jaŋe siŋ qatara-jareekac .
46001029	Mâreŋŋic moczi Anuture maio sahac-ticne bafezacte iŋuc hâcne ewec .
46001030	E mitio juju-ŋeŋicte bâbâfua i Kristo Jesu râe-nârewec . Kristo e hâcne Anutuzi maŋɋârâŋ dâŋte rowaŋ-nâŋec â kiŋroro-nâŋec â maŋɋaɋac bâbâfua-nâŋec â kikitâc-nâŋec râe-nârewec .
46001031	Irec dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc fokac i sanaŋkezejec : “ Moc e mumuteŋ dâŋ muzo murâ Wofuŋtao muzejec . ”
46002001	Âgo bureŋ , no ŋoŋerao fisipo ine Anuture mumutaniŋ dâŋ ŋazapemurâ dâŋ ericke bâpiaŋ ehuc me maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ moc muhuc mi ŋazapo .
46002002	No šiŋuc mana sanaŋkehuc fâpo : Dâŋ gâcne aricne , Jesu Kristo maripoŋko qakicne ere dâŋ jâmbâŋ jaha muzepac .
46002003	Erâ ŋoŋerao dodocne enarehame hâhâwic â memezac faio boc jupo .
46002004	Ehuc miti mumu i maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ mu bâpiaŋ ekicne irec sâcko mi mupo , aricne , tâpiri â Mâro ŋoŋerao fuaocte irec sâcko mupo .
46002005	I mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋiczi ŋic maŋɋârâŋ dâŋko mâcne , Anuture tâpirio fosiŋneocte iŋuc epo .
46002006	Maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ hukicne ine maŋjeŋic ɋârâŋkekicne jaŋe jazaeŋgopeneŋ , erâ i mâreŋ kecširec maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ me mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋ sisirowenezi dâŋ hukicne mueŋgopieŋ irec sâc mi eekac , aricne .
46002007	Nâŋe Anuture dâŋsoŋ hukicne mufuaeŋgopeneŋ . Dâŋ i ŋic nâŋâc taniŋke ɋaɋac enaŋte Anutuzi mârâc jaha dameŋmâc juwecko mu bâmoc ewec .
46002008	Mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋ jaŋeraonec moczi moc dâŋ hukicne i hâcne mi mana tarambiŋ , mana tararâ muzac eri tatamac Wofuŋ maripoŋko mi qanšapiŋ .
46002009	Irec dâŋqâreŋ fokac ine šiŋuc : “ Ʒâŋezi mi honekicne â hazeczi mi manakicne , â ŋicmaŋ moczi moc mi manasukicne , Anutuzi maŋjauŋ ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋere biŋe bâmockewec i hâcne . ”
46002010	Nâŋe ine Anutuzi Mâro-ticne ecneme dâŋ i mufua-nârewec . Mâro e wiac sasawa irec fuŋne mana gufuc efâreekac . Anutu e jahacne fuŋne bâutuckekicne i mâmâc manaekac .
46002011	Mo ŋiczi âgo-ticnere maŋte fuŋne manaocmu ? Maŋ rune eki sawa manaocmu . Eme Anutu maŋticnere fuŋne iŋuc jaha ŋic moczi mi manaocmu , Anutu Mâro-ticnezi buc manaocmu .
46002012	Eme nâŋe ŋickonec mâro i mi rombeŋ , nâŋe Anuturaonec miti kâdoc hone mana tarac enaŋte Anuturaonec Mâro i rombeŋ .
46002013	Nâŋe miti kâdoc irec hâcne mu binaŋ eeŋgopeneŋ . I ŋic maŋɋârâŋheczi mi qazu-nârembiŋ , i Mârozi qazu-nârewec . Eme Mârore dâŋ i Mârore dâŋmaracko mueŋgopeneŋ .
46002014	Ŋic Mâro tâmiric moczi ine Anutu Mâro-ticnere dâŋ mi manaocmu . E wemo-ticnezi manaocmu , aricne , e maname dâŋ fârimâc eocmu . I Mâroheczi mamanane sawa eekac .
46002015	Ŋic Mâroheczi wiac sasawa sâcne mana wosâeocmu , ŋic Mâro tâmiriczi ine ere fuŋne kâuc baocmu .
46002016	Wofuŋ maŋticnere dâŋ i mozi manaweczi sâcne âzâcne mutâc eocmu ? Nâŋe ine Kristo maŋbuc-ticnere dâŋ bajuŋgopeneŋ .
46003001	Âgofâc-nane , no ŋoŋerao fisirâ ŋic Mârohec dâŋ jajazane i wemocko ŋazazapo ? Aricne , ŋic Mâro tâmiric jajazane i Kristore ɋiefâc ŋoŋe ŋazapo .
46003002	No nânâ sanaŋne mi ŋarehuc susu sawa gumec-ŋopapo , nânâ sanaŋne wemocko nanšapiŋ . Erâ šiŋuczia nânâ sanaŋne nâniŋte sâc wâc mi eŋgopieŋ .
46003003	Ŋoŋe Mârohec sâcne mi embiŋ . E tâmiric juhuc hâcne iiriac â kikisâ bâfuahuc ŋic omane jaŋe iŋucne jueŋgopieŋ .
46003004	Ŋoŋe “ no Paulore ŋic ” , “ no Apolore ŋic ” mueŋgopieŋte ŋic iŋucne ŋoŋe ŋic omane hâcne muŋarezo .
46003005	Apolo e mo ? Á Paulo no mo ? Nâhe kiŋaŋ qaqa sawazi miti ŋazapere manambiŋ . Erâ Wofuŋzi gie munâctewec sâc bapec .
46003006	No he sarac epo , Apolo e hofâ gie bawec , â Wofuŋzi ine jambuŋkeme fârine fuawec .
46003007	Irec he sarac eekac ere mi muzo , â hofâ gie baekac ere mi muzo , jambuŋkeme fârine fuaekac , Anutu hâcne ere mocjaha muzo .
46003008	He sarac eekac â hofâ gie baekac jahe sâcjekic mocjaha , furine ine gie-jekicte sâc bârâwiŋ ronicmu .
46003009	Nâŋe Anuture babafic , ŋoŋe ine Anuture gie â Anuture fic .
46003010	Anutuzi gie tahacnuwec sâc no ficbapa fârinezi simeŋ wâtuŋ râepe huwec . Eme irec fainao ŋic moczi fic šuhuckerâ baekac . Iŋucnezi mana manahuc bazejec .
46003011	Wâtuŋ huwec domakac , Jesu Kristo hâcne , e unucke behec erâ moc râepene huhune mi fokac .
46003012	Eme wâtuŋ irec fainao moczi goì siliwa me qânâ sanaŋzi , me pipisac sopâc bacrehaczi šuhuckerâ baocmu , ine juku fic bapa-ticnere fuŋne taniŋkeocmu .
46003013	Juku dameŋ sâkoo hâcne fuŋne taniŋkeocmu . Ira šocsâko bâruŋkeocmu , eme šoc izi hâcne ficgiere fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu .
46003014	Ŋic moczi wâtuŋ faio fic baocmu , i šoczi šâipieme furine roocmu .
46003015	Á ŋic mocte fic šoczi šafâreme furine tâmiric juocmu , e jahacne ine akickezo , akickehuc šockonec batarazo .
46003016	Ŋoŋe Anuture miti ufuŋ , â Anuture Mârozi maŋŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju eekac , i mi manaŋgopieŋ me ?
46003017	Ŋic moc e Anuture ufuŋ ima baocmu e Anutuzi wâc ima baocmu . Anuture miti ufuŋ i furu mukicne , eme ufuŋ-ticne i ŋoŋe hâcne .
46003018	Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic mi eatuckenšepieŋ . ŋoŋeraonec moc e ŋicdâŋ mana maŋ ehuc mamana-ticnere maname fefene eocmu , iŋucnezi mamana i qikiŋnehuc mutucne erâ mamana fârine bâfuazejec .
46003019	Mâreŋte maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ i Anutuzi maname fârimâc eekac . Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ E ŋic maŋɋârâŋhec jaŋe maŋsioc gie bahapie somâc-jopame somâmaŋ-ticnao hueŋgopieŋ . ”
46003020	Erâ moc šiŋuc : “ Wofuŋ e ŋic maŋɋârâŋhec jaŋere dâŋ maname racne eekac . ”
46003021	Irec ŋoŋe mâreŋŋic nâŋere muhuc maŋfefe mi enšepieŋ . Wiac sasawa i ŋoŋere biŋe .
46003022	Paulo â Apolo â Kefa nâŋe ŋoŋere biŋe . Erâ mâreŋko wiac sasawa , juju me hâhâmo , šiŋuczia fofone â juku fufuane , i ŋoŋere biŋe sasawa .
46003023	Ŋoŋe ine Kristore biŋe â Kristo eki ine Anuture biŋe .
46004001	Ŋoŋe nâŋere manapie Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa â Anutu boreŋ šeŋaŋ-ticnere soŋaŋ ezejec .
46004002	Eme soŋaŋ e ine metâne juocte mucnekicne .
46004003	Erâ no nahacnere mupe : Ŋoŋe me ŋic tutumaŋ moczi nore dâŋ muniŋmu i manape fârine mi eocmu . Erâ no nahac wâc fuŋne-nane sâcne mi mupemu .
46004004	No bahac-nane moc mi manakopac , erâ irec bahacmâc jukopac mi muzo . Nore fuŋne babataniŋ mocjaha jukac , Wofuŋ hâcne .
46004005	Irec ŋoŋe fuŋne babataniŋte fâro mi enšepieŋ . Wofuŋ e jahac fisirâ wiac soŋsoŋ fokac i wâc hewirickeocmu , â ŋicmaŋko wiac fokac i mâmâc bâfua-fâreocmu . Eme Anutuzi ŋic sasawa sâcjeŋic manahuc mumbiaŋ-jopaocmu .
46004006	Âgofâc , dâŋ mukopac i Apolo â no nâhe nâhâcnao iticnehuc mukopac . Eme ŋoŋe nâherao fuŋne kecšiŋuc honehuc mana taranšepieŋ : Mitidâŋko sâc mukicne i mi jâuruhuc wiac efezo â mâreŋŋic bafec bawahac enârehuc maŋfefe mi ezo .
46004007	Me go ŋiczi wiac hezu hegareniŋte mozi mugarewec ? Me go wiac fogarekac i wenimoi gare tahac mi ekicne ? Aricne , i gare tahac efârekicne , eme go wemocte manatec mi garekicne tinac eme sahacge bafeekic ?
46004008	Ŋoŋe ine biac gapec-ŋopakicne , biac mâriri sâkohec embiŋ juŋgopieŋ , nâŋe tâmiric ŋicwofuŋ embiŋ juŋgopieŋ . Jâmbomac ŋicwofuŋ enšapiŋ me , ehuc hefârec-  nâpopie ŋoŋerao šuhuckehuc ŋicwofuŋ jaha enšapeŋ .
46004009	No manape Anutuzi aposolo nâŋe ŋic jawane jaŋere guruo râec-nâpowec ekac , šikare biŋe ekicne tinac . Mâmâc sâko , aŋelo mecne ŋic mecne , honec-nâpopie mamakucne eeŋgopeneŋ hâcne .
46004010	Nâŋe Kristore erâ ŋic mutucne embeŋ , ŋoŋe ine Kristorao šuhuckerâ mamana sâkohec embiŋ , nâŋe gegec dodocne , ŋoŋe ine sasanaŋhec , ŋoŋe fekicne , nâŋe ine waha qaqane .
46004011	Nâŋe nânâ opâre hâmo sipiric embeŋzi eeŋgopeneŋ , erâ ŋaqi tâmiric â šika faio â fic hae tâmiric jumbeŋzi juŋgopeneŋ .
46004012	Á wiac piticne hotâckenaŋte nâŋe nâŋâcne mezi gie baeŋgopeneŋ . Musoriŋ-nâpohapie jambuŋ-jopaeŋgopeneŋ , fific guguriŋ enârehapie mana urueeŋgopeneŋ .
46004013	Musâqorec-nâpohapie mu bâmiriŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ , nâŋe ŋic mâmâc sâko jaŋere jawa sânšâŋ tinac jumbeŋzi juŋgopeneŋ hâcne .
46004014	No mimi qaqa eŋarepere mâcne , no naru motecfâc-mae ŋoŋe uŋ sawaŋ eŋarehuc dâŋ ši qâreŋkekopac .
46004015	Kristoo wišecfâc-ŋeŋic guruhec juŋareŋgopieŋ mecne , â mamac ine wemocko bocjaha juŋarenšapiŋ , Kristo Jesure erâ Biŋebiaŋ ŋazahuc no mocjahazi mamac-ŋeŋic epo jukopac .
46004016	Eme irec nore kike hata bâjâpehuc juniŋte hazec qâuŋ ŋazape mananšepieŋ .
46004017	No irec erâ hâcne Timoteo , Wofuŋko motec biaŋ-mae junarekac , e ŋoŋerao sorepe fakac , fârâ no Kristore miti hata kikefuŋ hae sâc jaza jowatuc eekopac i manasu-ŋareme mananšepieŋ .
46004018	Ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi e mi wareocmu , nore iŋuc muhuc mukac mupe embiŋ .
46004019	No ine Wofuŋzi maname sâckeme mi šoraha ŋoŋerao fâpemu , fârâ mukac mupe eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe dâŋjeŋicte mi muhuc tâpiri-jeŋicte fuŋne bataniŋkepemu .
46004020	Anuture miti hata i dâŋko mâcne , sasanaŋko fua taniŋkeekac .
46004021	Eme ŋoŋe nore weniŋuc muŋgopieŋ ? Kâcbiŋhec fâpemurâ muŋgopieŋ , me maŋjauŋ â buuruchec fâpemurâ muŋgopieŋ ?
46005001	No šiŋuc ine jâmbomac mupie manaekopac : Ŋoŋerao mamakâc hâhâwicne , qâpuc jaŋerao mi fufuane , iŋucne fuawec fokac . Ŋic moczi mamac-ticnere ŋonâŋhec juekac , irec mukopac .
46005002	Eme ŋoŋe wemocte wiac iŋucne fuarâ fohame pepecne eeŋgopieŋ ? Ŋoŋe busâqoc manahuc ŋic wiac ewec e behenšapiŋ me ¡
46005003	No sahac-nanezi wiwicko juhuc maŋnanezi iqic-ŋoparâ ŋic wiac ewec ere dâŋ ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko juhuc tinac kecšiŋuc mutarapo :
46005004	Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ Jesu ere šâŋeo tumaŋnehapie no ere tâpirio ŋesiŋnehuc maŋnanezi iqic-ŋopape
46005005	ŋic e Sataŋ qikiŋnecnepene maŋ sahac raŋɋa-ticne sipirickezejec , eme Wofuŋ Jesure dameŋ maickeme mâro-ticnezi aakic bâfuazejec .
46005006	Wiac iŋucne foipiehame sahac-ŋeŋic bafeeŋgopieŋte manape sâqorekac . Bec hâhâtâne i wiac piticnezi fârine ruacneme rikepie isirickeme hâtâne efâreocmu , i mi manaeŋgopieŋ me ?
46005007	Irec hâhâtâne wosâerâ behepie rahame fârine nocne enšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe hâhâtâ-ŋeŋic ŋowac rofârekicne . Nâŋâcne aakic lama okac-nâŋec qakicne wâc , Kristo hâcne .
46005008	Irec hombaŋ-ticne ŋenaŋte wiac hâhâtâne behenšepeneŋ . Mamakâc â sindaŋ irec hâhâtâne qikiŋnerâ wiac ɋaɋacne â tiŋne irec fârine nocne bajuhuc hombaŋ-ticne ŋezo .
46005009	No mârâc papia moc šiŋuc qâreŋke-ŋarepo : “ Ŋoŋe sasecŋic jaŋehec wiac nâ nareŋ gareŋ â iiqic mi enšepieŋ ” ,
46005010	i ŋic qâpuczi sasecŋic me bâkiri bapa â fiuc serereŋhec me bawe qaŋgec wiac babaju jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere mi mupo . Jaŋe mâreŋ behehuc behec-jopazo i sawa fokac .
46005011	No kecšiŋucte qâreŋke-ŋarepo : Miti mamana âgo-ŋeŋic moczi sasecko sâqoreocmu me bâkiri baocmu , me bawe qaŋgec wiac bajuocmu , me fiuc serereŋ eocmu , ŋic iŋucne behehuc ehec nâ nareŋ gareŋ moc mi enšepieŋ .
46005012	No ŋic râpene jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere dâŋ mumure wemocko qâreŋkezapo . ŋaŋacne ŋondeŋko miti mamana jaŋere bahacdâŋ mupie sâckeocmu .
46005013	Á râpene jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere bahacdâŋ i Anutuzi muocmu . Sâqocne bapa e behepie ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko mi juzejec .
46006001	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi âgo-ticnere bahacdâŋ bajuocmu , e dâŋ i mitiŋic jaŋerao mi rârâe ŋic miti tâmiric jaŋerao râeme sâckeocmu me ?
46006002	Mitiŋic nâŋâc juku miti tâmiric jaŋere dâŋ mutaranaŋmu , i mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Me juku gie iŋucne baniŋte muŋarekicnezi ŋaŋacne dâŋ jawane fuame sâcne mi mutaraniŋmu me ?
46006003	Nâŋâc aŋelo jaŋere dâŋ wâc mutaranšoŋgopeneŋzi wiac omanere dâŋ fuame wemocko bititienaŋmu .
46006004	Wiac omanere dâŋ fuame ŋoŋe wemocte kikefuŋzi mana-jareme wawahane eekac ŋic iŋucne jaŋerao barapie mutara-ŋareeŋgopieŋ ?
46006005	Ŋoŋe dâŋ i manapie miminehec eocte ŋazakopac . Ŋoŋerao ŋic maŋɋârâŋhec moc mi jukac me ? Eme dâŋŋeŋic fuame erao barapie mutiŋne-ŋarezac .
46006006	Ŋoŋe ine iŋuc mi eeŋgopieŋ , aricne , miti mamana moczi âgo-ticnehec dâŋbahac-jekic fuame miti tâmiric jaŋerao barame mutara-jacteniŋmu .
46006007	Ŋoŋerao dâŋgie fuaekac izi miti-ŋeŋic bawahaekac . Gâcnezi wiac hehesicne me bâbâsifucne eŋarezo murâ eŋarepie ŋifecpeaŋ fozac me ¡
46006008	Ŋoŋe ine ŋaŋac wiac hehesicne â fiuc serereŋ eeŋgopieŋ , ehuc mitio qomâfâc-ŋeŋic mâmâc ejareeŋgopieŋ .
46006009	Sâqocne bapazi Anuture uucmaŋko rarašine mi fokac , i mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic mi eatuckeniŋ , sau bapa , me  bawe qaŋgec babaju , me ŋokac ba behecne , me sasecŋic , me ŋiczia mamakâc eec eene ,
46006010	me fiuc roro , me bâkiri bapa , me maŋsifuc opâ nâ areŋ eene , me dâŋ bâbâiŋ , me kâŋgâc rohuc šika qaqa , iŋucnezi Anuture uucmaŋko mi rašiniŋmu .
46006011	Eme gâcne ŋoŋe mârâc sâc iŋuc hâcne jujumbieŋ ši ine šurec-ŋopakicne â maŋfuru bacŋopakicne â kiŋfâsâc bacŋopakicne . I Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore šâŋe bajueŋgopieŋte â Anutu-nâŋecte Mârohec jueŋgopieŋte iŋuc eŋarekicne .
46006012	Wiac sasawa eene fonarekac , erâ wiac sasawa epe izi sâcne mi baficnuocmu . Wiac sasawa eene fonarekac , erâ wiac moczi ŋicbomboŋ enareme irec kiŋaŋ qaqa juju ine misac .
46006013	Nânâ qowizi hobure biŋe â hobuzi nânâ qowire biŋe . Juku Anutuzi e â e mâmâc imac-jofame arictac enicmu . Sahaczi ine sasecte biŋe mâcne , i Wofuŋte biŋe , Wofuŋ e sahacte ru .
46006014	Eme Anutuzi Wofuŋ bâɋârewec iŋuc jaha tâpiri-ticnezi nâŋâc bâɋârec-nâpozokac .
46006015	Sahac-ŋeŋic Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa , i mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Eme Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa e weniŋuc qârisiepene sasecte kiŋaŋ qaqa eocmu ? Iŋuc aricne .
46006016	Me ŋoŋe šiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ , ŋic moczi ŋokac sâqocne moctao qohotame jahe maŋ sahac mocjaha enicmu . Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Jahe jajaheczi mocjaha erâ junicmu . ”
46006017	Á moc e Wofuŋtao qohotame ehec maŋ qâqâtâc mocjaha enicmu .
46006018	Ŋoŋe sasec boe sau dic bacnenšepieŋ . Ŋic moczi wiac hehesicne gâcne eocmu izi sahac-ticne mi heuaocmu , â boe sau eocmuzi ine e jahacne sahac bâbieocmu .
46006019	Me ŋoŋe šiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ , sahac-ŋeŋic i Tiri Mârore ufuŋ , e ŋoŋere sahacmaŋko ŋeŋe juju eocte Anutuzi râe-ŋarewec . Ŋoŋe maŋ sahac rune aricne .
46006020	Ŋoŋe furi-ŋeŋic rokicne . Irec sahac-ŋeŋiczi Anuture šâŋe biŋe dopeckezejec .
46007001	Ŋoŋe papia râe-narehuc dâŋ wio-narembiŋ , irec šiŋuc mufuape mananiŋ : Ŋic moczi ŋokac tâmiric juzo mume sâckeocmu .
46007002	Erâ sasecte eesâic fokacte ŋiczi ŋokac rorâ ehec paŋšâic juzejec , â ŋokaczi iŋuc jaha ŋic rorâ ehec paŋšâic juzejec .
46007003	Eme ŋiczi sahac-ticne i ŋonâŋ-ticne mi sakarecnezejec , â ŋonâŋzi sahac-ticne ŋowe-ticne mi sakarecnezejec .
46007004	Ŋonâŋ e sahac-ticnere dâŋ mumu i jahacne mâcne , ŋowe qikiŋnecnekicne , â ŋowe e iŋuc jaha sahac-ticnere dâŋ mumu i jahacne mâcne , ŋonâŋ qikiŋnecnekicne .
46007005	Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋoŋe sahac sasakarec kosa mi enšepieŋ . Mâc nunumure afeckeniŋte qanaŋ muc manac erâ dameŋ bahuc iŋuc epie sâckeocmu . Dameŋ tâmiric mâc jufepie Sataŋzi esâic-ŋopazacte iŋuc mukopac .
46007006	Ŋic â ŋokac roroc eniŋte mukopac i mana urue-ŋarehuc mukopac , mupaŋke-ŋarehuc mâcne .
46007007	Nahacne maŋzi šiŋuc mukac : Ŋic sasawa no jukopac iŋuc jufârenšapiŋ me . Anutu e ine tâpiri buc buc tahac-nâpoekac i hatane bârâwiŋ , moc iŋuc â moc iŋuc .
46007008	Ŋic ŋokac šeŋoŋ â hozec jaŋere ine šiŋuc mukopac : Jaŋe no iŋucne jufepie sâckeocmu .
46007009	Me sasec tâmiric sâcne jujune mi fojarekacko ine sasecte šoczi sipiric-jopazacte ŋowe ŋonâŋ erâ junšepieŋ .
46007010	Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋoŋere dâŋ mupe mananiŋ , erâ i nore dâŋ mâcne , i Wofuŋte micdâŋ : Ŋokac moczi ŋowe-ticne mi behezejec .
46007011	Á ŋowe-ticne biac behewecko ŋic tâmiric juzejec , me ŋowe-ticnehec mocwâc âgo babac ezepirec . Erâ ŋic moczi iŋuc jaha ŋonâŋ-ticne mi behezejec .
46007012	Gâcne jaŋere dâŋ ši mupe manapie Wofuŋte mâcne , no nahacne ezejec : Opâ ruac ŋic moc ere ŋonâŋ qâpuc juocmu , eme ŋokac izi ehec juocte ecneocmuo mi behezejec .
46007013	Me opâ ruac ŋokac moc ere ŋowe qâpuc juocmu , eme ŋic izi ehec juocte ecneocmuo mi behezejec .
46007014	Ŋic qâpuc erao ŋonâŋ-ticnere jambuŋzi fotâcnewec , â ŋokac qâpuc erao ŋowe-ticnere jambuŋzi fotâcnewec . Eme irec hâcne naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic jambuŋhec embiŋ juŋgopieŋ , I tâmiric muzac qâpuc junšapiŋ .
46007015	Oapuc ŋiczi me qâpuc ŋokaczi ine âgo-ticne miti mamana beheocte qizec qame mi sakarezejec . Irec niŋgiŋne mi fokac . Anutu e wamao ââgo erâ juniŋte hefârec-ŋopawec .
46007016	Ŋokac go ŋowege miti hatao fâretec wareocmu me mâcne , i moc manakic me ? Me ŋic go ŋonâŋge miti hatao fâretec wareocmu me mâcne , i moc manakic me ?
46007017	Moc e Wofuŋzi ju ju bâfuacnewec , â moc e Anutuzi gie mucnewec , sâc ijaha mitio juzejec wâc . No dâŋ iŋuc kikefuŋ hae sâc jaza mutâc eekopac .
46007018	Moc e mahec juhame Wofuŋzi hefârewecko ma i mi behezejec . Á moc e ma tâmiric juhame Wofuŋzi hefârewecko mare mi muzejec .
46007019	Mahec juju me ma tâmiric juju izi fârine mâcne , Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋ izi fârine ekac .
46007020	Moc e dodoma ira me ira domahame Wofuŋzi hefârewecko dodoma ijaha domazejec .
46007021	Go kiŋaŋ qaqa juhaŋtec hefârecguwecko manabâc tâmiric Juzemec . Mâc firuecguzo mupie mi qikiŋnezemec .
46007022	Moc e kiŋaŋ qaqa juhame Wofuŋzi hefâreme Wofuŋte ŋicfâri ewec Jukac . Á moc e ŋicfâri juhame Wofuŋzi hefâreme Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa ewec jukac .
46007023	Ŋoŋe furi-ŋeŋic rokicnere ŋic jaŋere kiŋaŋ qaqa mi enšepieŋ .
46007024	Âgo bureŋ , moc e mârâc domahuc miti manawec , biri ijaha dameŋ šiŋuczia domahuc Anuturao qohotazejec .
46007025	Naru šeŋoŋ jaŋere Wofuŋte micdâŋ mi bajukopac . Erâ Wofuŋzi roroŋ fâre-nareme mitihec epore nahacne dâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ :
46007026	Dameŋ šiŋuczia šârâ hâriŋ boc fuaekacte ŋic moc ŋonâŋ tâmiric juzo mume manape biaŋkeocmu .
46007027	Á ŋokac biŋe biac mugarekicko ine mi qikiŋnezemec , me go mesawane jukicko ine ŋokacte mi muzemec .
46007028	Me ŋokac rozo murâ rotec wâc mi sâqoreocmu , â naru šeŋoŋ moczi ŋic rome wâc mi sâqoreocmu . Erâ iŋucnezi sahackopec wiacte hume serereŋ juniŋmu . No ine i tâmiric mac juniŋte enareha mukopac .
46007029	Âgofâc-nane , dâŋ ši mupe mananiŋ : Dameŋ rifirekac . Eme dameŋ bembeŋne fokacte ŋonâŋhec jueŋgopieŋzi jupie ŋonâŋ tâmiric juju tinac ezejec ,
46007030	â kioeŋgopieŋzi jupie ki tâmiric tinac ezejec , â šeri eeŋgopieŋzi jupie šeri tâmiric tinac ezejec , â wiac furi baeŋgopieŋzi jupie mafa tâmiric tinac ezejec ,
46007031	â wiac nâ bac eeŋgopieŋzi jupie i tâmiric tinac ezejec . Mâreŋ hawari qâreŋne ši hone manac eeŋgopeneŋ i siroweocmu ekac , irec hâcne dâŋ i mukopac .
46007032	Ŋoŋe ine wiac omanere mana mezac tâmiric erâ juniŋte manasuhuc mukopac . Ŋonâŋ tâmiriczi Wofuŋte giere mana mezac eocmu , ehuc Wofuŋzi manacneme biaŋkeocte muocmu .
46007033	Ŋonâŋheczi ine sahackopec wiacte mana mezac eocmu , ehuc ŋonâŋ-ticnezi manacneme biaŋkeocte muocmu .
46007034	Iŋuc erâ maŋguru eocmu . Eme ŋokac šeŋoŋ â naru šeŋoŋ jaŋe iŋuc jaha Wofuŋte giere mana mezac eniŋmu , ehuc maŋ sahac-jeŋic Wofuŋte biŋe eocte manasuniŋmu . Á ŋokac ŋoweheczi ine sahackopec wiacte mana mezac eocmu , ehuc ŋowe-ticnezi manacneme biaŋkeocte muocmu .
46007035	Ŋoŋe sâcne juhâmoniŋte dâŋ ši ŋazakopac , qaisoc-ŋopahuc mâcne , ŋoŋe kosa mi juhuc maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic qâzuckepie Wofuŋtea hâcbuc domaocte mukopac hâcne .
46007036	Me ŋic moc e otâ-ticne ŋic roronere sâc bâfuaha sakareocte maname mi sâckeme ŋicko râezo murâ râezejec , i mi sâqoreocmu .
46007037	Ŋic moc e ine maŋticnezi šiŋuc mana sanaŋkeocmu , otâ-nane mâc juzejec , iŋuc murâ maname mi quŋkeocmu , ehuc afeckerâ iŋuc mupaŋkeme sâckeocmu .
46007038	Irec ŋic moc e otâ-ticne ŋicne ŋicko râeme sâsâckecne eocmu , â moc e otâ-ticne sakareme ine sâcke-hâmoocmu .
46007039	Ŋokac moc e ŋowe-ticne juocmu sâc gâjoŋnao bohotarâ domazejec . Ŋowe-ticne hâmome ine ŋic moc me moc rozo murâ rozejec , erâ kosa ehuc mâcne , Wofuŋtao roweckehuc ezejec .
46007040	Ŋowe tâmiric mâc juocmu irec ine manape sâcke-hâmoocmu . I nahacne dâŋ , erâ i Anuture Mâro wâc fonarekacte mukopac .
46008001	Ʒi nemure tiwâ šepecte mupe . Nâŋâc fuŋne mamana jufâreŋgopeneŋ i manaŋgopeneŋ . Erâ fuŋne mamana saware sahac fefe fuaocmu , maŋjauŋhec juhuc ine hehešakiec erâ sâcne juzo .
46008002	Moc e mamana-ticne mana sokame ere muzo , mamana fârine mi focnekac .
46008003	Moc e Anutu maŋjauŋ ecneocmu , e ine Anutuzi manariŋkewec .
46008004	Nemure tiwâ šepecte ine šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Nemu e wiac fârine mâcne , Anutu e mocjaha fârine .
46008005	Nemu sambâŋko me mâreŋko juŋgopieŋ , dâŋ iŋuc mupie nemu â wofuŋ burec burec wemo afecne foraŋgopieŋ ekac .
46008006	Á nâŋâc ine Anutu Mamac-nâŋec mocjaha junârekac , eraonec hâcne wiac sasawa fua-fârewec â nâŋâc erea juŋgopeneŋ . Erâ Wofuŋ mocjaha , Jesu Kristo , ere meo wiac sasawa â nâŋâc jufâreŋgopeneŋ .
46008007	Ŋic gâcne jaŋe ine fuŋne iŋuc sâcne mi mana-hâmoŋgopieŋ . Eme iŋucnezi nemu e wiac fârine muwarehuc juku maŋjeŋic ewecte tiwâ šepec e araŋ bacnehuc manabâcko nâpie maŋjeŋic hegâpâreekac .
46008008	Anutu e nânâre erâ mi mana-nâreme biaŋkeocmu . Tiwâ šepec qikiŋnepene mi mana wahac-nâpoocmu , me nâpene mi mana-nâreme feocmu .
46008009	Mâc gâcne ŋoŋe mana jaŋgeŋkehuc nâeŋgopieŋzi âgofâc-ŋeŋic miti afecne fojareekac jaŋe maŋ bâsifuc ejarenšipiŋte manabâc enšepieŋ .
46008010	Go qarâ sanaŋgere nemu ufuŋko šepecne nâhuc ŋehaŋtec âgoge moc manabâcheczi honecgurâ , nakacte nâpe muhuc mi ijaha nâocmu me ?
46008011	Eme âgoge miti afecne focnekac e Kristore soczia wâc kitâcneweczi gore qarâ sanaŋte mi docke sâqorec eocmu me ?
46008012	Ŋoŋe iŋuc ehuc âgofâc-ŋeŋic wâwânâŋ ejarehuc maŋ bâsifuc ejareniŋmu , ine Kristo wâwânâŋ ecneniŋmu .
46008013	Irec no tiwâ šepec nâpe âgo-nanezi irec erâ docke sâqorec ezacte ere manabâc ehuc tiwâ šepec qikiŋnehuc mâc juku hâmozepac .
46009001	No niŋgiŋhec juekopac me ? No aposolo aricne me ? No Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu mi honepo me ? Gie-nanere fârine Wofuŋte jambuŋko fuakicne i ŋoŋe mi eŋgopieŋ me ?
46009002	No gâcne jaŋere aposolo mi mecne juekopac , â ŋoŋere ine jâmbomac juekopac . Aposolo gie-nanere ma Wofuŋte jambuŋko fuakicne i ŋoŋe hâcne .
46009003	Fuŋne-nanere mueŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikie-jarekopac .
46009004	Gâcne nâŋe ŋoŋeraonec nânâ opâ mi ronaŋte muac-nâpokicne me ?
46009005	Aposolo tucne â Wofuŋte ɋafâc â Petoro jaŋe ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋehec miti kiŋaŋ raeŋgopieŋ , ehame gâcne nâŋe sâc ijaha enaŋte mi mana-nârekicne me ?
46009006	Me no â Banaba nâhe sawa mezi gie bapa behenacte mi mana-nâctekicne me ?
46009007	Me mo momori ŋiczi šikare wiac e jahacne moneŋzi furine baocmu ? Me mozi gie he sarac eme fârine fuame mi ro nâc eocmu ? Me mozi noniŋ bulimakao gie bahuc jaŋere susu ba nâc mi eocmu ?
46009008	Ʒi ŋicdâŋ sawa mukopac me ? Sâcmutâc dâŋzi ijaha mi mufuakac me ?
46009009	Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ moc šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Bulimakaozi gie bagarehuc sopâc kecɋaŋ nâzo mume mi sakarecnezemec . Eme Anutuzi dâŋ i bulimakao jaŋere sawa manasuhuc muwec me ?
46009010	Ŋic nâŋâcne mâmâc mi muwec me ? I nâŋâcne hâcne mukicne . Gie he rikec eekaczi mâc mi eekac , fârine fuame nâocte manasuhuc eekac , â sara mamac eekac e iŋuc jaha fârine fuacneocte manasuhuc eekac .
46009011	Nâŋe ŋoŋerao maŋte wiac sara mamac embeŋko okacne ŋoŋeraonec sahacte wiac ronaŋte manapie ŋemâckekac me ?
46009012	Gâcne jaŋe ŋoŋeraonec nânâ mafa rohapie nâŋe gie fuŋkembeŋzi rorone mi fokac me ? Erâ ine Kristo Biŋebiaŋ-ticne aka hecnenšipeŋte ŋoŋeraonec nânâ mafa rorore mukicne i qikiŋnehuc mâc hume serereŋ jueŋgopeneŋ .
46009013	Taha ufuŋko gie baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe taha ufuŋkonec nânâ nâeŋgopieŋ , â alatao bâzi ririke gie baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe alatare wiac nâ bac eeŋgopieŋ , i ŋoŋe mi manaeŋgopieŋ me ?
46009014	Eme Wofuŋ e Biŋebiaŋ mumu ŋic nâŋe iŋuc jaha Biŋebiaŋzi sahacte dope wiac kifua-nâreocte muwec .
46009015	No ine hata i mi âteekopac . Erâ ŋoŋe irec sâcko enareniŋte manasuhuc mi qâreŋkekopac , aricne . Hâmoczi rocnuzac irec manape afeckezac , â šeridâŋ-nane i babawaha-nare irec ine manape ŋic moczi mi enare-jâmbâŋkezejec ekac .
46009016	Biŋebiaŋ muromackeekopac irec mumumbiaŋ dâŋ mupe wemocko sâckeocmu , gie i hâcne nore faio râekicne i ¡ Eme hetarepe , jei , Wofuŋzi weniŋuc enareocmu ¡
46009017	Gie i no nahacne maŋte fuarâ bazapo muzac juku furine rozapo . Nahacne maŋte mi ropore šiŋuc ekac : Micne gie fai-naneo fewec .
46009018	Hâc , eme wemo furi roekopac ? Furine šiŋuc : No miti kiŋaŋ rahuc ŋic Biŋebiaŋ furimâc jazaekopac , ehuc Biŋebiaŋ mumure furi sahackopec wiac rorore mukicne i qikiŋneekopac .
46009019	No ŋic sasawa jaŋere kiŋaŋ qaqa mi jukopaczi sifu kiŋaŋ qaqa-jeŋic epo jukopac . I ŋic bocjahazi miti manarâ biaŋkeniŋte manasuhuc epo hâcne .
46009020	Judaŋic jaŋerao juhuc Judaŋic hawari epo , i Judaŋiczi biaŋkeniŋte . Sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qaeŋgopieŋ jaŋerao juhuc sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa hawari epo , i no nahac sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qahuc mâcne , i kiŋaŋne qaeŋgopieŋzi biaŋkeniŋte epo .
46009021	Qâpuc sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric jaŋerao juhuc sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric hawari epo , i Anuture maio sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric juhuc mâcne , no Kristore sâcmutâc dâŋ bajuekopac , erâ qâpuc jaŋe biaŋkeniŋte iŋuc epo .
46009022	Ŋic dodocne jaŋerao juhuc dodocne hawari epo , i dodocnezi biaŋkeniŋte epo . Ŋic fuŋne fuŋne jaŋerao juhuc hawari fuŋne fuŋne epo , i gâcnezi sipirickehapie sifu gâcnezi biaŋkeniŋte .
46009023	Wiac sasawa i mâc mâcne , Biŋebiaŋzi fua raocte eekopac , erâ no nahac wâc irec kâdoc ropemurâ eekopac .
46009024	Ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Sâsâc eere hofao ira motec jaŋe gagasa i mâmâc gasacke-fâreniŋmu , â eri roro ine mocsâkoazi mao bâbâni fisirâ roocmu . Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha eri-ŋeŋic roniŋte gasackenšepieŋ
46009025	Motec jaŋe sasanaŋte sâsâc ehuc sowa fuŋne fuŋne jueŋgopieŋ , jaŋe eri sisirowenere iŋuc eeŋgopieŋ , nâŋâc ine eri fofo sanaŋte iŋuc enšepeneŋ .
46009026	No nahac wâc gasackeekopac , i ma hone dendeŋnehuc gasackeekopac . No sându-nane sawao kosa mi wickeekopac .
46009027	No ŋic miti muromacke-jarehuc juku nahacne rârâricne ezipore sahac-nane ro waha âte ecnehuc ŋicbomboŋ-ticne juekopac .
46010001	Âgofâc-nane , no mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec wiac embiŋ irec manasu-ŋarepe mananiŋ Jaŋe mâmâc sasawa karoraczi sâoc-jopaha rahuc hâwec fotâcnembiŋ .
46010002	Ehuc Mosere ŋicfâc eniŋte karorac â hâweczi miti opâ-jeŋic eme ruambiŋ .
46010003	Erâ Mârozi nânâ bâfua-jarewec i jaŋe mâmâc sasawa nârambiŋ ,
46010004	â Mârozi opâ bâfua-jarewec i wâc mâmâc sasawa nârambiŋ . Mârore qânâzi bâjâpec-jopawec , eraonec hâcne opâ wahame nâmbiŋ , qânâ šâŋene Kristo .
46010005	Eme sifu Anutuzi gâcne sâko mana sâqore-jareme mâreŋ sawao hâmo sipiric efârembiŋ .
46010006	Jaŋerao wiac fuawec i uŋsawaŋ-nâŋec ekac , jaŋe sâqocnere andac embiŋ iŋuc jaha enšipeŋte .
46010007	Jaŋeraonec gâcnezi nemu qaŋgec wiacte kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ , iŋuc wâc mi enšepeneŋ . Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Ŋic jaŋe waha ŋehuc tiwâ šepec nâku faharerâ gae wohuc domambiŋ .
46010008	Erâ sasec boe sau wâc mi enšepeneŋ . Jaŋeraonec gâcnezi sasec boe sau embiŋ , ehuc šoaŋ gie bapa ijaha ŋic 23 tauseŋ hâmombiŋ .
46010009	Erâ Wofuŋ maŋbâiŋ wâc mi ecnenšepeneŋ . Jaŋeraonec gâcnezi maŋbâiŋ ecnepie homazi kicjopame hâmo sipiric embiŋ .
46010010	Erâ kâroŋ wâc mi qanšepeneŋ . Jaŋeraonec gâcnezi kâroŋ qapie sisipiric runezi sipiric-jopawec .
46010011	Jaŋerao wiac fuawec izi ma âkendâŋnekicne ekac . Eme mâreŋte dameŋ qândâŋkeha juŋgopeneŋ nâŋâcnere uŋsawaŋ muhuc dâŋbinaŋ i hâcne qâreŋkekicne .
46010012	Irec hâcne moc e jahacnere maname sasanaŋ eekaczi dockezacte rumehuc juzejec .
46010013	Ŋoŋerao eesâic fua warewec i ŋic tâpiri-ŋeŋicte sâcko fuawec . Erâ Anutu e mume sasanaŋzi eesâic baafeckeme tâpiri-ŋeŋicte sâc mi jâuruocmu . Erâ eesâic fuaocmu sâc âte sâoc-ŋopame sâcne sanaŋkeniŋmu .
46010014	Irec hâcne , âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe nemu qaŋgec wiacte geŋkerâ junšepieŋ .
46010015	Ŋoŋe maŋ mamanasuhec juŋgopieŋ , irec dâŋ ši mupe ŋaŋac mana honeniŋ .
46010016	Râqâcko waiŋ jambuŋkewecte jambuŋkerâ nâhuc Kristore sochec šušuhuc mi eeŋgopeneŋ me ? Á poroŋ nâhuc Kristore sahachec šušuhuc mi eeŋgopeneŋ me ?
46010017	Nânâzi mocjaha , i gugumec ehuc ŋic bocjahazi âgo guru mocjaha eeŋgopeneŋ .
46010018	Ŋoŋe sahackopec Israe ŋic juŋgopieŋ jaŋere manasuniŋ . Ŋic taha bâzi nâeŋgopieŋ jaŋe alatahec šušuhuc mi eeŋgopieŋ me ?
46010019	Dâŋ i weniŋucte mukopac ? Nemure tiwâ šepec i wiac fârine me ? Á nemu e jahacne wâc fârine me ?
46010020	Iŋuc aricne . Qâpuc jaŋe tiwâ šepec rikeeŋgopieŋ i Anuture biŋe mâcne , i demoŋ jaŋere biŋe eekac . Eme no ŋoŋere šiŋuc mukopac : Ŋoŋe demoŋ jaŋehec šušuhuc mi enšepieŋ .
46010021	Wofuŋte râqâckonec nâhuc demoŋ jaŋere râqâckonec mâmâc nânâ i sâcne mi eniŋmu . Á Wofuŋte teboonec nâhuc demoŋ jaŋere teboonec mâmâc nânâ i wâc sâcne mi eniŋmu .
46010022	Me nâŋâc Wofuŋ maŋbâiŋ ecnenaŋ me ? Nâŋâcne tâpirizi ere sirickekac me ?
46010023	Wiac sasawa eene fokac , erâ wiac sasawa epene izi sâcne mi bafic-nâpoocmu . Wiac sasawa eene fokac , erâ wiac sasawa ehuc mitio dodopec eene ine mi fokac .
46010024	Moc e jahacnere mi manasuhuc , âgo-ticnere manasuzejec .
46010025	Ŋoŋe buŋko bec qowi furine bazo murâ kosa banšepieŋ , ehuc keci omane me nemure ufuŋkonec , iŋuc muhuc mu manabâc mi enšepieŋ .
46010026	Mâreŋ â wiac sasawa mâreŋ fusucmarâ fokac i Wofuŋzi rune Jukac .
46010027	Qâpuc moczi hezu hewâneŋ eŋareme ficticnao fezo murâ fenšepieŋ , erâ nânâ qowi gumec-ŋopame manabâc tâmiric kosa nâhuc mu wioc mi enšepieŋ .
46010028	Á nahapie ŋic moczi šiŋuc moc ŋazaocmu : “ Bec ši nemu ufuŋkonec ” , eme mi nânšepieŋ . I mufua-ŋareocmu ŋic ere manabâc ehuc qikiŋnenšepieŋ .
46010029	I nâpie ŋaŋacne maŋ sâqorezacte mâcne , âgo-ŋeŋicte maŋ sâqorezacte mukopac . No nahacne maŋ manabâc tâmiric fome wemocte moczi e jahacne maŋte sâc norao âke hotaocmu ?
46010030	No Anutu daŋge âzâcnehuc nunumu faio nâpe moczi wemocte mana sâqore-nareocmu ?
46010031	Irec ŋoŋe nânâ qowi nâniŋte , me i me i eniŋte Anutu mumbiaŋkehuc enšepieŋ .
46010032	Ŋoŋe Judaŋic â Grikŋic â Anuture kikefuŋ jaŋere maio bahacmâc jupie moc mi mana sâqore-ŋarenšepieŋ .
46010033	No iŋuc jaha ŋic fuŋne fuŋne jaŋe honecnupie sâckeocte juhuc no nahacne wiac biaŋkeocte mâcne , ŋic bocjaha miti manarâ biaŋkeniŋte giene baekopac .
46011001	No Kristore hata âtehuc bâjâpeekopac , eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha nore hata âtehuc bâjâpecnunšepieŋ .
46011002	Ŋoŋe wiac ebac epo Irec manasu-fârehuc mumutâc dâŋnanere sâcko jueŋgopieŋ , irec manape biaŋkekac .
46011003	Eme ši moc mupe mananiŋ , Kristo e ŋicte kâcɋene , ŋic e ŋokacte kâcɋene , Anutu e Kristore kâcɋene .
46011004	Ŋic moc e qârufac rojuhuc numuocmu me Anuture micdâŋ mufuaocmu , e kâcɋene-ticne mimi qaqa ecneocmu .
46011005	Á ŋokac moczi qârufac tâmiric juhuc numuocmu me Anuture micdâŋ mufuaocmu , e iŋuc jaha kâcɋene-ticne mimi qaqa ecneocmu , erâ ŋokac kosa jujune qizec-jeŋic rokicne jaŋehec sâc mocjaha eocmu .
46011006	Irec ŋokac moc qârufac tâmiric jume qizec rocnezo . Me ŋokac moc e irec mimierâ qizec susuc-ticne sakareocmuzi qârufac rojuzejec .
46011007	Ŋic e ine qizectuc juzejec . E Anuture hawari â Anuture eri tofa bakicne irec . Ŋokac e ine ŋicte eri tofa bakicne .
46011008	Ŋic e ŋokactaonec mi rokicne , ŋokaczi ŋictaonec rokicne .
46011009	Ŋic e ŋokacte erâ mi bâfuakicne , ŋokac e ine ŋicte erâ bâfuakicne .
46011010	Ŋokac e ŋicte wahamicne jukacte irec ma moc qârufac hâcne rojuzejec , mâc jume aŋelo jaŋe honepie sâqorezacte .
46011011	Erâ sifu ŋic e mocbuc-ticne juju â ŋokac e mocbuc-ticne juju i Wofuŋte maio mi fokac .
46011012	Ŋokac e ŋictaonec rokicne , iŋuc wâc ŋiczi ŋokackonec fua sawec eeŋgopeneŋ . Erâ wiac i sasawa Anuturaonec .
46011013	Ŋoŋe ŋaŋac mana honeniŋ , ŋokac moc qârufac tâmiric juhuc Anutu numucneme sâckeocmu me ?
46011014	Á ŋic moc e qizec susuc šoricne rojume iŋuc jaha honepie mi sâckeocmu , irec fuŋne mârâc miti tâmiric juhuc wâc manambiŋ .
46011015	Á ŋokac moc qizec susuc šoricne rojume e ine honepie biaŋkeocmu . Qizec susuc šoricnezi qârufac-ticne eekac .
46011016	Moc e dâŋ ši qâsuazo murâ šiŋuc manazejec : Mâsi i nâŋe â Anuture kikefuŋ gâcne mi bajueŋgopeneŋ .
46011017	Wiac moc ši ine mana-ŋarepe bahacnehec eha uŋ sawaŋ eŋarehuc mupe : Ŋoŋe tumaŋnehuc maŋ biaŋ qaqac mi ehuc maŋ bâbâsâqorec eeŋgopieŋ .
46011018	Erâ mitire tumaŋnepie ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko fâfâuc fuaekac , iŋuc nazapie manape jâmbomac tinac ekac .
46011019	Erâ fâfâuc i mâc mâcne , ŋoŋeraonec wenizi mitio sanaŋkeŋgopieŋ jaŋe fua tâcneniŋte hâcne fuakac .
46011020	Eme ŋoŋe Wofuŋte Tiwâ nâniŋte tumaŋnerâ hesifuckeeŋgopieŋ .
46011021	Ŋaŋacne nânâ bafisirâ boki mi bahuc fâro erâ buc buc nâpie moc e hâmoekac â moc e gapecmâc nâekac .
46011022	Hâc , ŋaŋacne fic basahuc iŋuc eeŋgopieŋ me ? Ŋoŋe nânâ opâ nâzo murâ ira nanšapiŋ ¡ Wemocte Anuture gurufâc jaŋere manapie wawahane eme hapetac busâqoc ejareeŋgopieŋ ? Wemo ŋazape ? Mumbiaŋ-ŋopape ? Wiac kecirec mi mumbiaŋ-ŋopazo .
46011023	No Wofuŋtaonec hâcne ropo i ŋarepo wâc . Ine šiŋuc : Wofuŋ Jesu e Judazi doc bawec ŋafe ira poroŋ rorâ
46011024	daŋge murâ bazurâ muwec : “ Kecši fâri-nane , ŋoŋere due bahuc qikiŋnekicne . Nore manasuhuc iŋuc nâhuc junšepieŋ . ”
46011025	Poroŋ nâpie waiŋ râqâc iŋuc jaha rorâ šiŋuc muwec : “ Râqâc kecšira šâšâfic ɋâricnere socnane ŋekac . Nâniŋmu sâc nore manasuhuc iŋuc nâhuc junšepieŋ .
46011026	Ŋoŋe poroŋ â waiŋ i nâniŋmu sâc Wofuŋ hâmoc biŋe-ticne mutaniŋkehuc juhapie risieocmu .
46011027	Irec moc e poroŋ â Wofuŋte waiŋ i enšaŋauc ecnehuc nâocmu , e Wofuŋ fâri â socticne nâsifuckeme kiŋnehec eocmu .
46011028	Irec moc e poroŋ â waiŋ nâzo murâ qanaŋ maŋticnere fuŋne hone manac ehuc bajaŋgeŋkerâ nâzejec .
46011029	Moc e Wofuŋte fâri hone šâŋitac mi ehuc nâocmuzi kiŋticne nâfuaocmu .
46011030	Ŋoŋe iŋuc hâcne eeŋgopieŋte huc dodoc â huc šâic boc eŋareekac , â gâcnezi biac hâmocko foŋgopieŋ .
46011031	Nâŋâc nâŋâc fuŋne-nâŋec bataniŋkenšapeŋ muzac , Wofuŋzi mi bataniŋkezac .
46011032	Qâoma epene ine Wofuŋzi fuŋne-nâŋec bataniŋkehuc bâtiŋ-nâpoocmu , miti tâmiric jaŋehec juku behec-nâpome sipirickenšipeŋte iŋuc hâcne enâreocmu .
46011033	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe tiwâ wirec nâniŋte tumaŋnerâ woŋec ŋehapie fisi-fârepie fuŋkenšepieŋ .
46011034	Moc e nânâre boc ecneme qanaŋ e jahacne ficko nâzejec , tutumaŋ bâbâsifucne epie okacne fua-ŋarezacte . Dâŋ gâcne i no nahac fârâ mutâcne-ŋarepemu .
46012001	Âgo bureŋ , Mâroraonec miti kadahe irec fuŋne kâuc banšipiŋte ŋazape mananiŋ .
46012002	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha qâpuc juhapie maŋšoc fua-ŋarewec sâc nemuɋâŋ kâpâne jaŋerao ra qohota jumbieŋ .
46012003	Eme irec ŋifecne mupe mananiŋ : Moc e Anuture Mârozi bufahac qacnehame wemocko muocmu “ Jesu go sâwecgukopac ” , â moc e Tiri Mârozi bufahac mi qacnehame wemocko muocmu “ Jesu e Wofuŋ ” .
46012004	Mitire kadahe fuŋne fuŋne fokac , Mâro ine mocjaha ,
46012005	mitire kiŋaŋ gie fuŋne fuŋne fokac , gie rune ine Wofuŋ mocjaha ,
46012006	mitire tâpiri fuŋne fuŋne fokac , tâpiri rune ine Anutu mocjaha . Eki hâcne bâfua-nâre-fâreekac .
46012007	Mâro e mitio juhâmonaŋte ŋic ru sâc tâpiri-ticne kâdoc qanâreekac .
46012008	Moc e Mârozi ecneme miti maŋɋârâŋhec muocmu , moc e Mâro izia ecneme sâc mitire fuŋne hukicne muocmu ,
46012009	moc e Mâro izia ecneme mamanasiŋ sâkohec juocmu , moc e Mâro izia ecneme ŋic huc šâichec ɋiɋicne bacjopaocmu ,
46012010	erâ moc mâsi baocte tâpiri bâfuacneocmu , moc findaŋdâŋ muocte maŋne bâuŋtoocmu , moc e mâro fuŋne fuŋne šâŋitaocte maŋne batamaeocmu , moc e miti marac furuo muocte micne baafeckeocmu , moc e miti marac furu manarâ ŋic dâjeŋicko bâtikieocte bafickeocmu .
46012011	Wiac i sasawa Mâro izia bafâreekac , ehuc maŋticnere ŋic ru sâc wiac bârâwiŋne-nâreekac .
46012012	Ŋic nâŋâc sahac-nâŋeczi mocjaha â sahacte kiŋaŋ qaqafâc ine bocjaha , eme jaŋe bocjahazi qâturepie sahac mocjaha ekac ” eme Kristorao sâc ijaha fokac .
46012013	Mâro mocjahazi nâŋâc Miti Opâo bâturec-nâpome sahac-nâŋecte sâc erâ mocjaha embeŋ . Judaŋic â Grikŋic , kiŋaŋ qaqa â ŋicbomboŋ , nâŋâc Mâro i jaha sasawa ro maŋ efârekicnere mocjaha embeŋ .
46012014	Eme sahacte kiŋaŋ qaqa iŋuc jaha mocjaha mâcne , bocjaha .
46012015	Eme kike e wemocko šiŋuc muzac : ` No me aricne , irec  sahacte tofa mi ekopac ” , iŋuc murâ wemocko sahac beherâ buc juocmu ?
46012016	Me hazeczi wemocko šiŋuc muzac : “ No šâŋe aricne , irec sahacte tofa mi ekopac ” , iŋuc murâ wemocko sahac beherâ buc juocmu ?
46012017	Sahacko šâŋe sasawa fome muzac sahaczi hazec basazac . Me hazec sasawa fome muzac sâke basazac .
46012018	Anutu e ine mana tarahuc sahacte kiŋaŋ qaqa gie fuŋne fuŋne mujarewec .
46012019	Sahacte kiŋaŋ qaqa fuŋne-jeŋic mocjaha efâreme muzac sahac e sâqorerâ arictac ezac .
46012020	Ʒi ine kiŋaŋ qaqazi bocjaha â sahaczi mocjaha .
46012021	Eme šâŋezi wemocko me âzâcneocmu , “ No go tâmiric sâcne jupemu . ” Me qizeczi wemocko kike jasaocmu , “ No ŋohe tâmiric sâcne jupemu . ”
46012022	Aricne , sahac-nâŋecte tofafâc dodocne jaŋe tâmiric hâcne sâcne mi juzo .
46012023	Á sahac-nâŋecte tofafâc wawahane jaŋe hâcne hone jauŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ , â miminehec jaŋe foŋjopapene biaŋne hawari eeŋgopieŋ .
46012024	Hawari biaŋ jaŋe ine tâtâc foeŋgopieŋ . Anutu e sahac bâfuahuc tofafâcne gâcne wahakicne jaŋe gie fekicne mujarewec .
46012025	I sahac-nâŋecte tofafâc fâfâuc mi ehuc kiŋaŋ qaqac sâckoa eniŋte iŋuc hâcne ewec .
46012026	Irec tofane moczi šâic maname gâcne jaŋe mâmâc mana-fâreniŋmu , me moczi šeri eme gâcne mâmâc šeri efâreniŋmu .
46012027	Ŋoŋe mâmâc sâko qâturerâ Kristore sahac eŋgopieŋ â buc buc sahac-ticnere kiŋaŋ qaqafâc eŋgopieŋ .
46012028	Anutu e kikefuŋfâc-ticne nâŋâcnao ŋic šiŋuc râec-jopawec : Qanaŋ aposolo , izi porofete , izi qaqazu , erâ ŋic mâsi bapare tâpirihec â ŋic huc šâic bâbâpiaŋ irec tâpirihec , erâ jauŋ bapa , erâ soŋaŋ , erâ dâŋ marac furuo mumu , iŋuc hâcne râec-jopawec .
46012029	Nâŋâc aposolo sasawa râec-nâpowec me ? Me porofete me qaqazu sasawa râec-nâpowec me ? Me mâsi bapare tâpiri
46012030	me huc šâic bâbâpiaŋ irec tâpiri fonâre-fârekac me ? Me dâŋ marac furuo mumu me ŋic dâŋjeŋicko bac bâtikic eene jufâreŋgopeneŋ me ?
46012031	Ŋoŋe mitire kadahe fekicne bâfuaniŋte šoɋac enšepieŋ . Eme noni irec hata biaŋne jâmbâŋ ši ŋowatupe honeniŋ .
46013001	No ŋicmaracko me aŋelo maracko miti muzapo , ehuc maŋjauŋ tâmiric juzapo , ine qeŋ goŋgoŋ iŋucne erâ dâŋ fânâŋ sawa ezapo .
46013002	Me no porofete juhuc dâŋ soŋne mana-fârezapo â mitire šuhucne mana utucke-fârezapo â tiki mupe rârieocte irec sâc mamanasiŋ fonarezac , ehuc maŋjauŋ tâmiric juzapo , ine ŋic jawane ezapo .
46013003	Me wiac-nane sasawa hapetac bâmec bajarezapo â sahac-nane qikiŋnepe šocte nânâ ezac , ehuc maŋjauŋ tâmiricko ezapo , ine racne efârezac .
46013004	Maŋjauŋheczi wama ruaine juocmu , maŋjauŋheczi iiŋguuŋ mi eocmu , maŋjauŋheczi penaroŋ mi eocmu , e jahacnere maname fefene mi eocmu
46013005	e šaubac tâmiric , iiriac tâmiric , aaric tâmiric , kiŋ babaju tâmiric juocmu ”
46013006	sâqocnezi haŋ bame busâqoc manaocmu , â mitizi haŋ bame bubiaŋ manaocmu ”
46013007	maŋjauŋhec e dede ââsic-ticne ɋârâŋne , mamanasiŋ-ticne ɋârâŋne , maŋzi woworic-ticne ɋârâŋne , maŋuruc-ticne ɋârâŋne .
46013008	Maŋjauŋ i tatarane tâmiric . Findaŋdâŋ mumu i tataranehec , erâ dâŋ marac furuo mumu i wâc tataranehec , â fuŋne mamana i wâc tataranehec .
46013009	I šiŋucte : Fuŋne mamana-nâŋec i faisuc â findaŋdâŋ mumu-nâŋec i faisuc jaha wâc .
46013010	Juku ine wiac fofo dunduŋne fuame wiac faisuc eenezi omaezokac .
46013011	No ɋiene juhuc ɋiedâŋ mujupac â ɋiemaŋhec jujupac â ɋie mamana mana jupac . Izi juku ŋic erâ ɋie wiac hetarapo .
46013012	Dameŋ šiŋuczia wiac honeeŋgopeneŋ i turuŋzi hawari bâtikie-nâreme sisifucne honeeŋgopeneŋ irec sâc , juku ine fârine šâŋeo hehec erâ hone mana tarac ezokopac , i Wofuŋzi no hone mana tarac enarewec irec sâc .
46013013	Eme fofo sanaŋ foniŋmu ine mamanasiŋ , woworic â maŋjauŋ , jaŋe jahec â moczi . Maŋjauŋzi ine micne ekac .
46014001	Ŋoŋe maŋjauŋhec juniŋte ɋicwânšâŋ enšepieŋ . Erâ miti kadahe gâcne roniŋte irec wâc šoɋac enšepieŋ , ehuc Anuture micdâŋ mumufuare manapie fefene ezejec .
46014002	Moc e dâŋ marac furuo muekac e ŋic mi jazahuc Anutu âzâcneekac . E Mârozi ecneme dâŋ marac furuo mume ŋic jaŋe kâuc baeŋgopieŋ .
46014003	Á Anuture micdâŋ mufuaekaczi ine ŋic faŋ qajareekac â âkesiŋ-jopaekac â buuruc qajareekac .
46014004	Marac furuo dâŋ muekaczi e jahacne maŋ âkesiŋkeekac , â Anuture micdâŋ mufuaekaczi ine kikefuŋ guru âkesiŋ-jopaekac .
46014005	Ŋoŋe dâŋ marac furuo mufârepie manape sâckeocmu , Anuture micdâŋ mufuapie ine manape sâcke-hâmoocmu . Anuture micdâŋ mufuaekac ŋic e marac furuo dâŋ mumuŋic ere sâc sirickekac . Mocjaha , marac furuo dâŋ muku kikefuŋ guru bâtikie-jareme manarâ fârine bajupie ine sâcjeŋic mocjaha eocmu .
46014006	Âgofâc , no ŋoŋerao fârâ marac furuo dâŋ ŋazape wemocko âkesiŋ-ŋopaocmu ? No muraruŋ dâŋ me miti hukicne me findaŋdâŋ me mu qaqazuc dâŋ muratie-ŋarepe ine sâcne maŋfâri-ŋeŋic eocmu .
46014007	Wiac omane , woŋgâŋ mimi ŋokac wiac , i qapie dâŋ hawarine tâtâc mi fuame wemocko šâŋitazo ?
46014008	Me qeŋ kosa qapie dâŋ eme manarâ wemocko “ wiac mocte kuku qanâreŋgopieŋ ” muhuc ra bafic-jopaniŋmu ?
46014009	Á ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha marac furuo dâŋ foŋnehec mupie gâcnezi wemocko mananiŋmu , i dâŋŋeŋiczi qahameŋkeocmu .
46014010	Mâreŋ sâc ŋic dâŋmarac fuŋne fuŋne forakac i mamanane sasawa .
46014011	Mâc noni dâŋmarac moc kâuc bapemuo dâŋ irec runezi nore maname mutucne eocmu , â noni ere iŋuc jaha manape mutucne eocmu .
46014012	Eme ŋoŋerao fuŋne ijaha fokac . Mârore tâpiri ŋoŋerao fuaocte mueŋgopieŋ i sâcne , erâ i hâcne mitizi kikefuŋ âkesiŋ-jopaocte šoɋac enšepieŋ
46014013	Irec marac furuo dâŋ muocmu e fuŋne mana-hâmorâ ŋic ŋokac bâtikie-jareocte Wofuŋ numucneme bafickezejec .
46014014	No marac furuo numupemu , ine maŋ qâqâtâc-nanezi sawa epemu , â mamana-nanezi mâc foocmu .
46014015	Eme irec weniŋuc ezo ? Kecšiŋuc ezo : No maŋ qâqâtâc-nanezi numume mamana-nanezi mana tararâ miczi mutaniŋkezejec .
46014016	Me go maŋ qâqâtâcgezi Wofuŋ muteŋketec ŋic omane moczi dâŋge kâuc bahuc wemocko baficgurâ “ Jâmbomac ” muocmu ?
46014017	Go mumuteŋ dâŋ fârinehec mucmu mecne , erâ âgogezi kâuc baha wemocko maŋne âkesiŋkeocmu ?
46014018	Anutu daŋge âzâcnekopac , marac furuo dâŋ mumu i no ŋoŋere sâc mâcne , sâc fekicne fonarekac .
46014019	Eme irec manape fârine eme muzac , tutumaŋko marac furuo dâŋ šoricne šora muzo murâ muzapo . Erâ no irec manape wahakac , â mitidâŋ jahec mac sawa mutaniŋkehuc ŋic ŋokac jaza qazuc ee , irec ine manape fekac .
46014020	Âgofâc , dâŋ mana wosâc eere mamana-ŋeŋiczi ɋie jaŋere sâc mi ezejec , sâqocnere i ɋiene jaŋere sâc enšepieŋ , â mana wosâcte ine maŋ mamana-ŋeŋiczi sokakicne jaŋere sâc ezejec .
46014021	Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko dâŋ moc šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Wofuŋ e mukac , ` No ŋic furune ejarepe jaŋe ŋicguru ši dâŋmarac furunao micdâŋ-nane jazapie i wâc sifu mi mananiŋmu . Ž ` à
46014022	Eme irec ŋifecne mupe : Marac furuo dâŋ mumu i fuŋne qaqa mâsi moc , erâ i opâ ruac jaŋere biŋe mi ekac , i qâpuc jaŋere biŋe , â Anuture micdâŋ mumufua ine qâpuc jaŋere biŋe mâcne , i opâ ruac jaŋere biŋe .
46014023	Irec kikefuŋ guru tumaŋne-fârehuc mâmâc sasawa marac furuo dâŋ muhapie ŋic omane me qâpuc moczi hefârâ honec-ŋoparâ muocmu : “ Maŋsifuc ejarekac . ”
46014024	Á Anuture micdâŋ mufuahuc ŋehapie ŋic qâpuc me omane moczi ŋoŋerao hefârâ miti i manaocmu , ine mâmâc sasawa maŋticnere fuŋne bataniŋkeniŋmu â mumu hehec ecneniŋmu .
46014025	Eme maŋticnao wiac hesoŋkeme foekac i fua taniŋkeme šâŋe maine mâreŋko hetutuckerâ Anutu muafeckehuc muocmu , Anutu e jâmbomac ŋoŋehec jukac .
46014026	Âgo bureŋ , irec weniŋuc ? Ŋoŋe tumaŋneniŋte murâ maŋ metariŋ mi fisieŋgopieŋ . Moc e miti gae bafisiekac , moc e mu qaqazuc dâŋ , moc e Anuture micdâŋ furune , moc e marac furu dâŋ , â moc e marac furu dâŋ irec fuŋne . Wiac i sasawa miti fua sawec eŋareocte enšepieŋ .
46014027	Marac furuo dâŋ muzo murâ boczi mâcne , jajahec me jahec â moc sawazi munšepieŋ . Erâ buc buc mupie sâc moczi fuŋne bâtikierâ ŋazazejec .
46014028	Bâbâtikie ŋic basaniŋmuo tutumaŋko marac furu dâŋ mi muzo . Moc e muzo murâ bucticne â Anuturao muzejec .
46014029	Anuture micdâŋ mumufua ine iŋuc jaha ŋic jajahec me jahec â moc munšepieŋ , eme gâcne mana wosâerâ ŋifecne munšepieŋ .
46014030	Moc e ŋehame Mârozi maŋticnao miti râeme muzo mume mârâc fuŋkejeczi behezejec .
46014031	Anuture micdâŋ mumufua i ezo murâ sâcne efârenšepieŋ , ehuc buc buc mupie gâcne sasawa jaŋe mitihec erâ maŋafec bâfuanšepieŋ .
46014032	Anuture micdâŋ mumufua ŋic mârofâc-jeŋic jaŋe porofete âgofâc-jeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋkenšepieŋ .
46014033	Anutu e hesi qâsifuc Anutu mâcne , e wama Anutu .
46014034	Kikefuŋ gâcnao mitire tumaŋnehuc ŋokac jaŋe dâŋemâc ŋeeŋgopieŋ , ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha enšepieŋ . Ŋokac jaŋe iŋuc ehuc wahamicne juniŋte i sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko mukicne wâc .
46014035	Wiac moc manazo ejareme ficjeŋicko ŋowefâc-jeŋic mu wioc ejarenšepieŋ . Ŋokac moczi kikefuŋ tutumaŋko dâŋ mume mimi qaqanehec eocmu .
46014036	Me Anuture dâŋzi ŋoŋeraonec fuawec ? Me ŋoŋe buc manambiŋ ?
46014037	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi e jahacnere maname porofete me ŋic Mârohec eocmu , e dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac i Wofuŋte mumupaŋ , iŋuc mana tarazejec .
46014038	Moc e dâŋ ši maname fârine mi eme e mana suazo .
46014039	Irec , âgofâc , šiŋuc mananiŋ : Ŋoŋe Anuture micdâŋ mumufua irec šoɋac enšepieŋ , â marac furuo dâŋ mumure aka wâc mi henšepieŋ .
46014040	Wiac sasawa epie pec sererec â tiŋbenoŋ fozejec .
46015001	Âgofâc-nane , Biŋebiaŋ ŋazape manambiŋ , erâ wâc bajueŋgopieŋ , irecteaŋ manasu-ŋarepe .
46015002	Qazu-ŋarepo irec sâckoa bajuŋgopieŋko sâcne bâpiaŋ-ŋopaocmu . Me bajuhapie biac sifucke-ŋare wiac moc ewec ?
46015003	Miti qizecne no narekicne ijaha ŋoŋe ŋarehuc kecšiŋuc muhuc fuŋke-ŋarepo : Kristo e miti papiao mucnekicne irec sâcko erâ sâqocne-nâŋecte okacne hâmowec .
46015004	Erâ miti papiao mucnekicne irec sâckoa šâŋeruŋko hurâ šoaŋ jahec â moc eha ɋârerâ faharewec .
46015005	Faharerâ qanaŋ Kefa fuacnewec , izi motecfâcne 12 fua-jarewec .
46015006	Izi mitiŋic šare-jeŋic 500 jâuruwec jaŋe tumaŋnehapie fua-jareme hone-fârembiŋ . Jaŋeraonec bocjahazi ɋâricne juŋgopieŋ , â gâcnezi hâmombiŋ .
46015007	Izi Jakobo fuacnewec , izi aposolo mâmâc sasawa fua-jarewec .
46015008	Ʒâhecko ine ombâŋtâc no wâc fua-narewec .
46015009	No aposolo waha qaqane jâmbâŋ , no Anuture kikefuŋ guru jopa sipiric ejarepore aposolo šâŋe munarepie mi sâckeekac .
46015010	No aposolo epo i Anutu aki anonoc-ticnere erâ epo . Erâ aki anonoc-ticnezi norao racne mi ewec . No gie bapo i gâcne jaŋere sâc jâurukac , erâ no nahac wemo-nanezi bazapo , Anuture aki anonoc norao fowec izi bawec .
46015011	Eme no mecne jaŋe mecne miti iŋuc hâcne muromackeeŋgopeneŋ , eme ŋoŋe i hâcne manambiŋ bajuŋgopieŋ .
46015012	Kristo e hâmockonec ɋârerâ faharewec , miti iŋuc muhuc ŋazapene wemocte ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi hâmockonec fafahare mi fokac mueŋgopieŋ ?
46015013	Hâmockonec fafahare-nâŋec i mickehuc Kristo fafahare-ticne mâmâc mickezo .
46015014	Kristo mi faharezacko ine miti mumu-nâŋec fârimâc ezac â mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic iŋuc jaha fârimâc ezac .
46015015	Erâ i sawa mâcne . Nâŋe Anuture mumbeŋ , e Kristo hâmockonec bafaharewec . Eme hâmockonec fafahare mi fozacko Anutuzi wemocko Kristo bafaharezac . Irec dâŋ mumbeŋ i Anutu micko itic ecnehuc burecŋicfâc-ticne eŋgopeneŋ ezac .
46015016	Ŋic hâmockonec mi fahareniŋmu , iŋuc murâ Kristore iŋuc jaha hâmockonec mi faharewec muzo .
46015017	Kristo e hâmockonec mi faharezacko ine mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic racne ezac â kiŋŋeŋic foŋarezac ,
46015018	â Kristo manasiŋkehuc hâmombiŋzi sipirickembiŋ ezac .
46015019	Nâŋâc mâreŋko šira sawa Kristore mamanac maŋgâŋ junšapeŋko , ine mamakucne fuŋmoc ehuc gâcne siric-jopa-fârenšapeŋ .
46015020	Erâ iŋuc mâcne , Kristo e jâmbomac hâmockonec ɋârerâ ŋic hâmokicne jaŋere micne barâ faharewec jukac .
46015021	Ʒiŋucte hâcne : Ŋiczi hâmoc fuŋke-nârewec iŋuc jaha ŋiczi hâmockonec fafahare fuŋke-nârewec .
46015022	Adamhec šušuhuc-nâŋec fokacte hâmo-fâreeŋgopeneŋ , iŋuc jaha Kristohec šušuhuc-nâŋec fokacte fahare-fârenšoŋgopeneŋ .
46015023	Erâ birine mukicne sâc faharezo : Micne bapazi Kristo , izi fifisi-ticnao Kristore bufuŋfâc ,
46015024	izi dameŋ taraocmu ” Kristo e fekicne â tâpirihec â šoɋac sasanaŋhec bawahac-jopame munaŋke-fârehapie Wofuŋ gie-ticne i Anutu Mamac-ticne bârisiecneme dameŋ taraocmu hâcne .
46015025	Ʒi ine Wofuŋ gie-ticne bahuc juocmu , juku râsifâc-ticne ro waha âte ejare-fârerâ gie-ticne bataraocmu .
46015026	Râsi sâko mimic qa imac ecneocmu šâŋene hâmoc .
46015027	Anutuzi ŋic â wiac sasawa Kristore wahamicnao râec-nâpo-fârewec hâcne . Erâ dâŋ šiŋuc fokac , “ Ŋic â wiac sasawa bawahac-joparâ ere wahamicnao guruc-jopa-fârewec ” , dâŋ i manapene Anuture mâmâc mukicne mi ezejec . E hâcne Kristore wahamicnao guruc-nâpoweczi rurumaŋnao mi huocmu .
46015028	Mamac e ŋic â wiac sasawa Ŋokâ rurumaŋnao guruc-nâpo-fâreme Ŋokâ e Mamacte wahamicnao waharâ domaocmu . Eme Anutuzi qâhuc-nâpo-fârerâ juju isiricke-fâreocmu .
46015029	Ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi hâmokicne jaŋere erâ Miti Opâ ruaeŋgopieŋ , i hâmockonec fafahare mi fokacko wemocte iŋuc eeŋgopieŋ ?
46015030	Erâ wâc nâŋe ine wemocte šârâ hâriŋ faio gâbâmâc qâmâc jumbeŋzi jueŋgopeneŋ ?
46015031	Âgofâc-nane , Kristo Jesu Wofuŋ-nâŋeczi eri-nane râec-ŋopawec ŋoŋere maio mukopac : No šoaŋ gie bapa sâc hâmoczi bâmbeŋnuha juekopac .
46015032	No Efeso haeo qowi mimicne jaŋehec juju gie bapo i ŋicdâŋko siŋkehuc epoo wemo fârine mo fua-nareocmu ? Hâmockonec fafahare mi fokacko šiŋuc mupene sâckezac : “ Tomâcko moc hâmonšipeŋte miŋecgac jaha nânâ qowi ro nâc qânâc enaŋ . ”
46015033	Moczi moc ba qâsoric eŋarenšipiŋ ine ¡ Kosa jujune jaŋerao qohotaocmu e eebapa biaŋne sifuckecneocmu .
46015034	Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic ɋâreme pectâc juhuc sâqocne geŋkenšepieŋ . Ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi Anuture kâuc baŋgopieŋ , i manarâ mimieniŋte mukopac .
46015035	Gâcnezi šiŋuc mecne muniŋmu : Hâmokicne jaŋe weniŋuc erâ fahareniŋmu â sahac hawari-jeŋic weniŋucnehec fuaniŋmu ?
46015036	I dâŋ mutucne ” ŋoŋe wiac saraeŋgopieŋ i mâc mi wefuekac , mimiŋne šaŋkeha bâpâŋne wefuekac .
46015037	Á wiac saraeŋgopieŋ , i borâcne mi saraeŋgopieŋ , hândâŋne sawa saraeŋgopieŋ , jacgoŋ me wiac gâcnere hândâŋ , eme borâcne â rehacne šâhec fuaekac .
46015038	Eme Anutu e mana tararâ hawari mucnewec ijaha wefurâ fuaekac , hândâŋne sâc hawari fuŋne fuŋne fuaekac .
46015039	Sahacte fuŋne iŋuc jaha mocjaha mi fokac , ŋic nâŋâcne sahac i moc â bec qowi jaŋere sahac i moc â wipe jaŋere moc â opâ qowi jaŋere moc .
46015040	Sambâŋko wiac fâri ŋerakac â mâreŋko wiac fâri ŋerakac . Erâ sambâŋko ŋerakac i eri-ticne moc , â mâreŋko ŋerakac i eri-ticne moc .
46015041	Ʒoaŋ e tatamacne moc , mosa e tatamacne moc , bâpiŋ jaŋe tatamac-jeŋic moc , erâ bâpiŋ tatamac-jeŋic mocjaha mâcne , fuŋne fuŋne fokac .
46015042	Hâmockonec fafahare irec fuŋne ijaha fokac . Sarakicnezi sisirowene , fahareocmuzi mi sisirowene ”
46015043	sarakicnezi joŋtawekicne , fahareocmuzi erinehec ” sarakicnezi weweaŋne , fahareocmuzi tâpirinehec ”
46015044	sarakicnezi mâreŋ sahachec , fahareocmuzi sambâŋ sahachec . Mâreŋ sahac fokac , iŋuc jaha sambâŋ sahac fokac .
46015045	Dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ Ŋic mârâc fufua Adam e maŋ qâqâtâchec erâ ɋârewec . ” Ʒâhec Adam e ine Mârohec ehuc juju bâbâfua irec rune ewec .
46015046	Sambâŋte wiaczi mi bâniewec , mâreŋte wiaczi bânieha sambâŋte wiaczi šâhec ewec .
46015047	Mâreŋŋic e mâreŋzi bakicnere mâreŋkonec ŋic ewec â šâhecŋic e ine sambâŋkonec .
46015048	Mâreŋkonec ŋic juwec sâc ijaha mâreŋkonec ŋicfâc-ticne jueŋgopeneŋ , â sambâŋkonec juwec sâc ijaha sambâŋte biŋefâc-ticne nâŋâc junaŋmu .
46015049	Eme mâreŋkonec ere hawari rombeŋ , iŋuc jaha sambâŋkonec ere hawari ronaŋmu .
46015050	Âgofâc , dâŋ moc ši mupe mananiŋ : Mâreŋ sahac-nâŋeczi Anuture uucmaŋ sâcne mi rauckeocmu , â wiac gârecke šaŋ eenezi wiac fofo sanaŋ mi wâc rauckeocmu .
46015051	Manaŋgopieŋ , ši dâŋ soŋne moc mufua-ŋarepe : Nâŋâc mi hâmo-fârenaŋmu , hetikierâ hawari moc ee ine šeŋgoma efârenaŋmu .
46015052	Qeŋ mimic dâŋeme ututuŋ , ɋeŋfâfâc jaha iŋuc hâcne enaŋmu . Qeŋ dâŋeme hâmokicnezi faharerâ gârecke šaŋ tâmiric juniŋmu , â ɋâricne junaŋmuzi wâc hetikierâ hawari moc enaŋmu .
46015053	Sahac ši gârecke šaŋ eenezi juju saric i ŋaqi iŋucne  heme huzejec , â hâmocte biŋe ekicnezi juju sanaŋ heme huzejec .
46015054	Eme gârecke šaŋ eenezi juju saric heme huocmu , â hâmocte biŋe ekicnezi juju sanaŋ heme huocmu , dameŋ ira dâŋ kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne i deŋkeocmu : “ Jujuzi hâmoc ɋâckewec . ”
46015055	“ Hâmoc go tâpirige weni ? Hâmoc go šârâge weni ? ”
46015056	Sâqocnezi hâmocte šârâ ekac , â sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ sâqocnezi tâpirinehec ekac .
46015057	Anutu e Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ecneme jujure tâpiri bâfua-nâreekacte muteŋkenšepeneŋ .
46015058	Irec âgofâc-mae , ŋoŋe sanaŋkerâ qiŋ herâ domanšepieŋ , ehuc Wofuŋ gie-ticnere dameŋ sâc henširiŋnehuc banšepieŋ . Wofuŋte erâ gie bapie fârimâc mi eocmu , iŋuc manahuc banšepieŋ .
46016001	Mitiŋic jaŋere moneŋ râezo murâ ine Galatia mâreŋkonec kikefuŋ guru jaza mutâc epo ijaha enšepieŋ .
46016002	Ŋoŋe moneŋ hotâckekicne irec sâc manahuc Sondane Sondane tucne bâtâc barâ buc buc râe guruc ehuc junšepieŋ , mâc juhapie fâ fisipe moneŋ qânusuckeniŋte âecke guruc enšipiŋte .
46016003	Ŋoŋerao fâpe ŋic mucjopaniŋmu jaŋe papia jarehuc sorec-jopape bubiaŋte wiac-ŋeŋic Jerusalem haeo baranšepieŋ .
46016004	Me moneŋ bocjaha eme nohec mâmâc ranšepeneŋ .
46016005	No Makedonia mâreŋ fotâcne-fârerâ ŋoŋerao fâpemu , Makedonia mâreŋko boc mi jupemu , i mâc fotâcnepemu .
46016006	Ŋoŋerao fârâ piticne jupemu , me jufehape hoemaŋ taraocmu mecne . Eme ŋoŋe hatare baficnupie ira me ira razepac .
46016007	No dameŋ šiŋuczia mâc fofotâc fâhuc honec-ŋopape mi sâckeocmu , irec Wofuŋzi manaha ŋoŋerao fârâ piticne jupemurâ mukopac .
46016008	No ši Efeso haeo juhape Mâro Hombaŋ maickeocmu .
46016009	Ʒira Wofuŋzi mitire hata bâšâweme gie sâko-nane fuakac . Erâ mitire kisâ bocjaha juŋgopieŋ wâc .
46016010	Timoteozi ŋoŋerao fâme âgo ecnepie hâwic sahac mi juzejec . E no Wofuŋte gie baekopac iŋuc jaha baekac .
46016011	Irec ere manapie wawahane mi ezejec . Erâ aimuŋ ecnerâ bârisiepie norao mocwâc warezejec ” no â opâ ruac gâcne woŋec-ticne juŋgopeneŋ .
46016012	Âgo-nâŋec Apolo e opâ ruac gâcne jaŋehec ŋoŋerao fâocte âzâcne sorec epe sâcne mi afeckekac ” e šiŋuczia mâcne , dameŋ mocte maname sâckeme ŋoŋerao fâocmu .
46016013	Ŋoŋe rucjaric-ŋeŋic bahuc mamanasiŋko qiŋ henšepieŋ , ehuc hâbi-ŋeŋic rorâ sanaŋkenšepieŋ .
46016014	Erâ wiac sasawa maŋjauŋhec enšepieŋ .
46016015	Erâ âgofâc-nane , dâŋ moc ŋazape mananiŋ : Ŋoŋe Stefana â wiacfâc-ticne jaŋere manaeŋgopieŋ , jaŋe Akaia mâreŋko micne barâ miti manambiŋ , erâ mitiŋic ŋoŋerao kiŋaŋ qaqa gie baeŋgopieŋ .
46016016	Irec ŋoŋe jaŋe mecne â gâcne miti gie bahuc šâic manaeŋgopieŋ honec-jopapie micnefâc-ŋeŋic enšepieŋ .
46016017	Stefana â Fotunato â Akaiko jaŋe norao fisipie bunane biaŋkewec . Jaŋe ŋoŋere âkehoc dâŋjauŋ enarembiŋ .
46016018	Ehuc no â ŋoŋe mâmâc maŋuruc qanârembiŋ . Ŋoŋe ŋic iŋucne jaŋere manapie biaŋkezejec .
46016019	Asia mâreŋ masunao kikefuŋ guru jaŋe ŋoŋere mamanac juŋgopieŋ . Aqila â Prisika â ficjekicko mitire tumaŋneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe Wofuŋte erâ mu šeri boc eŋareeŋgopieŋ .
46016020	Opâ ruac mâmâc sasawa mu šeri eŋare-fâreŋgopieŋ . Ŋoŋe ŋaŋac mitio meo babac enšepieŋ .
46016021	Ʒi Paulo no nahac mu šeri eŋarehuc šâŋe qâreŋ-nane râekopac .
46016022	Moc e Wofuŋte takickeme hârâcte biŋe ezejec . Wofuŋ-nâŋec go warezemec .
46016023	Wofuŋ Jesure aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec .
46016024	Maŋjauŋ-nanezi Kristo Jesure erâ ŋoŋerao fofârekac .
47001001	Anuture micdâŋte Jesu Kristore aposolo epo Paulo no hâcne , erâ qomâ-nâŋec Timoteo nâhe Korinti haeonec Anuture kikefuŋ â Akaia mâreŋko mitiŋic juraŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe papia ši qâreŋke-ŋarehuc šiŋuc mukoperec :
47001002	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
47001003	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Mamac â Anutu muteŋkenšepeneŋ . E buuruc Mamac â bâbâmiriŋ rune juekac .
47001004	Ehuc šârâ hâriŋ fuŋne fuŋne enâreme bâmiriŋ-nâpoekac . Eme Anutuzi bâmiriŋ-nâpoekac , bâbâmiriŋ izia nâŋe iŋuc jaha âgo gâcne šârâ hâriŋ fuŋne fuŋne maŋnao juhapie sâcne bâmiriŋ-jopanaŋmu .
47001005	Kristo e šâic manawec irec tofane nâŋerao ɋârâŋne fuaekac , iŋuc jaha bâbâmiriŋ-ticne ɋârâŋnea bâfua-nâreekac .
47001006	Nâŋerao fific guguriŋ fuaekac , i ŋoŋerao bumâteŋ â bâbâpiaŋ fuaocte fua-nâreekac , â bâbâmiriŋ fua-nâreekac i wâc ŋoŋere erâ fua-nâreekac , ine bâbâmiriŋ izi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ dopec-ŋopahame fific guguriŋ nâŋerao fuaekac ijaha ŋoŋerao fuame irec šâic maŋuruc jaha mananiŋte .
47001007	Eme nâŋe ŋoŋere manabâc mi ehuc šiŋuc manapaŋkeŋgopeneŋ : Ʒârâ hâriŋte kâdoc rohuc bâbâmiriŋte kâdoc mâmâc roeŋgopieŋ .
47001008	Nâŋe Asia mâreŋko šârâ hâriŋ faio juwefumbeŋ irec kâuc banšipiŋte mupe mananiŋ : Ira wiac hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ fai-nâŋecko ferâ kimâc-nâpome juju-nâŋecte mâretec mana maŋbahac embeŋ .
47001009	Eme ši hâmocte biŋe eŋgopeneŋ muhuc maŋnâŋec ŋeŋgoroŋkewec . Erâ i mâc mi fua-nârewec , nâŋe nâŋâcne tâpirire manapene waha qaqane eha Anutu hâmoc qâŋɋâŋ bâɋâreekac e mocjaha manasiŋkenaŋte wiac i fua-nârewec .
47001010	Eme eki hâcne hâmockonec batarac-nâpowec . Erâ e batarac-nâpoweczi juku wâc batarac-nâpozokac , dâŋ iŋuc mana šakiehuc erao siŋkeeŋgopeneŋ .
47001011	Eme ŋoŋe nunumuzi bafic-nâpopie Anutu e buafec-ticnere erâ ŋezic-nâpome micne micne musereckerâ nâŋere erâ daŋge mumuteŋ ecnepie sâckezejec .
47001012	Nâŋe nâŋâcnere piticne mana biaŋkeeŋgopeneŋ ine kecšiŋucte : Maŋfâsâc â mitio maŋtaniŋ jupene maŋnâŋeczi wiac mocte tutuc mi qanâreekac . Nâŋe miti tâmiric jaŋere maio iŋuc hâcne juhuc miti mamana ŋoŋere maio wâc jujâmbâŋkeeŋgopeneŋ . I mâreŋko maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ fokac ira siŋkehuc mâcne , Anuture uruc jauŋko siŋkehuc eeŋgopeneŋ .
47001013	Nâŋe dâŋ hetac herirec ehuc mâcne , dâŋ fârine sasawa qâreŋke-ŋarepene wose manac eeŋgopieŋ . No manakopac , ŋoŋe šâhec mana tara-jâmbâŋkeniŋmu .
47001014	Ine hâcne gâcne ŋoŋe šiŋuc biac mana tarazo eŋgopieŋ : Nâŋe ŋoŋere boreŋfâc â ŋoŋe Wofuŋ Jesu dameŋ sâko-ticnao nâŋere boreŋfâc eniŋmu .
47001015	No dâŋ i hâcne maŋkehuc qanaŋ ŋoŋerao fârâ bubiaŋ qaŋarepemurâ mupo .
47001016	Erâ fâ honec-ŋoparâ Makedonia mâreŋko razo mupo . Ira ra jurâ mocwâc ŋoŋerao risiepe gâcnezi bâjâpecnupie Judaia mâreŋko ranaŋte manasupo .
47001017	Eme no iŋuc muhuc âkesac eŋarepo muŋgopieŋ me ? Me no ŋic miti tâmiric , irec dâŋ mupaŋkepe moc i fârine â moc i racne eekac ?
47001018	Anutu e jâmbomac rune jukacte dâŋ ŋazapene wemocko racne â fârine ataŋ eocmu ?
47001019	Anuture Ŋokâ Jesu Kristo ere fuŋne i no â Siliwano â Timoteo nâŋe ŋazapene gâcne fârine â gâcne racne iŋuc mi ewec . Aricne , ere fuŋne i fâri fideteŋ sasawa .
47001020	Anuture biŋedâŋ fuŋne fuŋne i erao hâcne deŋke-fârekac . Irec hâcne esoc-nâpome “ Jâmbomac ” muhuc Anutu mucne bacneeŋgopeneŋ .
47001021	Ŋoŋehec Kristorao râec-nâpo sanaŋkewec i Anutu eki hâcne .
47001022	Erâ ekizia wâc ma qâreŋ banârehuc šâšâfic-ticne Mâro maŋnâŋecko râeme huwec .
47001023	No Korinti haeo fârâ imac-ŋopazipore mi fâpo . Dâŋ i Anutuzi manaha jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mukopac .
47001024	Erâ nâŋe mitio ŋicbomboŋ eŋarenaŋte mi muŋgopeneŋ , mâc ŋoŋerao bubiaŋ fuaocte babaficko gie baeŋgopeneŋ . Ŋoŋe mamanasiŋko qiŋ herâ domaŋgopieŋ i manakopac .
47002001	No ŋoŋerao fârâ busâqoc mocwâc bâfua-ŋarezipore manabâc erâ jupo .
47002002	Noni busâqoc eŋarehape weni jaŋe bubiaŋ bâfua-nareniŋmu ? Busâqoc ecnekicnezi wemocko iŋuc eocmu ?
47002003	Eme no dâŋ i hâcne šiŋucte qâreŋke-ŋarepo : No fâpe ŋoŋe bubiaŋ bâbâfua-narezi busâqoc bâfua-narenšipiŋ . No nâŋâcnere šiŋuc hâcne manapaŋkepo : Nore bubiaŋzi mâmâc sâko-nâŋec ekac .
47002004	No bunane gufeme ŋoŋere šâic wemo afecne manahuc kifaio papia qâreŋke-ŋarepo , i bu ririke eŋarepemurâ mâcne , maŋnane ŋoŋerea sanaŋne domakac , irec fuŋne ŋowatupemurâ epo .
47002005	Ŋic busâqoc bâfua-nârewec , eki no sawa mâcne , ŋoŋe gâcne mâmâc bâfua-ŋarewec , weniŋuc musokahuc “ mâmâc sâko bâfua-ŋarewec ” mupemu .
47002006	Ŋoŋe bocjahazi bâtiŋnehuc wiac ecnembiŋ , i manape tarakac .
47002007	Ʒi ine busâqocko juku sipirickezacte kiŋticne behehuc mu bâmiriŋ ecnenšepieŋ .
47002008	Irec hâcne harierâ âgo jauŋ ecneniŋte mukopac .
47002009	No bâbâtiŋte mârâc qâreŋke-ŋarepo , i dâŋnane sasawa reŋkepie fuŋne taniŋkeocte esâic-ŋopapo .
47002010	Ŋoŋe ŋic mocte kiŋ behepie no iŋuc jaha behepemu . Kiŋ behekopac ( bahac bâfuawec i norao moc qacnewecko behekopac ) ine ŋoŋere manasuhuc Kristore micte ekopac .
47002011	I Sataŋzi eatuc-nâpozacte iŋuc eŋgopeneŋ . E wiac enâreocte manasuekac , irec kâuc mi baŋgopieŋ .
47002012	No Troa haeo fisihape Kristore Biŋebiaŋ mupemurâ irec hatane Wofuŋzi bâšâwe-narewec .
47002013	Eme qomâ-nane Tito ( e ŋoŋeraonec biac mi risiewecte ) basahuc maŋhâhâŋ enareme ŋicbureŋ mâzoc-joparâ Makedonia mâreŋko warepo .
47002014	Opoŋ , Anutu e Kristore gieŋicfâc-ticne nâŋe saoreŋ qahuc bataniŋ-nâpoekac , ehuc enâreme miti-ticnere âsu aŋac biaŋ bâiŋnepene ŋezurâ mâreŋ sâc raekac , irec mumuteŋ sâko ecnezo .
47002015	Nâŋe Kristore âsu mumundoŋ eŋgopeneŋzi Anutu bâiŋnecnepene ŋic jujure biŋe â sisipiricte biŋe mâmâc jopaekac .
47002016	Sisipiricte biŋe jaŋe fârepie hurâ hâmoc âsu erâ jopame hâmoeŋgopieŋ , â jujure biŋe jaŋe fârepie hurâ juju âsu erâ âke ɋârec-jopame jueŋgopieŋ . Gie iŋucne mozi bame sâckeocmu ?
47002017	Nâŋe ŋic gâcnezi eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc mi eeŋgopeneŋ . Ŋic gâcne bocjahazi Anuture dâŋte manapie âbârâ gie-jeŋic eekac . Nâŋe ine maŋtaniŋ juhuc Anuture micte â Anuture maio Kristorao qohotahuc miti mueŋgopeneŋ .
47003001	Nâŋe ŋoŋe bâmiriŋ-ŋopanaŋte dâŋ iŋucne mocwâc fuŋkeŋgopeneŋ me ? Me ŋic tucnezi eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc erâ ŋoŋerao fisirâ bâbâmiriŋ papia moc ŋowatueŋgopeneŋ ? Me ŋoŋe moc qâreŋkerâ nâreeŋgopieeŋ ?
47003002	Iŋuc aricne , papia-nâŋec i ŋoŋe hâcne . Erâ papia I maŋŋeŋicko qâreŋkekicne , ŋic mâmâc sasawa hone wosec eene .
47003003	Nâŋe ŋoŋerao gie bapene Kristore papia embiŋ , irec fuŋne tâtâc fokac . Erâ papia i tiŋtezi mi qâreŋkekicne , i Anutu jujune ere Mârozi qâreŋkewec , tafe omanao mâcne , ŋicmaŋ tafeo qâreŋkewec .
47003004	Qacfiric dâŋ iŋucne ine Kristore erâ Anutu manasiŋkepene fonârekac .
47003005	Gie fârine moc nâŋe nâŋâcnaonec fuaekac iŋuc mu manasuc enaŋte ropaŋ mi fonârekac , wiac epene bibiaŋkene i Anuturaonec sasawa .
47003006	Anutu eki hâcne bašawiec-nâpome šâšâfic ɋâricnere gie baeŋgopeneŋ . I dâŋqâreŋte giene mâcne , i Mârore gie . Dâŋqâreŋzi hâcne sisipiric bâfua-nâreekac , â Mârozi ine juju bâfua-nâreekac .
47003007	Miti gie raŋɋane , sisipiricte biŋe mumu hâcne , i qorac tapao qâreŋkekicne , erâ gie i sifu tatamac tâmiric mi fowec . Irec hâcne Mosere šâŋe maio tatamac hâhâwicne fome Israe ŋic jaŋe wemocko ira firâ honenšapiŋ . Erâ tatamac i fofone mâcne .
47003008	Miti gie raŋɋanere tatamac iŋuc hâcne fowec . Ehame wemocko miti gie ɋâricne , Mârore biŋe mumu , i tatamac tâmiric foocmu ?
47003009	Sisipiricte biŋe mumu irec giezi tatamac wawahanehec , â kiŋfâsâc eere biŋe mumu irec giezi tatamac fekicne sâkohec .
47003010	Gie raŋɋanere tatamac i gie ɋâricnere tatamac sâkozi sâockeme weaŋkeekac .
47003011	Wiac fotâmireweczi mârâc tatamacnehec fuawec , â wiac forašihuc jujune irec tatamaczi ine fekicne sâko .
47003012	Mamanac-nâŋec iŋuc fokacte gie maŋafec jaha baeŋgopeneŋ ,
47003013	ehuc Mose mi sâckeeŋgopeneŋ . E Israe ŋic jaŋe tatamac rârâriene i fotâmirehame honenšipiŋte šâŋe maine foŋkewec .
47003014	Eme maŋjeŋic sanaŋkewecte miti raŋɋanezi wâc foŋnehec eweczi eekac . Irec wose manac ehuc mi mana taraeŋgopieŋ . Erâ foŋ i mâc mi raruŋkeocmu , Kristo e mocjahazi bararuŋkeocmu .
47003015	Jaŋe dameŋ šiŋuczia Mosere dâŋqâreŋ woseeŋgopieŋ sâc maŋjeŋic foŋnehec eekac .
47003016	Jaŋe maŋjeŋic bârisierâ Wofuŋ maickepie izia foŋ i firue-jareocmu .
47003017	Wofuŋ e Mâro rune , eme Wofuŋte Mârozi juekacko wiac omaraŋ foekac .
47003018	Nâŋâc ine šâŋe mai-nâŋec foŋ tâmiric fokacte Wofuŋte tatamaczi âke tamaec-nâpome bâtikiepene wefuekac , ehuc Wofuŋte hawari sâc erâ tatamacheczi tatamachec eeŋgopeneŋ . I Wofuŋ Mâro ere mâsi .
47004001	Wofuŋ e buafec-ticnere gie iŋucne munârewecte mi pârâweeŋgopeneŋ .
47004002	Ehuc bahac , mimi fuazacte soŋsoŋko eene , i râpecke-fârembeŋ Me sioc faio juhuc Anuture dâŋ bâbâsifucke i wâc mi eeŋgopeneŋ , aricne Nâŋe Anuture maio miti mutaniŋkehuc ŋic jaŋere maŋ bâmiriŋkepene fuŋne-nâŋec manaeŋgopieŋ .
47004003	Eme Biŋebiaŋ mueŋgopeneŋ izi foŋnehec moc eekacko ine sisipiricte biŋe jaŋerao sawa foŋnehec eekac .
47004004	Miti qiqikiŋ jaŋe hâcne mâreŋ širec ŋicbomboŋzi maŋjeŋic bâzickeme wemocko Biŋebiaŋte tatamaczi hume Kristo e Anuture sâc jâmbâŋ jukac muhuc Wofuŋ qâreŋ-ticne šâŋitaniŋmu ?
47004005	Nâŋe miti muhuc nâŋe nâŋâcne dâŋ mi ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ , Jesu Kristo eki Wofuŋ â nâŋe ine Jesure erâ kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ŋeŋic sawa juŋgopeneŋ , iŋuc ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ .
47004006	Anutu e mârâc jaha fuŋnao dapâc fohame hae mâreŋ fureocte mume furewec , ekizia hâcne mume maŋnâŋecko mitire tatamaczi uŋ heme Kristore šâŋe maio Anuture huriri qâreŋ fua tâcneha šâŋitambeŋ .
47004007	Tâpiri šâkâŋ i nâŋerao mâcne , Anuturao fokac , irec fuŋne taniŋkeocte boreŋ šeŋaŋ-ticne kuši mâreŋzi bakicne nâŋerao duckekicne .
47004008	Hume serereŋ faio juipiehuc sifu docke šaŋ mi eeŋgopeneŋ . Bebekâne juipiehuc sifu mi mana utuckeeŋgopeneŋ ,
47004009	fific guguriŋ faio juipiehuc sifu mamac babasa mi eeŋgopeneŋ , qa imac enâre-bipiehapie sifu hâmo sipiric mi eeŋgopeneŋ .
47004010	Iŋuc ehuc sahac-nâŋecko Jesu hâmoc-ticnere ma amecke jueŋgopeneŋ , i Jesu juju-ticnere ma iŋuc jaha sahac-nâŋecko fuaocte hâcne .
47004011	Ŋic jaŋe Jesure erâ dameŋ oombâŋko gâbâ sipiric-nâpohuc hâmocko râec-nâpoeŋgopieŋ , i Jesu juju-ticnere tâpirizi sahac hâhâmo-nâŋecko fua taniŋkeocte iŋuc fua-nâreekac .
47004012	Eme šiŋuc fokac : Nâŋerao hâmoczi gie baekac , â ŋoŋerao jujuzi gie baekac .
47004013	Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc fokac : “ No Wofuŋ manasiŋkeekopacte miti muekopac . ” Eme nâŋe dâŋqâreŋ irec sâcko Mârozi esoc-nâpoha Wofuŋ manasiŋkeeŋgopeneŋte miti mueŋgopeneŋ .
47004014	Ehuc šiŋuc manapaŋkeeŋgopeneŋ : Wofuŋ Jesu bâɋârewec eki nâŋe iŋuc jaha Jesuhec bâɋârec-nâporâ ŋoŋehec mâmâc erao râec-nâpoocmu .
47004015	Nâŋe wiac sasawa i ŋoŋere erâ kecšiŋuc muhuc eeŋgopeneŋ : Mitizi haŋ barahame ŋic bocjahazi manahuc Anutu šeri mumuteŋ sâko ecnepie Izi šuhuckeme šuhuc forahuc fozejec .
47004016	Nâŋe šiŋuc manahuc mi pârâweeŋgopeneŋ : Sahac-nâŋec bâmuzuckehame maŋnâŋec šoaŋne šoaŋne soka biaŋ eekac .
47004017	Mâreŋko šâic busâqoc-nâŋec mâmâŋne â tatarane izi eri aŋac biaŋ ŋemâc bâmâcne â fofo sanaŋ bâfua-nârehame guru dindiŋ fonârezokac .
47004018	Erâ wiac tâtâc fokac irapec mâcne , wiac soŋsoŋ fokac irapec firâ râqârepene i fua-nârezokac . Wiac hohonene izi sisirowene , wiac mi hohonene izi fofo sanaŋ .
47005001	Nâŋe šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Mâreŋte ficboze-nâŋec raruŋkeme Anutuzi sambâŋko ficsanaŋ moc bâfua-nâreocmu , fic i mezi mi bakicne , mâc qiŋ sanaŋ qaŋqaŋ qakicne .
47005002	Eme nâŋe irec hâcne sambâŋkonec fic i henâreme huocte aŋac-nâpome harac huacbuc ehuc jueŋgopeneŋ .
47005003	Maŋ qâqâtâc-nâŋeczi biuctac ezacte i hâcne rojupene sâckeocmu .
47005004	Sahac boze-nâŋecko junaŋmu sâc ŋeŋe rârâqâc enâreme hujâi ehuc jueŋgopeneŋ . Nâŋe ŋaqi-nâŋec raŋɋane hetaranaŋte mi enâreekac , i fohame fainao ɋâricne henareme huocte enâreekac . Ehuc hâmocte biŋe ekicne i jujuzi ɋâckeocte mueŋgopeneŋ .
47005005	Wiac biaŋ i fua-nâreocte bâmoc-nâpowec i Anutu eki hâcne , ehuc irec kifac Mâro hâcne râe-nârewec .
47005006	Nâŋe irec hâcne mana afeckehuc jueŋgopeneŋ . Ehuc šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : Mâreŋ sahaczi haefuŋ-nâŋec eha jueŋgopeneŋ , i Wofuŋ basahuc mâreŋ jabao jueŋgopeneŋ .
47005007	Dameŋ šiŋuczia maŋzi wiac manasiŋkehuc jujune sawa fokac , fârine hohone aricne .
47005008	Erâ sifu mana afeckeeŋgopeneŋ . Ehuc sahachec mâreŋ jabao juju i beherâ mame sâko hae-nâŋecko Wofuŋhec juju irec aŋac-nâpoekac .
47005009	Eme juju i mame sâko haeo me mâreŋ jabao junaŋmu ine kecšiŋuc muhuc ropaŋ eeŋgopeneŋ : Aimuŋ jupene Wofuŋzi honec-nâpome sâckezejec .
47005010	Ʒiŋuc hâcne manaŋgopeneŋ : Juku šeŋgoma Kristore dâŋ mumutara ŋeŋe fuŋnao fua tâcnepene , sahachec juhuc wiac hurekicne , biaŋne me sâqocne , irec tofa ru sâc bazu-nâreocmu .
47005011	Wofuŋ araŋ bacnehuc junaŋte mukicne i manahuc ŋic mu hemiriŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ . Iŋuc ehapene Anutuzi maŋnâŋec honeekac , â ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha maŋŋeŋiczi fuŋne-nâŋec ŋazame manaeŋgopieŋ .
47005012	Nâŋe iŋuc mupene manapie nâŋe harierâ bâbâmiriŋ dâŋ muŋgopeneŋ mi ezejec . Nâŋe mâc ŋaza qâmoc eŋgopeneŋ , eme ŋoŋe ŋic gâcne , maŋtac juhuc sahackopec wiacte sawa penaroŋ eeŋgopieŋ , jaŋe dâŋ i jazahuc bâsâoc-nâponšepieŋ .
47005013	Nâŋe maŋnâŋec ŋeŋgoroŋkeekacko ine Anutu gie-ticnere erâ ŋeŋgoroŋkeekac , me maŋnâŋec fâretiŋ foekacko ine ŋoŋe mitihec eniŋte iŋuc foekac .
47005014	Kristore maŋjauŋzi maŋnâŋec fenšoŋkehame juhuc šiŋuc mana sanaŋkeeŋgopeneŋ : Mocjahazi okac-nâŋec hâmowecte mâmâc sâko hâmombeŋ ekac .
47005015	Mâmâc sâko okac-nâŋec hâmowec ine kecšiŋucte : Juju i nâŋâc nâŋâcnere mâcne , okac-nâŋec hâmorâ faharewec ere erâ junšepeneŋ .
47005016	Irec ši miti dameŋko sahac hawari sawa hohonec erâ šâšâŋitac i sâcne mi enaŋmu . Erâ wâc Kristo iŋuc jaha mârâc sahac hawarine honehuc šâŋitambeŋ , irec sâc šiŋuczia mocwâc mi enaŋmu .
47005017	Irec ŋic moc Kristorao šuhuckeekac e fuŋmoc eekac . Ine wiac raŋɋane omaewec , ŋicbureŋ , wiac ɋâricne fuawec .
47005018	Wiac i Anuture mâsi sasawa . Eki hâcne Kristozi jahacnehec miriŋ bacnâpowec . Erâ nâŋâc miriŋ babac biŋedâŋ mupene haŋ baocte irec gie munârewec .
47005019	Ine hâcne Anutu e Kristoo juhuc mâreŋŋic jahacnehec miriŋ bacnâpowec , ehuc kiŋnâŋec behewec . Erâ miriŋ babac dâŋ ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko âkendâŋnewec domakac .
47005020	Irec nâŋe Kristore biŋe mumuzi Anuture mu baafec dâŋ ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ . Nâŋe Kristo âkehockehuc numu-ŋareeŋgopeneŋ : Anutuhec miriŋ babac enšepieŋ .
47005021	Sâqocnere kâuc bawec e Anutuzi nâŋâcnere erâ sâqocne bapa mucnewec , i nâŋâc Jesuhec qâfâsâehuc Anuture tiŋne jujufâc enaŋte iŋuc hâcne ewec .
47006001	Anuture babaficfâc nâŋe mu âkesiŋ eŋarehuc šiŋuc ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ : “ Anuture aki anonoc tahac-ŋopakicne i fârimâc mi ezejec . ”
47006002	Dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ No dameŋ biaŋko mana-garepo â bâbâpiaŋ dameŋko baficgupo . ” Manaŋgopieŋ , dameŋ biaŋ jâmbâŋ šine hâcne , â bâbâpiaŋ dameŋ iŋuc jaha šine hâcne .
47006003	Nâŋe ŋic jaŋe gie bapa-nâŋec surenšipiŋte gâŋ ŋezic mi ejareeŋgopeneŋ .
47006004	Nâŋe Anuture gieŋic jueŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne bataniŋkehuc wiac šiŋuc eraeŋgopeneŋ : Ʒâicmaŋko maŋuruc jueŋgopeneŋ , šârâ hâriŋ faio jueŋgopeneŋ , fific guguriŋ faio jueŋgopeneŋ , hâhâwic maŋko jueŋgopeneŋ ,
47006005	šika faio jueŋgopeneŋ , kâpâcwâru ficko ŋeeŋgopeneŋ , râsi ŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ , giere šâic manaeŋgopeneŋ , guŋɋâri jueŋgopeneŋ , nânâ tâmiricko jueŋgopeneŋ ,
47006006	bahac fâsâc jueŋgopeneŋ , mamana tarahec jueŋgopeneŋ , bumâteŋ jueŋgopeneŋ , âgo jauŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ , Tiri Mârohec jueŋgopeneŋ , maŋjauŋ fârihec jueŋgopeneŋ ,
47006007	dâŋ fâri qizecne mueŋgopeneŋ , Anuture tâpirio jueŋgopeneŋ , mitire sându marohec jueŋgopeneŋ ,
47006008	mumumbiaŋ â mimi qaqa ŋoŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ , mu bâsâoc â mufec muriŋ ŋoŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ , burecŋic munârehapie siocmâc jueŋgopeneŋ ,
47006009	fuŋne-nâŋec basahapie biŋe rarahec jueŋgopeneŋ , hâmozo eeŋgopeneŋzi sifu ɋâricne jueŋgopeneŋ , nâpo sipiric ekicnezi sifu mi omaeeŋgopeneŋ ,
47006010	busâqoc enârekicnezi sifu bubiaŋko jueŋgopeneŋ . hapetaczi sifu ŋic bocjaha bâmec bajareeŋgopeneŋ , wiac babasanezi sifu mâriri sâkohec jueŋgopeneŋ .
47006011	O Korinti ŋicbureŋ , maŋnâŋec ŋoŋerea kâcɋene domame micnâŋec afeckekac hâcne .
47006012	Maŋzi sanaŋnea šâfic-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ , ŋoŋere maŋjauŋ ine afecne mac fokac .
47006013	Eme no naru motecfâc-nane ŋoŋe ŋazape : Ŋoŋe okacne bazuhuc iŋuc jaha maŋŋeŋic nâŋere râepie kâcɋenea domazejec .
47006014	Ŋic qâpuc jaŋe jâcjeŋic reŋkepie ŋoŋe mi bafic-jopanšepieŋ . Tiŋne â hehesic jahe wemocko ââgo enicmu ? Me tatamac â dapâc jahe wemocko šâšâfic enicmu ?
47006015	Me Kristo â râsi qizec-ticne jahe wemocko maŋ mocjaha enicmu ? Me opâ ruac â qâpuc jaŋe wemocko qâfâsâeniŋmu ?
47006016	Me Anuture ufuŋ â nemuɋâŋ jahe wemocko šušuhuc enicmu ? Manaŋgopieŋ , Anutu jujunere ufuŋ i nâŋâc . Anutuzi šiŋuc hâcne muwec : “ No ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko ŋeŋe juju epemu , ehuc Anutu-jeŋic ehape jaŋe ŋicfâc-nane junšepieŋ .
47006017	Irec qâpuc behec-joparâ bâtâcko junšepieŋ , Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac . Erâ wiac mamakâcne ba bâuac mi enšepieŋ , eme noni hezu hewâneŋ eŋarepemu .
47006018	Erâ mamac eŋarehape naru motecfâc-nane erâ junšepieŋ . Wofuŋ bapa-fâre e dâŋ iŋuc mukac . ”
47007001	Âgo bureŋ , wiac iŋucnere biŋe qanârekicnere wiac mamakâcnezi maŋ sahac-nâŋec hegâpâreekac i šure ɋaɋackenšepeneŋ . Erâ Anutu araŋ bacnehuc maŋɋaɋac jaha junšepeneŋ .
47007002	Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic mi sakare-nârenšepieŋ . Nâŋe ŋoŋerao wiac hehesic mi embeŋ , me wiac-ŋeŋic ima mi qambeŋ , me wiac-ŋeŋic moc kâŋgâc mi rombeŋ .
47007003	No dâŋ i musâqorec-ŋopahuc mi mukopac . No miŋecne mac ŋazapac , maŋnâŋeczi šâfic-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ , i ŋoŋehec mâmâc hâmonaŋte me junaŋte .
47007004	Maŋnanezi ŋoŋerao siŋkeha wemo afecne muafec-ŋopakopac , no bunane boc bâmiriŋkekicne , šâic busâqocko šeri kâcɋene fua-narekac .
47007005	Makedonia mâreŋko ware fisirâ wemocko âke uruerâ junšapeŋ . Ʒira sahacte biŋe šika â maŋte biŋe hâhâwic , wiac izi fuarâ sisi hâhâŋ enâreha jumbeŋ .
47007006	Bebekâne bâmiriŋ-jopaekac Anutu eki hâcne ine nâŋere bâbâmiriŋte Tito ecneme risiewec .
47007007	Erâ risiewec irec sawa mâcne , ŋoŋe bubiaŋ dâŋ âzâcnembiŋ , i bafisime manarâ bunâŋec uruewec . Erâ no woricnuhuc jueŋgopieŋ â ki busâqochec jueŋgopieŋ â nore erâ gie-ŋeŋic dopeckehuc šoɋac eeŋgopieŋ , i nâzâme bubiaŋ fekicne manapo .
47007008	No mârâc papia moc qâreŋke-ŋarehuc maŋšâic bâfua-ŋarepo , irec bunane mi sâqorekac . Qâreŋkepo ira jâmbomac bunane sâqorewec . Ʒi ine manakopac , i dameŋ bembeŋne sawa maŋšâic bâfua-ŋarewec .
47007009	Eme ši bubiaŋ manakopac , ine bušâic manambiŋ irec mâcne , bušâiczi ŋoŋerao maŋ bâbârisie bâfuawec , irec bunane biaŋkekac . Anutu mamana-ticnere sâcko bušâic ɋaɋacne manambiŋte dâŋnâŋeczi mi bâsâqorec-ŋopawec .
47007010	Bušâic ɋaɋacne izi maŋ bâbârisie bâfuame ŋiczi biaŋkezo , eme bušâic iŋucne bâfuaocmuzi šâhec irec mi maname sâqoreocmu . Á bušâic gâpâcne , ŋic mamanare sâcko fuaekac , izi ine maŋmutuc bâfuame sipirickezo .
47007011	Honeniŋ me , bušâic ɋaɋacnezi ŋoŋerao fârine wemo afecne bâfuawec : Fâro , fuŋne babataniŋ , sâqocne bâbâsue , hâhâwic , mu hejâpec , šoɋac , bâbâtiŋ , wiac iŋuc hâcne bâfuawec . Eme sâqocnere hehesoŋ â ŋeŋezic ŋoŋerao mi fokac , irec fuŋne taniŋkewec .
47007012	Mârâc papia qâreŋke-ŋarepo , i ŋic sâqocne bawec ere erâ mâcne , me sâqocne bajarewec jaŋere erâ wâc mâcne , dâŋ ŋazapene Anuture maio micrereŋ-ŋeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeocte irec qâreŋke-ŋarepo . Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc hâcne ehuc bunâŋec bâmiriŋkembiŋ .
47007013	Erâ bunâŋec bâmiriŋkembiŋ sawa mâcne , ŋoŋe Tito bubiaŋ qacnepie risieme nâŋe wemo afecne mana biaŋ embeŋ .
47007014	No mârâc jaha muafec-ŋopahuc Tito âzâcnepo , dâŋ i burec mi ewec . Ŋoŋe dâŋ ŋazape fârinehec efârewec , iŋuc jaha Tito ŋoŋere mumumbiaŋ dâŋ âzâcnepo i wâc fârinehec jaha ewec .
47007015	Tito ŋoŋerao fâme araŋ bacnehuc micne reŋkembiŋ , e irec manasuhuc maŋne ŋoŋere boc ecneekac .
47007016	No ŋoŋere erâ maŋbahac tâmiric sâcne jupemu , irec bunane biaŋkekac .
47008001	Âgo bureŋ , Makedonia mâreŋkonec kikefuŋ jaŋerao Anuture jauŋ fuawec irec ŋazanaŋ .
47008002	Jaŋe šârâ hâriŋ sâkoo juhuc bahac qahameŋ erâ tac qararacne jueŋgopieŋ , ehame sifu mitire šeri fekicne fojareekacte bubiaŋ wiac ɋâfoŋne bâmockembiŋ .
47008003	No jaŋere mana-jâmbâŋkekopac , jaŋe jaŋacne maŋte afeckerâ tâpiri-jeŋicte sâc , erâ wâc sâc i jâuruhuc râembiŋ .
47008004	Nâŋe mi ejarehapene jaŋe jaŋac hota-nârehuc mitiŋic jaŋere bubiaŋ wiac bâfuarâ bafic-nâponiŋte mumbiŋ .
47008005	Erâ wiac afecne eniŋmu muhapene šiŋuc embiŋ : Qanaŋ maŋjeŋic Wofuŋ qikiŋnecnerâ nâŋe mâmâc Anuture erâ qikiŋne-nârembiŋ .
47008006	Jaŋe iŋuc embiŋte Titozi ŋoŋerao bubiaŋ gie barâ tofane râewec i bataraocte mucneŋgopeneŋ .
47008007	Eme mamanasiŋ â miti mumu â miti fuŋne mamana tara â giere šoɋac â maŋjauŋ eenare , wiac iŋucnere fârine bocjaha bâfuambiŋte bubiaŋ gie mukicne irec iŋuc jaha afeckenšepieŋ .
47008008	No hotâ-ŋarehuc mi mukopac , miti mamana gâcne jaŋerao aafec fuawec , eme ŋoŋere maŋjauŋ sâc weniŋucne fokac irec fuŋne taniŋkeocte mukopac .
47008009	Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo uruc jauŋ-ticnere manaeŋgopieŋ , e mâriri sâkoheczi ŋoŋere erâ hapetac ewec , i ŋoŋe hapetac-ticnere erâ mâririhec eniŋte iŋuc hâcne ewec .
47008010	Eme ši dâŋ mâc ŋazakopac i reŋkepie fârinehec ezejec . Ŋoŋe hâcne jara raŋɋanao biac moneŋ bâtureniŋte afeckerâ fuŋkembiŋ .
47008011	Eme i šuhuckerâ etarapie aafec-ŋeŋicte fârine , wiac foŋarekac sâc fuazejec .
47008012	Wiac buafecte rârâe irec mamana biaŋ fuaocmu , rârâe ine moc e focnekac irec sâc râezejec , mi focnekac irec sâc mâcne .
47008013	Bubiaŋte wiac rârâere mukicne i jaŋe sahac mâteŋ juhapie ŋoŋe šocne šâicne mananiŋte mâcne ,
47008014	ŋoŋere mafa mâririzi dameŋ šiŋuczia jaŋere roroc jâpeme wiac sâckoa fuaocte mukicne , eme juku dameŋ mocko jaŋere mâririzi ŋoŋere roroc jâpeme iŋuc jaha sâckoa fua-ŋarezejec .
47008015	Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Bocjaha nusembiŋzi mâririhec mi embiŋ , â afecne nusembiŋzi roroc mi embiŋ . ”
47008016	Anutu e Tito esockeme , maŋnâŋezi ŋoŋere erâ bâruŋkekac sâc ijaha erao fuakacte muteŋkenaŋ .
47008017	Nâŋe mucnepene manawec sawa mâcne , e jahac maŋticnere afecke-jâmbâŋkerâ fâzo ekac .
47008018	Opâ ruac âgo-nâŋec moc , kikefuŋ sasawa jaŋe Biŋebiaŋte gie bapa-ticnere mana biaŋ eeŋgopieŋ , e mâmâc sorepene fâkopirec .
47008019	Kikefuŋ jaŋe ŋic e hâcne bubiaŋ moneŋ rorore bafic-nâpoocte bâwosâembiŋ . Gie i Wofuŋ sâsehuc buafec-nâŋecte baŋgopeneŋ .
47008020	Mumusifuc fuazacte moneŋ sâko i šâŋe šereŋko sosoŋaŋ ehuc ro qâzuc eeŋgopeneŋ .
47008021	Nâŋe wiac epene Wofuŋzia maname biaŋkeocte mâcne , ŋiczi mâmâc manapie sâckeocte mueŋgopeneŋ .
47008022	Nâŋe jahehec âgo-nâŋec moc mâmâc sorec-jopapene fâŋgopieŋ , ŋic e dameŋ gâcnao esâicke honepene šoɋac-ticnere fuŋne taniŋkewec , ši ine ŋoŋere bubiaŋ manahuc šoɋac fekicne bâfuakac .
47008023	Ŋoŋe Titore manaeŋgopieŋ , e âgo babafic-nane , mâmâc gie bapa ŋicjahec-ŋeŋic jukoperec , â âgo jahec-nâŋec jahere wâc manaŋgopieŋ , jahe kikefuŋ jaŋe sorec-jofaŋgopieŋ , erâ jahe Kristore šuŋe gâpiŋ hâcne .
47008024	Nâŋe ŋoŋe muafec-ŋopaeŋgopeneŋ irec dâŋ i fârinehec eocte ŋic iŋucnezi fâpie âgo jauŋ ejarepie kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋe mananšepieŋ .
47009001	Mitiŋic ehâmo-jarehuc moneŋ jareniŋte i sâcne manaŋgopieŋ , irec wemocte boc qâreŋke-ŋarepemu .
47009002	Akaia opâ ruac ŋoŋe jara raŋɋanao biac afeckerâ moneŋ bâbâfua fuŋkembiŋ , irec binaŋ Makedonia ŋic bajarepe ŋic gâcne sâko jaŋe šoɋac-ŋeŋicte biŋe manarâ bujeŋic âeckewec .
