47009003	No muafec-ŋopapo i racne ezacte âgofâc-nane sorec-jopape fâpie mupo iŋuc hâcne erâ šawienšepieŋ .
47009004	No nahac šâhec Makedonia ŋic jaŋehec fâpe moneŋ rârâere bititiepie dâŋnane wawahane eme no â ŋoŋe mâmâc mimienšipeŋ .
47009005	Irec hâcne ŋic ejarepe bânierâ fâŋgopieŋ . Fâ fisipie bubiaŋ moneŋ râeniŋte nazambiŋ i qanaŋ râe bâmoc epie ŋezejec . Eme micneneŋte moneŋ mâcne , mitire bubiaŋte moneŋ ezejec .
47009006	Erâ ine šiŋuc mukopac : Moc e wiac afecne he sarac eocmu , e wiac afecnea nâ roroc eocmu , â moc e wiac ŋemâcne he sarac eocmu e wiac ŋemâcnea nâ roroc eocmu .
47009007	Irec šiŋuc efârezo : Moc e buafec-ticnere sâcko wiac-ticne qikiŋnezejec , jâiŋko me micneneŋte misac . Wiac buafec qikiŋneocmu , ŋic iŋucnere Anutuzi maname biaŋkeocmu .
47009008	Anutu e tâpiri runezi buafec-ticnere jambuŋ-ŋopame mâriri fua-ŋareme ŋaŋacne nâ bac eipiehuc bâmec gie fuŋne fuŋne baniŋte wiac mi basaniŋmu .
47009009	Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ E kada bahuc ŋic hapetac bâmec bajareekac , â buafec-ticne i tofamâc fohuc juocmu . ”
47009010	Ŋic ukicne bâfua-jareme he sarac eeŋgopieŋ â fârine bâfua-jareme nâ bac eeŋgopieŋ , Anutu e hâcne ŋoŋe wâc he sarac eniŋte ukicne bâfua-ŋarerâ jambuŋkeme buafec-ŋeŋicte fârine fua sawec eocmu .
47009011	Eme mâriri sâkohec erâ ŋic bâmec fuŋne fuŋne bajarepie jaŋe nâŋâcnere erâ Anutu daŋge mumuteŋ ecneniŋmu .
47009012	Ŋoŋe mitiŋic bubiaŋ wiac ejarepie izi roroc-jeŋic jâpeocmu sawa mâcne , izi daŋge mumuteŋ irec mâriri wâc bâfuame Anuturao qacneocmu .
47009013	Ŋoŋe Kristore Biŋebiaŋ mana rereŋ eeŋgopieŋ irec fuŋne bubiaŋ wiac-ŋeŋiczi bataniŋkeme Jerusalem haeonec mitiŋic â opâ ruac gâcne sasawa jaŋehec ââgo šušuhuc-ŋeŋic fuame Anutu mumbiaŋkeniŋmu .
47009014	Erâ ŋoŋerao Anutu miti-ticnere fârine fua sawec ekacte maŋzi šâfic-ŋopahuc ŋoŋere erâ Anutu numucneniŋmu .
47009015	Anutu buafec-ticne i wemocko sâcne mutaniŋkezo , irec mâc wareckehuc daŋge âzâcnenaŋ .
47010001	Ʒi Paulo noni Kristo bumâteŋ-ticnere â uruc-ticnere erâ ŋazape mananiŋ . Gâcnezi nore mueŋgopieŋ , “ Ʒira ware juhuc miriŋdâŋ enâreekac , â ocna ra juhuc momori dâŋ enâreekac . ”
47010002	Âgofâc , ŋoŋerao fâ juhuc momori dâŋ ŋazapemurâ irec mi qafeŋnunšepieŋ . Gâcnezi “ sahacte wiacko utuckerâ juekac ” , nore iŋuc mueŋgopieŋ , ŋic i jaŋe momori dâŋ jazapemurâ maŋnane afeckekac .
47010003	Wiac nâŋe sahachec juju i jâmbomac jueŋgopeneŋ , â momori juju ine sahacte hata fokac iŋucko mi jueŋgopeneŋ .
47010004	Sându maro bajuhuc juju gie baeŋgopeneŋ , i mâreŋkonec mâcne , i Anuture tâpiri sanaŋhec . Eme izi râsire sac bazueŋgopeneŋ , â qac momori-ticne qapene wahaekac ,
47010005	â hârâc huec Anuture dâŋ sirickeekac i qa imac eeŋgopeneŋ , erâ Kristore micrereŋ sawa fuaocte mamana fuŋne fuŋne kâpâcwâru baeŋgopeneŋ .
47010006	Ŋoŋe micrereŋte afecke-fârehapie nâŋe ŋic gâcne jaŋe qaqatara-jeŋicte bâtiŋ-jopazore woŋec juŋgopeneŋ .
47010007	Wiac moc ši tâtâc fokac i honeniŋ : Ŋoŋe wemocte sahackopec wiac omanere manapie fârine eekac ? Ŋoŋeraonec ŋic moczi e jahacnere maname Kristore ŋic fârine eekacko šiŋuc manazejec : E buc Kristore ŋic mi juekac , nâŋe wâc Kristore ŋicfâc jaha jueŋgopeneŋ .
47010008	Erâ Wofuŋzi giere tâpiri râe-narewec , ŋoŋe âkesiŋ-ŋopapere , sipiric-ŋopapere mâcne , no irec erâ ropaŋdâŋ piticne murašihuc mupe boc mi sâqore-nareocmu .
47010009	Á papia qâreŋke-ŋareekopac irec manapie mu hâhâwic dâŋ mi ezejec .
47010010	Ʒiŋuc hâcne munareeŋgopieŋ : “ Papiao dâŋ bipinehec â tâpirinehec qâreŋkeekac , sahaczi maic-nâpoekac ine weweaŋne , â dâŋ mumu-ticne ine wawahane . ”
47010011	Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe šiŋuc mananšepieŋ : Nâŋe šoricko juhuc dâŋ qâreŋkeeŋgopeneŋ , dâŋ irec fârine ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko juhuc bâfuaeŋgopeneŋ .
47010012	Ŋic sahac fefe jueŋgopieŋ jaŋerao nâŋe iŋucnezi wemocko šuhuckerâ sâc babac enaŋmu . Ŋic i jaŋe hâcne gâcne nâŋere eebapa irec mi manasuhuc jaŋacnere sawa muhuc sahac fefe dâŋ kosa woseeŋgopieŋ .
47010013	Nâŋe ine Anutuzi giere sâc banârewec iŋuc bafâku ŋoŋerao fisimbeŋ , irec mac manasuhuc mumuafec dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ , â sâc tâmiricko kosa mumu ine mi eeŋgopeneŋ .
47010014	Nâŋe gie-nâŋecte sâc i mi musokaeŋgopeneŋ , gie rukec-nâŋec i jâmbomac ŋoŋerao fokac , nâŋe hâcne bâbâni ŋoŋerao fisirâ Kristore Biŋebiaŋ qanaŋ ŋazambeŋ .
47010015	Nâŋe ŋic gâcne jaŋere gieo kâŋgâc raši domahuc sahac fefe dâŋ kosa mumu i mi eeŋgopeneŋ . Mamanasiŋzi ŋoŋerao fua sawec eme gie rukec-nâŋec bâsokanaŋte ine jâmbomac maŋnâŋec domaha jueŋgopeneŋ .
47010016	Eme ŋic râpe-ŋeŋicko juŋgopieŋ jaŋerao Biŋebiaŋ muranaŋmu . Á ŋic mocte gie fârine rauckehuc pepec dâŋ mumu i mi eeŋgopeneŋ .
47010017	Moc e mumuteŋ dâŋ muzo murâ Wofuŋte erâ muzejec .
47010018	Moc e jahacne sahac mumbiaŋkeme e miti fârihec ekac mi mucnezo , Wofuŋzi mumbiaŋkeme miti fârihec ekac muzo .
47011001	Ŋoŋe manahapie mutucdâŋ piticne ŋazape . Sifu mac mananšepieŋ .
47011002	No ŋoŋere erâ qizec qaekopac , erâ qizec qaqa dâŋnane i Anuturaonec . Noni ŋoŋe Kristore biŋefâc erâ pectâc juniŋte ŋic mocjaha ehec bâturec-ŋopapo .
47011003	Ʒi ine homazi Ewa sioc ecnehuc bâdockewec iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe ŋic gâcnezi eatuc-ŋopapie maŋŋeŋic fâuckeme Kristo râŋgeŋ rocnenšipiŋte manabâc ekopac .
47011004	Ŋoŋerao ŋic moczi fisirâ Jesure fuŋne nâŋe ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ ijaha mâcne , hawarine moc ŋazaocmu , â Mâro nâŋeraonec rombiŋ i mâcne , furune moc ŋareocmu , â Biŋebiaŋ nâŋeraonec manambiŋ i mâcne , maracne moc ŋazaocmu , i ŋoŋe mi qatarahuc mâc manapie sâckeekac .
47011005	No nahacnere manape norao wiac i me i basahuc aposolo fekicne sâko jaŋere jujuwicnao jukopac mi eekac .
47011006	No miti muminširiŋkerâ mumu i mi mecne fonarekac , â mitire fuŋne mamana ine manaekopac , erâ irec fuŋne baratie-fârehuc mâmâc-ŋeŋic bataniŋke-ŋarepo .
47011007	Me nahac wahamicne juhuc ŋoŋe ikisiŋ-ŋopahuc Anuture Biŋebiaŋ katucmâc ŋazapo i sâqorewec me ?
47011008	Ŋoŋerao miti gie bapemurâ kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋe jâmbomac moneŋ mafa jowac ropo .
47011009	Ŋoŋerao ine wiac basac bahameŋ juhuc mubâre mi eŋarepo . No batac qatac juhape Makedonia mâreŋkonec âgofâc-nane fisirâ wiac nare gumec embiŋ . Á ŋoŋerao ine mâc juhape nore šâic mi manambiŋ â jufehuc wâc mi mananiŋte mukopac
47011010	Kristore dâŋfâri maŋnaneo foha mukopac : šeridâŋ inane Akaia mâreŋko moc mi bawaha-narezo .
47011011	Muŋgopieŋ , ŋoŋere mi enarehame iŋuc eekopac ? Iŋuc aricne , i Anutuzi manakac .
47011012	Wiac eekopac i ehuc jupemu , erâ i mâc mâcne , ŋic gâcne jaŋe Paulore sâcko juŋgopeneŋ muhuc maŋjeŋic bafenšipiŋte siŋ qatara-jareekopac
47011013	Ŋic iŋucnezi aposolo burecne â miti gie bapa siochec juhuc Kristore aposolofâc nâŋere sahac hawari sawa eeŋgopieŋ .
47011014	Erâ i wiac furune mi eeŋgopieŋ , Sataŋ e jahacne wâc aŋelo tatamachec jaŋere hawari tinac eekac ,
47011015	eme irec gie bapa ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋe iŋuc jaha tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa jaŋere hawari rojueŋgopieŋ .
47011016	Mupac i mocwâc mupe , nore manapie ŋic mutucne mi ezejec . Erâ sifu muzo murâ muniŋ , ehuc mana-narehapie sahac-nane piticne muteŋkepe
47011017	No ši dâŋ mupemu i Wofuŋte micsâcko mi mupemu , mâc mumuteŋ dâŋ fuŋkekicnere sifu mutuc erâ mupemu .
47011018	Ŋic gâcnezi sahackopec wiacte mumumbiaŋ dâŋ mueŋgopieŋte no iŋuc jaha epemu .
47011019	Oi , fuŋne mamana ŋoŋe , gâcnezi mutucdâŋ ŋazapie manapie sâckeekac hâcne .
47011020	Á kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-jeŋic bacŋopapie iŋuc jaha manapie sâckeekac , â ŋowac ro nâc eŋareniŋmu me eatuc-ŋopaniŋmu me ŋicbomboŋ eŋareniŋmu me imac-ŋopaniŋmu , i ŋoŋe manapie sâcke-fâreocmu hâcne .
47011021	Nâŋe gegec dodocnezi iŋuc sâko wemocko eŋarenšapeŋ , i mana sâqorehuc mukopac . Moc e wiac irec me irec penaroŋ eocmu , i no ezo murâ sâcne epemu . Dâŋ i mutucne , i mana-bipiehuc mukopac .
47011022	Jaŋacnere Judaŋic mueŋgopieŋ , no wâc ijaha . Jaŋacnere Israe ŋic mueŋgopieŋ , no wâc ijaha . Jaŋacnere Abrahamte ɋâric mueŋgopieŋ , no wâc ijaha .
47011023	Jaŋacnere Kristore gieŋic mueŋgopieŋ , no ši sifu maŋmutuc dâŋ mupe , no Kristore gieŋic sâc moc . No giere šâic manaekopac i sâc moc , â kâpâcwâru ficko feekopac i sâc moc , â šika kiekopac i sâc moc , â sipirickezo eekopac i sâc moc .
47011024	Judaŋic jaŋe dameŋ memoc repazi 39 numbiŋ ,
47011025	dameŋ jahec â moc kâcbiŋzi nukicne , moc i qânâzi hehâmocnumbiŋ , dameŋ jahec â moc woke hericke fâuc eme hâwecko hurâ hu epo , ŋafe šoaŋ moc woke sâqoreme hâwecko qac qâsoriehuc jupo .
47011026	Erâ sopâc kâte hârâc tiki fotâcne qâqâwiric bazu bâfeŋ ehuc jupo , opâ rumio šârâ šâpâ faio fehuc jupo , râsi ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , Judaŋic ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , qâpuc ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , ŋic jujuo šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , tuhuo šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , hâwecko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo , mitiŋic burecne jaŋere ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo .
47011027	Iŋuczi iŋuc ehuc hume serereŋ â huacbuc qâbucne juwarepo , ehuc ŋafeo guŋɋâri juju , nânâ opâre hâhâmo , hoe mâmâteŋte ɋarac ɋarac qaqa , ŋaqi bilaŋke babasa , iŋuc ehuc juekopac .
47011028	Erâ i sawa mâcne , šoaŋne šoaŋne kiŋaŋ fisihuc fâro âkefec enarepie hae sâc kikefuŋ jaŋere mana mezac ehuc juekopac .
47011029	Wemocko hae moczi qau bititicne juhapie âke uruerâ sâcne jupemu ? Wemocko hae moczi qâsoriehapie sâcne ŋemâteŋkepemu ?
47011030	Eme no irec wemo-nane musokapemu ? Gegec dodoc-nane mocjaha musokape sâckeocmu .
47011031	Wofuŋ Jesu ere Anutu â Mamac , e mumuteŋ hatizi dâŋ jâmbomac mukopac i manakac .

47012010	Eme Kristore erâ dodoc rorokac epemu me šika kipemu , me hume serereŋ jupemu , me fific guguriŋ â imaŋ gomaŋ faio jupemu , i sifu bubiaŋ manaekopac . No dodoc rorokacko sanaŋkeekopac hâcne .
47012011	Ʒi mutucdâŋ mupac , i ŋoŋe enarepie mupac . Ŋaŋac mumbiaŋnupie sâckezac . No jawa omane juekopac i manakopac , erâ aposolo fekicne jaŋere wahamicne juju ine mi juekopac .

47012013	Eme ŋoŋe wemo basahuc kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋere sâc mi embiŋ ? Mâc wiac ŋowac ro nâc ee i mocjaha mi eŋarepo . Hehesic-nane i mi mana sâqore-narenšepieŋ .
47012014	No jajahec iqic-ŋopapo , eme ši mocwâc fâpere šawiehuc jukopac . Fârâ mârâc epo ijaha ehuc sahacte dopere mi bâšâic-ŋopapemu . No moneŋ mafa-ŋeŋicte mâcne , ŋaŋacnere harac eekopac . 47012016	Ŋic gâcnezi nore šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ : Wiac tâtâc nânâwoc ro i mi ewec . Á soŋsoŋko ŋic eatuc-jopahuc wiac jojowac ro i ewec mecne .

47012019	Dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ i esecne mana warepie sahac ŋeŋezic dâŋ eekac me ? Erâ iŋuc mâcne , nâŋe Kristohec juhuc Anuture maio dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ , erâ âgofâc , irec me irec mâcne , ŋoŋe âkesiŋ-ŋopanaŋte dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ .
47012020	No ŋoŋerao fârâ honec-ŋopape mi sâckezacte , â ŋoŋe nore iŋuc jaha manapie mi sâckezacte manabâc ekopac . Ŋoŋerao kisâ , iiŋguuŋ , kimbeŋ , hehefaric , micko âkec , gupe , penaroŋ , hesi qâsifuc , wiac i fohame fâ bâfuazipore maŋbahacnukac .

47013001	Ʒi ŋoŋerao mocwâc fâpe jahec â moc eocmu . Fâ fisipe ŋic jajahec me jahec â moczi mocte bahacte fuŋne mupie dâŋticne munaŋmu .

48003016	Eme miti merâfâc i Abraham â ɋâric-ticne biŋe qajactekicne hâcne . Ɋâricfâc-ticne bocjaha jaŋere mi mukicne , mocjahare mukicne Kristo hâcne .
48003017	No kecšiŋucte mukopac : Anutuzi mârâc jaha miti merâfâc irec biŋedâŋ muwec , ehame šâhecko jara 430 tarame sâcmutâc dâŋ mufuawec , eme sâcmutâc dâŋ šâhec mufuakicne izi wemocko biŋedâŋ mârâc mukicne qame wahaocmu .
48003018	Miti merâfâc i sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ rorone eme muzac ine biŋedâŋte erâ rorone i arictac ezac . Anutuzi ine miti merâfâc i katucmâc-ticnere erâ Abraham biŋe qacnewec .
48003019	Hâc , eme sâcmutâc dâŋ wemocte mukicne ? I qaqatarare mufuakicne , erâ fofo sanaŋ foocte mâcne , Abrahamte ɋâric biŋedâŋ rune fuame rârieocte mukicne . Sâcmutâc dâŋ i aŋelo miczi mukicne â ŋicwirec ere meo râekicne .
48003020	Ŋicwirec moczi ŋic mocjahare mâcne , bocjaha jaŋere qâqâhâc domaocmu . Anutu eki ine mocjaha .
48003021	Eme sâcmutâc dâŋzi Anuture biŋedâŋ âkehockeocmu me ? Iŋuc aricne . Sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋicmaŋ mi heɋâreocmu . I eene eme muzac , ine jâmbomac sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee i fuazac .
48003022	Ŋic mâmâc sasawa sâqocnere niŋgiŋko jueŋgopeneŋ , fuŋne-nâŋec iŋuc hâcne miti papiao mufuakicne . Eme irec hâcne Jesu Kristo manasiŋkehuc mitihec erâ biŋedâŋte fârine ronaŋmu , i sawa fokac .
48003023	Judaŋic nâŋâc mârâc jaha mamanasiŋ tâmiric juhapene sâcmutâc dâŋzi kâpâcwâru bacnâpome niŋgiŋko fokuhapene mamanasiŋte biŋedâŋzi fua tâcnewec .
48003024	Eme irec sâcmutâc dâŋzi bâbâtiŋ-nâŋec erâ Kristorao râec-nâpowec , i mamanasiŋhec erâ kiŋfâsâc enaŋte iŋuc ekicne .
48003025	Nâŋâc mamanasiŋte hata fuame i âtepene bâbâtiŋte niŋgiŋ tâcnewec .
48003026	Eme ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeŋgopieŋte šeŋgoma Anuture naru motecfâc embiŋ juŋgopieŋ .
48003027	Miti Opâ rua-ŋarehuc Kristorao šuhuc-ŋopakicne ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa Kristozi ŋaqi-ŋeŋic ehame hepie huwec .
48003028	Eme irec Judaŋic â Grikŋic , fekicne â wahakicne , ŋic â ŋokac , bârâwiŋ juju i tarame ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa Kristo Jesurao sâc mocjaha embiŋ .
48003029	Ŋoŋe Kristore biŋe embiŋzi Abrahamte ɋâricfâc fârine juŋgopieŋ , erâ biŋedâŋte sâcko merâfâc-ticne bajuniŋmu .
48004001	Moc šiŋuc mupe mananiŋ : Motec ɋiene moc e mamac hâmocnere merâfâc raucke-bipiehuc sifu kiŋaŋ motec hawari juocmu .
48004002	Ehame wawa rau â âgo tofazi merâfâc qâzuckerâ bacne juhapie dameŋ mamaczi bawec i maickeocmu .
48004003	Nâŋâcne sâc ijaha fokac . Mârâc jaha maŋzi ɋiene juhuc mâreŋte wiac omanere kiŋaŋ qajumbeneŋ .
48004004	Eme šâhecko dameŋ bakicne i qosackeme Anutuzi Ŋokâ-ticne soreme ŋokackonec fuawec â sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qawec .
48004005	Ine nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋte niŋgiŋkonec goroŋ-nâpome Anuture naru motecfâc enaŋte iŋuc ewec .
48004006	Eme ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ticne eŋgopieŋte Anutuzi Ŋokâ-ticnere Mâro maŋnâŋecko soreme hurâ šiŋuc wirâ wâwâsic eekac : “ O Mamac biaŋ . ”
48004007	Irec go kiŋaŋ qaqa-ticne mâcne , motec-ticne juekic . Erâ motec-ticne juhuc Anutu katucmâc-ticnere erâ merâfâc rune wâc juekic .
48004008	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha Anuture kâuc bahuc nemu , Wofuŋ fârine mi jujune , jaŋe kiŋaŋ qajare jumbieŋ .
48004009	Eme šâhec Anutuzi hone šâŋitac eŋareme ŋoŋe e wâc hone tarambiŋ . Ehame wiac tâpiri tâmiric â fârimâc i wemocte mocwâc maickehuc kiŋaŋne qaŋgopieŋ ?
48004010	Ehuc hombaŋ fuŋne fuŋnere manapie fârine eme ŋeeŋgopieŋ .
48004011	Gie-nanezi ŋoŋerao fârimâc ezacte mana mezac boc eekopac .
48004012	Âgofâc-nane , no numu-ŋarehuc mupe : No ŋoŋere sâc epore ŋoŋe nore sâc enšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe ši juwarehuc wiac hehesicne moc mi enarembiŋ .
48004013	Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ , no mârâcko huc šâic enarehame Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapo .
48004014	Eme sahac dodoc mâretec enareme ŋoŋe nore sifu tatakicne mi eŋarewec â mi mamakâc-ŋopawec . Aricne , ŋoŋe honecnupie Anuture aŋelo tinac epo , opoŋ , Kristo Jesu tinac epe hefârecnumbiŋ .
48004015	Joi , dameŋ ira mu šeri embiŋ i weniŋucte omaekac ? Ŋoŋe šâŋe hândâŋ-ŋeŋic unuckerâ no nanarene fome muzac enšapiŋ , i jâmbomac manahuc mukopac .
48004016	Eme dameŋ šiŋuczia dâŋ fârine ŋazape honecnupie râsi-ŋeŋic ekopac me ?
48004017	Ŋic gâcnezi ŋoŋere harac baeŋgopieŋ i âke râwiŋ-nâpopie ŋoŋe jaŋere harac eniŋte manasuhuc eeŋgopieŋ . Ine hâcne sioc ehuc ŋoŋere harac baeŋgopieŋ .
48004018	Wiac biaŋnere erâ harac ee i biaŋne . Ine ŋoŋerao fârâ juhape sawa mâcne , dameŋ sâc epie biaŋkeocmu .
48004019	Naru motecfâc-nane , no ŋoŋere erâ gozi kicnuha šâic manapo , ijaha harierâ manakopac , erâ Kristore hawari ŋoŋerao fua tâcneocte šâic i mana rahuc jupemu .
48004020	No ŋoŋere mana guruc boc ekopacte ŋoŋerao biac fârâ dâŋ mu hetikic ehuc ŋazazore enarekac .
48004021	Wio-ŋarepe nazaniŋ , sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qazo mueŋgopieŋzi irec papia wose manac mi eeŋgopieŋ me ?
48004022	Ira hâcne šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : Abrahamte ŋokâ jajahec fuapic , moc i kiŋaŋ naruzi rowec â moc i ŋonâŋzi rowec .
48004023	Eme kiŋaŋ naruzi rowec e omanao fuawec , â ŋonâŋzi rowec e Anuture biŋedâŋte sâcko fuawec .
48004024	Eme dâŋ irec ŋifecne šiŋuc fokac : Ŋokac jahe mitire šâšâfic jajahec irec sâsâcne epic . Ʒâšâfic moc Sinai tikio ekicne , ere kikefuŋzi ine kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ , eme irec sâsâcne Hagazi ewec .
48004025	Haga i Sinai tiki , Arabia mâreŋko ŋekac , irec šâŋe moc . Á Jerusalem hae i Sinai tikihec sâcjekic mocjaha ekopirec , ere kikefuŋ jaŋe kiŋaŋ qaqa jaha wâc eŋgopieŋ hâcne .
48004026	Á Jerusalem hae faic ŋekac izi Sara ere sâc , hae izi hâcne neŋgoc jâmbâŋ-nâŋec ekac .
48004027	Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Ŋokac hufiŋne , motec mi roro go bubiaŋ manazemec , gozi mi kicguekac go šeri ehuc kiwaezemec . Ŋokac ŋichec e ɋâric afecne fuacnehapie me sawanezi naru motec bocjaha rocjopaocmu . ”
48004028	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe Isakare sâc erâ biŋedâŋte fuambiŋ .
48004029	Eme mârâc jaha motec omanao fuakicnezi Mârore dâŋte fuakicne e râsi ecnewec , sâc ijaha miŋecgac fokac .
48004030	Eme miti papiao dâŋ weniŋuc fokac ? “ Kiŋaŋ naru e ŋokâ-ticnehec jâpec-jofatec ranic , kiŋaŋ narure ŋokâzi ŋonâŋte ŋokâhec merâfâc mi rauckezejec . ”
48004031	Âgofâc-nane , nâŋâc kiŋaŋ narure ɋârifâc aricne , nâŋâc ŋonâŋte ɋâricfâc .
48005001	Niŋgiŋ tâmiric junaŋte Kristozi goroŋ-nâpowec . Irec gâcnezi niŋgiŋko râec-ŋoparâ kiŋaŋ qaqa eniŋte muŋarepie qikiŋnenšepieŋ .
48005002	No Paulozi ŋazape mananiŋ , ŋoŋe sahac-ŋeŋicko ma bapie Kristozi ŋoŋerao wiac omane tinac eocmu .
48005003	Mocwâc harierâ ŋaza-jâmbâŋkepe , moc e sahac-ticnao ma baocmuzi sâcmutâc dâŋ gâcne sâko mâmâc hâpo-fâreme sâckeocmu .
48005004	Sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc ezo mueŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe Kristohec šâšâfic embiŋ i tâcnekac â aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fârimâc ekac .
48005005	Nâŋe ine Mârorao ŋesiŋnehuc mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee bâfuanaŋte irec mamanac jueŋgopeneŋ .
48005006	Kristo Jesurao fisirâ mahec juju â ma tâmiric juju irec mâmâc jaha fârimâc muzo , mamanasiŋte qâreŋ maŋko fuame irec mocjaha fârine muzo .
48005007	Ŋoŋe mitire hata sâcne fuŋkerâ âtembiŋ . Âtehapie mozi aka heŋareme dâŋ fâri qizecne râpeckeŋgopieŋ ?
48005008	Hefârec-ŋopawec eki irec esoc qafeŋ mi eŋarekac .
48005009	Qowi hâhâtâcne pitic siŋgaŋ gaucnezi nânâ sicko hurâ mâmâc sâcke-fâreocmu .
48005010	Erâ ŋoŋe nore dâŋ mi qikiŋneniŋmu , i Wofuŋte erâ manabâc tâmiric mukopac . Á ŋic izi me izi maŋ bâsifuc eŋareocmu , e kiŋ irec okacne fisicneocmu .
48005011	Âgofâc , no ine mahec eniŋte ŋic jazazapo muzac , wemocko fific guguriŋ moc enarenšapiŋ ? Iŋuc jazazapoo maripoŋte mamana gâpâre i mâmâc omaezac .
48005012	Maŋqaqa eŋareeŋgopieŋ ŋic iŋucnezi sahac-jeŋic hetâc qâtâcnenšapiŋ me !
48005013	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe niŋgiŋ tâmiric juniŋte hefârec-ŋopakicne , erâ niŋgiŋ tâmiric jujuzi âki eha sahacte dâŋ reŋkeniŋte mâcne , maŋjauŋko kiŋaŋ qaqac eniŋte irec hefârec-ŋopakicne .
48005014	Irec hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋte qâqâhâc šiŋuc mukicne : “ Gahacnere egareekac , sâc ijaha âgogere egarezejec . ”
48005015	Ŋoŋe ine miczi nânâc ehuc kikic qaqac boc erâ oomaec enšipiŋte uŋ ŋazakopac .
48005016	Erâ ine šiŋuc mukopac : Ŋoŋe Mârore tâpirio siŋkerâ junšepieŋ , iŋuc ehuc maŋraŋɋare sasec gie mi baniŋmu .
48005017	Maŋraŋɋare aŋaczi hâcne Mâro kisueekac â Mârozi maŋraŋɋa kisueekac , eme jahe hâcne rârâsi epire ŋoŋe wiac ezo mueŋgopieŋ i sâcne mi afeckerâ eeŋgopieŋ .
48005018	Mârozi jowa baafec eŋareme ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋicbomboŋ mi eŋareocmu .
48005019	Maŋraŋɋare gie i soŋsoŋko mi foekac , i šiŋuc fuaekac : Boe sau , mamakâc , nâ areŋ ,
48005020	nemu araŋ babajare , hafec qaŋgec , rârâsi , sosopec , iiŋguuŋ , kimbeŋ , hehefaric , fâfâuc , rârâwiŋ ,
48005021	mu kâroŋ , opâ momori me bec qowi âmbâŋ nânâ , erâ wiac gâcne . Wiac iŋucnere mârâc jaha ŋazapo erâ ši mocwâc ŋazape : Sâqocne i baniŋmuzi Anuture uucmaŋko mi rašiniŋmu .
48005022	Mârore fârine ine kecšiŋuc fuaekac : Maŋjauŋ , bubiaŋ , wama , bumâteŋ , buafec , buuruc , ââgo sanaŋ ,
48005023	ruaine , maŋzi sowa juju . Mârore fârine hâcne irec aka mi fokac .
48005024	Kristo Jesure biŋe jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe juju raŋɋa-jeŋic sasec â sâqocnere andachec i maripoŋko qapie omaewec .
48005025	Mârore tâpirire jueŋgopeneŋko Mârore hata jaha âtenšepeneŋ .
48005026	Sahaczi fecko fec ehuc hehesuac mi enšepeneŋ , erâ wâc iiŋguuŋ mi eec enšepeneŋ .
48006001	Âgofâc-nane , ŋic moczi dockerâ bahac bâfuame ŋoŋe Mâroheczi bumâteŋ erâ iŋucne mu bâtiŋ ecnenšepieŋ . Ehuc go gahac eesâicko pârâckezicte rucge bazemec .
48006002	Wiac kihuhuŋ-ŋopaekac i nowac gowacroŋ ehuc babaficko banšepieŋ . Iŋuc ehuc Kristore sâcmutâc dâŋ sâcne reŋkeniŋmu .
48006003	Ŋic moc e wiac fârine moc mi ehuc e jahacnere maname fefene eocmu , iŋucnezi maŋticne fagac ecnekac muzo .
48006004	Irec moc e jahacne juju bapa hone šâŋitac ezejec . Eme šeridâŋ i e jahacnere erâ fuaocmu , ŋic mocte erâ mâcne .
48006005	Giere ŋemâc kâdoc qakicne i ru sâc areckezo .
48006006	Miti ŋaza qazuc eeŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe wiac fuŋne fuŋne boki bahuc jare gumec enšepieŋ .
48006007	Anutu mu qâtimbuc ecnepie mâc foocmu , iŋuc moc mupie . I aricne jâmbâŋ , ŋic moc gie baocmu e irec fârine juku ijaha roocmu .
48006008	Moc e maŋraŋɋare gie baocmu , e juku maŋraŋɋa-ticnere fârine sisipiric bâfuaocmu , â moc e Mârore gie baocmu , e juku Mârore fârine juju sanaŋ bâfuaocmu .
48006009	Wiac biaŋne i rorokac tâmiric enšepeneŋ , eme mi betaŋkenaŋmuo juku dameŋ-ticnao mâriri bâfuanaŋmu .
48006010	Irec dameŋ-nâŋec fohame ŋic sasawa ehâmo-jarenšepeneŋ . Ehuc mitio âgofâc-nâŋec wiac bafehuc ejarenšepeneŋ .
48006011	Ŋoŋe qâreŋ sâko ši honeniŋ , no nahacne mezi qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
48006012	Ŋic gâcne jaŋe sahaczi miti hawari biaŋ erâ ŋoŋe sahacko mahec eniŋte fotarie-ŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋe Kristo maripoŋ-ticnere erâ fific guguriŋ faio fenšipiŋte iŋuc hâcne eeŋgopieŋ .
48006013	Sahacko mahec embiŋ ŋic i jaŋe jaŋac wâc sâcmutâc dâŋ mi reŋkeeŋgopieŋ . Jaŋe mâc ŋoŋe mahec erâ jaŋerao šuhuckepie sahac-jeŋic muteŋkeniŋte manasueŋgopieŋ .
48006014	No ine wiac irec mi Irec mâcne , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo maripoŋ-ticnere biŋedâŋ irec mocjaha mumuteŋ bajuekopac . Ere erâ mâreŋkonec wiaczi maripoŋko hâmo-narewec , â no iŋuc jaha maripoŋko mâreŋkonec wiac hâmocnepo .
48006015	Sahacko mahec juju me ma tâmiric juju izi fârine aricne , juju ɋâricne izi mocjaha fârine ekac .
48006016	Gaŋ rukec ira hâcne domaeŋgopieŋ sâc ŋoŋerao wama â buuruc fotâcnerâ fozejec , erâ Anuture Israe ŋic jaŋerao mâmâc .
48006017	Ʒi moczi moc neneŋ gie mocwâc mi narezejec . No Wofuŋ Jesure râfu qâreŋ sahac-naneo fome bajuekopac .
48006018	Âgofâc-nane , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore aki anonoczi maŋŋeŋicko fozejec . Jâmbomac .
49001001	Paulo no Anuture micte Jesu Kristore aposolo epozi Efeso haeonec mitiŋic , Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ hâcne , ŋoŋere papia ši râekopac
49001002	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnera fozejec .
49001003	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Anutu â Mamac , eki sambâŋkonec miti jambuŋ-ticne fuŋne fuŋne Kristore erâ nâre tahac ewecte mumbiaŋkenšepeneŋ .
49001004	Eki mârâc jaha jâmbâŋ mâreŋte hobeteŋne mi fuahame mai-ticnao maŋfuru â bahacmâc junaŋte Kristore erâ mana wosâc enârewec .
49001005	E qanaŋ maname fowecte hâcne Jesu Kristore erâ maŋjauŋ enârehuc naru motecfâc-ticne erâ junaŋte buafec-ticnere mupaŋke-nârewec .
49001006	E joroc Ŋokâ-ticnere erâ aki anonoc biaŋ-ticne tahac-nâpowecte muteŋ bâteŋ ecnenšepeneŋ .
49001007	Jesu e socticnezi kitâc-nâpowecte sâqocne bâbâtâmire fua-nârewec , i aki anonoc-ticnere šâkâŋ fokac irec sâc hâcne .
49001008	Eme šâkâŋ-ticnao maŋɋârâŋ â mamana fâri bâmâckehuc qoŋgiŋke-nârewec .
49001009	Ehuc maŋbuc-ticnere dâŋ , qanaŋ maname biaŋkeme šiŋuc âkendâŋnewec i mujaŋgeŋke-nârewec :
49001010	“ No guriŋne bahape dameŋ maŋkepo i qosackeme Kristozi wiac sasawa , sambâŋko mecne mâreŋko mecne , qâturehuc irec fuŋqizecne ezejec . ”
49001011	Ere erâ , wiac sasawa maŋticnere mupaŋkerâ baekaczi mârâc jaha hone wosâec-nâporâ miti merâfâc rauckenaŋte munârewec .
49001012	Eme irec Kristore mamanac jumbeŋ jueŋgopeneŋzi Anutu šâŋe rara-ticnere mumuteŋfâc erâ junšepeneŋ .
49001013	Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha dâŋ fâri qizecne , bâbâpiaŋ-ŋeŋicte Biŋebiaŋ hâcne , ro maŋ ehuc Kristo manasiŋkepie Tiri Mâro qanaŋ biŋe qanarekicne i ŋareme maqâreŋhec embiŋ .
49001014	Sambâŋko huhure biŋe-nâŋec fokac , irec šâšâficne Mâro nârekicne . Eme Anutu šâŋe rara-ticnere mumuteŋ sâko fuaocte biŋefâc-ticne nâŋâcnao Mârozi bâbâpiaŋ gie fuŋkewec i batarazokac .
49001015	Eme ŋoŋe Wofuŋ Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ â mitiŋic âgofâc-nâŋec maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ , irec biŋedâŋ manapore
49001016	ŋoŋere dameŋ sâc manasuhuc Wofuŋ daŋge mumuteŋ ecneekopac .
49001017	Ehuc ŋoŋere šiŋuc numuekopac : Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere Anutu , eri tatamac Mamac hâcne , eki Mâro ŋareme izi maŋɋârâŋhec bacŋoparâ Wofuŋte fuŋne mufua-ŋareme mana taranšepieŋ .
49001018	Erâ maŋšâŋe-ŋeŋic bâtâcneme ine Wofuŋzi rocŋopahuc sambâŋ šeŋaŋ biŋe qaŋarewec , irec manapie fârine ezejec , â fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne ŋoŋe huhure šâŋe rara biaŋ kadahe ŋarewec , irec wâc manapie fârine ezejec ,
49001019	â mamanasiŋhec nâŋâcnao tâpiri soka makakicne i teqâ saki-ticnezi gie baekac sâc bâfuawec , irec iŋuc jaha manapie fârine ezejec .
49001020	Tâpiri irec fuŋne Kristo hâmockonec bâɋârerâ sambâŋko mefâre-ticnao râehuc bataniŋkewec .
49001021	Ehuc kia gawamaî â ŋicwofuŋ â fekicne fuŋne fuŋne jaŋere femicne sâko râewecte mâreŋko â sambâŋko šâŋe biŋe fokac izi gâkowakac , dameŋ šiŋucziare sawa mâcne , iŋuc fohuc juocmu sanaŋ .
49001022	Erâ wiac sasawa maŋfuŋnao heteckehuc kike-ticnere rurumaŋko guruc-jopahuc qizec-jeŋic eocte âkendâŋnerâ kikefuŋ gurufâcne jaŋerao râewec .
49001023	Eme jaŋe me kikefâc-ticne ehapie ŋihe umbiŋ ejarehuc fofotâc juhuc wiac sasawa sâcke raekac .
49002001	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha sindaŋ hârindaŋ ehuc hâmocne jujumbieŋ .
49002002	Ine mâreŋte juju hata maŋnao juhuc saware tâpiri irec ŋicbomboŋ erao qohota jumbieŋ . Ere mârozi hâcne dameŋ šiŋuczia wâc qaqatara ŋic jaŋerao gie baekac .
49002003	Nâŋâc mârâc jaha jaŋere sâc jaha jufârehuc maŋraŋɋa-nâŋecte aŋac bâjâpembeŋ . Ehuc sahac-nâŋecte â maŋ mamanasu-nâŋecte dâŋ reŋkehuc gâcne jaŋe iŋucne kimbeŋte biŋefâc embeŋ .
49002004	Anutu eki buuruc-ticne bocjaha fokacte maŋjauŋ kâcɋene enârehuc
49002005	qaqatara-nâŋecte erâ hâmokicne nâŋâc Kristohec mâmâc bâɋârec-nâpowec . Manaŋgopieŋ , katucmâc-ticnere erâ bâpiaŋ-ŋopawec ŋoŋe .
49002006	E Kristo Jesuhec bâɋârec-nâporâ ehec mâmâc sambâŋte jujuo ŋec-nâpowec hâcne .
49002007	i nacnere mocko šiŋuc fuaocte ewec : Aki anonoc-ticnere rowaŋ sâko i Kristo Jesuo maŋuruc qanârehuc qaratie-nâreocmu .
49002008	Manaŋgopieŋ , e aki anonoc eŋarehuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte erâ bâpiaŋ-ŋopawec , i ŋaŋacnere mâcne , Anutu buafec-ticnere iŋuc eŋarewec .
49002009	Mo gie mo bambiŋte iŋuc eŋarezac , i aricne . Irec sahac mumuteŋ moc mi fuazejec .
49002010	Nâŋâc Anuture metofafâc , eki Kristo Jesuo bâfuac-nâpowec hâcne , erâ hata biaŋne Anutuzi hâcne mušâwe-nârewec i âtehuc junaŋte munârewec .
49002011	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha qâpuc jujumbieŋ , irec manasuhuc junšepieŋ . Eme dameŋ ira ma tâmiric juhapie Judaŋic jaŋe sahac-jeŋicko maheczi šâgu muŋare jumbieŋ .
49002012	Dameŋ ira Kristo tâmiric jumbiŋ , erâ Israe ŋic jaŋe hae fâri juhapie ŋoŋe mafa jumbiŋ , â jaŋe fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne bacjopame biŋedâŋ-ticne bajuhapie ŋoŋe šoŋifecfâc-ticne erâ metariŋ jumbiŋ , erâ maŋzi wiac fârine moc mi worickehuc Anutu tâmiric hâcne jumbiŋ .
49002013	Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine ŋoŋe kâteo jumbiŋzi Kristo Jesurao šuhuckehuc Kristo socticnere erâ haeo fisimbiŋ jueŋgopieŋ .
49002014	E jahac wama-nâŋec juekac . E ŋic jâcne jajahec ŋondeŋ-jekicko rârâsizi aka sanaŋ fowec i qâropiehuc , mocjaha bacjofawec .
49002015	Ine sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko bâtâc â mumuac bocjaha mukicne i e jahacne sahac qaisockehuc bârâriewec . Ehuc ŋic jâcne jajahec jahere dodoma tacko ŋic ɋâricne mocjaha ine e jahac fuarâ domahuc wama bâfuawec .
49002016	E maripoŋlo hâmowecko ŋic jâcne jajahec fâri ombâŋ mocjahao qâturec-nâpohuc Anutuhec miriŋ bacnâpowec , ehuc rârâsi qame wahawec .
49002017	Erâ fisirâ kâteo jukicne ŋoŋe â haeo jukicne nâŋe mâmâc wamare biŋedâŋ nâzâme manambeŋ .
49002018	Erâ wâc hata bâšâwe-nârewecte nâŋâc Mâro mocjaha rauckerâ Mamactao fisieŋgopeneŋ .
49002019	Eme irec dameŋ šiŋuczia mafa â jaba mocwâc mi jueŋgopieŋ , ŋoŋe mitiŋic gâcne jaŋehec hae fâri â Anuture kikefuŋfâc embiŋ juŋgopieŋ .
49002020	Ŋoŋe aposolo â porofete jaŋe wâtuŋ ŋokacne ehuc decŋopapie doma raŋgopieŋ , â Jesu Kristozi wâtuŋ ŋicne ekac .
49002021	Erao ŋicne ŋicne šuhucke itic epene Wofuŋte furu ufuŋ fua feekac .
49002022	Mârozi ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha erao râe šuhuc eŋareme Anuture fic eŋgopieŋ hâcne .
49003001	Eme Paulo no irec hâcne qâpuc ŋoŋere erâ Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic epo jukopac .
49003002	Ŋoŋe nore manambiŋ , Anutuzi uruc jauŋ-ticnere erâ ŋoŋerao miti gie bapemurâ munarewec .
49003003	Munarehuc dâŋ soŋne mufua-narewec , dâŋ i hâcne biac bembeŋne qâreŋkepac ,
49003004	ŋoŋe i wosehuc , no Kristore dâŋ soŋne maŋzi hone raruŋkekopac iŋuc sâcne mananiŋmu .
49003005	Dâŋ soŋne i mârâc jaha ŋic juwarembiŋ jaŋerao mi mufuakicne , tiri aposolo â porofete nâŋerao šâhec Mârozi mufuawec .
49003006	Dâŋ soŋne kecšiŋuc : Biŋebiaŋte fârine qâpuc ŋoŋe Judaŋic nâŋehec sâc mocjaha â guru mocjaha erâ Kristo Jesurao biŋedâŋ deŋkewec i mâmâc rauckerâ bajuniŋte mukicne .
49003007	Eme Biŋebiaŋ irec kiŋaŋ qaqa jupemurâ Anutuzi uruc jauŋ-ticnere erâ tâpiri sâko-ticnere fuŋne norao bataniŋkewec . Dâŋ soŋnere fârine Jesuzi bâfuawec
49003008	Kristorao mâriri sâko fofone fokac irec dâŋ soŋne qâpuc mutaniŋke-jarepemurâ irec gie biaŋ mitiŋic wawahane jâmbâŋ no hâcne munarekicne .
49003009	Dâŋ soŋne muraruŋkepere mukicne , i Anutu bapafâre e maŋbuc-ticnere dameŋne dameŋne baju warehuc juwec .
49003010	Ʒi ine Anutuzi kikefuŋ gurufâc-ticne nâŋâcnao maŋɋârâŋ-ticnere fârine qaratiekume qâreŋne fuŋne fuŋne fuame sambâŋko ira fekicne â tâpirihec jaŋe wâc hone šâŋitac eeŋgopieŋ .
49003011	Anutu e mârâc jaha dameŋ tâmiricko maŋnezi dâŋ mupaŋkewec irec fârine hâcne Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu sorehuc bâfuawec .
49003012	Eme eki hâcne hata bâšâwe-nâreme e manasiŋkehuc hâhâwic tâmiric Anutu maickeeŋgopeneŋ .
49003013	Irec šiŋuc ŋazape mananiŋ : No ŋoŋere erâ fific guguriŋ faio jupe irec maŋŋeŋic mi wahazejec , aricne , ŋoŋe irec manapie eri qoqonaŋ-ŋeŋic ezejec .
49003014	Irec hâcne sambâŋko â mâreŋko ŋic guru sâc jueŋgopeneŋ
49003015	nâŋâcne Mamac fârine e dieŋzi hecnehuc ŋoŋere erâ numucnehuc šiŋuc muekopac :
49003016	Anutu e hahaŋnehec sâkozi Mâro ecneme tâpiri bâfua-ŋareme maŋŋeŋiczi soka sanaŋ ezejec .
49003017	Eme Kristo manasiŋkepie maŋŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ezejec . Eme ere maŋjauŋko gâtâ barâ qiŋ herâ domanšepieŋ .
49003018	Ehuc mitiŋic gâcne sasawa jaŋehec mâmâc mitire fuŋne botâŋne , hâŋne otecne . i afeckerâ mana taranšepieŋ ,
49003019	erâ wâc Kristore maŋjauŋ , ŋic mamana jâuru-fâreekac , i sifu mana-hâmonšepieŋ . Ehame Anuturao maŋ mâriri fufusuc fokac izi bâfusec-ŋopazejec .
49003020	Tâpiri-ticnere fuŋne nâŋâcnao bataniŋkeekac Anutu hâcne , e wiac bapa-ticnezi nunumu-nâŋec â mamanasu-nâŋec siricke-fâreekacte
49003021	kikefuŋko â Kristo Jesurao mumuteŋ-ticne mimiŋzi ɋâric šuhuckeme šuhuc fofehuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
49004001	No Wofuŋte kâpâcwâru ŋiczi faŋ qaŋarehuc ŋazape : Wiac fekicnere hefârec-ŋopakicne irec sâcko junšepieŋ .
49004002	Ehuc maŋhuhuŋ â buuruc â bumâteŋ juhuc maŋjauŋko dedec ââsic enšepieŋ .
49004003	Erâ Mâro e wamare muczi qâzuc-ŋoparâ dâtâc-ŋopawec , i qâtâcnenšipiŋte ruc babac ehuc junšepieŋ .
49004004	Fâri ombâŋzi mocjaha â Mârozi mocjaha erâ wâc sambâŋ šeŋaŋ mocjahare biŋe qaŋarehuc hefârec-ŋopakicne .
49004005	Ine hâcne , Wofuŋzi mocjaha , mamanasiŋzi mocjaha , Miti Opâzi mocjaha .
49004006	Erâ Anutu e Mamac wirec-nâŋec mocjaha , eki mâmâc sasawa qâhuc-nâpokac erâ maŋnâŋec sâc tâpiri sicne-nâreekac â mâŋnâŋec sâc ŋeŋe juju eekac .
49004007	Kristo e ŋicne ŋicne mitire kâdoc nârewec sâc bajueŋgopeneŋ .
49004008	Irec hâcne dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc fokac : “ E faic jâmbâŋ fehuc kâpâcwâru ŋic bacjopa rawec , e ŋic wiac tahac-jopawec . ”
49004009	“ Faic fewec ” , i mâc mi mukicne , mâreŋko juwic jâmbâŋ wahaweckonec risie fewec .
49004010	E wahaweczia risierâ sambâŋne sambâŋne fotâcnerâ fewec , i sambâŋ â mâreŋ fusucmarâ jufâreocte fewec hâcne .
49004011	Erâ ekizia wâc ŋic gâcne aposolo râec-nâpowec , gâcne porofete , gâcne miti kiŋaŋ ŋic , gâcne lama guru jaŋere soŋaŋ â qaqazu ,
49004012	i mitiŋic ŋokac bašawiec-jopapene kikefuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa gie bapie Kristore me kike fâri ombâŋ soka sanaŋ eocte ŋic iŋuc râec-nâpowec .
49004013	Iŋuczi iŋuc gie bakupene mamanasiŋ-nâŋec â Anutu ŋokâ-ticnere fuŋne mamana-nâŋec i niniweme maŋ mocjaha enšepeneŋ . Ehuc mitio sosoka-nâŋecte sâc mukicne i Kristore rowaŋkonec tâpiri fârehuc fua sokac eku ŋic kâcɋene erâ bâfuanšepeneŋ .
49004014	Nâŋâc ɋiene hati mi ee sanaŋkerâ juhapene eeatuc ŋic jaŋe sioc enârepie gibioc dâŋ â mumusifuc-jeŋicte mâŋâŋzi ba bâsoriŋ â qac qârândiŋ moc mi enârezejec .
49004015	Aricne , nâŋâc dâŋfâri paŋšâic bajupene maŋjauŋ-nâŋeczi fua sawec ehame qizec-nâŋec Kristo erao šuhucke sanaŋkenšepeneŋ .
49004016	Erao šuhuckepene ruazi ŋeturec-nâporâ bândeŋ-nâpome ɋâɋâdoc erâ me sahac-ticne eeŋgopeneŋ . Ehuc tofafâc-ticne erâ tâpiri fonâreekac sâc gie bahuc maŋjauŋko soka sawec enaŋmu .
49004017	No Wofuŋte maio ŋaza-jâmbâŋkepe : Ŋoŋe qâpuc , maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic wiac jawanere foekac , jaŋere sâc mi junšepieŋ .
49004018	Jaŋe maŋjeŋic dapâc ekicnere mutuc â maŋsanaŋ erâ Anuture juju râpeckembiŋ .
49004019	Eme maŋjeŋic šickeme nânâ qowire nâ areŋ ehuc sasec mamakâc fuŋne fuŋne takicmâc ebac eeŋgopieŋ .
49004020	Ŋoŋe ine juju iŋucne juniŋte Kristore fuŋne mi qazu-ŋarekicne .
49004021	Ŋoŋe fuŋne-ticne qazu-ŋarekicko Jesurao dâŋfâri kecšiŋuc fokac i hâcne manambiŋ :
49004022	Qâpuc juju râpeckerâ maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic burec ehuc sasecko sipirickeekac , i heunuckenšepieŋ .
49004023	Erâ mâro manacnepie mamanasu-ŋeŋic heɋârehame
49004024	maŋɋâri hepie huzejec . I hâcne Anuture hawari iŋucne tiŋne â furu jâmbâŋ bâfuakicne .
49004025	Irec ŋoŋe burec beherâ dâŋ jâmbomac sasawa nazaŋ gazaŋ enšepieŋ , nâŋâc qoqomâ efâreŋgopeneŋte .
49004026	Kimbeŋko mi sâqorenšepieŋ . Kimbeŋ aaric mi bajuhapie šoaŋ ŋeutuckezejec .
49004027	Erâ Sataŋ mi mana uruecnenšepieŋ .
49004028	Fiuc rorozi fiuc qikiŋnerâ meticnezi gie šoɋac bahuc nânâ mafa bâfuarâ waha qaqane boki bajarezejec .
49004029	Dâŋ simbiŋne micŋeŋickonec mi wahazejec , dâŋ biaŋne sawa , ine dodopec eere hatane fuame mupie ŋic âgo bacjopazejec .
49004030	Anuture Tiri Mâro mi qaisockenšepieŋ , e hâcne roroc-nâpo dameŋko maqâreŋ-ŋeŋic eocte tahac-ŋopakicne .
49004031	Râsidâŋ , kimbeŋ aaric , mu ojowa , susurec , erâ wiac gâgâpâcne gâcne i ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko mi fuazejec .
49004032	Ŋoŋe ââgo erâ eehâmoc ehuc kiŋ bebehec enšepieŋ , Anutu e iŋuc jaha Kristore erâ kiŋŋeŋic behewec .
49005001	Ŋoŋe joroc naru motecfâcne juŋgopieŋzi Anutu sâckehuc junšepieŋ .
49005002	Erâ maŋjauŋhec junšepieŋ . Kristo e iŋuc jaha maŋjauŋ enârehuc nâŋâcnere erâ sahac-ticne qaisockerâ Anutu taha bâzi biaŋ ecnewec .
49005003	Boe sau , sasec mamakâc , buchâro , irec saŋuc wâc mitiŋic ŋoŋere ŋondeŋko mi fuazejec .
49005004	Dâŋ miminehec , mutucdâŋ , dâŋ simbiŋne , i epie sâqoreocmu . Daŋge mumuteŋ ine epie sâckeocmu .
49005005	Ŋoŋe šiŋuc mana sanaŋkenšepieŋ : Boe sau ŋic â sasec mamakâchec â buchâro , nemu qaŋgec ŋic hâcne , jaŋe Kristo â Anutu uucmaŋ-ticnao ŋeŋe basaniŋmu .
49005006	Eatuc-ŋopahuc siocdâŋ ŋazapie manapie fârine mi ezejec . Sâqocne iŋucnere hâcne Anuturaonec okacne qaqatara ŋic jaŋerao fuaocmu .
49005007	Irec ŋoŋe mi bafic-jopanšepieŋ .
49005008	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha dapâchec jujumbieŋ , ši ine Wofuŋtao fisirâ tatamachec embiŋ juŋgopieŋ . Irec tatamacte ɋâricfâc erâ irec hawari junšepieŋ .
49005009	Tatamacte fârine fuaekac i maŋbiaŋhec juju â tiŋne ju ju â jâmbomac dâŋ mumu .
49005010	Wiac ezo murâ ine Wofuŋzi maname biaŋkeocmu me mâcne , i qanaŋ mana wosâerâ enšepieŋ .
49005011	Gâcnezi dapâcte wiac jawane epie mi qâsuec-jopanšepieŋ , aricne . Ŋoŋe irec tapa qararuŋkehuc qatara-jarenšepieŋ .
49005012	Wiac soŋsoŋko eeŋgopieŋ i mu bâuac epene miminehec jaha eocmu .
49005013	Wiac iŋucne tapane qararuŋkepene tatamaczi âeckeme fuaocmu . Eme tâtâc fuakac wiac izi wâc tatamac bâfuaocmu .
49005014	Irec hâcne šiŋuc mukicne : “ Guŋ foekiczi faharec , â hâmockonec ɋârec , eme Kristozi batamaecguocmu . ”
49005015	Ŋoŋe juju bapa-ŋeŋicte ruc bahuc junšepieŋ . Erâ mutuc matacne mâcne , maŋ mamanasuhec junšepieŋ .
49005016	Dameŋ šira sâqocnezi haŋ bawec fokacte dameŋ gâcne mi behehuc gie šoɋachec banšepieŋ .
49005017	Maŋ tâmiric tinac mi junšepieŋ , Wofuŋzi gie muŋareekac i hone šâŋitac enšepieŋ .
49005018	Waiŋ opâ wiacte âmbâŋ mi enšepieŋ , izi maŋ sisipiric gie . Mârore ine âmbâŋ enšepieŋ .
49005019	Mârozi esoc-ŋopaocmu sâc gae mânec hehuc maŋ nareŋ gareŋ enšepieŋ . Á maŋŋeŋicko Wofuŋ gaezi â musizi mu šeri ecnenšepieŋ .
49005020	Erâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ dameŋ sâc Anutu Mamac wiac fuŋne fuŋnere daŋge mumuteŋ ecnenšepieŋ .
49005021	Ŋoŋe Kristo araŋ bacnehuc micrereŋ eec efârenšepieŋ .
49005022	Ŋonâŋ ŋoŋe Wofuŋte rereŋfâc juŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere junšepieŋ .
49005023	Ŋowezi ŋonâŋte qizec ekac hâcne , iŋuc jaha Kristozi kikefuŋte qizec ekac , ehuc me sahac-ticnere bâbâpiaŋ wâc ekac .
49005024	Eme kikefuŋzi Kristore mic reŋkeekac , iŋuc jaha ŋonâŋ jaŋe ŋowefâc-jeŋic jaŋere mic dameŋ sâc reŋkenšepieŋ .
49005025	Ŋowe ŋoŋe ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarenšepieŋ . Kristo e iŋuc jaha kikefuŋ-ticne maŋjauŋ ecnehuc ere due bawec .
49005026	Erâ kikiruhucne â sâfânehec â wâc wiac gâcnehec juzacte mitidâŋzi opâ umbiŋkeha šurehuc jambuŋkerâ
49005027	ericke bâpiaŋ ecnerâ e jahacne biŋe furu â bahacmâc juocte mucnewec .
49005028	Eme ŋowe jaŋe jaŋacne sahac jauŋ bacneeŋgopieŋ , sâc ijaha ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic bajarenšepieŋ . Moc e ŋonâŋ-ticne maŋjauŋ ecnehuc e jahacne sahac mâmâc ecneocmu .
49005029	Ŋic moczi moc sahac-ticne râsi mi eecne , gume jauŋ ecnehuc jaha juekac , Kristozi kikefuŋ ecnehuc juekac iŋuc ”
49005030	nâŋâc me sahac-ticnere tofafâc juŋgopeneŋ hâcne .
49005031	“ Irec hâcne ŋic moczi neŋgoc mamac jahec-ticne behec-jofarâ ŋonâŋ-ticnerao qohotame jahe maŋ sahac mocjaha erâ junicmu . ”
49005032	I dâŋ soŋne , qame hukicne . Ine Kristo â Kikefuŋ jahere muhuc mukopac .
49005033	Ŋoŋe ine ŋic sasawa sahac-ŋeŋic jauŋ baeŋgopieŋ sâc ijaha ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic jauŋ bacjopanšepieŋ . Á ŋokac ine ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic araŋ bajarenšepieŋ .
49006001	Naru motec ŋoŋe Wofuŋte erâ neŋgoc mamacfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋkenšepieŋ . Izi hata biaŋne .
49006002	“ Go neŋgoc mamac jahecge sâsec-jofazemec ” , i sâcmutâc dâŋ fekicne , erâ biŋedâŋ-ticne šiŋuc šuhuckerâ mukicne :
49006003	“ Iŋuc erâ mâreŋko dameŋ šora juhâc qâhâmocmu . ”
49006004	Mamac ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic aaric bâfuanšipiŋte wiac kosa mi ejarenšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe mitio jaza bâtiŋ â uŋ sawaŋ ejarehuc soŋaŋ-jopahapie sokanšepieŋ .
49006005	Kiŋaŋ qaqa ŋoŋe mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic araŋ bajarehuc , maŋŋeŋiczi qâzuc foha , Kristo ecneŋgopieŋ tinac , mana mezac ehuc micjeŋic reŋkenšepieŋ .
49006006	Ŋoŋe ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic maizi qambaraŋ ejarepie honec-ŋopapie biaŋkeocte mâcne , nâŋe Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa , iŋuc muhuc Anutuzi hata muwec i maŋafec jaha âtenšepieŋ .
49006007	Ŋic jaŋere manasuhuc aricne , Wofuŋte manasuhuc gie-ŋeŋic tatakic tâmiric banšepieŋ .
49006008	Ŋoŋe manaeŋgopieŋ , moc e kiŋaŋ qaqa me ŋicbomboŋ juhuc wiac biaŋne ehuc juocmu , e Wofuŋzi okacne sâc ijaha bazucneocmu .
49006009	Erâ ŋicbomboŋ ŋoŋe kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ŋeŋic iŋuc jaha ehâmo-jarenšepieŋ , ehuc mu imac mi ejarenšepieŋ . Erâ šiŋuc mananšepieŋ : Kiŋaŋ qaqa â ŋicbomboŋ ine sambâŋko Wofuŋ wirec-ŋeŋic jukac , e ra rowec ware rowec mi focnekac .
49006010	Mutarahuc mupe : Wofuŋtao roweckepie tâpiri sâko-ticnezi ŋoŋerao fotâcneme qaboc-ŋeŋichec junšepieŋ .
49006011	Erâ Anuturaonec sându maro šika wiac ro barâ juhapie Sataŋzi rucko râsi fisi-ŋareme hâbi-ŋeŋic rorâ jâpenšepieŋ .
49006012	Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ , nâŋâc râsi sahac biuchec jaŋehec šika qaqa mi eeŋgopeneŋ , aricne , ŋicbomboŋ sâko â momori sanaŋ , dameŋ ši dapâc fokac irec guriŋ bapa , demoŋ sâqocne sambâŋ rurumaŋko jueŋgopieŋ , jaŋe râsi enâreeŋgopieŋ .
49006013	Irec Anuturaonec sându maro šika wiac ro bajuhuc šika dameŋko qiŋ herâ domahapie râsi jaŋe bâipiec-ŋoparâ wisenšepieŋ .
49006014	Ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc domanšepieŋ : Dâŋ fâri qizecnezi umbika-ŋeŋic eme jomanšepieŋ , kiŋfâsâczi maruku-ŋeŋic eme rufanšepieŋ ,
49006015	wamare Biŋebiaŋ bašawiehuc badomanšepieŋ , izi kikehuhu hepie hume âte sanaŋkeŋgopieŋ ezejec .
49006016	Erâ neŋgocne sâko ine mamanasiŋzi maro-ŋeŋic eme dameŋ sâc he bâfeŋnerâ domahapie sâqocne runere šoc tepe moteczi kisowarierâ hâpozejec .
49006017	Erâ wâc aeŋdu šâŋene bâbâpiaŋ hepie huzejec , â Mâroraonec šika , Anuture dâŋ hâcne , i bajunšepieŋ .
49006018	Ŋoŋe šâfo sâc Mârore tâpirio Wofuŋ šušuhuc jaha numucnehuc wâsickenšepieŋ , erâ qâoma mi ehuc rucjaric-ŋeŋic banšepieŋ , erâ hae sâc mitiŋic guru jaŋere nunumu gie banšepieŋ wâc .
49006019	Erâ nore mâmâc numuhuc jupie Wofuŋzi micnane baafeckeme Biŋebiaŋ soŋsoŋ fowec i asa feferaŋko mutaniŋkezepac .
49006020	No irec biŋe mumu kâpâcwâruo foekopaczi hâhâwic tâmiric mutaniŋkepe sâckezejec .
49006021	Juju-nanere fuŋne â gie baekopac i kâuc banšipiŋte Tikikozi fârâ dâŋ binaŋ eŋare-fâreocmu , e âgo biaŋ-nâŋec â Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec .
49006022	Eki nâŋere dâŋ binaŋ eŋarehuc bubiaŋ qaŋareocte sorepe fakac hâcne .
49006023	Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eki âgofâc-nane ŋoŋe wama bâfua-ŋarehuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic basanaŋkeme maŋjauŋhec junšepieŋ .
49006024	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo erao qohota sanaŋkeeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋerao aki anonoczi fozejec .
50001001	Paulo â Timoteo , Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa , nâhe Filipi haeonec Kristo Jesure mitiŋic ŋokac â soŋaŋ babafic ŋoŋere papia ši râekoperec .
50001002	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
50001003	No ŋoŋere manasuhuc Sâc Anutu-nane daŋge âzâcneekopac .
50001004	Ŋoŋe Biŋebiaŋ manahuc izia nâŋehec qâturerâ giene bawarehuc jumbiŋ ,
50001005	eme irec numuekopac sâc mâmâc-ŋeŋicte bubiaŋ manahuc Wofuŋ daŋge numumu ecneekopac .
50001006	Erâ šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac , gie biaŋ ŋoŋerao fuŋkeweczi baku bataraha Jesu Kristo fifisi dameŋ-ticne maickezokac .
50001007	No ŋoŋe sasawa iŋuc mana-ŋarekopac i fuŋne šiŋucte sâckekac : No šira kâpâcwâru ficko Biŋebiaŋte erâ dâŋgie bahuc feŋeŋ râecnepe ŋoŋe sasawa baficnuhuc ŋesiŋ ŋenareeŋgopieŋ ” eme no irec hâcne maŋnanezi šâfic-ŋopaekopac .
50001008	Jesu Kristozi maŋjauŋ enâreekac ira hesiŋnehuc no ŋoŋere erâ maŋhâhâŋ boc enareekac , i Anutuzi manaha jâmbomac mukopac .
50001009	Erâ maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋiczi maŋ mamanasu â mamana wosâc-ŋeŋic bâsoka raocte numuhuc juekopac .
50001010	Eme ŋoŋe wiac fâri wâmbuŋne hone šâŋitac erâ Kristo fifisi-ticnere manasuhuc maŋtaniŋ â bahacmâc junšepieŋ ,
50001011	ehuc Jesu Kristozi hume keteŋ eŋareme mitire fârine mâririhec bâfuapie Anuture šeri mumuteŋ ezejec .
50001012	Âgofâc-nane , kâuc banšipiŋte ŋazape , no šira wiac fua-narewec izi Biŋebiaŋ hatacke hâmoocte fuawec .
50001013	No Kristore erâ kâpâcwâru ŋic epo , dâŋ izi šira kia â momori â ŋic gâcne jaŋere hazecko hufârewec .
50001014	Eme kâpâcwâruo ŋehape širecnec âgofâc-nâŋec gâcne sâko jaŋe Wofuŋte manasuhuc afeckerâ Anuture dâŋ hâhâwic tâmiric mueŋgopieŋ .
50001015	Tucne Kristore miti i iiŋguuŋko â hehefaricko mueŋgopieŋ , â tucnezi ine buurucko mueŋgopieŋ .
50001016	I jaŋe mueŋgopieŋ ine no šira fohuc Biŋebiaŋ ŋezickeekopac irec maŋjauŋ enarehuc mueŋgopieŋ ,
50001017	â gâcnezi ine sioc ehuc iiriacko Kristore šâŋe muromackeeŋgopieŋ , i kâpâcwâru-nanere faio bušâic bâfua-nareniŋte eeŋgopieŋ .
50001018	Erâ iŋuc me iŋuc , miti qâtiŋ ehuc muniŋmu me jâmbomacko muniŋmu irec wemocte boc muzo , mâc Kristore dâŋzi haŋ baocmu izi fârine , eme i fuakacte bunane biaŋkekac .
50001019	Erâ šiŋuc muhuc bubiaŋ hati jupemu : Ŋoŋe nore erâ nunumu gie bapie Jesu Kristore Mârozi baficnume wiac kecšizi bubiaŋ bâfua-nareocmu .
50001020	Erâ mimi mi bâfuapemu , i manapaŋkepe šickeha maŋzi worickehuc jupemu . Ewarepo iŋuc erapemu , jujure me hâhâmore sahac-nane maŋafec jaha Kristo qikiŋnecnepe izi mumuteŋ-ticne ezejec .
50001021	Kristozi juju-nane ekac â hâmoczi wiac fekicne bâfua-nareocmu .
50001022	Me mâreŋko šuhuckerâ jupemu , ine giere fârine mocwâc bâfuapemu . Irec wenimoire afeckepe muhuc maŋguru ekopac .
50001023	No mocte â mocte mâmâc enarekac . Mâreŋ beherâ Kristo bâfuarâ ehec juju irec aŋacnukac , izi hâcne wiac fekicne .
50001024	Á ŋoŋe bekâ enšipiŋte ine ŋoŋere erâ mâreŋko mocwâc šuhuckerâ jupe sâckeocmu .
50001025	Eme irec hâcne šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac : No mi hâhâmo ŋoŋehec jupemu , erâ bafic-ŋopape mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic ɋârâŋkeme bubiaŋhec junšepieŋ .
50001026	Á ŋoŋerao mocwâc fârâ jupe nore erâ Jesu Kristo muteŋkeeŋgopieŋzi hati erâ muteŋkenšepieŋ .
50001027	Mocjaha , ŋoŋe kikefuŋte maio Kristore furu Biŋebiaŋ irec sâcko junšepieŋ . Erâ maŋ mocjaha ehuc šâšâfic erâ keketeŋ domahuc Biŋebiaŋte juju gie bapie fârâ honec-ŋopazepac , me taicko juhuc biŋe-ŋeŋic manazepac .
50001028	Keketeŋ epie kisâfâc-ŋeŋic hâhâwic heŋarepie hâbi-ŋeŋic mi goroŋkezejec . Iŋuc epie Anutuzi jaŋe behec-jopaocmu â ŋoŋe rocŋopaocmu irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu .
50001029	Anutuzi Kristo wiac ecneniŋte mana-ŋarewec i manasiŋkeniŋte sawa mâcne , ere erâ šâic fâro faio juniŋte mâmâc mana-ŋarewec .
50001030	Eme no mârâcko juju gie bape honecnumbiŋ â šiŋuczia bape biŋene manaeŋgopieŋ , juju gie ijaha ŋoŋe baeŋgopieŋ .
50002001	Ŋoŋerao Kristore erâ sawaŋ qaqac me maŋjauŋko muketeŋ , me Mârohec šâšâfic , me miriŋ â buuruc , wiac i sasawa fokacko
50002002	bubiaŋ-nane ferâ foocte mamanasu-ŋeŋic qâturenšepieŋ , erâ maŋzi šâšâfic ehuc mocjaha efârerâ wiac irecteaŋ henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ .
50002003	Ŋoŋe hehefaricko â sahac mumuteŋko wiac mi enšepieŋ , moc e jahacne maŋ bawahahuc âgofâcne jaŋere maname fezejec .
50002004	Erâ moc e jahacne wiac embiaŋkeocte sawa mâcne , âgofâcne jaŋere fua biaŋ eocte mâmâc manasuzejec .
50002005	Kristo Jesure maŋ mamanasu fowec , iŋuc jaha ŋoŋerezi fozejec .
50002006	E Anutu juju juweczi ine , Anuture sâcko juekopac weniŋuc behepemu , iŋuc muhuc mi sakarewec .
50002007	Aricne , e juju-ticne hetararâ kiŋaŋ qaqa hawari rohuc ŋic iŋucne fuawec , â eebapa-ticne honepie ŋic nâŋâcne sâc ewec .
50002008	E wahakicne erâ juhuc micrereŋte hata âte raku hâmoc maickewec , maripoŋko hâmoc hâcne .
50002009	Iŋuc ewecte Anutuzi bafehuc fekicne sâko âkendâŋnewec . Âkendâŋnerâ šâŋe biŋe-ticne fuŋmoc izi haŋ bahuc ŋic šâŋe biŋe getâcke-fâreocte mucnewec .
50002010	Eme sambâŋko â mâreŋko â mâreŋ jujuwicnao jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeŋgoma Jesure šâŋe muhuc dieŋzi hecnenšepieŋ
50002011	â micne mic sâc Jesu Kristo e Wofuŋ jukac iŋuc musereckenšepieŋ . Eme mumuteŋ izi Anutu Mamacte biŋe ezejec .
50002012	Jorocfâc-nane , ŋoŋe dameŋ sâc micrereŋ eeŋgopieŋ , ŋoŋehec juhape sawa mâcne , taicko juhape wâc ejâmbâŋkeeŋgopieŋ , irec bâbâpiaŋ-ŋeŋicte fârine bâfuaniŋte mezac-ŋopaha fotac qatarienšepieŋ .
50002013	Anutu e jahac hâcne , honec-ŋopame biaŋkeocte aafecke mecne fârine bâbâfua mecne irec tâpiri ŋareekac .
50002014	Ŋoŋe wiac sasawa kâroŋ â maŋguru tâmiric enšepieŋ .
50002015	Erâ bahacmâc â maŋtaniŋ junšepieŋ , ehuc ŋicguru bac bâŋoricne â qaqaharicne jaŋere dapâc ŋondeŋko Anuture naru motecfâc maŋɋaɋac erâ juhuc bâpiŋ iŋucne tamaenšepieŋ .
50002016	Tamaehuc jujure dâŋ paŋnea bajunšepieŋ . Iŋuc epie juku Kristo fifisi dameŋ-ticnao , šâic mi mana-bipiepo â gie mi bâipiepo , irec fuŋne taniŋkeme šeri bubiaŋ manazepac .
50002017	No mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic Anutu taha bacnehuc sahac-nane due bapemuo sifu irec šeri ehuc ŋoŋehec bubiaŋ manapemu .
50002018	Á ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha šeri ehuc nohec bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ .
50002019	Wofuŋ Jesuzi maname sâckeme Timoteo biac ŋoŋerao sorepe fâocte mukopac . Eme ŋoŋere dâŋ biŋe moc risie wareme manarâ bunane mâteŋkezejec .
50002020	Ŋic e iŋucne moc mi junareŋgopieŋ , eki jâmbomac ŋoŋere manoniehuc maŋticnezi dopec-ŋopaocmu .
50002021	Ŋic gâcne jaŋe jaŋacnere sawa manasuhuc Jesu Kristo gie-ticnere mi mueŋgopieŋ .
50002022	Timoteo ine juju-ticnere fuŋne manaeŋgopieŋ , ŋokâzi mamac-ticne bafickeekac iŋuc jaha no Biŋebiaŋte giere baficnuekac .
50002023	Eme no nahacnao wiac iŋuc me iŋuc fuaocmu i mana-hâmorâ e hâcne biac sorepe fâocmu .
50002024	Erâ Wofuŋzi mana-nareme no nahac wâc mi šoraha ŋoŋerao fâpemu , iŋuc manakopac .
50002025	No wiac basahuc juhape ŋoŋe Epafodito sorepie ware dope hutuŋ enarewec , ehuc qomâ-nane â babafic-nane â momori âgo-nane juekac , e sifu bârisie-ŋarezo mukopac .
50002026	E huc bame biŋene manambiŋ , eme ere manabâc enšipiŋte ŋoŋere maŋhâhâŋ ecnekac .
50002027	E huc ŋemâcne bame hâmozo ewec . Anutuzi ine ehâmocnewec , erâ e sawa mâcne , norao busâqoczi busâqoc fuazacte no mâmâc ehâmo-narewec .
50002028	Ŋoŋe honerâ buŋeŋic biaŋkeocte â no iŋuc jaha manabâc tâmiric jupemurâ e mi sakarehuc šiŋuczia râepe fakac .
50002029	Irec fâme bubiaŋ manacnehuc Wofuŋte erâ âgo ecnenšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe ŋic iŋucne hâcne sâsec-jopanšepieŋ .
50002030	E Kristore giere erâ hâmozo ewec . Ŋoŋere okacne kiŋaŋ qanareocte sahac-ticne qaisockewec .
50003001	Âgofâc-nane , moc mupe . Wofuŋte erâ bubiaŋhec junšepieŋ . Dâŋ hâsine ijaha qâreŋke-ŋarezore manape mi quŋkekac , â ŋoŋe ine hume keteŋ eŋarezejec .
50003002	Ŋoŋe qâto jaŋere rucsoŋaŋ junšepieŋ , miti gie bapa bâbâsifucne , sahac hehetâc ŋic jaŋere rucsoŋaŋ hâcne junšepieŋ .
50003003	Anutu maŋzi kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopeneŋ â Kristo Jesurao qohotaeŋgopeneŋ â mamanasiŋ-nâŋec sahacko mi râeeŋgopeneŋ , nâŋâc hâcne ma fârine bajueŋgopeneŋ .
50003004	No nahac sahacko siŋkezo murâ sâcne ezapo . Ŋic gâcne jaŋe sahacko siŋkeeŋgopieŋ no ijaha ezo murâ siric-jopazapo .
50003005	No fuarâ fohape šoaŋ 8 eme sahac-naneo ma bambiŋ , no Israe ŋicguruonec , Benjamiŋte ɋâric , no Judaŋiczi Judaŋic jaŋeraonec fuakicne hâcne , sâcmutâc dâŋte neŋgocne farisaio ŋic jupo ,
50003006	šoɋac-nanere erâ kikefuŋ jaŋere râsi epo , sâcmutâc dâŋ sâcko tiŋne juju â bahacmâc jupo .
50003007	Eme no mârâc wiac bajuhuc manape fârine ewec , i šâhec ine Kristore erâ manape racne ewec .
50003008	No Wofuŋ-nane Kristo Jesu ere fuŋne hone šâŋitâc erâ manape furi sâko eme wiac mârâc epo bapo irec jâmbomac manape racne eekac . No Kristo rauckepemurâ ere erâ wiac sasawa ho jawa muhuc qikiŋne-fârepo .
50003009	No erao qohotahuc , sâcmutâc reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc bâbâfua i mâcne . Kristo manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc juju irec enareekac . Mamanasiŋhec jupe Anutuzi kiŋnanere maname tatara , irec mukopac .
50003010	Erâ no Kristo maŋzi hemiriŋkepe fafahare-ticnere tâpiri norao fuame šâic manawecko šuhuckerâ ehec manazepac . Eku hâmoc-ticnere hawari wâc bâfuazepac .
50003011	Iŋuc eerâ raku hâmockonec fafahare bâfuapere enareekac .
50003012	No nahacnere šiŋuc mi mukopac : Biac mao fisirâ eri bâfuapo . Mâc Kristo Jesuzi no rocnuwecte eri bâfuapemurâ hata gagasa i gasackeekopac
50003013	Âgofâc-nane , eri biac bâfuarâ ropo , i no nahacnere manape iŋuc mi ekac Kecšiŋuc ine eekopac : Wiac hetarapo i râpeckeekopac , â wiac mai-naneo râekicne irec menane sicneekopac ,
50003014	ehuc Anutuzi Jesu Kristore erâ sambâŋte hefârecnuhuc mao eri râe-narewec , i bâfuapemurâ šâŋezi hone dendeŋnehuc gasackeekopac .
50003015	Soka tarakicne nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa wiac irecteaŋ hâcne henširiŋnehuc junšepeneŋ . Eme wiac mocte manapie hatane moc ekacko Anutuzi maŋŋeŋic batamaeme mana taraniŋmu .
50003016	Mâc hata âte warembeŋ ijaha âte ranšepeneŋ .
50003017	Âgofâc-nane bânie-ŋarepe honecnuhuc ijaha bâjâpecnunšepieŋ . Á ŋic gâcne sâc ijaha juhuc bânie-ŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋerao wâc šâŋe fihuc junšepieŋ .
50003018	Ŋic tucne jaŋere ŋaza warehuc jupo , ši ine ki busâqochec mocwâc ŋazape : Jaŋe Kristo maripoŋ-ticne râsi ecneeŋgopieŋ .
50003019	Ŋic i jaŋe hâcne sisipiric bâfuaniŋmu . Hobu-jeŋiczi wofuŋ ejareekac , â wiac mimineheczi bubiaŋ qajareekac , â mâreŋkonec wiac maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic rofâreekac .
50003020	Nâŋâc ine sambâŋ hae irec fârine , eme irecnec hâcne bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo , e waharâ rocnâpoocte woŋec jueŋgopeneŋ .
50003021	E ŋic â wiac sasawa bawahac-joparâ jahacne rurumaŋko guruc-jopaocte tâpiri focnekac , tâpiri izi sahac-nâŋec waha qaqane bâtikieme e jahacne sahac iŋucne tatamac huririnehec eocmu .
50004001	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , maŋnane ŋoŋere boc ecneekac , ŋoŋe hâcne eri bubiaŋfâc-nane , ŋoŋe Wofuŋtao qohota sanaŋkenšepieŋ , jorocfâc-mae .
50004002	Euodia â Sintike ŋokac jahec jahe Wofuŋte erâ maŋ mocjaha erâ juzepirec .
50004003	Á babafic fâri-nane go ine ŋokac jahec hâcne hone maiŋ ejactezemec . Jahe mecne â Kelemento â âgo gâcne jaŋe Biŋebiaŋte giere dopecnumbiŋ . Ʒâŋe-jeŋic juju sanaŋte papia qizecko fofârekac .
50004004	Ŋoŋe Wofuŋte erâ šeri bubiaŋ manahuc junšepieŋ , no harierâ mupe , šeri bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ .
50004005	Wofuŋzi bâqiŋ-nâpokacte ŋic sasawa wamane ejarenšepieŋ .
50004006	Wiac irec me irec mana mezac mi ee maŋŋeŋicte dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne i Anutu daŋge nunumu ecnehuc mutaniŋkecnenšepieŋ .
50004007	Eme Anuture wama e ŋic mamana sirickeekaczi maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic qâzuckeme Kristore fosanaŋkeocmu .
50004008	Erâ âgofâc , dâŋ moc mupe : Wiac fârine â wiac araŋ bapanehec , wiac tiŋne â wiac ɋaɋacne , wiac hohone šiziwene â wiac mamana šiziwene , wiac eesaricne â wiac bubiaŋ bâbâfuane , wiac i sasaware henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ .
50004009	No wiac mu qazuc â ŋaza ŋowatuc epe hone manac embiŋ , ijaha ehuc jupie Anutu wama runezi ŋoŋehec juocmu .
50004010	Ŋoŋe ŋondeŋne moc mâc juwareku ši nore mocwâc manasurâ buafec-ŋeŋicte ehâmo-narembiŋ , irec manape Wofuŋtao qacneme bubiaŋ kâcɋene manakopac . Ŋoŋe nore mamanasu i manasumbiŋ , mâc wiac enareniŋte hata basarâ quŋkembiŋ .
50004011	No kâroŋ qaŋarehuc mi mukopac , no wiac i me i basarâ mâc juhuc manape mi sâqoreekac .
50004012	No qafec qawahac juju me fofo dunduŋ fonareha juju , iŋuc me iŋuc juzo murâ sâcne jupemu . Nâ gapehec juju â natac qatac juju , mâriri faio juju â roroc faio juju , irec fuŋne mâmâc manaekopac .
50004013	Tâpiri nareme sanaŋkeekopac , ere erâ jupe bape sâcke-fâreekac .
50004014	Ŋoŋe ine busâqocko juhape ehâmo-narembiŋte manape biaŋkekac .
50004015	Filipi haeonec ŋic ŋokac ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ , no Biŋebiaŋte gie fufuŋke dameŋko Makedonia mâreŋ behepoo kikefuŋ gâcnezi mâc juhapie ŋoŋe buc nohec nareŋ gareŋ embeŋ .
50004016	Erâ Tesalonike haeo juhape sahacte wiaczi dopecnuhuc jumbiŋ wâc .
50004017	No moneŋ mafare mi mukopac , mâc miti-ŋeŋicte fârine fuaocte mukopac , eme fârine izi ŋoŋeraopec hamârekao hâcne .
50004018	Ʒi wiac bâfuacnu-fârewec , bocjaha fonarekac . Epafoditozi ŋoŋeraonec wiac bafisi-nareme mâririhec epo jukopac . Ŋoŋe no wiac enarembiŋ , irec manape Wofuŋ taha bâzi biaŋ âsu mumundoŋnehec ecnembiŋ ekac .
50004019	Anutu-nane e mâriri bâbâfuazi Kristo Jesure erâ wiac hezu heŋareme hâmoc huriaŋ tâmiric juniŋmu .
50004020	Anutu Mamac-nâŋec erao ine mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
50004021	No Kristo Jesure erâ manasuc-ŋopakopac , i mitiŋic ŋokac jaza-fârenšepieŋ . Á âgofâc-nane nohec juŋgopieŋ jaŋe wâc manasuc-ŋopaŋgopieŋ .
50004022	Mitiŋic sasawa â Sisare ŋicfâc jaŋe wâc boc manasuc-ŋopaŋgopieŋ .
50004023	Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicko fofârezejec . Jâmbomac .
51001001	Paulo no Anuture micte Jesu Kristore aposolo epo , erâ âgo-nâŋec Timoteo ,
51001002	nâhe Kolosai haeonec mitiŋic â âgofâc-nâhec Kristorao qohotaŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe papia ši râe-ŋarekoperec . Anutu Mamac-nâŋec eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
51001003	Nâŋe Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Mamac Anutu hâcne ŋoŋere erâ dameŋ sâc daŋge nunumu ecneeŋgopeneŋ .
51001004	Ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ â mitiŋic hae gâcnaonec maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ irec mecne ,
51001005	â sambâŋ miti šeŋaŋ ŋoŋere biŋe râekicne irec mâmâc Anutu muteŋkeeŋgopeneŋ . Ŋoŋe miti šeŋaŋte kâuc mi baeŋgopieŋ . Dâŋ fâri qizecne Biŋebiaŋ hâcne ŋoŋerao fuawec irec biŋe mârâc manambiŋ .
51001006	Biŋebiaŋ i mâreŋ sâc fua bâbâriŋ rahuc fârinehec eekac . Eme Anutu akidâŋ-ticne ŋoŋerao fâme jâmbomacko mana maŋ embiŋ , dameŋ ira ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha fârinehec ewec .
51001007	Joroc âgo babafic-nâŋec Epafara , Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec , eki qazu-ŋareme manambiŋ hâcne .
51001008	Erâ ekizia wâc , Mârozi ŋoŋerao maŋjauŋ bâfuawec , irec dâŋ binaŋ enârewec .
51001009	Eme nâŋe dâŋ binaŋ-ŋeŋic manarâ izia fuŋkerâ Anutuzi maŋ mamana-ŋeŋic bâsokame micdâŋ-ticnere â Mârore maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ mana taraniŋte numucne warehuc jueŋgopeneŋ .
51001010	Wofuŋzi iŋuc hâcne eŋareme ju ju-ŋeŋiczi fuŋne-ticne mutaniŋkeme honec-ŋopame biaŋkezejec . Á mitio gie fuŋne fuŋne fokac , i bahuc irec fârine bâfuanšepieŋ , ehuc Anuture fuŋne mana ɋârâŋke rahuc junšepieŋ .
51001011	Erâ Anuture tâpiri mu wawarec-ticnehec izi âkesiŋ-ŋopame hâbi sâko hepie hume juhapie fai-ŋeŋicko wiac ŋemâcne feme sâc docke pârâc tâmiric bumâteŋ jaha de domahuc bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ .
51001012	Erâ Mamac-nâŋec e faic tatamacko merâfâc-ticne râe-nârewec , i mitiŋic nâŋâc ru sâc enaŋte bâmoc-nâpoekacte buafec jaha daŋge âzâcnenšepeneŋ .
51001013	Anutu e dâpac runere tâpirionec batarac-nâporâ joroc Ŋokâ-ticnere uucmaŋko râec-nâpowec .
51001014	Ŋokâ-ticne eki hâcne sâqocne-nâŋec tâmireote kiwiric-nâŋec rowec .
51001015	Anutu soŋne ere hawari tâtâc fufua Ŋokâ-ticne hâcne . E wiac sasawa mi fuahame micne barâ juweczi juwec .
51001016	Ere jujuo wiac sasawa sambâŋko â mâreŋko fua-fârewec , wiac hohonene â mi hohonene , ŋic me aŋelo ɋuŋɋasaŋhec me tâpirihec , fekicne sâko me araŋ bapa-jarene , i mâmâc sasawa ere tâpirio â ere biŋe fuakicne .
51001017	E wiac sasawa irec juwicnao juwec erâ wiac sasawa irec micne sâko , erâ wiac sasawa ere dope sisiŋko fowarehuc juekac .
51001018	Erâ e me sahac-ticne , kikefuŋ-ticne hâcne , nâŋâcne qizec juekac . Erâ fufuŋke ŋic , hâmockonec micne barâ faharewec , ehuc wiac sasawa irec jâcne ewec .
51001019	Anutu e juju â tâpiri-ticnere rowaŋ Ŋokârao guru fufusuc foocte maname sâckewec .
51001020	Erâ wiac sasawa sambâŋko â mâreŋko Anutu jahacnehec miriŋ bacnâpoocte mucneme eki hâcne maripoŋko socticnezi wama bâfuahuc iŋuc ewec .
51001021	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha Anutu râpeckerâ nâme nikecne erâ sâqocne fuŋne fuŋne bahuc maŋšârâhec jujumbieŋ .
51001022	Eme Kristo sahac biuchec fuarâ hâmoc-ticnezi miriŋ bacŋoparâ Anuture maio furu â maŋɋaɋac â bahac fâsâc juniŋte râec-ŋopawec .
51001023	Eme irec ŋoŋe mamanasiŋko qiŋ herâ domahuc , Biŋebiaŋzi woworic bâfua-ŋarewec i sifucke-ŋarezacte biric borocne mi enšepieŋ . Biŋebiaŋ i ŋoŋe qazu-ŋarekicne , erâ ŋoŋe sawa mâcne , ŋicne ŋicne mâreŋ sâc jaza rakicne . Paulo no hâcne irec kiŋaŋŋic juekopac .
51001024	No ŋoŋere erâ šâic serereŋ faio juekopac irec ši manape biaŋkeekac . Kristozi me sahac-ticne , kikefuŋ-ticne hâcne , ere erâ šâic serereŋ manawec , šâic irec tofanao šuhuckehuc mamanane fokacte nore sahacko fehuc micne qazejec .
51001025	No Anutu dâŋbiri-ticnere sâcko kikefuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa erâ ŋoŋerao micdâŋ-ticnere qaqazu gie batarapemurâ munarekicne .
51001026	Dâŋ i dameŋne dameŋne soŋne fome mimiŋzi ɋâric mi mamana mâc juwefuhuc jumbiŋ , eme dameŋ šiŋuczia ine mitiŋicfâc-ticne mufua-nârekicne .
51001027	Erâ qâpuc jaŋerao dâŋ soŋnere mâriri biaŋ sâko fuakac i mitiŋicfâc-ticne mutaniŋke-nârekac . Kristo maŋŋeŋicko juekac e hâcne dâŋ soŋnere fârine â sambâŋ šeŋaŋ irec hozine .
51001028	Ere fuŋne mutaniŋkehuc ŋicne ŋicne uŋ sawaŋ ejarerâ maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ sasawa jaza qazuc eeŋgopeneŋ , i Kristoo ŋic fârine epie erao guruc-jopanaŋte iŋuc eeŋgopeneŋ .
51001029	Ere tâpirizi eferenšoŋnume gie i hâcne fotariehuc baekopac .
51002001	No ŋazape mananiŋ , ŋoŋe mecne â Laodikea haeonec â ŋic gâcne šâŋe mai-nane mi honembiŋ , ŋoŋere šâic afecne mi manaekopac .
51002002	Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋiczi âte tâcnerâ roroc efâreme Anutu dâŋsoŋ-ticnere fuŋne , Kristo hâcne , mana maŋ ehuc mana utuckerâ mana taranšepieŋ .
51002003	Erao hâcne maŋɋârâŋ â mamana tara irec šâkâŋne soŋkekicne fokac .
51002004	Moczi moc mu hemiriŋ eŋarehuc maŋ bâsifuc eŋarenšipiŋte dâŋ mukopac .
51002005	No sahac-nanezi wiwicko juekopac , maŋnanezi ine ŋoŋehec juhuc ŋoŋe Kristo manasiŋkehuc šišimic erâ sosoŋaŋko domapie honec-ŋoparâ bunane biaŋkekac .
51002006	Ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu Wofuŋ eŋareocte rombiŋ erao qohotahuc junšepieŋ ,
51002007	ehuc eraoa gâtâ barâ fua-hâmonšepieŋ , â mamanasiŋte hata ŋaza ŋowatuc ekicne ijaha âte sanaŋkerâ daŋge mumuteŋ ecnehuc jupie ferâ fe ehuc fozejec .
51002008	Moczi moc ŋickonec mamana dâŋ , eeatuc dâŋ racne hâcne , qazu-ŋarehuc maŋŋeŋic bawisenšipiŋte rucŋeŋic banšepieŋ . Dâŋ iŋucne i mimiŋne jaŋere maŋko fuac dâŋ â mâreŋte wiac tâpirihec ira roweckehuc mueŋgopieŋ , Kristorao siŋkehuc mâcne .
51002009	Manaŋgopieŋ , Anuture sâc i Kristo maŋ sahac-ticnao qaja fuserâ qâniniwerâ fokac .
51002010	Irec ŋoŋe erao wiac moc mi basaniŋmu , eki hâcne micne â fekicne sasawa jaŋere qizecne .
51002011	Eraonec maŋeŋic wâc rombiŋ , mezi sahacko ma bapa i mâcne , juju-ŋeŋic raŋɋane heunuckehuc Kristore maqâreŋhec embiŋ hâcne .
51002012	Ihec eniŋte Miti Opâ rua-ŋarehuc ere hâmocko šuhuc-ŋopakicne , erâ Anutu e tâpiri-ticnezi Kristo hâmockonec bâɋârewec , tâpiri ijaha manasiŋkepie ŋoŋerao fotâcneme fafahare-ticnao wâc šuhuc-ŋopakicne .
51002013	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha ma tâmiric juhuc sâqocne kosa barâ hâmocne juhapie Anutu e kiŋŋeŋic behehuc Kristohec bâɋârec-ŋopawec .
51002014	Erâ dâŋ qaqatara-nâŋec qâreŋkekicne i âke sifuckehuc irec kiŋ papia i bâsuckerâ maripoŋko ɋetickeme arictâc ewec .
51002015	Iŋuc ehuc fekicne â tâpirihec hâbi-jeŋic bâŋgoroŋkerâ saoreŋ qahuc fuŋne-jeŋic bataniŋkewec .
51002016	Ŋic moczi nânâ qowi soware me sabata hombaŋ me mosa hombaŋ i me i ŋeŋere me mi ŋeŋere mu supaic mi eŋarezejec .
51002017	Wiac iŋucnere nâkumucne muzo , fârine šâhec fuaocte irec nâkumucnezi qanaŋ bâniewec . Á fârine ine Kristorao fuawec fokac .
51002018	Ŋic gâcnezi maŋhuhuŋ hawari erâ juhuc aŋelo araŋ bajareeŋgopieŋ , â maŋnâŋec ŋerisieme wiac honeeŋgopeneŋ muhuc irec manapie fârine eme sahac-jeŋic maŋgâŋ mušoraeŋgopieŋ , ŋic iŋucne jaŋe boreŋ fâri-ŋeŋic mi ŋowac ronšepieŋ .
51002019	Jaŋe hâcne Kristorao sâcne mi siŋkeeŋgopieŋ . Eki qizec-nâŋec â nâŋâc me sahac-ticne . Eme qizeckonec ruazi fâuckerâ wahahuc me kike fâri ombâŋ-ticne basanaŋ-nâpohuc bândeŋ-nâpoekac . Ehuc gume hesiwiŋ enâreme soka sanaŋte tâpiri Anuturaonec fua-nâreekac .
51002020	Ŋoŋe Kristore hâmocko šuhuckehuc mâreŋte wiac tâpirihec râpeckembiŋko wemocte mâreŋte hae fâri juhuc tinac sâcmutâc dâŋticne reŋkeeŋgo-pieŋ ?
51002021	Dâŋ kecšiŋuc : “ Keci mi bâuac , keci mi nâc , keci mi roc . ”
51002022	Wiac nâ bac erâ bebehene hâcne , irec kibâtâc dâŋ i ŋiczi maŋjeŋicte manasurâ mu qaqazuc eeŋgopieŋ .
51002023	Ŋic iŋucnezi maŋɋârâŋ hawari erâ “ bâtâcko â sowa juhuc sahac bâpitiwazo ” iŋuc mupie dâŋ izi fârine tinac eekac . Erâ wiac iŋucnezi fârine aricne , izi sasec aka sâcne mi hecneocmu .
51003001	Ŋoŋe Kristo fafahare-ticnao šuhuckembiŋko ine faic Anuture maŋfuŋko Kristo jukacko wiac fokac , irec henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ .
51003002	Mâreŋko wiac fokac irec mâcne , faic wiac fokac irec maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic râepie fozejec .
51003003	Ŋoŋe hâmombiŋ hâcne , eme juju-ŋeŋic Kristohec Anuturao soŋkekicne fokac .
51003004	Juku Kristo e juju runâŋeczi fua taniŋkeme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ehec mâmâc tatamac huririnao fua taniŋkeniŋmu .
51003005	Wiac kecšiŋucte ine sowa juhuc sahac-ŋeŋic bâhâmonšepieŋ : Boe sau , maŋwânâŋ , bu gâgâpâcne , sasec sâqocne , buchâro , i eocmu e sahac-ticnezi wofuŋ ecnekac muzo .
51003006	Wiac i sasaware Anuturaonec okacne fisiocmu .
51003007	Ŋoŋe mârâcko iŋuc jaha wiac i bajupie maŋ fâri-ŋeŋic ejujec .
51003008	Ʒi ine wiac iŋucne sasawa hetaranšepieŋ . Ehuc aaric , kimbeŋ , râŋgeŋ bârâŋgeŋ , dâŋ gâgâpâcne â simbiŋne i qikiŋnenšepieŋ .
51003009	Burec eec i wâc mi enšepieŋ . Maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic mâsi qâqâreŋ-ticnehec heunucke behec erâ
51003010	maŋɋâri-ŋeŋic hepie hume rojuŋgopieŋ . Maŋ i hâcne bâbâfuazi bâpiaŋkeme mamanahec erâ e jahacne hawari iŋucne fuahuc jukac .
51003011	Irec bârâwiŋ juju i tarawec , Grikŋic â Judaŋic , mahec â ma tâmiric , hâwecŋic â kâte sanaŋ , kiŋaŋ qaqa â ŋicbomboŋ , mâmâc sasawa Kristozi qâhâc-nâporâ micne junâre-fâreekac .
51003012	Eme Anuture biŋefâc , e jahac maŋjauŋ eŋarehuc rowosâec-ŋopawec , ŋoŋe buuruc â buafec â maŋhuhuŋ â miriŋ â bumâteŋ izi ŋaqi-ŋeŋic eme hepie hume rojunšepieŋ .
51003013	Ŋoŋe aakic enšepieŋ , â ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko dâŋ fuame kiŋ bebehec enšepieŋ . Wofuŋzi kiŋ behe-ŋarewec iŋuc jaha eec enšepieŋ .
51003014	Eme wiac sasawa irec fainao maŋjauŋ bajupie izi wiac bâture-fârehuc ematauckezejec .
51003015	Erâ Kristore wamazi maŋŋeŋicko guriŋne bazejec . Ŋoŋe wamahec erâ me sahac mocjahao juniŋte rocŋopakicne hâcne . Erâ wâc daŋge mumuteŋ ehuc junšepieŋ .
51003016	Kristore dâŋzi ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko sawe mâririackezejec . Eme maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne qaqazuc ehuc faŋ qaqac enšepieŋ . Erâ miti gae mânec i Mârozi baafec-ŋopaha maŋŋeŋiczi Anutu muteŋkehuc hecnenšepieŋ .
51003017	Eme maŋzi me mezi wiac ezo murâ i Wofuŋ Jesu manasiŋkehuc enšepieŋ , ehuc ere erâ Anutu Mamac daŋge âzâcnenšepieŋ .
51003018	Ŋokac ŋoŋe ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere rereŋfâc junšepieŋ , Wofuŋte biŋe ekicnezi iŋuc epie sâckeocmu .
51003019	Ŋic ŋoŋe ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarenšepieŋ , šâšâicne ine mi ejarenšepieŋ .
51003020	Naru motec ŋoŋe neŋgoc mamacfâc-ŋeŋic dâŋ mupie sâc reŋkenšepieŋ , iŋuc epie Wofuŋzi maname biaŋkeocmu .
51003021	Mamac ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic hâwic sahac enšipiŋte aaricko wiac mi ejarenšepieŋ .
51003022	Kiŋaŋ qaqa ŋoŋe mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere mic reŋke-fârenšepieŋ , maizi qambaraŋ ejarepie ŋiczi sawa honec-ŋopapie sâckeocte mâcne , maŋsiocmâc Wofuŋ araŋ bacnehuc epie sâckeomu .
51003023	Gie-ŋeŋic sasawa i ŋic jaŋere erâ mâcne , Wofuŋte erâ aafec faio banšepieŋ .
51003024	Kecšiŋuc manahuc : Gie furi sambâŋko merâfâc fokac i Wofuŋtaonec roniŋmu . Irec Wofuŋ Kristo ere kiŋaŋ qaqafâc juŋgopieŋ hâcne .
51003025	Moc e gie-ticne bâsâqoreocmu , e irec okacne jaha roocmu . Wofuŋtao ra rowec ware rowec mi fokac .
51004001	Ŋicbomboŋ ŋoŋe kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ŋeŋic wiac sâkoa etiŋnehuc ejarenšepieŋ , ehuc ŋaŋacne femicne Wofuŋ sambâŋko jukac i manasunšepieŋ .
51004002	Paŋšâic jaha numuhuc junšepieŋ . Erâ rucgereŋ juhuc daŋge nunumu enšepieŋ .
51004003	Erâ nâŋere wâc numupie Anutuzi mitire hata bâšâwe-nâreme Kristore dâŋ soŋne mufuanšepeneŋ . Dâŋ irec hâcne niŋgiŋko fokopac .
51004004	Nunumuzi dopecnupie dâŋ afeckehuc mujaŋgeŋkepe sâckezejec .
51004005	Qâpuc jaŋehec bâbâfuac erâ wiac mana tara-hâmohuc enšepieŋ . Ehuc gie bapa dameŋ mi sipirickenšepieŋ .
51004006	Dâŋŋeŋic hâwec ruacnepie aŋacne ezejec . Eme ŋic dâŋ iŋuc me iŋuc bâtikie-jareniŋte mi bititienšepieŋ .
51004007	No nahacne dâŋ binaŋ i Tikikozi eŋareocmu . E joroc âgo babafic-nâŋec â Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec .
51004008	E hâcne juju-nâŋecte dâŋ binaŋ eŋarehuc mu âkeriŋ eŋareocte ŋoŋerao sorepe fakac .
51004009	Erâ Onesimo , miti mamana âgo biaŋ-nâŋec , ŋoŋere haeonec , e mâmâc ecnepe fârâ širec dâŋ binaŋ eŋare-fâreocmu .
51004010	Kâpâcwâru ŋic âgo-nane Aristako â Banaba nafe-ticne Mareko â Jesu , šâŋe-ticne moc Justo , jaŋe manasu-ŋareŋgopieŋ . Mareko ere sâcmutâc eŋarepo , fâ fisiocmuo âgo ecnenšepieŋ .
51004011	Ŋic i jaŋe sawa Judaŋic jaŋeraonec fuakicnezi Anutu uucmaŋ-ticnere giere baficnueŋgopieŋ , ehuc bubiaŋ qanareeŋgopieŋ .
51004012	Erâ ŋoŋere haeonec ŋic moc Epafara , Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa , ere mamanac ŋoŋerao fokac , erâ ŋoŋe sanaŋkerâ Anuture micsâcko juhuc wiac mana tararâ etiŋneniŋte dameŋ sâc nunumuzi dopec-ŋopaekac .
51004013	No fuŋne-ticne manakopac , e ŋoŋere mecne erâ Laodikea haconec â Hierapoli haeonec mitiŋic jaŋere mecne mâmâc šâic gie wemo afecne baekac .
51004014	Luka dokta biaŋ-nâŋec â Dema jahe mu šeri eŋarekopirec .
51004015	Erâ no Laodikea haeonec mitiŋic â Nimfasi â wiacfâcne mu šeri ejarekopac i mufua-jarenšepieŋ .
51004016	Papia ši ŋic ŋokac wose-jarepie mana-fârepie Laodikea haeonec kikefuŋ jaŋerao râepie rame wosenšepieŋ . Á jaŋere moc qâreŋkepo iŋuc jaha ŋarepie wosenšepieŋ .
51004017	Arikipo e šiŋuc âzâcnenšepieŋ : “ Miti gie Wofuŋzi neŋgoc ŋeha mugarekicne i aijakic jaha bâhâmozemec . ”
51004018	Paulo no nahacne šâŋe qâreŋ ši râekopac . Kâpâcwâru ŋic nore manasunšepieŋ . Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec .
52001001	Paulo , Siliwano â Timoteo nâŋe Tesalonike haeonec kikefuŋ , Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere ŋicfâc , ŋoŋere papia ši râeŋgopeneŋ . Aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
52001002	Nâŋe dameŋ sâc ŋoŋere erâ Anutu daŋge âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ , erâ nunumu gie bahuc sâc ŋoŋere manasu-fâreeŋgopeneŋ .
52001003	Ŋoŋe mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte fârine bâfuaeŋgopieŋ â maŋjauŋte bâmec gie baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo paŋšâic jaha worickeeŋgopieŋ , irec Mamac-nâŋec Anutu ere maio hati manasurâ mufuahuc âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ .
52001004	Âgofâc , nâŋe manaŋgopeneŋ , Anutuzi maŋjauŋ eŋarehuc rowosâec-ŋopawec .
52001005	Iŋuc eŋarewecte Biŋebiaŋ bafârâ ŋazapene dâŋ sawa mi ewec , i tâpirihec â Tiri Mârohec â buâkecnehec ewec . Ŋoŋerao jumbeŋko ŋoŋere erâ wiac ebac embeŋ i manaŋgopieŋ .
52001006	Eme nâŋe bâjâpec-nâpombiŋ , bâjâpec-nâpohuc Wofuŋ e jahacne mâmâc bâjâpembiŋ . Ehuc miti i fific guguriŋ faio Tiri Mârozi bufahac qaŋarehame ro maŋ embiŋ .
52001007	Ŋoŋe iŋuc ehuc Makedonia â Akaia mâreŋkonec miti mamana jaŋe micne bajarehuc fuŋne qazu-jarembiŋ .
52001008	Ŋoŋeraonec hâcne Wofuŋte dâŋzi haŋ barahuc Makedonia â Akaia mâreŋko fuawec , erâ i sawa mâcne , ŋoŋe Anutu manasiŋkembiŋ irec dâŋ biŋe i hae sâc mana-fârepie nâŋe jajazane moc mi fuawec .
52001009	Jaŋe jaŋac ŋoŋerao gie bapene fârine fuawec irec dâŋ nâzâeŋgopieŋ . Erâ ŋoŋe nemuɋâŋ râpeckerâ Anutu jujune â fârine maickerâ ŋicfâc-ticne embiŋ ,
52001010	erâ Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârekicne , e juku sambâŋkonec waharâ okac dameŋko ŋezic-nâpozokac , ere šawiehuc jueŋgopieŋ , irec dâŋ binaŋ-ŋeŋic hae sâc eeŋgopieŋ .
52002001	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋerao fisirâ gie bapene fârimâc mi ewec i ŋaŋac manaŋgopieŋ .
52002002	Qanaŋ Filipi haeo qa imac enârembiŋ i manaŋgopieŋ wâc . Enârepie sifu mi dockembeŋ . Aricne , Anuturao roweckepene bubiaŋ qanâreme afeckerâ ŋoŋerao fârâ Anuture Biŋebiaŋ i juju gie sâko bahuc mufua-ŋarembeŋ .
52002003	Babaafec dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ i mamana sifuc faio mâcne , me maŋsifuc faio mâcne , me kege wage eŋarehuc mâcne ”
52002004	Anutuzi honec-nâpome sâckeme Biŋebiaŋ muromackenaŋte betoŋ-nâpowec irec sâc mueŋgopeneŋ . Ŋiczi mana-nârepie biaŋkeocte aricne , Anutu e maŋ hohonezi mana-nâreme biaŋkeocte mocjaha mueŋgopeneŋ .
52002005	Ŋoŋe nâŋere manaeŋgopieŋ , nâŋe bâbâmiriŋ dâŋ moc mi ŋazambeŋ mitio ake hehuc moneŋ mafare andac i wâc mi embeŋ , i Anutuzi manaha mukopac .
52002006	Kristore aposolo nâŋe mana-nârepie feme sâckeocmu i manahuc sifu ŋoŋe me hae gâcnaonec ŋicbomboŋ eŋarenaŋte mi mumbeŋ .
52002007	Aricne , neŋgoc moczi kogocfâcne hemiriŋ-jopaekac , iŋuc jaha nâŋe ŋoŋerao juhuc eŋarembeŋ .
52002008	Aŋac-nâŋec ŋoŋerao fowecte Anuture Biŋebiaŋ ŋaŋazare sawa mâcne , ŋoŋere erâ juju-nâŋec qiqikiŋ irec mâmâc afeckembeŋ , maŋnâŋec ŋoŋerao âeckewec irec .
52002009	Âgofâc , micneneŋ eŋarepene takic-ŋopazacte ŋafe furec sahacte gie mâmâc šocne fârone bahuc domambeŋ , i ehuc Anuture Biŋebiaŋ ŋazambeŋ , ŋoŋe irec manasueŋgopieŋ .
52002010	Nâŋe maŋtaniŋ â tiŋne â bahacmâc juhuc miti mamana ŋoŋe wiac eŋarembeŋ , i ŋoŋe mecne â Anutu mecne fuŋne-nâŋec manaŋgopieŋ .
52002011	Erâ moc šiŋuc wâc manaŋgopieŋ : Mamac moczi naru motecfâcne ejareekac , sâc ijaha nâŋe ŋoŋe eŋarehuc buc buc mu sawaŋ dâŋ ŋazambeŋ â esoc qafeŋ eŋarembeŋ â šiŋuc mušakiehuc ŋazambeŋ :
52002012	“ Uucmaŋ-ticne â eri tatamac-ticne rauckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopaekac Anutu hâcne , ere ŋicfâc fârine erâ irec sâcko junšepieŋ . ”
52002013	Nâŋe Anuture dâŋ ŋazapene manapie ŋicdâŋ mi ewec . Eme iŋuc sâcne manambiŋ , i Anuture dâŋ jâmbâŋ , eki miti mamana ŋoŋerao gie baekac . Eme nâŋe irec hâcne Anutu daŋge mumuteŋ kuduc jaha ecnehuc jueŋgopeneŋ .
52002014	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe Anuture kikefuŋ Judaia mâreŋko Kristo Jesurao qohotambiŋ jaŋehec sâc mocjaha embiŋ . Jaŋe Judaŋiczi jopa qâšâic ejarembiŋ iŋuc jaha âgofâc-ŋeŋic gâcnezi ŋoŋe ŋopa qâšâic eŋarembiŋ .
52002015	Judaŋic jaŋe Wofuŋ Jesu â porofete iŋuc jaha qâhâmoc-jopambiŋ , erâ wâc nâŋe nâpo jâpec enârembiŋ . Jaŋe Anutu âgo mi ecneeŋgopieŋ â ŋicne ŋicne kisuec-jopaeŋgopieŋ .
52002016	Ehuc qâpuc miti jazapene manarâ biaŋkenšipiŋte aka henareeŋgopieŋ . Jaŋe iŋuczi iŋuc ehuc sâqocne faio fefec hefekupie kiŋjeŋicte sâc micne qame Anuture kimbeŋ fisi-jarewec .
52002017	Âgofâc , nâŋe behec-ŋopambeŋ , erâ maŋzi mâcne , sahaczi dameŋ ŋondeŋ ši ŋoŋe tâmiric juhuc huacbuc eŋgopeneŋte mocwâc honec-ŋopanaŋte boc enâreekac .
52002018	Eme irec fârâ iqic-ŋopanaŋte mumbeŋ , Paulo no nahac dameŋ moc â moc fâzo mupe Sataŋzi aka henarewec .
52002019	Ŋoŋere aŋac-nâpoekac i šiŋucte : Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu ere fifisi dameŋko weni jaŋe gie fâri-nâŋec â šeri-nâŋec â eri-nâŋec eniŋmu ? Ŋoŋe wâc enâreniŋmu hâcne .
52002020	Ŋoŋe mumuteŋ-nâŋec â bubiaŋ-nâŋec .
52003001	Ŋoŋere maŋhâhâŋ boc enarekume nâŋe gâcnezi sifu Ateŋ haeo buc juhuc
52003002	Timoteo sorepene behec-nâporâ ŋoŋerao fâwec . E âgo-nâŋec â Anuture gieŋic juhuc Kristore Biŋebiaŋ muekaczi fârâ mitio hume keteŋ eŋarehuc faŋ qaŋareocte mucnembeŋ .
52003003	Ŋoŋe šârâ hâriŋ faio juhuc dockenšipiŋte iŋuc embeŋ . Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ , miti mâteŋne juhuc mananaŋte mi munârekicne .
52003004	Nâŋe ŋoŋerao juhuc qanaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc ŋazambeŋ : “ Ʒika biac fai-nâŋecko feocmu . ” Eme dâŋ i sanaŋkewec , i manaŋgopieŋ .
52003005	Eme eesâic runezi bârokawec-ŋopame gie-nanere fârine omaezacte maŋ kukumbuc boc enareme jupe bape sâqoreme ŋic e miti babaju-ŋeŋicte fuŋne manaocte sorepe fâwec .
52003006	Eme ši Timoteo e risie warerâ mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋicte biŋe biaŋ nâzâwec ” Erâ nâŋere boc manasueŋgopieŋ , â nâŋe ŋoŋe honec-ŋopazo muhapene ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha nâŋe honec-nâpozo mueŋgopieŋ , dâŋ i nâzâ-fârewec .
52003007	Âgofâc , nâŋe šârâ hâriŋ â bušâiczi maŋnâŋec hehâriŋkeme juhapene miti babaju-ŋeŋicte dâŋzi bunâŋec bâuruewec .
52003008	Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ heme hariŋ ecnehuc sanaŋkeeŋgopieŋ i manahuc maŋnâŋec fie ruruckekac .
52003009	Ŋoŋere erâ Anuture maio bubiaŋ sâko manaeŋgopeneŋte Anutu daŋge mo iŋucne ecnepene sâckeocmu ?
52003010	Mâc mana-nâreha ŋoŋerao fârâ hohonec erâ miti gâcne forakac i moc šuhucke-ŋarenaŋte ŋafe furec mu wâwâsic ecneeŋgopeneŋ .
52003011	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu e jahac hata bâfua-nâreme ŋoŋerao fânšepeneŋ .
52003012	Ŋoŋerao ine Wofuŋzi maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋic bâŋɋârâŋkeme ŋedâmâreme ŋaŋackoaŋ â gâcne jaŋehec eec enšepieŋ ” nâŋe iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe eŋareeŋgopeneŋ .
52003013	Erâ Anutuzi maŋŋeŋic keteŋkeme ŋoŋe Mamac-nâŋecte maio bahacmâc â maŋfuru juhapie Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu tiŋnefâc-ticne sasawa jaŋehec fisizejec .
52004001	Âgofâc-nane , Wofuŋ Jesure erâ uŋ sawaŋ eŋarehuc moc šiŋuc ŋazapene mananiŋ : Mitio juju bapa-ŋeŋiczi Anutu âgo ecneocte fuŋne ŋaza qazuc embeŋ , ijaha junšepieŋ . Mitio juju i sâcne jueŋgopieŋ , mâc juŋɋârâŋkeniŋte ŋazaŋgopeneŋ .
52004002	Wofuŋ Jesure micte dâŋ ŋaza qâmoc embeŋ , irec kâuc mi baŋgopieŋ .
52004003	Anutu e šiŋuc hâcne muekac : Boe sau qikiŋnehuc maŋɋaɋac junšepieŋ .
52004004	Ŋoŋerao moczi e jahacne ŋonâŋ maŋɋaɋacko â pectâcko rauckezejec ,
52004005	sasecte šocbâruŋko misac , i ŋic qâpuc Anuture kâuc baeŋgopieŋzi eeŋgopieŋ .
52004006	Moczi moc aka huckehuc wiac iŋucnao âgo-ticne mi eatuckezejec . Wofuŋ e wiac irec okacne bazu-fâreocmu ” nâŋe dâŋ i mârâc jaha mujomirerâ ŋazambeŋ .
52004007	Maŋwânâŋhec junaŋte aricne , maŋɋaɋac junaŋte Anutuzi hefârec-nâpowec .
52004008	Irec moc e dâŋ i bâsueocmu , e ŋic moc mâcne , Anuctu e jahacne bâsueocmu , Tiri Mâro maŋŋeŋicko râeekac e hâcne bâsueocmu .
52004009	Ŋoŋe miti mamanazi maŋzi jauŋ babac eniŋte wemocte boc qâreŋke-ŋarenaŋmu , Anutu e jahac maŋzi jauŋ babac eniŋte fuŋne ŋaza ŋowatuc ewec .
52004010	Erâ ŋoŋe Makedonia mâreŋ hae sâc opâ ruac juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋjauŋ ejarehuc jueŋgopieŋ . Erâ sifu mocwâc ɋârâŋkeocte ŋazaŋgopeneŋ .
52004011	Erâ dâŋ moc šiŋuc ŋaza qâmoc embeŋ : Rac warec juhuc dâŋ ojowa mi ee , hae-ŋeŋicko ŋezurâ ŋehuc mezi gie muŋarekicne aijakic jaha baniŋte ɋicwânšâŋ enšepieŋ .
52004012	Ehuc qâpuc jaŋere maio roroc tâmiric pectâc junšepieŋ .
52004013	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe hâmokicne jaŋere kâuc bârâ , miti tâmiriczi maŋjeŋic šickeme ki mamakuc eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc enšipiŋte ŋazapene mananiŋ :
52004014	Nâŋâc Jesu hâmorâ faharewec dâŋ i maŋkerâ šiŋuc mananšepeneŋ : Anutu e Jesu ecneme hâmokicne jaŋe e jahacnehec amec-jopa fisiocmu .
52004015	Á moc i Wofuŋ e jahacne micdâŋ ŋazanaŋ : Mâreŋko ɋâricne juhapene fisiocmu nâŋâc hâmokicne mi siric-jopanaŋmu .
52004016	Wofuŋ e sambâŋkonec wahaocte ine dâŋ wiwira â aŋelo qizecte micšonšoŋ â Anuture qeŋfânâŋ fuahame wahaocmu . Wahame Kristo manasiŋkehuc hâmombiŋ jaŋe bâbâni fahareniŋmu .
52004017	Faharepie ɋâricne junaŋmu , tiwâne hâcne , izi jaŋerao šuhuckepene karoraczi bafec-nâpome sawao Wofuŋhec bâbâfuac enaŋmu . Erâ Wofuŋhec juhuc junaŋmu sanaŋ .
52004018	Ŋoŋe dâŋ i hâcne muc manac ehuc maŋ bâbâmâteŋ enšepieŋ .
52005001	Âgofâc-nane , dameŋte â šâfore dâŋ wemocte moc qâreŋke-ŋare mu ?
52005002	Ŋaŋac šiŋuc sâcne manaŋgopieŋ : Râsi jaŋe ŋafeo ututuŋ fisieŋgopieŋ , iŋuc jaha dameŋ-ticne ɋeŋfâfâc jaha maickeocmu .
52005003	Eme ŋic jaŋe aki wama sâko fokac muhuc mana fâsâerâ juhapie wiac hâhâwicnezi acmâc jaha fisi-jareocmu . Ŋokac kiwechec moc e gozi onšoŋ jaha kime fâfâreocmu , iŋuc jaha ŋic iŋucne jaŋe wiac onšoŋ jaha fua-jareme wemocko moc wiseniŋmu .
52005004	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe ine dapâcko mi juŋgopieŋ , irec wemocko Wofuŋte dameŋzi râsi iŋucne erâ ututuŋ maic-ŋopame bipic tatara eniŋmu .
52005005	Ŋoŋe tatamacte â šoaŋte kikefuŋ ekicne , nâŋâc ŋafere me dapâcte biŋe aricne .
52005006	Irec ŋic gâcnezi guŋ fopie qâtec-joparâ guŋ mi fonšepeneŋ , rucgereŋ-nâŋec bahuc maŋte sowa junšepeneŋ .
52005007	Guŋ fofo jaŋe ŋafeo foeŋgopieŋ gae wowo jaŋe ŋafeo wohuc bâbâsifuc bâfuaeŋgopieŋ .
52005008	Ʒoaŋte biŋe ekicne nâŋâc ine maŋte sowa junšepeneŋ , ehuc mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ izi maruku enârezejec , â bâbâpiaŋte woworiczi dunâŋec ezejec .
52005009	I šiŋucte : Anutu e kimbeŋ-ticnere fârine hotâckenaŋte mâcne , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ bâbâpiaŋ rauckenaŋte muekac .
52005010	E hâcne okac-nâŋec hâmowec , i hâmohuc me ɋâricne juhuc ehec mâmâc junaŋte iŋuc ewec
52005011	Ŋoŋe irec hâcne faŋ qaqac â hehe šakiec eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha ehuc junšepieŋ .
52005012	Âgo bureŋ , wiac mocte esoc-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ : Ŋoŋerao šâic gie baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋte erâ micne baŋareeŋgopieŋ â mu bâtiŋ eŋareŋgopieŋ i jaŋe sâsec-jopanšepieŋ .
52005013	Ehuc gie-jeŋicte erâ maŋjauŋ ejarehuc mana-jarepie fejâmbâŋkezejec . Erâ wâc wama qaqac ehuc junšepieŋ .
52005014	Âgofâc , hazec qâuŋ dâŋ moc ŋazape mananiŋ . Ŋic kosa jujune jaŋe uŋ sawaŋ ejarenšepieŋ , ŋic manabâcne jaŋe mu âkeriŋ ejarenšepieŋ , betaŋkekicne jaŋe dopec-jopanšepieŋ , erâ mâmâc hezu hemiriŋ ejarenšepieŋ .
52005015	Sâqocnere okac babazuc enšipiŋte sosoŋaŋ enšepieŋ . Ŋaŋackoaŋ â ŋic gâcne sasawa jaŋehec eehâmoc erâ erahuc junšepieŋ .
52005016	Bubiaŋ faio jurâ jurahuc junšepieŋ .
52005017	Nunumu moc mi hetaranšepieŋ .
52005018	Wiac irec me irec daŋge mumuteŋ enšepieŋ , i Kristo Jesure erâ eniŋte Anutuzi muŋarekac .
52005019	Mârore šoc mi hehâponšepieŋ .
52005020	Anuture micdâŋ mufua-ŋarepie mana qâoma mi enšepieŋ .
52005021	Dâŋ sasawa mana wosâerâ bâtâc banšepieŋ , â biaŋne eme bajunšepieŋ .
52005022	Sâqocne fuŋne fuŋne ine qikiŋnenšepieŋ .
52005023	Anutu wama rune e jahac šure bâpiaŋ eŋareme maŋfuru ejâmbâŋkenšepieŋ , eme mâro â maŋ qâqâtâc â sahac-ŋeŋic furu fohame Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere fifisi dameŋko bahacmâc domanšepieŋ .
52005024	Hefârec-ŋopakac e mume sasanaŋ , irec gie-ticne baku batarocmu .
52005025	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe nâŋere erâ numunšepieŋ .
52005026	Opâ ruac ŋoŋe mitio meo babac efârenšepieŋ .
52005027	No Wofuŋte maio ŋaza sanaŋkepe : ŋoŋe papia kecši opâ ruac mâmâc sasawa wose-jarepie mananšepieŋ .
52005028	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
53001001	Paulo , Siliwano â Timoteo nâŋe Tesalonike haeonec kikefuŋ guru , Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere ŋicfâc , ŋoŋere papia ši râeŋgopeneŋ .
53001002	Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
53001003	Âgofâc , maŋnâŋeczi jâiŋ-nâpome ŋoŋere erâ Anutu dameŋ sâc daŋge âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ . Mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic boc fua ɋârâŋ eekac , â maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋic fua sawec eme qame qoŋgiŋ eeŋgopieŋ . Eme irec Anutu daŋge âzâcnepene i jâmbomac sâckeekac .
53001004	Erâ ŋoŋe fific guguriŋ eŋarepie šâic busâqochec juhuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic mi ŋeŋgoroŋkeha sifu sanaŋkerâ jueŋgopieŋ , irec dâŋ binaŋ hae sâc Anuture kikefuŋfâc ejareeŋgopeneŋ .
53001005	Ŋoŋe wiac fua-ŋareekac , irec šiŋuc muzo : Anutuzi okac dameŋko wiac sâckoa enâreocmu , irec sâsâcne ši qanaŋ fuakac . Anutuzi ŋoŋere maname sâckeme uucmaŋ-ticnao rarašire sâc bâfuaniŋte šârâ hâriŋ faio jueŋgopieŋ .
53001006	Eme juku Anutu mana wosâc-ticne tiŋne fokac irec sâc enâreocmu : Ŋoŋe šâic fâro eŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋe šâic fâro jaha bâfua-jareocmu ,
53001007	â šâic fâro manaeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe ine nâŋehec mâmâc bâgunuc-nâpoocmu . I juku Wofuŋ Jesu e aŋelo guru hâhâwicne jaŋehec sambâŋkonec waha fua tâcneocmu ira iŋuc enâreocmu .
