53001008	E šocbâruŋko waharâ ŋic Anuture kâuc baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋ Jesu Biŋebiaŋ-ticne mana rereŋ mi eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne jareocmu .
53001009	Ŋic i jaŋe Anutuzi furine sisipiric sanaŋ jarehuc šâŋe mai-ticnaonec â tâpiri-ticnere huriri biaŋkonec bârâriec-jopaocmu .
53001010	Eme dameŋ ira fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne jaŋerao eri tatamac-ticne fuaocmu , â miti-ticne ro maŋ embiŋ jaŋe hone warec ecneniŋmu . Ŋoŋe ine mumutaniŋ dâŋnâŋec mana šakiembiŋ hâcne .
53001011	Irec hâcne ŋoŋere erâ dameŋ sâc numuhuc šiŋuc mueŋgopeneŋ : Anutu-nâŋec e hefârec-ŋopaweczi irec sâcko juniŋte bašawiec-ŋopazejec , erâ tâpiri-ticnezi dopec-ŋopahame wiac biaŋnere mu manasuc ehuc mamanasiŋte gie fâri bâfua-fârenšepieŋ .
53001012	Iŋuc epie Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu ere šâŋe qâreŋzi ŋoŋerao fua jaŋgeŋkezejec , â ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha erao taniŋke biaŋ enšepieŋ . I Anutu-nâŋec â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eki aki anonoc-ticnere iŋuc eŋarezejec .
53002001	Âgofâc , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo fifisi-ticnere â ehec bâbâfuac ee irec dâŋne moc ŋazapene mananiŋ .
53002002	Ŋic gâcne jaŋe Wofuŋte dameŋ maickekac muhuc Mârorao muhotaniŋmu , me nâŋe micko itic enâreniŋmu me papia-nâŋecte mu ɋetic eniŋmu , eme ŋoŋe mi mutuc erâ fâfârepie maŋŋeŋic hockezejec .
53002003	Eatuc dâŋ iŋuc me iŋuc ŋazapie mi mananšepieŋ . Wofuŋ dameŋ-ticne maickezo eha qanaŋ miti ima qaqa sâko fuaocmu , erâ sindaŋŋic sisipiricte biŋe eki hâcne fua tâcneocmu .
53002004	Eme šâŋene Anutu me miti wiac mueŋgopieŋ i sasawa râsi ecnehuc qâhuckerâ ro waha âte ecne-fâreocmu . Erâ Anuture ufuŋko ferâ ŋehuc e jahacnere muocmu , “ No Anutu . ”
53002005	No ŋoŋerao juhuc irec hâcne ŋazapo , i moc manasuŋgopieŋ me ?
53002006	Dameŋ šiŋuczia aka fokac , i manaŋgopieŋ , i hâcne rârieme dameŋ-ticnao fua tâcneocmu .
53002007	Ʒi ine sindaŋzi soŋsoŋko biac gie-ticne baekac . Á aka hecneekac e rârieme sindaŋŋic fua tâcneocmu .
53002008	Eme Wofuŋ Jesu e micrombâŋ-ticnezi qarâ fifisi-ticnere šâziriŋnezi imackeocmu .
53002009	Ŋic e Sataŋzi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ ŋecnehame tâpiri wiac fuŋne fuŋnehec fuarâ burecko mâsi â qaŋgec wiac šâŋe furu baocmu .
53002010	Erâ ŋic gâcne , dâŋ fâri qizecne manarâ bibiaŋke i qaisockerâ sisipiricte biŋe eeŋgopieŋ , jaŋe sâqocnere maŋ bâsifuc ejareocmu .
53002011	Ŋic jaŋe iŋuc eeŋgopieŋte Anutuzi eeatuc neŋgoc qizecne sâko mume fuame burecko qohotaniŋmu hâcne .
53002012	I mâc mâcne , dâŋ fâri qizecne qikiŋnerâ wiac hehesicnere aŋac-jopaekac , ŋic i jaŋe okacne fisi-jareocte iŋuc hâcne eocmu .
53002013	Âgofâc-nâŋec , Wofuŋte jorocfâc , ŋoŋe Mârozi baɋaɋac-ŋopame dâŋ fâri qizecnao qohotahuc biaŋkeniŋte Anutuzi mârâc jaha rowosâec-ŋopawec , irec daŋge hati âzâcnenaŋte maŋnâŋeczi jâiŋ-nâpoekac .
53002014	Irec hâcne Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapene manarâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo eri tatamac-ticne rauckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopawec .
53002015	Eme irec âgofâc ŋoŋe sanaŋkerâ dâŋ miczi â papiazi ŋaza qazuc embeŋ i paŋšâic bajunšepieŋ .
53002016	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo â Anutu Mamac-nâŋec eki maŋjauŋ enârehuc katucmâc-ticnere erâ bubiaŋ fofo sanaŋ bâfua-nârewec â šeŋaŋ fâri woŋec-nâŋec râewec ,
53002017	eki hâcne maŋŋeŋic bâinaŋkerâ dopec-ŋopame dâŋfâri â gie fâri i ŋoŋerao mi wahazejec .
53003001	Âgofâc , dâŋ moc fokac mananiŋ : Nâŋere erâ numupie Wofuŋte dâŋzi fofotâc haŋ barame qâreŋ biaŋ-ticne ŋoŋerao fuawec iŋuc jaha fua razejec .
53003002	Erâ ŋic maŋbâiŋ bâbâfuane â sindaŋne jaŋere erâ Anutuzi ŋezic-nâpoocte nunumuzi wâc bafic-nâponšepieŋ . Miti i ŋiczi furu ninic ro maŋ mi eeŋgopieŋ .
53003003	Wofuŋzi ine mume sasanaŋ , irec hume keteŋ eŋarehuc sâqocne runere roroŋ sasapec eŋareocmu .
53003004	Ŋoŋe dâŋ ŋazapene reŋkerâ reŋke rahuc juniŋmu , irec Wofuŋte erâ ŋoŋere maŋjahec mi eŋgopeneŋ
53003005	Wofuŋzi maŋŋeŋic jowame Anuture maŋ jauŋko â Kristore bumâteŋko iticnezejec .
53003006	Âgofâc , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere micte ŋazapene mananiŋ , dâŋ qazu-ŋarembeŋ i opâ ruac gâcnezi mi reŋkehuc kosa jueŋgopieŋ , ŋic i jaŋehec mi junšepieŋ .
53003007	Nâŋe hata fuŋkerâ âte-ŋarembeŋ ijaha bâjâpec-nâponiŋte kâuc mi baŋgopieŋ . Nâŋe ŋoŋerao ojoŋ mi jumbeŋ .
53003008	Erâ ŋoŋeraonec nânâ furimâc mi nâmbeŋ , aricne , nânâ mafare micneneŋ eŋarenšipeŋte ŋafe furec mezi gie šocnehec bahuc šâic manambeŋ .
53003009	Erâ iŋuc enaŋte mi munârekicne , nâŋe qaŋeŋ-ŋopahuc fuŋne ŋowatupene nâŋere mimiŋ qâjâpec juniŋte iŋuc eŋarembeŋ .
53003010	Ŋoŋerao juhuc šiŋuc hâcne boc ŋazambeŋ : Ojoŋ juocmuzi nânâ mi nâzejec .
53003011	Eme ši ŋoŋeraonec dâŋ šiŋuc wareme manambeŋ : Ŋic gâcnezi gie-jeŋic hetârarâ qâoma erâ jueŋgopieŋ .
53003012	Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe Wofuŋ Jesu Kristore micte uŋdâŋ šiŋuc jazapene mana-jâmbâŋkenšepieŋ : Ŋezu ŋewâneŋ erâ gie-jeŋic bapie fârine fuame jaŋacneonec nânšepieŋ .
53003013	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe ine eehâmo gie tatakic tâmiric banšepieŋ .
53003014	Ʒi papiao dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋareŋgopeneŋ , i ŋic moczi qikiŋneme fuŋne-ticne mujaŋgeŋkerâ behepie buc juhuc mimiezejec .
53003015	Râsi ecneniŋte mi mukopac , âgo-nâŋec muhuc mu bâtiŋ ecnehuc tutuc qacnenšepieŋ .
53003016	Wofuŋ e wama runezi ine wama bâfua-ŋareme ŋoŋerao dameŋ sâc sâcke-fârerâ fozejec . Wofuŋ e ŋoŋehec jufârezejec .
53003017	Ʒi Paulo no nahacne mezi šâŋe qâreŋ-nane râekopac . Papia qâreŋkeekopac sâc ma izi fuaekac . Iŋuc hâcne qâreŋkeekopac .
53003018	Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
54001001	Paulo no Anutu bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋecte micte â Kristo Jesu mamanac-nâŋecte micte Kristo Jesure aposolo juekopaczi
54001002	mitio motec jâmbâŋ-nane Timoteo go papia ši qâreŋke-garekopac . Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc â uruc jauŋ â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
54001003	No Makedonia mâreŋko razo ehuc gazapo iŋuc ezemec , ehuc Efeso haeo šuhuckerâ juhuc , ŋic tucnezi miti musifuckeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe qatara-jaretec behenšepieŋ .
54001004	Jaŋe nemu binaŋ bahuc ŋic gaŋne gaŋne juwefumbiŋ irec fuŋne qapie rašic wefuc eme mu qaqataranehec fuaekac . Iŋuc epie Anutu manasiŋkehuc kiŋaŋ qaqacne i wahame sâqoreekac .
54001005	Miti mumure fârine ine šiŋuc fuame sâckeocmu : Maŋtaniŋ â maŋšuruc â maŋ mamanasiŋhec juhuc maŋjauŋ bâfuazo .
54001006	Ŋic tucnezi ine miti hata i qâsorierâ dâŋ jawane fârimâc bâfuambiŋ bajuŋgopieŋ .
54001007	Erâ jaŋacnere šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ : Nâŋe Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ irec qaqazu , iŋuc murâ dâŋ kosa muhuc irec sasanaŋ bâfuaeŋgopieŋ .
54001008	Nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋte šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : I dâŋ biaŋne , erâ fuŋneticne mana-hâmohuc bajuzo .
54001009	Fuŋne-ticne ine šiŋuc fokac : Sâcmutâc dâŋ i ŋic bahacmâc jaŋere biŋe mi ekac , ŋic sindaŋne , râŋgeŋne , araŋ bapa tâmiric , sâqocne bapa , maŋwânâŋhec , šaubacne , neŋgoc mamac sisipiric , šika qaqa ,
54001010	boe sau ŋic , ŋiczia ŋicko sasec gie bapa , ŋic ŋokac fiuc rocjoparâ gâcne qikiŋne-jarehuc moneŋ bâbâfua , burecŋic , Wofuŋte šâŋe muhuc burecko mumupaŋ ee , erâ wiac gâcne moc dâŋ fari biaŋ râsi ecneekac , wiac iŋucne eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋ mukicne .
54001011	Anutu juju aŋac rune ere Biŋebiaŋ eri tatamacnehec tahacnukicne izi hâcne iŋuc mufuakac .
54001012	Tâpiri narehuc basanaŋnuwec Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu e daŋge âzâcneekopac . Eki mana-nareme sâckeme betoŋnuhuc miti gie munarewec hâcne .
54001013	Juwicnao e musoriŋkehuc ŋicfâcne râsi ejarerâ jopa qâšâic ejarehape sifu iŋuc enarewec . No Wofuŋte fuŋne kâuc bahuc mamanasiŋ-nane tâmiricte iŋuc epore akicnuwec .
54001014	Eme Wofuŋ-nâŋecte aki anonoczi norao qaja fuseme Kristo Jesuraonec mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋhec epo .
54001015	Jesu Kristo e sâqocne bapa bâpiaŋ-nâpoocte mâreŋko wahawec , dâŋ i fârine jâmbâŋ â mâmâc sâko ro maŋ eenere sâc . Sâqocne bapa jaŋere micne no hâcne .
54001016	Eme Jesu Kristo e akicnurâ , uruc jauŋ-ticne ŋemâcne fokac , irec fuŋne norao furu jaha bataniŋkewec i mâc mâcne , ŋic šâhec mâsi i hâcne norao honerâ e manasiŋkerâ juju sanaŋko fisiniŋte iŋuc enarewec .
54001017	Juju sanaŋte Wofuŋ Sâko , mi hâhâmone â mi hohonene , Anutu sâko mocjaha hâcne , ere šâŋe biŋe â eri tatamac forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
54001018	Motec-nane Timoteo , qanaŋ gore findaŋdâŋ fuawec irec sâcko dâŋ mutâcne-garekicne i hâcne râe-garekopac . Go i bajuhuc momori gie biaŋ sanaŋkerâ bazemec .
54001019	Erâ mamanasiŋge fošakierâ fohame maŋge soŋaŋketec ɋaɋacnea fozejec . Ŋic tucnezi maŋɋaɋac juju râpeckembiŋte mamanasiŋ-jeŋic ŋeŋgoroŋkeme qâsoriembiŋ .
54001020	Jaŋeraonec moc Himenaio â moc Alesande , eme jahe Sataŋzi bâšâic-jofakume mumusoriŋ-jekic behenicte erao râec-jofapo .
54002001	No bâbâni dâŋ moc gaza qâmoc epe : Nunumu wâwâsic â daŋge mumuteŋ izi ŋaŋacne â ŋic gâcne sasawa dopec-jopahuc
54002002	ŋicwofuŋ â kia gawamaî mâmâc dopec-jopanšepieŋ . Eme soŋaŋ-nâpohapie wamao mâteŋne â mitine juhâmopene ŋiczi mana-nârepie fezejec .
54002003	Izi biaŋkeocmu , â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu e irec maname sâckeocmu .
54002004	Eki ŋic mâmâc sasawa biaŋkerâ dâŋ fâri qizecne mana maŋ eniŋte muekac hâcne .
54002005	Anutu mocjaha hâcne junârekac , erâ Anutu â ŋic ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko ŋicwirec-nâŋec mocjaha Jesu Kristo e ŋic ekicnezi junâre-fârekac .
54002006	Eki hâcne juju-ticne qikiŋnehuc mâmâc sâko kiwiric-nâŋec rowec , irec biŋezi dameŋ-ticnao haŋ baocte .
54002007	No irec biŋe mumu â aposolo jupemurâ râecnukicne , erâ ŋic qâpuc dâŋ fâri qizecne â mamanasiŋte fuŋne jaza mutâc epemurâ qaqazu gie munarekicne . Dâŋ i burec mâcne , jâmbomac mukopac .
54002008	Ŋic jaŋere mukopac , jaŋe hae sâc aaric â maŋjahec tâmiric juhuc mejeŋic ɋaɋacne foha Anuturao sicnerâ numunšepieŋ .
54002009	Á ŋokac jaŋere mukopac , jaŋe ŋaqi aickerâ rojuhuc rume rume jupie izi eri-jeŋic ezejec , â qizec susuc-jeŋicko mâsi qâreŋ ee , me eri wiac furi sâko qoqonaŋ , me ŋaqi hohonebâcne ro juju ine mi enšepieŋ .
54002010	Ŋokac mitio juzo muŋgopieŋzi eehâmo gie bapie sâckeocmu .
54002011	Ŋokac jaŋe wahamicne juhuc niniŋkerâ hazec râehuc mamana gie banšepieŋ .
54002012	Ŋokaczi qaqazu gie baocte me ŋic qâhuc-jopaocte mi manacnekopac , e mâc rumerâ juzejec .
54002013	Adam e bâbâni bâfuakicne â Ewa ine šâhec .
54002014	Adam e eesaic rune mi manacnewec , ŋokaczi ine manacnerâ qaqatara bâfuawec .
54002015	Ŋokaczi motec roro-ticnere biaŋkeocmu , ine mamanasiŋhec â maŋjauŋhec erâ maŋɋaɋac juniŋmu ŋokac i jaŋe iŋuc hâcne eniŋmu .
54003001	Moc e mitire micne bapa juocte muocmu , e gie furi sâkore ecnekac muzo , dâŋ i jâmbomac .
54003002	Eme mitire micne bapazi bahacmâc juhuc ŋokac mocjahahec juzejec , erâ maŋsowa juzejec , eesifuc tâmiric metâne juzejec , jauŋhec juzejec , qaqazu gie basarickehuc bapane ,
54003003	waiŋ opâ âmbâŋ mi nâzejec , šikafac aricne , urucne â wamane juzejec , moneŋ mafare mubâre mi ezejec ,
54003004	e jahacne wiacfâc sâcne soŋaŋ-jopazejec erâ pectâc juhuc naru motecfâcne mu bâtiŋ ejareme micrereŋhec junšepieŋ .
54003005	Moc e wiacfâc-ticne sâcne mi soŋaŋ-jopaocmu , e wemocko Anuture kikefuŋ mamac ejareocmu .
54003006	Erâ opâ ruac ɋâricne moczi mitire micne bapa mi juzejec , iŋucnezi penaroŋ eme Sataŋzi doc bazacte .
54003007	Ŋic ŋokac kikefuŋko mi rašimbiŋ jaŋe wâc manacnepie sâckeekac ŋic iŋucnezi mitire micne juzejec , jaŋe musoriŋkepie Sataŋzi maŋne bâsifuckeme ere bitiŋko kizacte .
54003008	Babafic jaŋe iŋuc jaha ŋic metâne junšepieŋ , nameŋ sosohoc mi junšepieŋ , waiŋ opâ nâ âmbâŋ mi enšepieŋ , moneŋ mafare mubâre mi enšepieŋ .
54003009	Miti boreŋ soŋsoŋ fowarehuc juwec i maŋɋaɋacko duckepie fozejec .
54003010	Jaŋe wâc qanaŋ ba esâic ejarezo ” eme fuŋne-jeŋic hone manac epie sâckeme gie jarezo .
54003011	Ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋe iŋuc jaha metâne junšepieŋ , gupe micko âkec mi enšepieŋ , maŋsowa juhuc wiac sasawa mu bac epie fâri fideteŋ efârezejec .
54003012	Babafic moc e ŋokac mocjahahec juzejec . Naru motecfâc-ticne â wiacfâc-ticne sâcne soŋaŋ-jopazejec .
54003013	Eme babafic moc e gie-ticne bame biaŋkeme maŋte juju šae biaŋne bâfuaocmu â Kristo Jesurao qohotahuc giere afecke-hâmoocmu .
54003014	No gorao biac fâpemurâ manasuhuc sifu kecšiŋucte dâŋ ši qâreŋke-garekopac :
54003015	Wiac moczi niŋgiŋnume jupe šorame Anuture ficko ju bac ezore fuŋne kâuc bazic . Anutu jujune ere kikefuŋfâc jaŋe hâcne ficticne erâ wâc dâŋ fâri qizecnere gumi â hobeteŋne juŋgopieŋ .
54003016	Miti-nâŋecte fuŋne qame hukicne mutaniŋkeeŋgopeneŋ i qeŋ bipinehec : E sahacko fua tâcnekicne , Mârozi fuŋne bataniŋkekicne , aŋelozi honekicne , qâpucko biŋene mukicne , mâreŋ sâc mana maŋ ekicne , eri tatamacko bafekicne .
54004001	Mâro e qanaŋ šiŋuc mujaŋgeŋkerâ muekac : Juku šâhec ŋic tucnezi miti beherâ maŋ bâsifuc bâbâfua jaŋere eeatuc dâŋko â demoŋ jaŋere burecdâŋko qohotaniŋmu .
54004002	Ine burecŋiczi maŋjeŋic šukiwic bakicnere ŋic eatuc-jopahuc šiŋuc jazaeŋgopieŋ :
54004003	“ Ŋokac mi rohuc ŋicšeŋoŋ juzo â nânâ gâcne mi nâhuc irec sowa juzo . ” Nânâ i Anutuzi râe-fârewec , erâ mamanasiŋhec juhuc dâŋfâri mana maŋ embeŋzi daŋge âzâcnehuc nanaŋte muwec .
54004004	Anuturaonec wiac fuakicne i biaŋne sasawa . Erâ daŋge âzâcnehuc nâ bac eeŋgopeneŋko qaqatarene mi fokac .
54004005	I Anuture dâŋzi â nunumuzi jambuŋkekicne hâcne .
54004006	Go opâ ruac dâŋ i jaza qâmoc ecmu , ine Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋŋic dâŋ rereŋhec jucmu , ehuc mamanasiŋte dâŋ â mitire dâŋfuŋne fârine mana rereŋ ewaremeŋ izi maŋgere nâqiŋ eha jucmu .
54004007	Á qeŋokac qizec dâŋ wose murarane ine qikiŋnezemec . Go Wofuŋ manasiŋkehuc jucmurâ maŋzi aafec bazemec .
54004008	Sahacte aafec gie bapa izi fâfârine , â maŋ baafeckehuc Wofuŋ manariŋ qâriŋ eecne ine fârine . Izi šira mâreŋko â juku sambâŋko juju bâfua-nâreocte mukicne .
54004009	Dâŋ i fârine jâmbâŋ â mâmâc sâko ro maŋ eenere sâc .
54004010	Irec fârine hâcne ronaŋte gie amec fâfâuc baeŋgopeneŋ , ine mumusoriŋzi fai-nâŋecko feipieha Anutu jujune ere mamanacko juhuc eeŋgopeneŋ . E hâcne mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere bâbâpiaŋ juekaczi mamana hec nâŋâcne ejâmbâŋkeekac .
54004011	Dâŋ mukopac sasawa i jaza mutâc ezemec .
54004012	Go motec ɋâri jukic irec ŋic jaŋe gore manapie wawahane mi ezejec . Go maŋjauŋhec â mamanasiŋhec â maŋɋaɋachec jutec miti mumugezi â juju bapagezi opâ ruac guru hata jowatuzejec .
54004013	Woŋec-nane juhuc miti wose qazuc â jaza qâmoc ehuc juzemec .
54004014	Micne bapa jaŋe Mâroraonec dâŋ mufuahuc mejeŋic qizecgao râehuc jambuŋgumbiŋ , jambuŋ irec fârine sifucke-garezacte bâiŋ basawec ezemec .
54004015	Go irec mana mezac ehuc giege bašihuc batec fârine fuarâ fua ehuc fome hone-fârenšepieŋ .
54004016	Gahacne maŋ sahac soŋaŋkehuc mitire dâŋfuŋne furu mimic foŋareocte mâmâc soŋaŋkezemec . Go i hâcne paŋšâic bajuzemec . Iŋuc ecmuo ine dâŋge manaeŋgopieŋ jaŋe mecne â go gahacne mâmâc juju biaŋko fisiniŋmu .
54005001	Ŋicqizec moc dâŋ âzâcnemurâ fâfâcnehec mi ecnezemec , mamac-nane muhuc urucko mu tutuc ecnezemec , ŋicmotec hahac ɋafâc-nane muhuc sâcjeŋicko jaza bâtiŋ ejarezemec .
54005002	Ŋokac qizec neŋgocfâc-nane muhuc iŋuc jaha uruc jauŋdâŋ jazazemec , ŋokac sahac ɋâri seŋfâc-nane muhuc rucge bahuc dâŋ wiac jazazemec .
54005003	Hozec sâsec-jopahuc dâŋjeŋic dopeckezemec , hozec jâmbâŋ jaŋere mukopac .
54005004	Hozec moc naru motec me ŋosafâcne juniŋmu , ine jaŋe qanaŋ jaŋacne ficko miti gie bahuc ŋic ŋokac qizefâc-jeŋic jauŋ-jopanšepieŋ , ehuc juwicnao wiac ejarekicne irec tofa bazunšepieŋ . Anutu e irec maname sâckeocmu .
54005005	Hozec fârine ine e jahackoaŋ juhuc Anuturao roweckeekac , ehuc ŋafe furec nunumu wâwâsic ecneekac .
54005006	Á hozec moc sasec gie baocmu ere ine ɋâricnezi hâmocne mucnezo .
54005007	Dâŋ i wâc jaza sanaŋketec manarâ bahacmâc junšepieŋ .
54005008	Moc e wiacfâcne â soctofafâcne hone jauŋ kime dopec mi ejareocmu e miti beherâ qâpuc sanaŋ ewec mucnezo .
54005009	Hozec moc jara-ticne 60 bazuwec , erâ ŋic mocjahahec juwec , iŋucne sawa šâŋe-ticne bâmec papiao râezo .
54005010	Erâ eehâmo gie bawec me mâcne , irec fuŋne taniŋkeocte kecšiŋuc mu wioc ezo : Naru motec rocjoparâ gume jowac ejarewec me mâcne ? Erao ŋic furune fisipie hezu hewâneŋ ejarewec me mâcne ? Mitiŋic bâmec bajarewec me aricne ? Jauŋ gie fuŋne fuŋne bawec me mâcne ? Fuŋne-jeŋic iŋuc hâcne manazo .
54005011	Hozec sahac ɋâri jaŋe šâŋe-jeŋic bâmec papiao feocte mupie ine qatara-jarezemec . Iŋucne jaŋe sasecte ejareme Kristo qâoma ecnerâ ŋicte sahac bapa eeŋgopieŋ .
54005012	Erâ mârâc dâŋ mupaŋkembiŋ i qâsuapie bahacnehec eekac .
54005013	Erâ wâc gie tâmiricte ficbiri juhuc oma qâoma erâ jueŋgopieŋ , erâ i sawa mâcne , dâŋ jawane â simbiŋne kosa wosepie feekac .
54005014	Irec no šiŋuc mukopac : Hozec sahac ɋâri jaŋe ŋic mocwâc rorâ naru motec rocjoparâ dete mamac â ro rikec qâ rikec enšepieŋ . Iŋuc ehuc jupie kisâ jaŋe sâqocnere ojowa baniŋmurâ dâŋ basarâ behenšepieŋ .
54005015	Hozec gâcne jaŋe ine biac hata qâsoriembiŋ Sataŋ bâjâpeeŋgopieŋ .
54005016	Hozec moc e miti ŋokac mocte ficko juhuc gie bafickeme ine eki bâmec bacnezejec , â qâqâhâc-jeŋickonec mi rozejec , qâqâhâc-jeŋic i hozec waha qaqane jaŋere ezejec .
54005017	Soŋaŋzi gie-jeŋic bapie biaŋkeme wiac bafehuc ehâmo-jarezo , ine miti mumu â qaqazu gie paŋšâic baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne iŋuc ejarezo .
54005018	Miti papiao dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Bulimakaozi gi bagarehuc sopâc kecɋaŋ nâzo mume mi sakarecnezemec . ” Erâ moc šiŋuc : “ Gie bapa ŋic e furi fuacneme sâckeocmu . ”
54005019	Ŋic mocjahazi soŋaŋ moc dâŋko râezo mume mi manacnezemec , ŋic 2 me 3 jaŋe mupie ine manarâ giene bazemec .
54005020	Moczi bahac bâfuame âgo guru jaŋere maio mu bâtiŋ ecnetec gâcne jaŋe manahuc hâwic-jopazejec wâc .
54005021	No Anutu â Jesu Kristo ere maio â aŋelo bufuŋfâc-ticne jaŋere maio kecšiŋuc mupaŋke-garekopac : Dâŋ gaza qâmoc ekopac i aimuŋ soŋaŋkehaŋ moc mi wahazejec , ehuc maŋgere ŋic ŋokac wiac sâctiri moc mi ejarezemec .
54005022	Go ŋic miti giere fâro ehuc biac mi jambuŋ-jopazemec , jaŋere kiŋzi gore faio fezacte . Gahacne maŋ sahac soŋaŋketec ɋaɋacnea fozejec .
54005023	Go bukiki â huc šâic gâbâ egareekacte opâ sawa mi nâzemec , waiŋ opâ afecne mac nâzemec wâc .
54005024	Ŋic tucne jaŋere sâqocne i fuŋne babataniŋ dameŋ mi maickeha qanaŋ fua taniŋkeekac , tucne jaŋere soŋsoŋ foku šâhec fuaocmu .
54005025	Eme eehâmo gie i iŋuc jaha fua taniŋkeekac , â iŋuc mi eekacko soŋsoŋ foku šâhec fua taniŋkeocmu .
54006001	Kiŋaŋ qaqa juŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa bomboŋfâc-jeŋic sâsec-jopahuc rume-jarenšepieŋ , Anuture šâŋe biŋe babawaha â miti susure fuazacte iŋuc enšepieŋ .
54006002	Erâ bomboŋfâc-jeŋic gâcne opâ ruac jaŋe ine šiŋuc mi muhuc bawahac­jopanšepieŋ : “ Mitio sâcnâŋec mocjaha eŋgopeneŋ . ” Aricne , “ bomboŋfâc-nâŋec jaŋe Wofuŋ manasiŋkepie âgo jauŋ ejareekacte ehâmo-nâreeŋgopieŋ ” , iŋuc muhuc kiŋaŋ maŋafec jaha qajarepie sâckeocmu . Go dâŋ i jaza mutâc ehuc faŋ qajarezemec .
54006003	Moc e dâŋ i âke sipurâ moc muhuc Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere dâŋbiaŋ qikiŋnehuc miti hatare sâcmutâc râpeckeekac ere šiŋuc muzo :
54006004	E maŋgâc erâ sahac-ticne bafehuc dâŋ giŋkeme giŋ bašihuc muraocmu , izi sasec-ticne eocmu hâcne . Eme irec iiŋguuŋ , hehefaric , mumusoriŋ , qoqoric ,
54006005	erâ wâc mu qaqatarac hati fuaekac . Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe maŋjeŋic sifuckerâ mamana-jeŋic šikeme , moneŋ mafa fua-nârezejec muhuc miti bajuniŋte mueŋgopieŋ .
54006006	Miti babajuzi jâmbomac sahacte dope bâbâfua-nârene , mocjaha mukâroŋ tâmiric bajunšepeneŋ .
54006007	šiŋuc manasunšepeneŋ : Fuanaŋte mâreŋko metariŋ warembeŋ , juku hâmonaŋte iŋuc jaha metariŋ jaha ranaŋmu .
54006008	Eme irec hâcne nânâ wiac â ŋaqi qoruc fonâreme manapene sâckeha junšepeneŋ .
54006009	Moneŋ mafa sâko qâhâckezo muniŋmu , jaŋe eesâicte wiwiticko feniŋmu , erâ wiac omane fuŋne fuŋnere sasec bâfuarâ mana utuckehuc sipirickeniŋmu .
54006010	Moneŋ mafare andaczi sâqocne gâcnere jâcne hâcne . Ŋic tucnezi irec harac ehuc miti hata qâsorierâ bušâic sâko bâfuambiŋ .
54006011	Anuture ŋic go wiac iŋucne geŋkezemec . Ehuc tiŋke biaŋ erâ mitihec â mamanasiŋhec â maŋjauŋhec â sasanaŋhec â buuruchec ecmurâ irec fotac qatariezemec .
54006012	Erâ mamanasiŋte juju gie biaŋ bazemec . Baku juju sanaŋte hešakiezemec . Go irec hâcne hefârecgukicne , erâ go gahac iŋuc ecmurâ ŋic tutumaŋko mupaŋketec manambiŋ .
54006013	Anutu wiac sasawa juju bâfua-jareekac ere maio â Jesu Kristo kia Pilatorao mumupaŋ fârine muwec ere maio musanaŋke-garekopac :
54006014	Go sâcmutâc dâŋ mugarekicne i bâbâsifuc tâmiric â bâbâbiene tâmiric reŋkehuc juhaŋte Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo fisizejec .
54006015	Irec dameŋ maickeme juju aŋac â tâpiri buc focneekac Anutu hâcne , eki motâc rome fua taniŋkeocmu . E ŋicwofuŋ jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko â fekicne jaŋere Fekicne .
54006016	E bucticne hâhâmo tâmiriczi , tatamac moczi moc mi rarašine irec maŋnao juekac . E ŋic moczi moc mi honekicne erâ mi honezo . Mumumbiaŋ â tâpiri focneweczi focnehuc juocmu sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
54006017	Ŋic mâreŋte moneŋ mafa ɋâfoŋne fojarekac jaŋe jazatec sahac-jeŋic mi bafehuc wiac sisirowenere manapie izi hobeteŋne-jeŋic eme ira mi âtesiŋnenšepieŋ . Anutu e mâriri bâfua-nâreme nâ bac ehuc jueŋgopeneŋ erao âtesiŋnenšepieŋ .
54006018	Erâ mu jaretec buafec â bokifac erâ eehâmo gie bahuc mitire fârine bocjaha bâfuanšepieŋ .
54006019	Ehuc hobeteŋne-jeŋic moc fofo sanaŋ i bâfuarâ juju fârine rauckenšepieŋ .
54006020	O Timoteo , go merâfâc garekicne i soŋaŋkehuc bajuzemec . Erâ dâŋ jawane â fârimâc , ŋic gâcnezi bajuhuc šâŋene “ dâŋ qame hukicne ” mueŋgopieŋ , i qikiŋnezemec .
54006021	Ŋic tucnezi dâŋ ira hâcne qohotahuc mamanasiŋte hata qâsoriembiŋ . Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec .
55001001	Paulo no Anuture micte , Kristo Jesuzi juju bâfuawec irec biŋedâŋ muiŋnepemurâ Kristo Jesure aposolo epozi
55001002	Timoteo motec biaŋ-nane gore papia ši qâreŋkekopac . Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc , uruc jauŋ â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
55001003	Mamac ŋosafâc-nane jaŋe maŋfâsâc juhuc tuczi tuc Anuture kiŋaŋ qawarekupie ɋâric-jeŋic noni iŋuc jaha eekopaczi daŋge âzâcnehuc nunumuo šušuhuc ŋafe furec manasucguhuc juekopac .
55001004	Nore ki busâqoc emeŋ , irec manasurâ honecguhuc bubiaŋ sâko manapemurâ enareekac .
55001005	Erâ mamanasiŋ fârine fogarekac , irec wâc manasuekopac , mamanasiŋ i hâcne mimige Loisi â neŋgocge Eunike jaherao foweczi gorao wâc fotâcnewec fokac i manakopac .
55001006	Eme no irec hâcne manasu-gararâ mupe : No menane qizecgao râepe Anutuzi jambuŋ tahacguwec i hehâroŋketec šocne fuazejec .
55001007	Ehuc šiŋuc manasuzemec : Anutu e hâbi-nâŋec goroŋkeocte mâro mi nârewec , tâpirihec â maŋ jauŋhec â maŋsowahec enaŋte nârewec .
55001008	Irec go Wofuŋ-nâŋecte biŋe mutaniŋkecmurâ mimi gaŋgaŋ mi ezemec , erâ kâpâcwâru ŋicticne nore dâŋ mucmurâ acmeruŋ wâc mi ezemec . Go Anutuzi tâpiri gareme sâc no qâsuecnurâ Biŋebiaŋte erâ šârâ hâriŋ faio juzemec .
55001009	Eki hâcne bâpiaŋ-nâporâ tiridâŋ-ticnezi hefârec-nâpowec . I biaŋ-nâŋecte mâcne , e jahac maname fowecte aki anonoc-ticnere erâ iŋuc enârewec . I mârâc jaha jâmbâŋ Kristo Jesure erâ biŋe qanârekicne .
55001010	Eme fârine fufua ine dameŋ ši bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu wahame fua tâcnewec . Eki hâcne hâmoc qâmizierâ juju â wiac fofo sanaŋ Biŋebiaŋko bajaŋgeŋke-nârewec .
55001011	Eme no irec biŋe mumu â aposolo â qaqazu jupemurâ munarekicne .
55001012	No irec hâcne šârâ hâriŋ faio juekopac , ehuc mi mimieekopac . No manasiŋkeekopac ere maŋjahec mi eekopac , aricne , no šiŋuc manapaŋkeekopac , e tâpiriheczi šeŋaŋ-nane sâcne soŋaŋke-narehame dameŋ sâko maickezokac .
55001013	Dâŋ fârine irec biri-ticne qazu-garepo ijaha bâjâpezemec , i Kristo Jesu manasiŋkehuc â maŋzi jauŋkehuc iŋuc ezemec .
55001014	Tiri Mâro maŋnâŋecko juekac eki neŋgoc ŋegarehame miti kâdoc qârârie-garekicne , i aimuŋ soŋaŋketec fogarezejec .
55001015	Asia mâreŋko behecnu-fârembiŋ i manameŋ , Figelo â Hemogene jahe mâmâc .
55001016	Wofuŋ e Onesiforo ere wiacfâc maŋuruc qajarezejec . Mamac-jeŋiczi kâpâcwâru ŋic nore mi takickeha bubiaŋ hati qanarehuc juwec .
55001017	E Roma haeo fisirâ šoɋac basacnuku bâfuacnuwec .
55001018	Wofuŋzi manaha dameŋ sâko Wofuŋtao uruc jauŋ bâfuazejec . E Efesoo wâc kiŋaŋ qaqa gie wemo afecne bawec i go gahac hone manac emeŋ .
55002001	Kristo Jesuzi aki anonoc tahacguwec i go motec-nanezi bajuhuc qabocge qame huzejec
55002002	Ŋic bocjahazi hone manac ehapie gie gaza gowatuc epo , gie i hâcne ŋic tucne Wofuŋte hatao jueŋgopieŋ â miti munusuŋkeniŋte tâpiri fojarekac iŋucne jaŋe qazu-jaretec banšepieŋ wâc
55002003	Go Kristo Jesure momori ŋic sanaŋne juhuc irec šârâ hâriŋ kâdocge rocmurâ mi takicguzejec .
55002004	Moc e momori gie baocmuzi wemocko sahackopec gie fuŋne fuŋne ameckeocmu . E momori jaŋere birio râeweczi wiac honeme sâckeocmu i sawa eocte muocmu .
55002005	Moc e sisiric gie bahuc sâcmutâc qâsuaocmuzi furine mi roocmu .
55002006	Moc e he sarac ehuc šâic-ticne manaocmuzi nânâ fârine micne barâ bâsurâ nâme sâckeocmu .
55002007	Dâŋ gazakopac i manatâc qâtâc ezemec . Wofuŋ eki maŋge bâwiŋkeme mana tara-fârezemec .
55002008	Go Jesu Kristore mamanac juzemec ” e Dawidire ɋâriczi hâmockonec ɋârerâ faharewec ” Biŋebiaŋ-ticne iŋuc hâcne muekopac .
55002009	Biŋebiaŋ irec erâ šâic fâro manaekopac , erâ wâc sâqocne bapa iŋucne niŋgiŋnumbiŋ ŋekopac Anuture dâŋ ine mi niŋgiŋkekicne .
55002010	No šâic gie sasawa i Anutu bâwosâefâc-ticne jaŋere erâ ŋetâcneekopac , jaŋe Kristo Jesure bâbâpiaŋzi ŋihe umbiŋ ejareha eri tatamac fofone mâmâc rauckeniŋte iŋuc eekopac hâcne
55002011	Dâŋ šiŋuc fokac i jâmbomac : Ere hâmocko šuhuckembeŋko juju-ticnao iŋuc jaha šuhuckenaŋmu ,
55002012	šâic mana takirenaŋmuo ehec guriŋ bapa gie wâc banaŋmu . E mic banaŋmuo eki iŋuc jaha mic bacnâpoocmu .
55002013	Mumupaŋ-nâŋeczi dockeocmuo ere mumupaŋzi sanaŋkeocmu . Moc murâ moc mu i erao mi fokac .
55002014	Go dâŋ i heɋâre-jarerâ Anuture maio mujomirehuc jaza sanaŋketec dâŋ racnere mu iigoc mi enšepieŋ . I wiac fârimâc , iŋuc ehuc miti mamana sipiric-jopaniŋmu .
55002015	Anutuzi mana-gareme sâckeocte šoɋachec juhuc giege bazemec , ehuc dâŋ fâri qizecne fâretiŋ jaha mujaŋgeŋkehuc jutec mimizi gieŋic gore faio mi fezejec .
55002016	Á dâŋ jawanere ojowane bapie mi bafic-jopazemec . Iŋuc eeŋgopieŋzi eraku miti beheniŋmu .
55002017	Burecdâŋ-jeŋiczi biac wicbâroŋ iŋucne erâ ŋedâmâreocmu . Ŋic iŋucne jaŋeraonec moc Himenaio â moc Fileto .
55002018	Jahe dâŋ fâri beherâ mukopirec , fafahare i biac fuawec . Iŋuc muhuc ŋic gâcne miti ba imac ejarekopirec .
55002019	Anutuzi qânâ wâtuŋ râeme huwec ine qiŋ herâ domakac . Maqâreŋ-ticne šiŋuc fokac : Wofuŋzi biŋefâc-ticne šâŋitac-jopaekac Erâ moc šiŋuc “ Wofuŋte šâŋe bajuŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeŋgoma bâbâsifuc râpeckenšepieŋ . ”
55002020	Ufuŋ sâkoo râqâc wiac goì â siliwazi bakicne i sawa mâcne , jâczi â mâreŋzi bakicne i mâmâc ŋekac . Râqâc gâcnao wiac furi sâkozi huocmu . gâcnao wiac omanezi huocmu .
55002021	Moc e bâbâsifuc wiac qikiŋneme maŋne ɋaɋackeme râqâc furi sâko eme ufuŋ runezi jambuŋkerâ bajuhuc izi gie biaŋ fuŋne fuŋne baocmu .
55002022	Socɋârizi wiac fuŋne fuŋnere andac eeŋgopieŋ i bâec bazemec . Ehuc maŋjeŋic biaŋkekicnezi Wofuŋ mu wâwâsic ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe bafic-jopatec tiŋke biaŋ eere â mamanasiŋte â maŋjauŋte â wamare henširiŋnenšepieŋ .
55002023	Mugufuc dâŋ mutucne â racne igockezemec , irec fârine mu qaqatarac sawa fuaekac i manakic .
55002024	Wofuŋte kiŋaŋŋiczi mu hehefaric mi ezejec , e ŋic sasawa âgo ejarehuc miti micafec qazu-jarezejec , â pepecne ecnepie wiac aaricko mi ejarezejec ”
55002025	erâ ŋic maŋrâŋgeŋ ine urucko mu bâtiŋ ejareme Anutu e jahac moc bawahac-jopame maŋjeŋic bârisierâ dâŋfâri šâŋitanšepieŋ .
55002026	Eme maŋjeŋic uŋtome , Sataŋte dâŋ reŋkeniŋte wiwitic-ticnao kicjopawec i hetaranšepieŋ .
55003001	Go šiŋuc manazemec : Dameŋ tarazo eha sâqocnezi sawe mâririackeocmu .
55003002	Ŋic kecšiŋucne juniŋmu hâcne : Jaŋe jaŋacnere sawa manoniehuc juju , moneŋ sasec , ruruc bâbâcne , sahac mumuteŋ , musurecne , neŋgoc mamac dâŋ qaqatara , nâme nikecne , araŋ bapa tâmiric ,
55003003	maŋjauŋ tâmiric , kiŋ babaju , micko âkechec , nâ areŋne , qicqucne , wiac biaŋne qaqaisoc ,
55003004	docbapa , enšaŋaucne , pepecne , sasecte aŋac kâcɋene bajuhuc Anuture aŋac mi mamana ,
55003005	sahaczi miti hawari juhuc mitio sasanaŋ tâmiric juju . Iŋucne hâcne jupie honec-joparâ râpec-jopazemec .
55003006	Ŋic mukopac jaŋeraonec tucnezi kamierâ ficbiri juhuc ŋokac kosane , bahac fuŋne fuŋne bâfuambiŋ â saseczi ejareme ra qa ware qa eeŋgopieŋ , iŋucnezi jaŋere eniŋte mu bâdoc ejareeŋgopieŋ ”
55003007	ŋokac dameŋ sâc mamana gie bahuc dâŋ fâri qizecnere fuŋne mi mana taraeŋgopieŋ iŋucne hâcne .
55003008	Mârâc jaha Jaŋe â Jambere jahe Mosere dâŋ bawahapic , iŋuc jaha ŋic mukopac jaŋe maŋjeŋic sifuckekicnere mamanasiŋte hata kâuc bahuc mutuc eeŋgopieŋ .
55003009	Erâ wiac eejeŋic wemocko boc efeniŋmu . Mutuc-jeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeme ŋic sasawa hone-fâreniŋmu , Jaŋe Jambere jaherao fuawec iŋuc .
55003010	Go jupe juju-nanezi ine miti mumu-nane , juju-nane , giebapa-nane , mamanasiŋ-nane , buuruc-nane , maŋjauŋ-nane , sasanaŋ-nane ,
55003011	fific guguriŋ-nane â šârâ hâriŋ-nane , irec hatane âtehuc bâjâpecnuekic . Antiokia haeo â Ikonioŋ haeo â Listera haeo fific guguriŋ enarepie šâic serereŋ mo iŋucne manapo ¡ Eme Wofuŋzi sifu wiac iŋucnaonec bataracnuwec .
55003012	Erâ ŋic gâcne wâc Kristo Jesurao qohotahuc miti hata âteniŋmu jaŋe mâmâc fific guguriŋ fua-jare-fâreocmu .
55003013	Ŋic repicne â eeatucne jaŋe ine jaŋacnao â gâcne jaŋerao eeatuc gie bafeku repire sanaŋkeniŋmu .
55003014	Go ine dâŋ qazu-garekicne â maŋge ekicne ira qohotahuc juzemec . Dâŋ moraonec romeŋ i kâuc mi bakomec .
55003015	Erâ go ɋieocnecteaŋ tiri papia wose manac ewefuhuc juekicte izi maŋge batamaeha Kristo Jesu manasiŋkehuc bâbâpiaŋ sâcne bâfuacmu .
55003016	Miti papia i Anutu Mâro-ticnere qafeŋko fua-fârewec , eme irec wose manac epene mitire fuŋne qazu-nâreekac â mu tutuc enâreekac â mu bâtiŋ enâreekac â tiŋne hata nâwotuekac .
55003017	Iŋuc enârehuc bašawiec-nâpokume nâŋâc Anuture ŋicfâri erâ eehâmo gie fuŋne fuŋne sâcne bâfuanaŋmu .
55004001	No Anuture maio â Kristo Jesu , juku Wofuŋ tâpirihec fisirâ ɋâricne â hâmokicne dâŋnâŋec mutaraocmu , ere maio gazapaŋkepe manac :
55004002	Go miti muminširiŋkezemec , ehuc ŋic irec ejareha me mi ejareha ɋicwânšâŋ jaha jazazemec . Erâ ŋic mu tutuc â mu bâtiŋ â mu sawaŋ ejarehuc qaqazu giege uneŋko tatakic tâmiric bazemec .
55004003	Juku dameŋ moc maickeme miti riucdâŋ manapie joŋtaweme qikiŋneniŋmu . Qikiŋnerâ miti hazecte nâpene-jeŋic sawa eme qaqazu mana wosâc ejarepie maŋjeŋic sâckeme iŋucnea guruhec rocjopaniŋmu .
55004004	Ehuc mitidâŋ fârine râpeckerâ nemu binaŋko qohotaniŋmu .
55004005	Go ine dameŋ sâc maŋtiec juzemec , šârâ hâriŋzi faigao feme sanaŋkezemec , Biŋebiaŋ muromackezemec , gie mugarekicne i basarickezemec .
55004006	No ine biac due bazo ekopac , rara dameŋ-nane bembeŋkekac .
55004007	No juju gie biaŋ batarakopac , hata-nane âte wareku mao fisikopac , mamanasiŋ-nane soŋaŋkehape mi ŋeŋgoroŋkewec .
55004008	Eme ši sambâŋte eri hendiŋ biŋe-nane râekicne fokac , i juku dameŋ sâkoo Wofuŋ , mumutara tiŋne eki narezokac , erâ no sawa mâcne , fifisi-ticnere aŋac-jopaha jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe mâmâc jarezokac .
55004009	Go fâro barâ norao biac warezemec .
55004010	Dema e mâreŋkopec wiac irec mana kikiwerâ behecnurâ Tesalonike haeo fâwec , Kereske e Galatiao rawec , â Tito e Dalimatia mâreŋko fâwec .
55004011	Ʒi Lukahec buc jukoperec . Mareko jowatec mâmâc warezepirec . E giere sâcne baficnuocmu .
55004012	Tikiko ine sorepe Efeso haeo fâwec .
55004013	Warezo ehuc hata ŋaqi-nane Troa haeo Karpo ere ficko hetarapo i bawarezemec , erâ papia-nane qizecne â rehacne mâmâc amecke warezemec .
55004014	Aeŋzi wiac bapa ŋic Alesande e sâqocne bocjaha enarewec , irec Wofuŋzi juku okacne bazucneocmu .
55004015	Dâŋnâŋec mâretec ro waha âte ewec . Go ere sawaŋge qazemec .
55004016	Dâŋgie-nane bâbâni fuawec dameŋ ira âgo moczi dâŋte mi baficnuwec , aricne , jaŋe behecnu-fârembiŋ ” kiŋjeŋic mi fojarezejec .
55004017	Wofuŋ eki ine miti musawe tarape qâpuc jaŋe mana-fâreniŋte dopecnurâ basanaŋnuwec , ehuc laioŋte mickonec bataracnuwec .
55004018	Wofuŋ e sâqocne irec me irec ŋezicnurâ sambâŋ uucmaŋ-ticnao râecnuocmu . Erao eri tatamac forahuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
55004019	No Prisika â Aqila â Onesiforo wiacfâc-ticne mâmâc manasu-jare-fârekopac , i jazazemec .
55004020	Erasto e Korinti haeo juwec â Trofimo e huc bame Milete haeo hetarapo .
55004021	Go hoemaŋ dameŋ mi maickeha biac warezemec . Eubulozi manasu-garekac , erâ wâc Pudeŋ â Lino â Klaudia â âgo sasawa jaŋe iŋuc jaha manasu-gareŋgopieŋ .
55004022	Wofuŋzi maŋ qâqâtâcgehec juzejec . Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec .
56001001	Paulo , Anuture kiŋaŋŋic â Jesu Kristore aposolo , no gie munarekicne i Anuture bâwosâecfâc jaŋe mamanasiŋhec eniŋte â dâŋ fâri qizecne mitio fokac i mana taraniŋte ”
56001002	ehuc juju sanaŋte biŋedâŋ , Anutu burec tâmiriczi mârâc jaha dameŋ mi fowecko muwec , i manahuc juju sanaŋ worickehuc juniŋte .
56001003	Dâŋticne i hâcne dameŋ-ticnao mufuahuc Anutu bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋeczi noni muromackepemurâ mupaŋke-narewec .
56001004	Eme mamanasiŋ wirec fonârekacte motec jâmbâŋ-nane jukomec Tito go hâcne papia ši râe-garekopac . Anutu Mamac â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
56001005	Gie tofane fokac i bataracmurâ Kreta nucko hetaracgupo , irec gazapo iŋuc ehuc hae sâc soŋaŋ râec-jopa razemec .
56001006	Ŋic moc bahac fâsâc â ŋokac mocjahahec juocmu , erâ naru motecfâcne mitihec â šaubac tâmiric â pepecne tâmiric juniŋmu , ŋic iŋucne râec-jopazemec .
56001007	Micne bapa moc e Anuture gie soŋaŋkeekaczi bahacmâc juzejec , ehuc pepecne tâmiric â šâšâicne tâmiric â waiŋ âmbâŋ mi nânâ â šikare aafec tâmiric â moneŋ mafare sasec tâmiric , iŋuc juzejec .
56001008	Erâ jauŋhec â wiac biaŋne sasawa dodopecke â wama ruaine , tiŋne , araŋ bapanehec â sowa bâtâchec juzejec .
56001009	Mitidâŋ mu qaqazuc ehuc hatane basanaŋkekicne i paŋnea bajuzejec . Eme izi tâpiri râcneme dâŋ fâri biaŋ ŋic qazu-jarehuc mu sawaŋ ejarezejec â miti âke sipueŋgopieŋ jaŋere dâŋ bawahazejec .
56001010	Ŋic bocjahazi râŋgeŋne â dâŋ racne mumu â eeatuc-jeŋichec juŋgopieŋ , Judaŋiczi opâ ruac jaŋerao wemo afecnezi iŋuc juŋgopieŋ .
56001011	Ŋic izi hâcne moneŋ mafare erâ , mumusifuc-jeŋic qatarakicne i musawehuc garikiŋ gâcne furu jaha ba sipiric ejareeŋgopieŋ ” ŋic iŋucne jaŋere mic qâbâzickezo .
56001012	Kreta jaŋacne porofete moczi šiŋuc muwec : “ Kreta ŋic jaŋe burec hati , qowi mimicne â wiac âmbâŋ nânâ . ”
56001013	No dâŋ i manape jâmbomac ekac . Irec go mu bâtiŋ sanaŋne ejaretec mamanasiŋzi bâɋârec-jopame ɋiɋic qanšepieŋ .
56001014	Ehuc Judaŋic jaŋere mamana gufuc dâŋ racne â ŋic dâŋfâri râpeckembiŋ jaŋere sâcmutâc dâŋ mi mananšepieŋ .
56001015	Maŋɋaɋachec jueŋgopieŋzi wiac sasaware manapie ɋaɋacne eekac . Á sâqocnezi maŋjeŋic bâbiekume mamanasiŋ tâmiric embiŋ jueŋgopieŋ , jaŋe ine mamana â maŋjeŋic mâmâc wâwânâŋhec efârewecte wiac mocte manapie ɋaɋacne mi eekac .
56001016	Jaŋe , Anuture fuŋne manaeŋgopeneŋ , miczi iŋuc muhapie eebapa-jeŋiczi ine mickeekac . Jaŋe ŋic mamakâcne â dâŋ qaqatara , â gie biaŋne moc bapanere sâc mâcne .
56002001	Go ine miti riucdâŋ fokac irec sâcko jaza mutâc ezemec .
56002002	Ehuc mutec ŋic kâcɋene jaŋe sowa bâtâc â metâne â wama ruaine jupie mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ â maŋuruc furu fojarezejec .
56002003	Erâ ŋokac kâcɋene iŋuc jaha jazatec miti ŋokac fârine erâ gupe micko âkec tâmiric â nârâmbe tâmiric juhuc juju biaŋte qaqazu enšepieŋ .
56002004	Ehuc ŋokac socɋâri jaza mutâc epie ŋowe ɋiefâc-jeŋic jauŋ biaŋne ejarenšepieŋ .
56002005	Erâ mimihec erâ sasec tâmiric juhuc nâ qofac â wiac bâpiaŋke emasaŋ ehuc ŋowefâc-jeŋic sâsec-jopanšepieŋ . I Anuture dâŋ susure fuazacte iŋuc enšepieŋ .
56002006	Ŋicmotec iŋuc jaha esoc-jopatec sowa bâtâc-jeŋichec junšepieŋ .
56002007	Ehuc go gahac wiac biaŋne sasawa irec micne bajarehuc eehâmo gie batec honerâ bâjâpecgunšepieŋ . Miti mutiŋnehuc â bâmâckehuc jazazemec .
56002008	Erâ hata sanaŋ fokac irec sâcko musaricketec kisâ jaŋere maŋ henšaŋneme jaŋe burec enâreniŋte dâŋ basarâ behenšepieŋ .
56002009	Kiŋaŋ qaqa jazatec bomboŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋke-fârehuc kiŋaŋ biaŋne qajarenšepieŋ , ehuc micjeŋicko mi ronšepieŋ .
56002010	Erâ fiuc serereŋ tâmiric juhuc wiac-jeŋic hone qâzuc ehâmonšepieŋ . Iŋuc ehuc bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu dâŋticne ba eric ecneniŋmu .
56002011	Mâreŋ sâc ŋic biaŋkenaŋte Anuture aki anonoczi bâtâcne bâtimuŋ ewec .
56002012	Erâ izi bâfiriec-nâpohuc bâtiŋ-nâpohame qâpuc hata â wiac jawanere andac i qikiŋnerâ mâreŋ šira wama ruaine â tiŋne â mitine junšepeneŋ .
56002013	Iŋuc juhuc Anutu sâko â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu ere eri tatamac fua tâcneme juju aŋacko fisinaŋte irec mamanac junšepeneŋ .
56002014	Eki hâcne nâŋâcnere due bahuc sindaŋkonec bâhoc-nâpowec , erâ fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne juhuc mitire fârine šoɋac erâ bâfuanaŋte šure bâpiaŋ enârewec .
56002015	Go paŋšâic erâ dâŋ i hâcne jazahuc mu sawaŋ â mu bâtiŋ ejarezemec . Ŋic jaŋe go mi hucgunšepieŋ .
56003001	Go dâŋ heɋâre-jarehuc jazatec ŋic jaŋe kia gawamaî â fekicne araŋ bajarehuc dâŋjeŋic reŋkenšepieŋ , erâ gie biaŋne fuŋne fuŋne fokac irec afeckerâ banšepieŋ .
56003002	Erâ mumusoriŋ â dâŋ mumuc mi enšepieŋ . Aricne , wamane juhuc ŋic maŋuruc ejare-fârenšepieŋ .
56003003	Nâŋâc mârâc jaha iŋuc jaha maŋmutuc erâ râŋgeŋne juhuc qac qâsoric ejumbeneŋ . Erâ sasec fuŋne fuŋne irec kiŋaŋ qahuc sindaŋ â iiŋguuŋ bâfuarâ mamakâcne erâ kikisuec ejumbeneŋ .
56003004	Izi šâhec ine bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu uruc jauŋ â buafec-ticne fua tâcneme
56003005	eki nâŋâc tiŋne juhuc gie moc bambeŋte mâcne , buuruc-ticnere erâ juju ɋârire opâzi â Tiri Mâroraonec fufua ɋâricnezi bâpiaŋ-nâpowec .
56003006	E bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ Tiri Mâro afecne mi qoŋgiŋke-nârewec .
56003007	I nâŋâc Kristore aki anonocte erâ kiŋnâŋec fâsâeme juju sanaŋte mamanac juku rauckenaŋte iŋuc enârewec .
56003008	Dâŋ i jâmbomac , eme go ɋicwânšâŋ erâ âkendâŋnetec Anutu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋzi eehâmo gie baniŋte šoɋac enšepieŋ . I wiac biaŋne , i epie ŋic jauŋ bacjopaocmu .
56003009	Á mugufuc dâŋ jawane â fuŋne qaqa dâŋbiri â sâcmutâc dâŋte mu qaqatarac â bac bârisic ine geŋkezemec . I wiac racne â fârimâc .
56003010	Ŋic hâme âkefâucne moc uŋdâŋ mocjaha me jajahec âzâcnetecne qikiŋneme behetec buc juzejec .
56003011	Go manakic , ŋic iŋucne e qaqaharicne , maŋnezi mumu hehec ecne-bipieha sâqocne baekac .
56003012	No Atema me Tikiko sorepe gorao fâ fisime biac Nikopoli haeo ware bâfuacnuzemec , no hae ira hâcne hoemaŋko juzo mukopac .
56003013	Sâcmutâc mamana ŋic Ʒena â Apolo jahe miti kiŋaŋ ranicte nânâ mafa wiac bâmocke-jactetec wiac mi basahuc bititiezepirec .
56003014	Ŋicfâc-nâŋec jaŋe wâc eehâmo gie baku maŋjeŋic ezejec , eme sahacte dope babasa fuaocmu sâc jauŋ gie bapie miti-jeŋiczi fârinehec ezejec .
56003015	Ŋic nohec jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa go manasu-gareŋgopieŋ . Mitio âgo enâreeŋgopieŋ jaŋe manasu-jareŋgopeneŋ irec wâc jazazemec . Aki anonoczi sâcŋopa-fârezejec .
57001001	Paulo , Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic no , â âgo-nâŋec Timoteo , nâhe Filemoŋ joroc babafic-nâhec gore papia ši râekoperec ”
57001002	erâ wâc ŋokac âgo-nâhec Apia â momori âgo-nâhec Akipo , erâ Filemoŋ gore ficko mitire tumaŋneeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋere mâmâc râekoperec .
57001003	Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec .
57001004	No nunumuo gore manasuhuc sâc Anutu-nane daŋge âzâcneekopac .
57001005	Go Wofuŋ Jesurao â mitiŋic jaŋerao maŋge domakac â jaŋere mamanac juekic irec biŋe manakopac hâcne .
57001006	Eme go mamanasiŋko nâŋehec maŋ mocjaha emeŋte wiac biaŋne Kristoraonec fua-nârewec fokac i sasawa mana taracmurâ numuekopac .
57001007	Âgo-nane , go mitiŋic bubiaŋ qajareekomec , irec no maŋjauŋgere bunane urueme wemo afecne šeri epo .
57001008	Go wiac ecmurâ i no Kristore micte mupaŋke-garezo murâ sâcne afeckerâ ezapo ,
57001009	erâ sifu maŋjauŋte erâ mâc mu hemunaŋ egarehuc mupe ” ŋicqizec Paulo no hâcne , erâ dameŋ ši wâc Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic epozi ,
57001010	no motec-mae Onesimo , kâpâcwâru ficko juhape fua-narewec , ere gazakopac .
57001011	E mârâcko jugareme mi sâckewec , ši ine no â go mâmâc junâcteme sâckekac .
57001012	Buhândâŋ-nane e hâcne sifu bârisie-garepe fakac
57001013	No Biŋebiaŋte erâ kâpâcwâru ficko ŋehape gore âkehoc kiŋaŋ qanareocte sakarezo mupo .
57001014	Erâ go mi manahaŋtecne sakarepe urucko mâcne , jâiŋko qikiŋne-narezicte manabâc ehuc bârisie-garekopac .
57001015	Behecgume e tâmiric piticne jumeŋ , i fuŋne šiŋucte mecne , risie-garerâ gohec jusanaŋkeocte .
57001016	Kiŋaŋ qaqage sawa mâcne , mitio âgoge erâ juocte fagarekac . No hâcne iŋucne junarewec , â go ine fehuc jugareocmu i šiŋucte : Sahaczi gore juweczi Wofuŋte erâ bufuŋge ekac .
57001017	Go nore manatec âgoge ekopacko ine e hefârockehuc manatec Paulo hefârockekopac ezejec .
57001018	Wiac moc sipiricke-garewecko me tofage moc erao fokacko ine nore muzemec .
57001019	Paulo no hâcne ši qâreŋke-garekopac , okacne bazu-garepemu . No nahacne tofa wâc gorao kâcɋene fokac , noraonec hâcne fuameŋ i ” erâ irec wemocte boc mupemu .
57001020	Âgo-nane , go Wofuŋte erâ wiac buafec tahacnucmurâ enarekac . Kristore erâ bubiaŋ qanarezemec .
57001021	Go micrereŋge fokac i manahuc dâŋ ši qâreŋke-garekopac . Erâ manakopac , gazakopac i sawa mi ehuc maŋgere gâcne šuhuckecmu .
57001022	Ŋoŋe nunumuzi bataracnupie Wofuŋzi no bâriesiecnu-ŋareme fâpemurâ mukopac , eme go irec ŋeŋe hewâneŋke-narezemec .
57001023	Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic âgo-nane Epafra e manasu-garekac .
57001024	Erâ babaficfâc-nane Mareko , Aristako , Dema â Luka jaŋe iŋuc jaha manasu-gareŋgopieŋ .
57001025	Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi maŋŋeŋicko fozejec .
58001001	Anutu e mârâc jaha porofete ejareme jaŋe mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec dâŋ hawarine fuŋne fuŋne â hatane fuŋne fuŋne jaza warekuhapie
58001002	ine šâhec tataranao , dameŋ šira hâcne , Ŋokâ ecneme dâŋ nâzâwec . ŋokâ e wiac sasawa irec rune juocte mucnewec , ehec hâcne wiac bâfua-fârepic .
58001003	Anutu eri tatamac-ticnere qâreŋ erao fuawec fokacte â ju ju-ticnere sâc juekacte tâpiri dâŋticnezi wiac sasawa dope siŋsiŋ ecneha foekac . Eki sâqocne šure bataniŋ gie bafârerâ faic fekicne sâko ere fâreo fewec ŋekac .
58001004	Aŋelo hucjopa-fârewec jukac , irec sâcko aŋelo šâŋe siricke-fârehuc šâŋe fekicne hotâckewec .
58001005	Anutuzi mo aŋelo mo kecšiŋuc moc âzâcnewec : “ Go hâcne ŋokâ-nane , no miŋecgac bâfuacgukopac ” ? Me kecšiŋuc : “ Noni Mamac ecnerâ jupemu â eki Ŋokâ enarerâ juzejec ” ?
58001006	Moc ine juku mârâc fufua e mâreŋko râeme wahaocmu irec dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Anuture aŋelofâc jaŋe dieŋzi hecne-fârenšepieŋ . ”
58001007	Aŋelo jaŋere kecšiŋuc mukicne : “ E aŋelofâcne hawari-jeŋic bâtikieme mâŋâŋ eeŋgopieŋ , â kiŋaŋ qaqafâcne hawari-jeŋic bâtikieme šocbâruŋ eeŋgopieŋ
58001008	Ŋokâre ine šiŋuc mukicne : “ Anutu go ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋege i ŋeŋe sanaŋ ŋerašihuc juocmu , â ŋicwofuŋ gunuge i bâbâtiŋ gunu biaŋ .
58001009	Go tiŋnere egareekac â hehesic ine râsi ecneekic . Irec Anutu , gore Anutu , eki šeri wokemaŋ rua-garewec , i âgofâcge jaŋere sâc jâuruhuc rua-garewec . ”
58001010	Moc šiŋuc mucnekicne : “ Wofuŋ go fufuŋkenao mâreŋte hobeteŋ râemeŋ , â sambâŋne sambâŋne jaŋe megere qâreŋ .
58001011	Jaŋe siroweniŋmu , go ine jusanaŋkekic , jaŋe ŋaqi iŋucne raŋɋaŋkeniŋmu .
58001012	Ŋaqi iŋucne epie goki bataforiec-jopacmu , eme jaŋe hawari moc eniŋmu . Goki ine juekic ijaha juekic , â jara dameŋge i moc mi taraocmu . ”
58001013	Anutu e mo aŋelo mo šiŋuc moc âzâcnewec : “ Ware fâre-naneo ŋehaŋtec râsifâcge guruc-jopape kikegere ââtesiŋ enšepieŋ ” ?
58001014	Aŋelo sasawa jaŋe mârozi kiŋaŋ qaqa , ŋic bâbâpiaŋ rauckeniŋte mukicne jaŋe bafic-jopaniŋte sorec-jopakicne .
58002001	Irec nâŋâc ma bâtirinšipeŋte dâŋ manambeŋ i mocwâc paŋšâic mana sakac enšepeneŋ .
58002002	Aŋelo mickonec dâŋ mukicne i mupaŋkekicne , eme huhucke â qaqatara fuame okacnehec ejujec ,
58002003	izi wemocko bâbâpiaŋ dâŋ fekicne qikiŋnepene okacmâc foocmu ? I Wofuŋ e jahac qanaŋ mufuawec , eme hazec fâri-jeŋiczi manambiŋ jaŋe muwarekupie sanaŋke-nârewec .
58002004	Ehame Anutu e jahac wâc mâsi â tâpiri wiac šâŋe furu bâfuahuc dâŋ i dopeckehuc Tiri Mârore taha biaŋ manawec sâc kâdoc qajarehuc feŋeŋ râecnewec .
58002005	Hae mâreŋ šâhec fuaocmu , dâŋne muŋgopeneŋ hâcne , i Anutuzi aŋelo jaŋe guriŋne baniŋte mi muwec .
58002006	Mitiŋic moczi irec dâŋ mutaniŋkewec ine šiŋuc : “ Go ŋic e wemomac-ticnere manasucneekic , â ŋicte ɋâric e wemo-ticnere hone maiŋ ecneekic ?
58002007	Go dameŋ ŋondeŋ bembeŋne mac aŋelo jaŋere wahamicnao juocte mucnemeŋ , go tatamac â šâŋe biŋezi erickemeŋ ,
58002008	ehuc wiac sasawa kike-ticnere rurumaŋko râemeŋ . ” Anutu e wiac sasawa ŋicte rurumaŋko râewec , i bâtâc mi bahuc wiac furu jaha qikiŋnecne-fârewec ekac . Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine wiac šeŋgoma ŋicte rurumaŋko guruckekicne i mi honeeŋgopeneŋ .
58002009	Jesu ine honeŋgopeneŋ , e dameŋ ŋondeŋ bembeŋne mac aŋelo jaŋere wahamicne juhuc hâmocte šâic manawecte tatamac â šâŋe biŋe tahackekicne hâporâ jukac . E Anutuzi aki anonoc enâreocte mume hâmoc hâtâne ŋic sasawa nâŋâcnere erâ manawec hâcne .
58002010	Wiac sasawa irec rune â bâbâfua e naru motecfâcne bocjaha eri tatamac-ticnao jowac-jopaocte manasuhuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋicte micne bapa e šâic serereŋ gie baku mao fisiocte mucnewec i sâcke-hâmowec .
58002011	Eme maŋfuru bacjopakac e mecne â furu bacjopakicne jaŋe mecne Mamac-jeŋic mocjaha , irec ɋafâc-nane mujareocte maname mi quŋkeekac .
58002012	Dâŋticne šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ No šâŋe biŋege ɋafâc-nane muromacke-jarepe , kikefuŋ guruo šeri mumuteŋ egarepe . ”
58002013	Erâ moc šiŋuc : “ No erao roweckehuc jupemu . ” Erâ moc šiŋuc : “ Ʒi no erâ Anutuzi ɋie guru narewec nâŋe mâmâc juŋgopeneŋ . ”
58002014	Eme ɋie jaŋe sahac biuchec sasawa jueŋgopieŋte eki ijaha wâc rowec . I e jahacne hâmoczi hâmoc rune Sataŋ hâcne tâpiri-ticne qame goroŋkewecte ,
58002015	erâ wâc hâmocte hâhâwiczi niŋgiŋ-jopame dameŋ-jeŋic sâc kâpâcwâru ficko ŋejumbieŋ jaŋe batarac-jopaocte iŋuc ewec .
58002016	Wiac i aŋelo kime dopec mi ejareekac i , e Abrahamte ɋâricfâc nâŋâc kime dopec enâreekac .
58002017	Eme irec hâcne ɋafâc-ticne jaŋehec sâc mocjaha jâmbâŋ eocte mucnekicne , hatane gâcne moc mi fowec . I taha bapa sâko urucne â hazec hâricne erâ Anuture maio taha gie bahuc ŋic ŋokac nâŋâcne sâqocne šure tâmireocte iŋuc ewec jukac hâcne .
58002018	E jahac šâic manahuc eesâicko rašiwecte ŋic eesâic fua-nâreha sâcne bafic-nâpoekac .
58003001	Mitiŋic âgofâc-nane , sambâŋte mâmâc hefârec-ŋopakicne , ŋoŋe miti kiŋaŋ ŋic â taha bapa sâko Jesu , šâŋene murâ rereŋ eeŋgopeneŋ , erao findendeŋnenšepieŋ .
58003002	Eki gie runere mume rereŋ juwec , Mosezi Anuture ficko juwec irec sâc juwec hâcne .
58003003	Fic baekac ere šâŋe biŋezi ficte šâŋe biŋe jâuruekac , sâc ijaha Jesu šai šonšoŋ-ticnezi Mosere sirickekac .
58003004	Ficne ficne i bâbâfua-ticnehec , wiac sasawa irec bâbâfua ine Anutu .
58003005	Mose e Anuture ficko jufârehuc mume rereŋ gie bawec , i dâŋ šâhec fufuanere biŋe muocte kiŋaŋ qaqa juwec .
58003006	Kristo e ine ŋokâzi fic rune jukac . Ficticne nâŋâc hâcne . Erâ i mâc mâcne , wiac biŋe qanârekicne irec mamanac paŋšâic â bubiaŋko juhapene taraocmu , ine ficticne eŋgopeneŋ muzo .
58003007	Irec Tiri Mârozi dâŋ šiŋuc muwec i nâŋâcne biŋe ekac : “ Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko ,
58003008	tuhuo eesâic fuame aaricko ekicne , maŋsanaŋ iŋuc mi enšepieŋ .
58003009	Mimiŋnefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋe ira wiac bapa-nane jara 40 honembiŋ , erâ sifu pepecne enarehuc esâicnumbiŋ .
58003010	Eme no irec manape gâpâreme jaŋere šiŋuc mupo : ` Jaŋe maŋjeŋiczi raŋɋa raŋɋa qâsorieeŋgopieŋ , jaŋe nore hata moc mi hone manac embiŋ . '
58003011	Iŋucte kimbeŋ qajarehuc mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc mupo : ` Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ ' . ”
58003012	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋeraonec moc e miti qikiŋnehuc maŋ gâgâpâc erâ Anutu jujune râpeckezacte soŋaŋ babac ehuc junšepieŋ .
58003013	Erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne miŋecgaczi miŋegac forahuc juocmu sâc faŋ qaqac enšepieŋ , sâqocnere eeatuczi ŋoŋeraonec ŋic moc ecneme maŋbâzic ezackohec .
58003014	Nâŋâc Kristore miti kâdoc babaju , ine fuŋkehuc manasiŋkembeŋ mamanasiŋ i paŋnea bajuku mao fisinaŋmuzi eŋgopeneŋ .
58003015	Dâŋ šiŋuc fokac : “ Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko , aaricko ekicne , maŋsanaŋ iŋuc mi enšepieŋ ” ,
58003016	ine weni jaŋe dâŋticne mana-bipiehuc aaric bâfuambiŋ ? I mockoneczi mâcne , Mosezi micne bajareme Aigita mâreŋkonec warembiŋ ŋicguru i sasawa jaŋe hâcne .
58003017	Me weni jaŋere Anutuzi maname gâpâreme jara 40 tarawec ? I sâqocne bahuc mâreŋ tuhuo hâmo sipiric embiŋ jaŋere hâcne iŋuc ewec .
58003018	Erâ weni jaŋere mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : Nore jujumana hae mâreŋko mi rašinšepieŋ ? I dâŋticne qahuc jumbiŋ jaŋere hâcne muwec .
58003019	Irec šiŋuc honeŋgopeneŋ : Jaŋe miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋicte quŋkerâ mi rašimbiŋ .
58004001	Jujumana hae mâreŋ-ticnao rašinaŋte mukicne . biŋedâŋ i mi hetâtieme omaewec , irec ŋoŋeraonec moczi hatao sifuckezacte mezac-nâpozejec .
58004002	Biŋe biaŋ dâŋ jaŋe jazakicne sâc ijaha nâŋâc nazakicne . Jaŋe ine dâŋ i manarâ maŋjeŋicko mi râepie hurâ fowecte jaŋerao fârimâc ewec .
58004003	Nâŋâc miti mana šakieeŋgopeneŋzi jujumana hae mâreŋko rašieŋgopeneŋ . E šiŋuc muwec : “ No kimbeŋ qajarehuc mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc mupo : Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ ” , i mâreŋ hobeteŋne râehuc wiac sasawa bafârerâ sifu iŋuc muwec .
58004004	Irec šoaŋ namba 7 irec dâŋ moc šiŋuc muwec : “ Anutu e wiac sasawa bafârereâ šoaŋ 7 ira jumanawec . ”
58004005	Ehame faic honembeneŋ ine šiŋuc muwec : “ Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ . ”
58004006	Eme ši ŋic gâcnezi jujumana hae mâreŋko rarašinere hata fokac jaha , â mârâc rarašire biŋe biaŋ jazakicne jaŋe qikiŋnehuc mi rašimbiŋ ”
58004007	irec “ miŋecgac ” šâfo i mocwâc bahuc šâhec Dawidire micko dâŋ mupac i râeme šiŋuc muwec : “ Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko maŋbâzic mi junšepieŋ . ”
58004008	Josuazi jujumana hae mâreŋ fârine bâfua-jareme muzac , Anutuzi šâhec dameŋ mocte mi muzac .
58004009	Irec šiŋuc mananšepeneŋ : Anuture ŋicfâc jaŋere jujumana hombaŋ moc fokac .
58004010	Anutuzi gie batararâ jumanawec , iŋuc jaha ŋic moc Anuture jujumanao rašiocmuzi gie-ticne hetararâ jumanaocmu .
58004011	Eme nâŋâcnaonec moczi docke sâqorec erâ ŋic mârâc qaqatara hata âtembiŋ ijaha âtezacte jujumana hae mâreŋko rašinaŋte šoɋac enšepeneŋ .
58004012	Anuture dâŋ i jujuhec â tâpirihec , erâ sâqe moc bune râpene micnehec irec sâc jâuruhuc mictara jâmbâŋ . Izi nâhuku qâqâtâc â maŋ , bibiric â siec wamboŋ šušuhuc-jeŋic nâtâcneekac , ehuc maŋte mamanasu â mamana wosâc irec fuŋne bataniŋkeekac .
58004013	Eme wiac bâfuakicne moczi moc Anuture maio soŋsoŋ mi foekac , erao wiac sasawa tâtâc â foŋ tâmiric foekac . Erao hâcne dâŋgie banaŋmu .
58004014	Taha bapa sâko hahaŋnehec moc junârekac , e sambâŋ fotâcne-fârerâ fewec jukac , Jesu Anuture Ŋokâ hâcne , eme iŋucne junârekacte šâŋe-ticne murâ rereŋ enšepeneŋ .
58004015	Erâ taha bapa sâko-nâŋec e dodocne enâreme hone qâoma mi enâreekac , nâŋâcnao eesâic fuaekac iŋuc jaha wâc erao eesâic fuŋne fuŋne fuawec , eesâicko dodocke mocjaha ine mi ewec .
58004016	Irec nâŋâc aki anonoc ŋeŋe rowaŋnao maŋafec jaha fisihuc junšepeneŋ , eme wiac izi me izi maic maic-nâpoha eki buuruc enârehuc aki anonoc-ticnere erâ bafic-nâpozejec .
58005001	Mâreŋŋic nâŋâcnaonec taha bapa sâko rowosâec-jopakicne sasawa jaŋe ŋic jaŋere erâ Anutu fuacnehuc kiŋ bahacte taha bâzi rikecne niŋte râec-jopakicne .
58005002	Taha bapa iŋucne e jahac ŋic dodocne jukacte ŋic mutucne â qâsoriekicne sâcne urucne ejareekac .
58005003	Erâ fuŋne iŋucte ŋic jaŋere kiŋ bahacte mecne â e jahacne mâmâc taha bâzi rikeocte mukicne
58005004	Gie fekicne i ŋic moczi maŋticnere mi rorâ bapane , taha bapa ŋic moc e Anutuzi rowosâerâ gie mucneme sâcne baocmu , Aroŋ iŋuc hâcne ecnewec
58005005	Eme Kristo e iŋuc jaha e jahacne maname fefene eha taha bapa sâko mi ewec , i Anutuzi šiŋuc muhuc mucnewec : “ Go hâcne Ŋokâ-nane , no miŋecgac bâfuacgukopac . ”
58005006	Erâ dâŋ moc šiŋuc muwec : “ Goki Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ . ”
58005007	Jesu e mâreŋko juwec dameŋ ira , hâmockonec bataraocte tâpiri focnewec erao numuhuc kio wâwâsic kâcɋene ecnewec . Ehuc Anutu araŋ bacnewecte manacnewec .
58005008	E ŋokâ juwec , erâ sifu šâic gie baku micrereŋte fuŋne mana tarawec .
58005009	Erâ wiac emataucke-fârerâ mume rereŋfâc-ticne sasawa jaŋere bâbâpiaŋ tatara tâmiric bâfuawec .
58005010	E hâcne taha bapa sâko erâ Melikisede ere sâcko juocte Anutuzi mucnewec .
58005011	Irec dâŋ bocjaha fokac , erâ ŋoŋe hazecfâŋ juŋgopieŋte ŋaza mutâc epemurâ manape ŋemâckekac .
58005012	Ŋoŋe dameŋ šora miti mana wareeŋgopieŋzi gâcne qazu-jarepie sâckezac ” eme iŋucne ŋoŋe miti maine i mocwâc qaqazu-ŋarenere sâc eŋgopieŋ . Ŋoŋe nânâ sanaŋnere sâc aricne , susu nânâre sâc sawa juŋgopieŋ .
58005013	Susu nâeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine ɋiene mujarezo , iŋucnezi dâŋ fârine wemocko mana taraniŋmu ?
58005014	Nânâ sanaŋne i sokakicne jaŋere biŋe , maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic fua tâcneme biaŋne sâqocne mana wosâeeŋgopieŋ jaŋere biŋe hâcne .
58006001	Irec nâŋâc ši Kristore dâŋ maine , fufuŋkeo mumune , i râepene foha dâŋ hukicne , wiac efehuc mumune , i moc šuhuckenaŋ . Wemocte miti hobeteŋne i hâsine râehuc maŋ bâbârisie â juju raŋɋa bebehe â Anutu mamanasiŋ ,
58006002	â Miti Opâ â qizecko me rârâe â hâmockonec fafahare â bâtâc sanaŋ irec dâŋ mocwâc fuŋkezo ?
58006003	Anutuzi maname sâckeme dâŋ moc šuhuckenaŋ .
58006004	Ŋic mitizi maŋjeŋic batamaeme sambâŋkonec nânâ nâhonembiŋ â Tiri Mârohec embiŋ ,
58006005	erâ Anuture dâŋbiaŋ â juju sanaŋte tâpiri mana aŋac embiŋ ,
58006006	ŋic iŋucne jaŋe miti behe sanaŋkehuc Anuture Ŋokâ jaŋacne maŋte mocwâc maripoŋko qahuc mamakâc ecnepie mitio bâbârisiec-jopane mi fokac .
58006007	Mâreŋ moc hoezi gâbâ hehuc bâgunuckekume , ŋic sara mamac eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere biŋe nânâ monšaŋ bâfuaekac , i Anutu jambuŋ-ticnere fârine fuacneekac .
58006008	Á mâreŋ mocko hofâ qinšiŋ sawa fuaocmu , ine fârimâc ekacte sâwec fâreme juku šoczi šaocmu .
58006009	Âgofâc , no dâŋ mukopac i ŋoŋe sipirickeniŋmu manahuc mâcne , mitio biaŋke-hâmoniŋmu , iŋuc manahuc mukopac .
58006010	Anutu e eesifucne mâcne ” ŋoŋe ere erâ ŋicfâc-ticne hone bafic ejarehuc jauŋ bacjopambiŋ erâ eeŋgopieŋ jaha irec wemocko nikeckeocmu .
58006011	Ŋoŋe šiŋuc eniŋte enârekac : ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa sâc ijaha ɋicwânšâŋ epie sambâŋ šeŋaŋ bâbâfuare buâkec mi omaezejec , fofehame dameŋ tarazejec .
58006012	Eme mi rokawehuc , mitiŋic gâcne mamanasiŋ â sasanaŋhec juhuc wiac biŋec-nâpokicne rauckeeŋgopieŋ , jaŋere hata âteniŋmu .
58006013	Jaŋeraonec moc Abraham e Anutuzi biŋedâŋ âzâcnerâ femicne mocte maio mupaŋkeocte basarâ e jahacnao râehuc mupaŋkewec .
58006014	Ehuc šiŋuc muwec : “ No jambuŋgurâ jambuŋgu epemu â basawecgurâ basawecgu epemu . ”
58006015	Eme Abraham e mumupaŋ dâŋ irec woŋec tatakic tâmiriŋ juku fârine rowec .
58006016	Ŋiczi fekicne moc ere maio mumupaŋ dâŋ mupene mu qaqatarac eene mi fuaocmu .
58006017	Irec Anutu e ŋic biŋe qajareme maŋjahec enšipiŋte , maŋticnezi sanaŋkeha muwec irec fuŋne bataniŋkehuc biŋedâŋ irec fainao mumupaŋ dâŋ šuhuckewec .
58006018	Anutu e burec tâmiriczi dâŋsanaŋ jajahec âkendâŋ-jofahuc nâŋâcnao suru râewec , i ere dapeŋko rašimbeŋzi wiac biŋe qanârekicne irec fârine fotarierâ ronaŋte manasuhuc ewec .
58006019	Biŋe qanârekicne irec fârinezi juju-nâŋecte aŋga sanaŋne â tâtâcne tâmiric iŋucne ekac , erâ aŋga izi faic qoruc ââketâc irec râpenao râekicne fokac .
58006020	Ââketâc i micne bapa-nâŋec Jesu eki bânie-nârehuc fotâcnerâ maŋnao rašiwec . E Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa erâ jusanaŋkeekaczi iŋuc ewec hâcne .
58007001	Melikisede e hâcne Salem haere ŋicwofuŋ â Anutu femicne sâko ere taha bapa juwec . Eki hâcne Abrahamzi ŋicwofuŋ râsifâc-ticne joparâ risiehame ra hatao bâfuarâ jambuŋkewec .
58007002	Erâ e hâcne Abrahamzi mafa mateŋ bâtâc barâ teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc râcnewec . Melikisede šâŋe-ticne nâŋâcne dâŋko “ Tiŋne ŋicwofuŋ ” , â Salem ŋicwofuŋ ine “ Wama ŋicwofuŋ ” .
58007003	Melikisede e neŋgoc mamac tâmiric , apa ŋosa fuŋne-ticne qahuc mi mufuakicne , e juju-ticne fufuŋke tâmiric â tatara tâmiric . E Anuture ŋokâ ere sâsâc eocte mukicnezi taha bapa juju hati ewec .
58007004	Ʒi honeniŋ , e ŋic fekicne mo iŋucne irec mimiŋne-nâŋec Abrahamzi mafa mateŋ biaŋne sasawa bâwosâerâ teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc râcnewec
58007005	Lewi-e ɋâricfâc gâcne taha gie baniŋte mujarekicne jaŋe ŋic ŋokac âgofâc-jeŋic Abrahamte tofafâc jaha sifu mafa wiac teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc jowac roniŋte sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko mutâcne-jarekicne .
58007006	Á Melikisede e jaŋere guruonec mi fuakicnezi ine Abrahamtaonec teŋkonec wâŋ rowec Ehuc miti biŋe qacnekicne e jambuŋkewec .
58007007	Á fekicnezi wahakicne jambuŋkeekac i mozi mickeocmu ?
58007008	Dameŋ ši ŋic sisirowenezi teŋkonec wâŋ roeŋgopieŋ ” ira ine juju hati mucnekicnezi rowec .
58007009	No manape šiŋuc ekac , Lewi e teŋkonec wâŋ roekaczi Abrahamte bifuŋko fohuc wiac i Melikisede râcnewec ”
58007010	e mamac-ticnere bifuŋko fohame Melikisedehec bâbâfuac epicte Abrahamzi râcneme Lewizi mâmâc râcnewec ekac .
58007011	Lewire ɋâricfâc jaŋere taha bapa gie sâcke-hâmozac muzac , wemocko šâhec taha bapa moc Melikisede ere sâcko fuazac â Aroŋte sâcko aricne ? Taha bapa giere erâ ŋic ŋokac sâcmutâc dâŋ jarekicne .
58007012	Eme taha bapa gie raŋɋane rârieha ɋâricne moc fuame , raŋɋanere sâcmutâc dâŋ iŋuc jaha râriehame ɋâricne moc fuaocmu .
58007013	Findaŋdâŋzi ŋic rokac e taha ufuŋko gie mujarekicne jaŋere guruonec mi fuawec , e guru mockonec .
58007014	Wofuŋ-nâŋec e Judare tofafâc jaŋeraonec fuawec , i mana-fâreŋgopeneŋ . Eme ŋicguru i jaŋe taha gie baniŋte Mosezi moc mi muwec .
58007015	Erâ irec fuŋne moc taniŋke-hâmokac wâc . Taha bapa moc Melikisedere sâcko fuaocte mukicne ,
58007016	e sahaczi fuakicnere sâcmutâc râekicne irec sâcko mâcne , juju fofo sanaŋte tâpirio taha bapa erâ juwec jukac .
58007017	Ere hâcne dâŋ šiŋuc mutaniŋkekicne : “ Goki Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ . ”
58007018	Ine hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋ mârâc mukicne i tâpirimâc â fâri tâmiric ewecte bârâriekicne .
58007019	Sâcmutâc dâŋzi wiac moc mi emataucke-fârewec ” eme irec okacne woworic fârine bâfuakicne , izi fârec-nâpome Anutu sâcne maickeeŋgopeneŋ .
58007020	Ɋâricne fuawec i mumupaŋ dâŋsanaŋ tâmiric mi fuawec raŋɋane jaŋe mumupaŋ tâmiricko taha bapa erâ jumbiŋ .
58007021	Ɋâricne ši ine mumupaŋ faio taha bapa ewec jukac . Ere dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc fokac : “ Wofuŋzi mumupaŋ dâŋ muwec i mi beheocmu : ` Goki taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ ' . ”
58007022	Fuŋne iŋucte šâšâfic fârinere jâcne ewec , Jesu hâcne .
58007023	Raŋɋane jaŋe hâmohuc tuczi tuc juwarembiŋte bocjaha juwarembiŋ .
58007024	Ɋâricne e ine juju sanaŋ jukacte taha bapa gie-ticne šušuhuc focnehuc juocmu sanaŋ .
58007025	Irec ere ŋesiŋko Anutu maickeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne bâbâpiaŋko râe basanaŋ ejareekac , e juju sanaŋ jukaczi hâcne dameŋ sâc roroŋ sasape ejareekac .
58007026	Taha bapa sâko-nâŋec hâcne e furu , bahacmâc , ɋaɋacne , sâqocne bapa jaŋere sâcko mi juhuc qâtâcnerâ pectâc jujune , erâ sambâŋ hucke-fârewec jukac . Iŋucnezi hâcne junâreme sâcke-hâmokac .
58007027	E taha bapa raŋɋane jaŋe iŋucne mâcne , e sindaŋ tâmiriczi wemocko šoaŋne šoaŋne qanaŋ e jahacne sindaŋte erâ taha bâzi rikerâ šâhec ŋic jaŋere rikezac , e jahacne maŋ sahac i taha bâzi-nâŋec mocjaha hâcne râeme tarawec .
58007028	Sâcmutâc dâŋko ŋic maŋjeŋiczi dodocne jaŋe taha bapa sâko juniŋte mukicne . Eme šâhec ine sâcmutâc dâŋ faicnao mumupaŋ dâŋsanaŋzi Ŋokâ âkendâŋnewec . Eki hâcne maŋfuru jaha jurašihuc juocmu sanaŋ .
58008001	Dâŋ mukicne irec hândâŋne šiŋuc : Taha bapa sâko junârekac e faic sambâŋko femicne sâko ere ŋeŋefuŋko mefârenao fewec ŋeekac .
58008002	E furu ufuŋ , mitific fârine hâcne , irec taha bapa jukac . Ufuŋ i ŋiczi mâcne , Wofuŋ e jahac bâfuawec .
58008003	Taha bapa sâko sasawa jaŋe nânâ qowi bâzi râe rikec eniŋte mujarekicne , irec taha bapa sâko-nâŋec wemocko taha bâzi tâmiric juzac ?
58008004	Erâ e mâreŋko juhuc muzac taha bapa mi juzac , mâreŋko sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko bâzi ririke ŋic sâcne juŋgopieŋ .
58008005	Jaŋe gie-jeŋic mitific jabane â sâsâcne ira baeŋgopieŋ , fârine ine sambâŋko ŋekac . Mose e mitire qoruc boze bazo ehame Wofuŋzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Manakic , tikio hawarine gowatukicne irec sâcko wiac sasawa bazemec . ”
58008006	Ʒi ine Jesuzi šâšâfic fekicnere jâcne juekacte taha gie fekicne jaha baekac . Ʒâšâfic fekicne ine biŋedâŋ fekicnezi hobeteŋ ecneha bâfuakicne .
58008007	Mârâc šâšâfic fowec , izi fârinehec eme muzac šâhec moc fuaocte dâŋne mi fuazac .
58008008	Anutu eki ine ŋic jaŋere maname mi sâckeme šiŋuc muwec : “ Juku dameŋ mocko Israe kikefuŋ â Juda kikefuŋ jaŋehec šâšâfic ɋâricne moc bâfuapemu , Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac .
58008009	Mârâc mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic Aigita mâreŋkonec jowac-jopapere mejeŋicko rohuc jaŋehec šâšâfic epo , šâšâfic iŋucne mâcne ; jaŋe šâšâfic irec maŋnao paŋšâic mi jupie noni râpec-jopapo , Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac .
58008010	Á šâhec Israe kikefuŋ jaŋehec šâšâfic epemu ine kecšiŋuc : No mumupaŋ dâŋnane maŋjeŋicko râepe huocmu , erâ buhândâŋ-jeŋicko qâreŋkepe foocmu , eme no Anutu-jeŋic jupemu â jaŋe kikefuŋfâc-nane juniŋmu .
58008011	Eme ŋic moczi ŋicâgo-ticne me ŋic moczi qomâ-ticne šiŋuc mi muhuc miti qazucneocmu : Ajoc , go Wofuŋte fuŋne manac â ! ' Macne , jaŋe wahakicnezi mecne fekicnezi mecne mâmâc manacnu-fâreniŋmu .
58008012	Ʒiŋucte manacnuniŋmu : No kiŋjeŋic behe-jarepemu â sindaŋ-jeŋicte mocwâc mi manasupemu , Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac . ”
58008013	Eme Wofuŋ e šâšâfic ɋâricnere dâŋ muhuc , mârâc fowec irec “ raŋɋaŋkekicne ” muwec . Eme wiac raŋɋaŋkekicne â gufekicne izi arictac ezo ekac hâcne .
58009001	Ʒâšâfic raŋɋanao Wofuŋ mai eecnere hata fowec â irec tiri qoruc boze mâreŋko ŋewec wâc .
58009002	Mitire qoruc boze hâcne kecšiŋuc bambiŋ : Maŋne moc maine , šâŋene Furufic mukicne , ira kendo kikenehec domawec erâ tebo ŋewec fainao poroŋ furu mukicne i fowec .
58009003	Eme bumec maŋne moc âke tâcnekicne fowec , šâŋene Furu Dindiŋ mukicne .
58009004	Ira hosâc ririke alata golzi bakicne ŋewec , erâ šâšâficte qorac tapa katapa golzi ɋorockekicne i ŋewec , erâ Aroŋte gunu ɋârerâ gitec hekicne i â qorac tapa mâmâc râekicne .
58009005	Fainao ine tatamacte kerubim hawari jajahec fakec-jekiczi katapa tapane sâockehuc domapic . Irec dâŋ ninic jaha wemocko mufârezo .
58009006	Wiac iŋuc râepie fohame fic maŋne maine ira taha bapa jaŋe dameŋ sâc fec wahac ehuc gie-jeŋic bajumbieŋ .
58009007	Fic maŋne moc ira ine taha bapa sâko e bucticne jara moc maŋnao arec mocjaha fejujec . Erâ soc tâmiric aricne , sochec sasawa fehuc e jahacne â ŋic jaŋere bahacte tie jujec .
58009008	Wiac irec fuŋne Tiri Mârozi šiŋuc nâwotukac : Maŋne maine izi ŋehame furu ufuŋko rarašire hata mi fua tâcnekac .
58009009	Maŋne maine izi dameŋ šiŋuczia mâreŋko juŋgopeneŋ irec sâsâcne ekac . Tiri qoruc bozeo nânâ qowi bâzi râe rikec ee izi wemocko ŋic Anutu mai ecnembiŋ jaŋere maŋ bâpiaŋkezac ?
58009010	I sahackopec sâcmutâc dâŋ sawa , nânâ opâre â sahac šušurere dâŋ fowec iŋucne , i šâhec fârinezi âkehockeocte jaba fowec .
58009011	Kristo eki ine wiac fârine fuaocte mukicne irec taha bapa sâko fuawec , ehuc qoruc boze sâc moc , fârine jâmbâŋ , mezi mi bakicne , mâreŋko mi ŋeŋene , ira rašiwec .
58009012	Noniŋ bulimakao sochec mâcne , e jahacne sochec Furuficko arec mocjaha rašihuc kitâc-nâpowec izi fofo sanaŋ foocmu .
58009013	Noniŋ bulimakao soc â bulimakao šafe i ŋic wâwânâŋ fua-jarewec jaŋe epie furu bacjopame sahackopec ɋaɋackembiŋ ”
58009014	Kristo e ine Mâro juweczi jukac eki neŋgoc ŋecneha maŋ sahac-ticne Anutu taha bâzi furu biaŋ ecnewec , eme nâŋâc eebapa aputacnezi maŋnâŋec hegâpârembeŋ i Kristore soczi sâcne šure ɋaɋackeme Anutu jujune kiŋaŋ qacnenaŋmu .
58009015	Irec hâcne Kristo e šâšâfic ɋâricnere jâcne ewec , erâ šâšâfic raŋɋanao juhuc kiŋ bâfuakicne i taraocte hâmowec , eme irec biŋefâc-ticne jaŋe juju sanaŋte merâfâc roniŋte mujarekicne i sâcne roniŋmu .
58009016	Merâfâcte hata šiŋuc fokac : Runezi hâmome jaha rauckezo .
58009017	Ɋâricne juhame merâfâcte dâŋ mukicne i mâc foocmu , hâmome ine dâŋ irec fârine fuaocmu .
58009018	Irec hâcne šâšâfic raŋɋane i soc tâmiricko wâc mi fuawec .
58009019	Mose e sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc jâcne jâcne , mutâcnekicnere sâcko ŋic jazaku jaza-fârerâ bulimakao â noniŋsoc opâhec bâsifuckerâ kâcbiŋko lama kanšaŋ bâbâroŋ qâfiserâ izi soc tieme miti papia mecne ŋic ŋokac mecne mâmâc rua-jarewec .
58009020	Ehuc šiŋuc jazawec : “ Anutuzi šâšâficte dâŋ mupaŋke-ŋarejec irec soc ši hâcne . ”
58009021	Erâ taha boze â taha giere râqâc wiac i iŋuc jaha soczi ruacne-fârewec .
58009022	Ine hâcne , sâcmutâc dâŋko mukicnere wiac šeŋgoma qâririŋ soczi šure ɋaɋackezo , â soc tâmiricko sâqocne bâbâtâmire mi fokac .
58009023	Sambâŋko wiac fârine fokac irec sâsâc wiac i soc omanezi šure ɋaɋackeocte mukicne , â wiac fârine e jahacne ine taha furi sâkozi šure ɋaɋackeocte hatane mocjaha fokac .
58009024	Irec hâcne Kristo e furu ufuŋ mezi bakicne , fârine irec sâsâcne mac , ira mi rašiwec , e sambâŋ maŋnao rašiwec , eme ira Anuture maio juhuc nâŋâcnere erâ taha gie-ticne baekac .
58009025	Erâ e maŋ sahac-ticne hâsi fâri taha-nâŋec qikiŋneocte wâc mi fewec , taha bapa sâkozi jâmbomac jarane jarane feekac , ehuc e jahacne soc mâcne , soc jabane rorâ tiri ufuŋko feekac .
58009026	Kristo e iŋucnere sâc erâ muzac mâreŋ fuaweckonecteaŋ wemo afecne hâmo warehuc juzac . E ine iŋuc mi ehuc dameŋ ŋondeŋ tataranao due-nâŋec bahuc kiŋnâŋec bârârieocte fua tâcnewec .
58009027	Ŋiczi mocjaha hâmonaŋte munârekicne , eme irec faicnao dâŋnâŋec mumutara fuaocte mukicne ”
58009028	eme Kristo e iŋuc jaha , ŋic bocjaha kiŋjeŋic âsickehuc mocjaha hâcne hâmoweczi mocwâc sâqocnere gie baocte mâcne , e worickehuc jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe rocjopaocte sawa fua taniŋkeocmu .
58010001	Sâcmutâc dâŋko wiac mukicne i mâc šâhec fârine fuaocmu irec mumucne sawa fuakac , fârine jâmbâŋ mâcne . Irec taha bapa jaŋe sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc jarane jarane taha barâ ba epie ŋic ira Anutu mai ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne maŋfuru mi bacjopaekac .
58010002	Iŋuc eme muzac , taha bâzi ririke omaezac i ¡ Ira Anutu mai ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe kiŋfâsâc enšapiŋ muzac , kiŋjeŋicte manabâc mocwâc mi enšapiŋ .
58010003	Taha bâzi izi ine jarane jarane fuame kiŋjeŋicte manasueŋgopieŋ .
58010004	Noniŋ bulimakao soczi wemocko kiŋjeŋic bâtâmirezac ? I aricne .
58010005	Irec hâcne Kristo mâreŋko wahaocte dâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Taha bâzi fuŋne fuŋnere mi egareekac , sahac ine bâfua-narekomec .
58010006	Qowi hâcbuc ririke me sâqocnere taha bapa i fua-gareocte mi muekic .
58010007	Eme mupo , ` Manakic , no Anutu gore mic reŋkepere fisikopac ' , miti papiao nore dâŋ qâreŋkekicne irec sâcko . ”
58010008	Faic dâŋ šiŋuc muwec fokac , “ Taha bâzi fuŋne fuŋne â qowi hâcbuc sâqocnere taha irec mi egareekac â irec takicguekac ” wiac i sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko râe rikec ekicne .
58010009	Erâ dâŋ šiŋuc šuhuckerâ muwec : “ Manakic , gore dâŋ reŋkepere fisikopac ” , iŋuc muhuc wiac raŋɋane bârârierâ ɋâricne moc âkendâŋnewec .
58010010	Irec Anuture micdâŋte erâ Jesu Kristo e sahac-ticnezi taha bame maŋfuru embeŋ , i arec mocjaha ekicnezi fofo sanaŋ .
58010011	Taha bapa sasawa jaŋe šoaŋne šoaŋne gie-jeŋic bahuc bâzi ijaha hati rikerâ rike ehuc jueŋgopieŋ , eme izi kiŋ bahac sâcne moc mi bâtâmireekac .
58010012	Kristozi ine sâqocne-nâŋecte taha mocjaha bame tarame faic Anutu mefârenao fewec jukac .
58010013	Eme ira râsifâc-ticne dockerâ waha fohuc kike-ticnere ââtesiŋ eniŋte woŋec juekac .
58010014	Maŋfuru eere hatao juŋgopieŋ jaŋere taha mocjaha bahuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋicte gie batarawec .
58010015	Eme Tiri Mârozi irec dâŋ mufua-nârekac wâc . Qanaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc fokac , Wofuŋ e kecšiŋuc mukac :
58010016	“ Ʒâhec dameŋko jaŋehec šâšâfic epemu ine kecšiŋuc : No mumupaŋ dâŋnane maŋjeŋicko râepe huocmu , erâ buhândâŋ-jeŋicko qâreŋkepe foocmu . ”
58010017	Erâ šuhuckekac , “ No kiŋjeŋic behe-jarepemu â sindaŋ-jeŋicte mocwâc mi manasupemu . ”
58010018	Sâqocne tâmire-fâreme ine irec taha bapa iŋuc jaha omaeocmu .
58010019	Âgofâc , Jesu e socticnezi motâc ronârewecte furu ufuŋko fenaŋte maŋnâŋe . afeckekac .
58010020	Irec hatane ɋâricne â jujune ine e jahac bâšâwe-nârewec . Ehuc ââketâc fowec , sahac-ticne hâcne , i fotâcnerâ fewec .
58010021	Eme taha bapa fekicne Anuture ufuŋ qizeckerâ junârekac .
58010022	Irec nâŋâc mamanasiŋzi maŋnâŋec baafeckeha siocmâc mai ecnehuc junšepeneŋ . Ine qanaŋ maŋnâŋec kiŋzi hegâpârekicne i socticnezi ruacneme taniŋkeha â sahac-nâŋec opâ ɋaɋaczi šureha iŋuc sâcne enaŋmu .
58010023	Erâ mume sasanaŋzi wiac biŋe qanârewecte biŋedâŋ i kiki papaŋ jaha bajuhuc muhaŋnenšepeneŋ .
58010024	Erâ wâc sosoŋaŋ ehuc maŋjauŋte â eehâmo giere qaqafeŋ enšepeneŋ .
58010025	Ehuc mitire tutumaŋko gâcnezi mi fisihuc qâoma eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc mi ezo . Dameŋ sâko bâqiŋ-nâpokac , iŋuc hâcne manahuc šoɋac erâ faŋ qaqac enšepeneŋ .
58010026	Nâŋâc dâŋ fâri qizecnezi maŋnâŋec âke tamaehame sâqocne mana jaŋgeŋkehuc bapene mozi irec taha bame tâmireocmu ? Aricne , iŋuc mi fokac ,
58010027	ine okacne hâhâwicne â šocbâruŋ sâko izi sawa woŋec-nâŋec foocmu . Ʒocbâruŋ izi mitire râsifâc šâmiziec-jopaocmu hâcne .
58010028	Ŋic moczi Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ mana suahuc qame ŋic jajahec me jahec â moczi mujaŋgeŋkepie acmâc jaha qapie hâmoekac .
58010029	Eme ŋic moc e Anuture Ŋokâ ro waha âte ecnehuc , šâšâficte soc ruarâ maŋfuru ewec i mana suahuc aki anonoc rune Mâro musoriŋkeocmu , e okacne mo iŋucne fisicneocmu muŋgopieŋ ?
58010030	Nâŋâc dâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec ere fuŋne manaeŋgopeneŋ : “ Kiŋ babatara i nore gie , okacne babazu i noni epemu . ” Erâ moc šiŋuc fokac : “ Wofuŋ e ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋere dâŋ mutara-jareocmu . ”
58010031	Anutu jujune ere meo fefe i wiac hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ .
58010032	Ŋoŋe mârâc wiac ejumbieŋ irec manasunšepieŋ . Dameŋ ira maŋŋeŋiczi hae furehame fific guguriŋ maŋko juju gie sâko bahuc sanaŋkembiŋ .
58010033	Eme gâcne ŋoŋe imaŋ gomaŋ â šâic busâqoc fai-ŋeŋicko feme ŋic jaŋere maio mamakâc embiŋ , â gâcne ŋoŋe ine âgofâc-ŋeŋic wiac iŋucne ejarepie šâic-jeŋic mâmâc manambiŋ .
58010034	Ŋoŋe âgofâc-ŋeŋic kâpâcwâru ficko fepie jaŋere erâ buheric fua-ŋarewec , â moneŋ mafa ŋowac ropie ine mafa fârine fofone fonârekac muhuc manapie bubiaŋnehec ewec .
58010035	Eme ši hâbi-ŋeŋic mi goroŋkezejec , hâbihec juku furine kâcɋene rozo .
58010036	Irec ŋoŋe sasanaŋ bâfuarâ Anuture micdâŋkoa juku wiac biŋe qaŋarekicne irec fârine ronšepieŋ .
58010037	“ Irec dameŋ bembeŋne mac moc fokac i tarame wareocte mukicne e ŋeŋe râqâc mi ehuc biac fisiocmu .
58010038	Ŋicnane biaŋkekicnezi ine mamanasiŋte erâ juju hotâckeocmu , â docke pârâc eocmuo maŋnanezi manacnepe mi biaŋkeocmu . ”
58010039	Nâŋâc ine docke pârâc ehuc sisipiricko rara irec biŋe mâcne , nâŋâc manasiŋkehuc maŋ qâqâtâc ŋeŋezic irec biŋe .
58011001	Wiac biŋe qanârekicne i manapaŋkerâ irec woŋec juju , â wiac mi hohonene maŋzi sakarerâ babaju , izi mamanasiŋ ekac .
58011002	Mitiŋic raŋɋane jaŋe mamanasiŋ iŋucnehec jupie Anutuzi honec-jopame biaŋkewec hâcne .
58011003	Mâreŋ i Anuture micte fuawec , ine mamanasiŋhec juhuc mana taraeŋgopeneŋ . Wiac hohonene i mi honekickonec fuawec hâcne .
58011004	Mamanasiŋhec juhuc Abezi Anutu bâzi rikecneme honeme sâckeha Kaiŋte qikiŋnewec . Mamanasiŋ-ticnere hâcne Anutuzi honeme kiŋfâsâc eme bâzi-ticne rohuc fuŋne-ticne bataniŋkewec . E mamanasiŋhec juwecte manapene hâmokicnezi sifu dâŋ nâzâkac ekac .
58011005	Enoko e mamanasiŋhec juwec , irec hâmoczi mi bâuaocte Anutuzi ɋâricne bafewec . Iŋuc ecnewecte ŋiczi basambiŋ . Erâ mi feha fuŋne-ticne biac šiŋuc mutaniŋkekicne : Anutuzi e honeme biaŋkewec .
58011006	Mamanasiŋ tâmiric jupene Anutuzi honec-nâpome bibiaŋke ine mi fokac . Anutu mâc mai mi ecnezo , jukac i mana šakiezo , â maŋzi hefârepene tahac-nâpoekac dâŋ i mana šakiehuc mai ecnezo .
58011007	Noa e mamanasiŋhec juwecte Anutuzi wiac šâhec fuaocmu irec biŋe qanaŋ âzâcnewec . Âzâcneme araŋ bacnehuc wiacfâc-ticne ɋâricne juniŋte murâ woke bawec . Iŋuc ehuc ŋic kiŋjeŋicte fuŋne bataniŋkewec . Erâ mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee irec fârine rauckewec .
58011008	Abraham e mamanasiŋhec juwecte mâreŋ-ticne beherâ moc rauckeocte irec dâŋ erao fuame reŋkewec . Erâ mâreŋ irec me irec mukicne kâuc bahuc sifu rawec .
58011009	Mamanasiŋhecte mâreŋ biŋe qacnekicne ira ra fisirâ jaba juwec . Jaba juhuc bozeo sawa ŋeŋerâ juwec . Isaka â Jakobo jahe biŋe mâmâc qajactekicnezi sâc ijaha epic .
58011010	Abraham e hae ŋeŋe sanaŋ moc Anutuzi bâfuarâ basarickewec irec mamanacko juwec .
58011011	Sara e iŋuc jaha mamanasiŋhecte tâpiri fuacneme ŋokac qizec juipiehuc kiwechec ewec . Ine ɋâricte biŋe qacnewec ere , mume fufuazi mukac , muhuc iŋuc ewec .
58011012	Eme irec hâcne ŋic mocjaha , fua sawecte tâpiri-ticne arictac ehame , eraonec ɋâric fua sawec embiŋ jaŋe sambâŋko bâpiŋ ŋerakac irec sâc , erâ hâwecmecko moŋgeŋ forakac , ŋiczi mi wowosene , irec sâc fuambiŋ .
58011013	Ŋic izi hâcne mamanasiŋhec juhuc hâmo-fârembiŋ . Wiac biŋe qajarekicne irec fârine ine mi roro mâc taicko fome honerâ worickehuc jumbiŋ . Iŋuc ehuc fuŋne-jeŋic šiŋuc manambiŋ : Nâŋe mâreŋko hotâ â jaba juŋgopeneŋ .
58011014	Dâŋ iŋuc muhuc mâreŋ qizec moc bâfuaniŋte maŋjeŋic âeckeba ewec .
58011015	Erâ jaŋacne hae mâreŋ râpeckembiŋ irec maŋhâhâŋ mi ejarewec , irec ejareme muzac risiezo murâ sâcne risienšapiŋ .
58011016	Jaŋe ine hae mâreŋ biaŋ mocte maŋhâhâŋ ejarewec , sambâŋko fokac irec hâcne . Irec Anutu e jaŋere Anutu , ere iŋuc mupene maname mi sâqoreekac . Wemocte ? E jahac hae sâko moc bâfua-jarewec .
58011017	Abraham e Anutuzi esâickeme mamanasiŋhec juwecte Isaka taha bâzire qikiŋnewec , e biŋedâŋ roweczi ŋokâ-ticne mocjaha qikiŋnezo ewec hâcne .
58011018	Biŋedâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnekicne : “ Isakaraonec ɋâricfâcge fua sawec eraniŋmu . ”
58011019	I kecšiŋuc muhuc ewec : “ Anutu e ŋic hâmockonec bâɋârec-jopaocte tâpiri focnekac . ” Eme irec hâmockonec tinac bârisiecnewec .
58011020	Isaka e mamanasiŋhec juwecte Jakobo â Esau jambuŋ-jofahuc wiac šâhec fuaocmu irec findaŋdâŋ wâc jasawec .
58011021	Jakobo e mamanasiŋhec juwecte hâmozo ehuc Josefe ŋokâ jahec-ticne jambuŋ-jofawec , ehuc gunuzi âkesiŋnerâ ŋehuc Anutu dapecnewec .
58011022	Josefe e mamanasiŋhec juwecte hâmozo dameŋ-ticne maickeme Israe ŋic jaŋe juku Aigita mâreŋ beherâ raniŋmu irec manasurâ siec-ticnere qanaŋ dâŋ mutâcne-jarewec .
58011023	Mose fuame neŋgoc mamacne jahe mamanasiŋhecte motec honebâckerâ ŋicwofuŋ dâŋticnere mi hâwic-jofaha mosa jahec â moc soŋkepic .
58011024	Mose e mamanasiŋhec juwecte ine sokarâ Farao otâ-ticne-e ŋokâ mucneniŋte mupie qikiŋnewec .
58011025	E sâqocnere aŋac bembeŋne qikiŋnerâ Anuture ŋicfâc jaŋehec šâic busâqoc manaocte wosâewec .
58011026	Ehuc Aigita mâreŋkonec moneŋ mafa mâriri irec maname jawane ewec , â Kristore erâ mamakucne juocte ine maname fârine ewec . I juku furine roocte mana suhuc iŋuc ewec .
58011027	E mamanasiŋhec juwecte ŋicwofuŋ aaric-ticne qamaserâ Aigita mâreŋ behewec . Erâ Anutu mi hohonene e šâŋezi honehuc tinac erao siŋkewec .
58011028	Mose e mamanasiŋhec juwecte mume aakic lama hezurâ socnezi ficmotâc ruacnepie aŋelo momorizi jowaruhuc mârâc ŋokâfâc-jeŋic akic-jopawec .
58011029	Eme Israe ŋic jaŋe mamanasiŋhec jumbiŋte Hâwec Bâbâroŋko tiŋko rara tinac rahuc fotâcnembiŋ . Aigita ŋic jaŋe i jaha ezo mupie hâweczi ɋâcjopawec .
58011030	Israe ŋic jaŋe mamanasiŋhec jumbiŋte Jeriko haesac orâŋkekuhapie šoaŋ gie bapa 7 eme hericke qawec .
58011031	Sasec ŋokac Rahaba e mamanasiŋhec juwecte ŋic mâreŋ hone t^ecnepic jahe âgo ejactewec . Eme qaqatara ŋic jopambiŋko e akickekicne .
58011032	Erâ dâŋ gâcne wemocko mufârezo . Gideoŋ â Baraki â Simsoŋ â Jefita â Dawidi â Samue â porofete jaŋere binaŋ bafârepe muzac mâretec šorazac .
58011033	Jaŋe mamanasiŋhec jumbiŋte ŋic guru sâko bawahac-jopambiŋ . Bâbâtiŋ gie bâhâmombiŋ , wiac biŋe qajarekicne irec fârine rombiŋ , laioŋ micjeŋic bâbâzickembiŋ ,
58011034	šocbâruŋ fâro-ticne hemâteŋkembiŋ , šika faio feipiehuc ɋâricne jumbiŋ , dockekicnezi mocwâc sanaŋkembiŋ , šikao momori wânšâŋ embiŋ , mâreŋ gâcnaonec râsi jopa jâpec embiŋ .
58011035	Ŋokac gâcne jaŋere ŋokâ hâmockonec bâɋâre-jarekicne . Ŋic tucne bâšâic-jopahuc mâsi qâsi ejarekicne , eme “ miti behepie akic-ŋopazo ” jazapie , juju sanaŋte ɋâreniŋte manasuhuc qikiŋnembiŋ .
58011036	Ŋic tucne jaŋe maric maŋgâpâc â qa imac ejarekicne , â tucne jaŋe me kike-jeŋic qarâ kâpâcwâru ficko râec-jopakicne .
58011037	Tucne jaŋe qânâzi hehâmoc-jopakicne , tucne jopa qâšâic ejarekicne , tucne jaŋe segezi bâtâc-jopambiŋ , tucne jaŋe šikazi upe-jeŋic qâtâcnembiŋ . Jaŋe lama â noniŋ sahacne rufarâ rorocko juhuc bebekâne erâ šâŋ goma faio jujumbieŋ .
58011038	Iŋucnezi ŋic wemo-jeŋicte mâreŋko jupie sâckewec . Jaŋe tiki tuhuo mâreŋ â qorac hawecko foforâ jujumbieŋ .
58011039	I jaŋe sasawa mamanasiŋ-jeŋicte Anutuzi honec-jopame biaŋkewec , erâ sifu wiac biŋe qajarekicne irec fârine mi bâfuambiŋ .
58011040	Fuŋne šiŋucte : Anutu e nâŋâcnao wiac fekicne râeocte maname fowec , irec jaŋe nâŋâc tâmiricko juju saric bâfuaniŋte mi manasuwec .
58012001	Wišec guru sâko iŋucnezi karorac tinac erâ orâŋ-nâpoŋgopieŋte wiac bâmâc-nâpoekac i hetera-fârenšepeneŋ , â sâqocnere muczi fâfâc-nâpoekac i wâc hetâcnenšepeneŋ , ehuc hata nâwotukicne ira tatakic tâmiric gagasac jaha ranšepeneŋ .
58012002	Ehuc Jesu , mamanasiŋte micne bapa â mamanasiŋte fârine bâbâfua , erao findendeŋnehuc junšepeneŋ . E šeri bubiaŋ fuacneocte mukicne irec manasuhuc maripoŋte šâic manawec â mimi faio fefe mana suawec . Iŋuc erâ Anuture ŋeŋefuŋko mefârenao fewec ŋekac .
58012003	Sâqocne bapa jaŋe mukac mupe mo iŋucne ecnepie mana-bipierâ sanaŋkewec , ŋoŋe ere hâcne manasuhuc mi takirepie maŋŋeŋic betaŋkezejec .
58012004	Ŋoŋe sâqocnezi herokawec-ŋopazo eme samandiŋkerâ sahac-ŋeŋic bapie wozeme dodoma , i juwarehuc iŋuc sâcne mi embiŋ .
58012005	Erâ dâŋ moc “ ŋokâ ” muŋarehuc faŋ qaŋarekicne fokac irec nikec-ŋopawec me ? Dâŋ šiŋuc : “ Ŋokâ-nane , Wofuŋzi bâtiŋgume manatec wawahane mi ezejec , â bâšâicgume maŋge mi rokawezejec .
58012006	Wofuŋ e ŋic moc jauŋkezo murâ ba bâtiŋ ecneekac , â ŋic fuŋfuŋfâcne bacjopahuc qa qâtiŋ ejare-fâreekac . ”
58012007	Wofuŋzi ba bâtiŋ eŋarezo mume hâbi-ŋeŋic mi ŋeŋgoroŋkezejec . Anutuzi honec-ŋopame naru motecfâc-ticne epie iŋuc hâcne eŋareekac . Me mo mamaczi ŋokâ-ticne ba bâtiŋ mi ecneocmu ?
58012008	Ba bâtiŋ i ŋic gâcne sasawa ejarewec , eme ŋoŋe i tâmiric jupie ine naru motecfâcne mâcne , fiuckonec fuakicne muŋarezo .
58012009	Erâ moc mupe : Mâreŋ mamacfâc-nâŋec jaŋe qa bâtiŋ enârepie araŋ bajare jumbeneŋ . Eme qâqâtâcte Mamac e araŋ bašihuc bacnepene sâckeocmu . Iŋuc ehuc juhâmonaŋmu .
58012010	Jaŋe mamana-jeŋicte sâc jara dameŋ bembeŋne sawa qa bâtiŋ enâre jumbieŋ , eki ine wiac fârine fua-nâreocte enâreekac , e jahacne tiri jujuo šuhuckenaŋte hâcne .
58012011	Bâbâtiŋ fuaocmu sâc i qanaŋ manapene bubiaŋhec mi ehuc busâqochec eekac ” â šâhecko ine bâbâtiŋko juhuc sanaŋkeeŋgopieŋ jaŋerao fârine wamane fuaekac , šâŋene bahac fâsâc juju .
58012012	Eme ŋoŋe meŋeŋic betaŋkekicne â hoqaŋeŋ-ŋeŋic ŋetarakicne , irec âte tiŋnehuc sanaŋkenšepieŋ .
58012013	Ehuc hata bâšâwepie wiŋkeme ŋoŋeraonec puriŋ ekicnezi ira qac qâsoric tâmiric âte rahuc biaŋkenšepieŋ .
58012014	Ŋoŋe ŋic mâmâc sasawa jaŋehec wamao jujure giene banšepieŋ , erâ maŋfuru erâ juniŋte henširiŋnenšepieŋ , maŋwânâŋhec juku Wofuŋ hohone i mi fokac .
58012015	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi Anuture aki anonoc ririzacte soŋaŋ babac enšepieŋ . Erâ ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko šâŋ opac moczi gitec herâ šacŋopame sâqorenšipiŋte rucŋeŋic banšepieŋ .
58012016	Erâ ŋoŋeraonec moczi Esaure hata mi âtehuc sasecŋic â ŋic araŋ bapa tâmiric mi ezejec . E nânâ mocjaha mac irec erâ mârâc fufuare merâfâc qikiŋnewec .
58012017	Ŋoŋe ere manaeŋgopieŋ , e šâhec jambuŋ rozo mume sakarecnekicne . E wiac ewec i suame arictac eocte kio-bipiehuc emâmâŋkewec .
58012018	Ŋoŋe tiki moc ba bâuac eene , šocbâruŋnehec ira mi ra fisimbiŋ , erâ hâweŋ , dapâc â mâŋâŋ šâšâkiriŋne irec maŋnao mi rašimbiŋ .
58012019	Erâ qeŋfânâŋ sâko â dâŋowa i wâc mi manambiŋ . Manambiŋzi dâŋ niniŋkeocte numu huacbuc embiŋ .
58012020	Dâŋ kecšiŋuc mukicne , irec manapie hâhâwicne ewec : “ Qowi tiki âteuame qânâzi hehâmozo . ”
58012021	Wiac i bipic tatarane hec fuakume Mosezi muwec : “ No hâwicnume ɋarac ɋarac qakopac . ”
58012022	Ŋoŋe tiki iŋucnao mâcne , ŋoŋe Zioŋ tiki , Anutu jujune ere hae sâkoo , sambâŋte Jerusalemko fisimbiŋ . Ehuc aŋelo mi wowosec-jopane â šeri tutumaŋ sâko
58012023	â fuŋfuŋ gurufâc-ticne šâŋejeŋic sambâŋko qâreŋkekicne jaŋe hâcne maic-jopambiŋ . Ehuc Anutu , ŋic sasawa nâŋâcne mumutara maickembiŋ , â ŋic tiŋne furu bacjopakicne qâqâtâcfâc-jeŋic jaŋerao šuhuckembiŋ ”
58012024	â Jesu , šâšâfic ɋâricnere jâcne , erao fisirâ rurua soc maickembiŋ , soc izi Abe socticnezi wira wâwâsic ewec iŋuc mâcne , sâc moc wira wâwâsic eekac .
58012025	Ŋoŋe dâŋ ŋazaekac e râpeckenšipiŋte ruc bahuc junšepieŋ . Mârâc jaha mâreŋko waharâ dâŋ jazame qikiŋnepie okacne fisi-jarewec . Eme ši sambâŋko juhuc dâŋ nâzâekac , e râpeckerâ wemocko okac tâmiric junaŋmu .
