58012026	Mârâc jaha dâŋ mume mâreŋ qiriŋ qawec . Eme ši ine dâŋticne šiŋuc fokac : No juku mâreŋ mocwâc itiriŋkehuc sambâŋ mâmâc itiriŋkepemu .
58012027	Mocwâc itiriŋkepemu , iŋuc muwec , ine wiac bâfuakicne i itiriŋkeme ŋerisieocte manasuhuc muwec . Ŋerisieme fofo sanaŋ i fuarâ qiriŋmâc fozokac .
58012028	Nâŋâc uucmaŋ moc qiriŋmâc fofo sanaŋ rauckenaŋmu , irec Anutu mucne bacnenšepeneŋ , ehuc rumerâ araŋ bacnehuc , jahac maname biaŋkeekac irec sâcko kiŋaŋ qacnenšepeneŋ .
58012029	Ehuc šiŋuc mananšepeneŋ : Anutunâŋec e šocbâruŋ iŋucne .
58013001	Qoqomâzi jauŋ babac eeŋgopieŋ i ŋoŋerao mi wahazejec .
58013002	Ŋic hezu hewâneŋ ejareniŋte qâoma mi enšepieŋ . Gâcnezi ŋic hezu hewâneŋ ejareŋgopeneŋ muhuc aŋelo ejarembiŋ .
58013003	Âgofâc-ŋeŋic kâpâcwâru ficko râec-jopakicne jaŋere manasuhuc manapie mâmâc râec-ŋopakicne tinac ezejec . Erâ ŋoŋe sahachec jaha juŋgopieŋte qa imac ejarekicne jaŋere wâc manasunšepieŋ .
58013004	Ŋowe ŋonâŋ jujure manapie wiac fârine eha fofo wirecko gâc mi hezejec . Boe sau â šuhuc bâtâc eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe Anutuzi okacne jareocmu .
58013005	Maŋŋeŋiczi moneŋ mafare harac mi ezejec . Wiac foŋarekac sâc mukâroŋ tâmiric bajunšepieŋ . Wofuŋ e jahac šiŋuc muwec : “ Noni mi behecgupemu , â hone qâoma moc mi egarepemu . ”
58013006	Irec nâŋâc hâbi-nâŋec rohuc šiŋuc munšepeneŋ : “ Wofuŋ e ŋeŋezic-nane , no mi hâwicnuzejec ; ŋic jaŋe wemo enareniŋmu ? ”
58013007	Micne bapafâc-ŋeŋic Anuture dâŋ ŋaza qazuc embiŋ jaŋere manasuhuc junšepieŋ , erâ miti hata âteku hâmombiŋ itirocne honehuc jaŋere bâjâpecne mamanasiŋhec junšepieŋ .
58013008	Jesu Kristo e juweczi jukac ijaha jurašihuc juocmu sanaŋ .
58013009	Mu qaqazuc dâŋ kosane hazec furu ŋazapie izi maŋŋeŋic mi hesifuckezejec ” maŋŋeŋic aki anonoczi keteŋneme qiŋ herâ fome biaŋkeocmu , wiac nâkicnezi sâcne mi basanaŋkeocmu . Hata i âtembiŋzi fârine mi bâfuambiŋ .
58013010	Nâŋâcne alata ŋekac , irec nânâ i qoruc boze kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe nâniŋte mi mana-jarekicne .
58013011	Ŋoŋe manaeŋgopieŋ , qowi hezurâ socjeŋic taha bapa sâkozi sâqocnere kiŋte furu ufuŋko bafeme fârine hae sahao bahurâ šoczi rikeeŋgopieŋ .
58013012	Eme Jesu e iŋuc jaha socticnezi ŋic maŋfuru bacnâpoocte hae sahao qapie hâmowec .
58013013	Irec nâŋâc iŋuc jaha hae sahao erao hurâ , eki mimi faio fewec ijaha enšepeneŋ .
58013014	Ʒiŋuc manahuc enšepeneŋ : Hae ŋeŋe sanaŋ moc šira mi ŋenârekac ” moc juku fufuane irec maŋhâhâŋ enâreekac .
58013015	Irec nâŋâc Jesure erâ Anutu šušuhuc jaha mumuteŋ ecnepene izi taha bâzi-ticne ezejec , micbipic-nâŋecte fârine šâŋe-ticne muac baafec enšepeneŋ hâcne .
58013016	Jauŋ â bâmec baniŋte qâoma mi enšepieŋ , Anutu e irec hâcne maname taha bâzi fârine eocmu .
58013017	Micne bapafâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋkehuc sâsec-jopanšepieŋ ” jaŋe maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋic hone soŋaŋ eeŋgopieŋzi juku gie-jeŋicte fuŋne mutaniŋkeniŋmu . Irec gie-jeŋic bubiaŋko bapie sâckeocmu , busâqocko bahapie ŋoŋerao wiac sâcne mi biaŋkeocmu .
58013018	Ŋoŋe nâŋere erâ numuhuc junšepieŋ . Nâŋe pectâc sasawa junaŋte šoɋac eeŋgopeneŋzi maŋnâŋecko bahac basaeŋgopeneŋ .
58013019	Nunumuzi baficnupie Wofuŋzi bârisiecnume ŋoŋerao biac fâpemurâ ŋaza sanaŋkekopac .
58013020	Wama Anutu e lama soŋaŋ sâko Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu šâšâfic fofo sanaŋ irec socte hâmockonec bârisiewec ,
58013021	Anutu eki hâcne wiac biaŋne fuŋne fuŋne tahac-ŋopahuc baafec-ŋopame dâŋticne reŋkenšepieŋ , erâ e jahac maname sâckeekac i Jesu Kristore erâ ŋoŋerao bâfuazejec . Erao mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
58013022	Âgofâc , no dâŋ šoricne boc mi qâreŋkepac , eme ŋoŋe uŋsawaŋ dâŋ i manapie mi sâqoreocte esoc-ŋopakopac .
58013023	Erâ ŋazape mananiŋ , âgo-nâŋec Timoteo e firuembiŋ , biac wareme jowape fanacmu .
58013024	Micnefâc-ŋeŋic â mitiŋic ŋokac sasawa manasu-ŋare-fârekopac . Italia mâreŋkonec jaŋe manasu-ŋareŋgopieŋ .
58013025	Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fofârezejec .
59001001	Jakobo no Anutu â Jesu Kristo ere kiŋaŋ qaqazi Israe ŋicguru 12 siŋsaŋ qarâ juraŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe mu šeri eŋarehuc papia ši ŋe-ŋarekopac .
59001002	Ŋoŋerao eesâic fuŋne fuŋne fuame manapie bubiaŋnehec sasawa ezejec .
59001003	Wiac iŋucnezi hâcne mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic ba esâic ecnekume gâtâ bame ŋoŋerao sasanaŋ fuaocmu .
59001004	Sasanaŋte fârine ŋoŋerao fua-hâmozejec , eme wiac moc mi basahuc bahacmâc â maŋfuru junšepieŋ .
59001005	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi maŋɋârâŋ basarâ Anutu numucnezejec . Eme e ŋic sasawa , dâŋ mi munârehuc , wiac maŋhumuc nâreekaczi bâfuacneocmu .
59001006	Nunumu ine maŋjahec ehuc mâcne , Wofuŋ manasiŋkehuc numucnezejec . Maŋjahec eocmu e hâwec siri , mâŋâŋzi ficne sueme fâuckerâ tâtieekac , iŋucne eocmu .
59001007	Ŋic iŋucnezi Wofuŋtaonec wiac moc roocmu mi muzejec .
59001008	Maŋguru â tie faranezi wemocko iŋuc eocmu .
59001009	Opâ ruac wahakicnezi fekicne jukopac muhuc maname šerine ezejec .
59001010	Á mafaŋiczi wahakicne jukopac muhuc maname šerine ezejec . Jâcârizi ŋeindaŋnerâ biac mârâŋkeekac , iŋuc jaha mafaheczi biac siroweniŋmu .
59001011	Ʒoaŋ e furicte wefurâ šocnezi šariŋ rikeme ɋaŋame ârine mârâŋkeme eri-ticne wahaekac , iŋuc jaha mafaŋic jaŋe ɋaŋapie qâŋtac-jeŋic sawa ŋeocmu .
59001012	Ŋic moc e eesâicko qiŋ herâ juocmu ere manape šerine ekac E sanaŋkeku maŋne eme Wofuŋzi eri hendiŋ juju sanaŋ hâcne râcneocmu maŋjeŋic ere domakac jaŋe biŋe qajarekicne .
59001013	Ŋic moc sâqocnere eesâic fuacneme šiŋuc mi muzejec : Anutuzi esâic nukac . Sâqocnere eesâic Anuturao fufuane mi fokac , â eki wâc ŋic moc sâqocnere mi esâickeocmu .
59001014	Eesâic ine kecšiŋuc fuaocmu , qanaŋ ŋic moc e jahacne saseczi beŋgisic sicnecnehuc hehawickeocmu .
59001015	Eme saseczi motec kiweckerâ roocmu , šâŋene sâqocne ” sâqocnezi ine woze qeuc eku hâmoc bâfuaocmu .
59001016	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , ŋoŋe dâŋ mi mana sifuckenšepieŋ ,
59001017	jauŋ biaŋne â taha fârine i faicnec sasawa , tatamac Mamac eraonec wahaekac , erao hâcne hec hetikic â sâsâoc mi fokac .
59001018	Anutu e manapaŋkewecte dâŋfârizi naru motecfâcne bâfuac-nâpowec , i wiac sasawa bâfuawec irec hata qaqasune tinac enaŋte iŋuc enârewec .
59001019	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , mananiŋ . Ŋiczi dâŋ mamanare afeckenšepeneŋ , dâŋ mumure â aaricte ine ŋemâckenšepeneŋ .
59001020	Aaricko wiac eeŋgopeneŋ izi Anuture tiŋne hata ririekac .
59001021	Irec ŋoŋe maŋwânâŋ â râŋgeŋ bârâŋgeŋ hetararâ urucko juhuc maŋŋeŋicko mitidâŋ râekicne i âgo ecnenšepieŋ . Izi hâcne maŋ qâqâtâc-nâŋec bâpiaŋkeocte tâpiri focnekac .
59001022	Ŋoŋe mitidâŋte fârine bâfuanšepieŋ , mâc hazecte nâpene sawa eme maŋŋeŋic eatuckeniŋmu .
59001023	Moc e mitidâŋ mana qâoma eocmu , e ŋiczi šâŋe mai-nâŋec hawario honerâ eeŋgopeneŋ , sâc ijaha eocmu .
59001024	Ʒâŋe mai-nâŋec hawario honerâ ra qâoma erâ izia hawari-nâŋecte nikec-nâpoekac .
59001025	Á moc e sâcmutâc dâŋ fârine , rambaŋko rârâec-nâpone , dâŋ ira mana utuckerâ juocmu , ehuc mana qâoma mâcne , mana rereŋ eocmu , iŋucnezi ine dâŋte fârine bâfuarâ mana aŋac eocmu .
59001026	Moc e mitio jukopac muekaczi micbipic-ticne mi soŋaŋkehuc maŋticne eatuckeekac , ŋic iŋucnere mitio juju i racne eocmu .
59001027	Hozec bekâ busâqocko juhapie hone maiŋ ejarezo â mâreŋko sâqocne fokac izi maŋnâŋec hegâpârezacte pectâc juzo , izi Anutu â Mamac ere maio wâwânâŋ tâmiricko mitio juju ekac .
59002001	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe tatamac Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋzi ŋic fekicne wahakicne wiac sâctiri mi ejarenšepieŋ .
59002002	No kecšiŋucte mukopac : Tutumaŋ-ŋeŋicko ŋic moc boreŋ qonaŋkerâ ŋaqi erinehec hefâocmu , eme ere râpefuŋko ŋic hapetac moc ŋaqi taocnehec hefâocmu .
59002003	Ehame ŋoŋe ŋic ŋaqi erinehec erao šâŋe firâ šiŋuc âzâcneniŋmu : “ Go šira ware popoo ŋec . ” Iŋuc murâ hapetac e šiŋuc âzâcneniŋmu : “ Go ocna domac , me ɋâriŋko waha ŋec . ”
59002004	Ŋoŋe ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko ŋic teŋtiri ejareeŋgopieŋ , i maŋŋeŋicko dâŋ repicne soŋkepie fokacte wiac esifuckeeŋgopieŋ hâcne .
59002005	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , dâŋ mupe mananiŋ : Anutuzi ŋic weniŋucne rowosâec-jopawec ? Mâreŋko hapetac jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne mamanasiŋko maŋ mâririhec erâ uucmaŋ rauckeniŋte rowosâec-jopawec . I irec ejareekac jaŋe hâcne biŋe qajarewec .
59002006	Eme ŋoŋe ine hapetac jaŋe šâŋe titikic honec-jopaeŋgopieŋ . Á weni jaŋezia bâuruŋ-ŋoparâ kiarao râec-ŋopaeŋgopieŋ ? Mafahec jaŋe hâcne iŋuc eŋareeŋgopieŋ .
59002007	Ehuc wâc šâŋe biaŋ fai-ŋeŋicko fewec e musoriŋkeeŋgopieŋ .
59002008	“ Gahacnere egareekac sâc ijaha âgogere egarezejec ” , sâcmutâc dâŋ neŋgocne iŋuc qâreŋkekicne fokac , i reŋkepie jâmbomac biaŋkeocmu .
59002009	Á ŋic sâctiri ejareniŋmu , ine bahac bâfuapie sâcmutâc dâŋzi qaqatara ŋic eŋgopieŋ irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu .
59002010	Moc e sâcmutâc dâŋ gâcne reŋke-fârehuc mocjaha qatarame sâcmutâc dâŋ qâqâhâc qatarawec eocmu .
59002011	“ Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋohe bebehec mi ezepirec ” muwec ekizia wâc “ go šika mi qazemec ” muwec . Eme go ŋonâŋge mi behecmu , šika ine qacmu , ine dâŋ qaqatara ŋic ecmu .
59002012	Sâcmutâc dâŋ rambaŋko rârâec-nâpo izi juku fuŋne babataniŋ dameŋko rambaŋko râec-ŋopaocte wiac mana tarahuc mu bac enšepieŋ .
59002013	Ŋic uruc jauŋ tâmiric juocmu e wâc juku uruc jauŋ mi ecnezo . Uruc jauŋhec juocmu e fuŋne babataniŋko hâhâwic tâmiric domaocmu .
59002014	Âgofâc-nane , ŋic moczi “ mamanasiŋhec jukopac ” muocmu , ehuc eehâmo gie mi baocmu , e mamanasiŋ-ticnezi moc bafickeocmu me ? Mamanasiŋzi wemocko sisipirickonec bataraocmu .
59002015	Ŋic me ŋokac âgo-ŋeŋic moczi qoruc ŋaqi me nânâ wiac basahuc juhame
59002016	ŋoŋeraonec moczi e šiŋuc âzâcneocmu : “ Go sâcne ra juzemec , erâ fâfârezicte sahacge foŋkezemec â nânâ nâ gapec ezemec ” , moc e miczi iŋuc sawa muhuc jauŋ mi bacneocmu , izi wemocko bafickeocmu ?
59002017	Irec mamanasiŋ bucticne , fârine eehâmo gie mi fuaocmuo , hâmo mâteŋ ekicne muzo .
59002018	Me moczi šiŋuc mecne muocmu : “ Go mamanasiŋ fogarekac , â no eehâmo gie fonarekac . ” Me , mamanasiŋge eehâmo gie tâmiric i nowatutec honepe . Á no eehâmo gie bahuc mamanasiŋ-nanere fuŋne sâcne gowatupemu .
59002019	Anutu mocjaha jukac , dâŋ i mana šakiekic ” i sâcne ekic . Dâŋ i demoŋ jaŋe wâc mana šakieŋgopieŋ , ehuc ɋarac ɋarac qaeŋgopieŋ .
59002020	Ŋic maŋtac go mamanasiŋ eehâmo gie tâmiriczi wiac jawane ekac irec fuŋne ši manac .
59002021	Mimiŋne-nâŋec Abraham e ŋokâ-ticne Isaka taha bâzi rikeocte alatao râewec ira Anutuzi manacneme kiŋfâsâc ewec i eebapa-ticnere hâcne .
59002022	Eme šiŋuc honekic : Abraham mamanasiŋ-ticne I eebapa-ticnezi bafickewec , ehuc mamanasiŋ-ticne qizecne qawec .
59002023	Eme irec hâcne Abrahamte dâŋqâreŋ kecšiŋuc fokac i sanaŋkewec : “ Abraham e Anutu manasiŋkeme ere maname kiŋfâsâc ewec . ” Eme irec šâŋe-ticne Anuture âgo mucnekicne
59002024	Honeŋgopieŋ , Anutu e ŋic moc mamanasiŋ-ticnere sawa mi maname kiŋfâsâc eocmu , fârine eehâmo gie bame manacneme kiŋfâsâc eocmu .
59002025	Á sasec ŋokac Rahaba e iŋuc jaha mamanasiŋ-ticnere fârine eehâmo gie bame Anutuzi manacneme kiŋfâsâc ewec . E ŋic mâreŋ hone tâcnepic jahe erao fisipire âgo ejacterâ hatasoŋko râec-jofame wisepic .
59002026	Irec šiŋuc fokac : Sahac e mâro tâmiric erâ qâŋɋâŋ eekac , iŋuc jaha mamanasiŋzi eehâmo gie tâmiric qâŋɋâŋne jaha eekac .
59003001	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe bocjahazi qaqazu gie baniŋte mi fotarienšepieŋ . Manaŋgopieŋ , mumutara dameŋko Wofuŋzi qaqazu nâŋe wiac bašihuc enâreocmu .
59003002	Nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa wiac gâbâ esifuckeeŋgopeneŋ . Ŋic moc e dâŋko moc mi sâqoreocmu , e ŋic saric sarahaŋne mucnezo . Iŋucnezi me sahac-ticne sasawa guriŋne sâcne bafâreocmu .
59003003	Becâsic jaŋe dâŋnâŋec reŋkeniŋte micko kiki râe-jareeŋgopeneŋ . Erâ izi becsâko bac bâtikic ejareeŋgopeneŋ .
59003004	Wokere wâc manaeŋgopeneŋ , jaŋe kâcɋene sâko , erâ mâŋâŋ sanaŋnezi ficne suec-jopame raeŋgopieŋ , eme sifu guriŋ bapa e guriŋ piticne i bac bâtikic ehuc hata muocmu ijaha wokezi raocmu .
59003005	Eme ŋicnameŋ e iŋuc jaha wiac piticne , erâ wiac wemo afecne efeekac . Manaŋgopieŋ , šoc masisi i wiac huŋgaŋne mac , eme iŋucne maczi sopâc sâko rikepene šafâreekac .
59003006	Eme nameŋ-nâŋec šoc masisi iŋucnea wâc . Eki hâcne me sahac gâcne siric-jopahuc sâqocnere neŋgocne eekaczi sahac-nâŋec bâbie-fâreekac â juju-nâŋecte ŋesiŋ rikeme šafâreekac ” e jahacne ine hârâckonec šoczi qâhâsâme šaekac .
59003007	Qowi fuŋne fuŋne tiŋkonec â hâweckonec erâ wipe homa wiac i ŋiczi bâmâteŋkezo murâ bâmâteŋkeeŋgopeneŋ .
59003008	Nameŋ ine mo ŋic mozi bâmâteŋkeocmu ? E gapec tâmiric ririsiehuc sâqocne baekac , qotâre micopâzi fusucmakicne tinac .
59003009	Nameŋ-nâŋeczi Wofuŋ Mamac muteŋkeeŋgopeneŋ , erâ nameŋzia ŋic Anuture hawarifâc sâwec-jopaeŋgopeneŋ .
59003010	Mic ijaha mumuteŋ â sâwec wahaekac . Âgofâc-nane , iŋuc wemocte ?
59003011	Opâ šâŋe ijaha nocne â hâtâne ataŋ wahaekac me ?
59003012	Âgofâc , hâmeŋko woraŋ fuaocmu ? Me saŋko hâmeŋ fuaocmu ? Me hâweczi nocne eocmu ?
59003013	Ŋoŋerao maŋɋârâŋhec â maŋ manahuc wiac ee iŋucne moc juŋgopieŋ me ? Ine wama ruaine juhuc eebapa biaŋne bâfuahuc maŋɋârâŋ-jeŋicte fuŋne bataniŋkenšepieŋ .
59003014	Á maŋjeŋicko iiŋguuŋ hâtâne â hehefaric fohame ine sahac-jeŋic bafehuc dâŋfâri manaŋgopeneŋ mupie burec eocmu .
59003015	Maŋɋârâŋ hata iŋucne i faicnec wahakicne mi muzo , aricne , mâŋɋârâŋ hata iŋucne i mâreŋkonec , ŋickonec , Sataŋtaonec .
59003016	Iiŋguuŋ â hehefaric foocmu ijaha wâc fâfâuc â wiac gâgâpâcne gâcne gâcne fofâreocmu .
59003017	Maŋɋârâŋ hata faicnec izi ine wiac šiŋuc bâfuaekac : Qanaŋ maŋɋaɋac , erâ wama , miriŋ , micrereŋ , uruc jauŋhec juju â mitire fârine gâcne , erâ wâc maŋguru tâmiric â siocmâc juju .
59003018	Wamare guriŋne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe wamao ukicne sara mamac epie fârine tiŋne juju fua-jareekac .
59004001	Ŋoŋerao šika â rârâsi foekac i fuŋne weniŋucte ? Me sahac-ŋeŋicko andac forakac izi hâcne šika gie baekac .
59004002	Ŋoŋe andac eipiehuc wiac mi rauckeeŋgopieŋ . Ŋoŋe qaqac â iiŋguuŋ eec ehuc sifu wiac sâcne mi hotâckeeŋgopieŋ . Ŋoŋe kikisâ â kikisuec ehuc wiac sâcne mi hure nâc eeŋgopieŋ . I nunumu tâmiric jueŋgopieŋ irec .
59004003	Moc i numu-bipiehuc wiac mi roeŋgopieŋ , ine maŋŋeŋicko dâŋ sâqocne šiŋuc foha numueŋgopieŋte : “ Wiac fua-nâreme samarierâ andac-nâŋecte fârine bâfuanšepeneŋ . ”
59004004	Oi , šâšâfic hehetâc ŋic ŋoŋe ¡ Mâreŋko wiac fokac irec biŋe juocmuzi Anutu râpeckeocmu , i mi manaŋgopieŋ me ? Irec moc e mâreŋkopec wiac kosa âgo ecneocmuzi Anutu kisâ ecneocmu .
59004005	Me dâŋqâreŋ kecšiŋuc fokac i ŋoŋe manapie racne eekac me ? “ Maŋnâŋecko mâro ŋewec i ere biŋe sawa juocte šoɋac sâko eekac . ”
59004006	Erâ ŋifec ine aki anonoc wemo afecne sicne-nâreekac . Irec dâŋqâreŋ hâcne kecšiŋuc fokac : “ Anutu e ŋic maŋfefe dope qatara-jareekac , ŋic maŋhuhuŋ ine aki anonoc sicne-jareekac . ”
59004007	Irec ŋoŋe Anuture rurumaŋko raširâ domanšepieŋ . Ehuc Sataŋ bâsuenšepieŋ , eme behec-ŋoparâ wiseocmu .
59004008	Ŋoŋe Anutu maickepie eki wâc maic-ŋopaocmu . Sâqocne bapa , maŋŋeŋic ra qa ware qa eekac , ŋoŋe meŋeŋic šurerâ maŋŋeŋic baɋaɋackenšepieŋ .
59004009	Ŋoŋe fuŋne-ŋeŋic mana tararâ ki busâqoc enšepieŋ . Gâgâwi-ŋeŋiczi rirehame busâqoc fuazejec , â šeri-ŋeŋiczi rirehame ki mamakuc fuazejec .
59004010	Wofuŋte maio maŋhuhuŋ jupie eki bafaharec-ŋopaocmu .
59004011	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe mumusâqoc mi enšepieŋ . Moc e âgo-ticne musâqorerâ okacne dâŋko râeocmu , e sâcmutâc dâŋ musâqorehuc hetâtieocmu . Go ine sâcmutâc dâŋ hetâtiecmuo rereŋŋic mi ehuc mumutara ŋic ecmu .
59004012	Sâcmutâc dâŋ irec mumufua â soŋaŋ mocjaha sawa jukac , aakic â bebehe irec gie ekizia baocmu . Go ine wemogezi âgoge okacne dâŋko râecmu ?
59004013	Ajoc , moc ši mananiŋ . ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ : Miŋecgac me tomâcko hae ira ra moneŋ mafa hurehuc juhapene jara moc tarame risienšepeneŋ . ”
59004014	Oi ŋoŋe , tomâcko wiac iŋuc me iŋuc fuaocmu , i moc manaeŋgopieŋ ? Me juju-ŋeŋic i weniŋucne ? I rombâŋ iŋucne , fua fuahuc izia qašueekac .
59004015	Irec ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mupie sâckeocmu : “ Wofuŋzi mana-nâreme ɋâricne juhuc iŋuc me iŋuc enšepeneŋ . ”
59004016	Ŋoŋe ine pacgoroŋ dâŋ boc muhuc sahac-ŋeŋic bafeeŋgopieŋ . Pacgoroŋ dâŋ i wiac sâqocne .
59004017	Ŋic moc e wiac biaŋne eocte mana tarahuc sifu qikiŋneekac , e bahac bâfuakac muzo .
59005001	Ajoc , mafa mâririhec ŋoŋe šârâ hâriŋ fua-ŋareocmu irec qanaŋ ki mamakuc enšepieŋ .
59005002	Mafa mâriri-ŋeŋic i šaŋke-fârewec , ŋaqi guru dindiŋ-ŋeŋic mâreŋte temane ewec ,
59005003	â moneŋ boreŋ-ŋeŋic gufewec , eme gufe izi ŋaŋacne fuŋne bataniŋkehuc sahac-ŋeŋic šoc iŋucne nâmizieocmu . Ŋoŋe dameŋ qândâŋkeha mafa sesuc sembureŋ hefembiŋ .
59005004	Manaŋgopieŋ , padi qaŋarepie gie furi sakare-jarembiŋ irec kiŋzi hohosâcne qakac , erâ qa roro ŋic jaŋere kio wâwâsiczi sambâŋ momori jaŋere Wofuŋte hazecko huwec .
59005005	Ŋoŋe mâreŋko wiac nâminširiŋkehuc mana aŋac embiŋ â okac dameŋ maickeha nâ areŋ embiŋ .
59005006	Ŋoŋe ŋic tiŋne dâŋne mutararâ šikao râembiŋ . E sahac-ticne mi ŋezickekac .
59005007	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋe Wofuŋ fisiocte woŋec tatakic tâmiric junšepieŋ . Manaŋgopieŋ , gie rune moczi iŋuc jaha nânâ he sarac erâ fârine fua biaŋ eocte woŋec juekac , ehuc hoe šoaŋ sâckoa bacneme fua sokac eocte mamanac juekac .
59005008	Eme Wofuŋte dameŋ bembeŋkekacte ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha tatakic tâmiric woŋec juhuc maŋŋeŋic keteŋnenšepieŋ .
59005009	Âgo bureŋ , ŋoŋe mu takic mi eec enšepieŋ ” manaŋgopieŋ mumutara ŋic e motâc râpeo domakac , fuŋne-ŋeŋic rituzacte dâŋ ere biŋe râepie fozejec .
59005010	Âgofâc-nane , porofete Wofuŋte micte dâŋ mumbiŋzi šâic busâqoc tatakic tâmiric manahuc jumbiŋ jaŋere kike hata bâjâpehuc junšepieŋ .
59005011	Manaŋgopieŋ , šâicmaŋko sasanaŋhec jumbiŋ jaŋere manapene šerine ekac . Hiobe sasanaŋ-ticnere manaeŋgopieŋ , â Wofuŋzi šâhec wiac afusecnewec i wâc manaeŋgopieŋ . Wofuŋ e buuruc â jauŋ-ticne kâcɋene fokac hâcne .
59005012	Âgofâc-nane dâŋ fârine moc ši : ŋoŋe sambâŋko ɋetickehuc mumupaŋ , me mâreŋko ɋetickehuc mumupaŋ , me wiac mocko ɋetickehuc mumupaŋ , i mi enšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe dâŋŋeŋic jâmbomacte fârine jâmbomac ezejec â aricnere fârine aricne jaha ezejec . I kiŋ bâfuanšipiŋte iŋuc enšepieŋ .
59005013	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi šâic busâqocko juocmu , e Anutu numucnezejec , me moczi bubiaŋko juocmu , e mumuteŋ gae hezejec .
59005014	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi huc foocmu , e kikefuŋte micne bapa hefârec-jopame fisirâ ere faio numunšepieŋ , erâ Wofuŋte šâŋe muhuc wokemaŋ opâ ruacnenšepieŋ .
59005015	Eme mamanasiŋko nunumu mukicne izi huchec bâpiaŋkeocmu â Wofuŋzi e ɋiɋicne baocmu . Á sâqocne bawecko i bâtâmirecneocmu .
59005016	Irec ŋoŋe ɋiɋic qaniŋte sâqocne mumufuac erâ nunumuzi dodopec enšepieŋ . Ŋic tiŋne moczi numume tâpirinehec eocmu .
59005017	Elia e ŋic jaha , nâŋâc iŋucne . Eme eki hoe mi heocte samarierâ numume mâreŋko jara jahec â moc â mosa 6 hoe mi hehe mâc fowec .
59005018	Eme šâhec mocwâc numume sambâŋkonec hoe wahame mâreŋko wiac ukicne âkešuwec .
59005019	Âgofâc-nane , ŋoŋeraonec moc e dâŋfârire hata qâsorieme âgo moczi bâtikieocmu ,
59005020	e dâŋ šiŋuc manazejec : Moc e âgo-ticne hata sâqocnaonec bârisieocmuzi e jahacne maŋ qâqâtâc hâmockonec bataraocmu â sâqocne guru sâko sâockeocmu .
60001001	Petoro no Jesu Kristo ere aposolo jukopaczi Anutu bâwosâecfâc-ticne Ponto â Galatia â Kapadokia â Asia â Bitinia mâreŋko ocŋondeŋ jaba juraŋgopieŋ ŋoŋere papia ši qâreŋkekopac .
60001002	Anutu Mamaczi maname fowecte rowosâec-ŋopawec ŋoŋe hâcne Mârozi maŋfuru bacŋopaocte â mume rereŋfâcne eniŋte Jesu Kristore soc ruambiŋ : Ŋoŋerao aki anonoc â wama fua bâbâriŋ fuahuc fozejec .
60001003	Nâŋâc Anutu , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Mamac , e muteŋkenšepeneŋ . Eki Jesu Kristo hâmockonec faharewecte uruc jauŋ sâko-ticnere erâ , juju fârire mamanac junaŋte bâɋârec-nâpowec .
60001004	Sambâŋko merâfâc-ŋeŋic šašaŋke tâmiric â bie gufec tâmiric â hâmo qanšaraŋ tâmiric woŋec-ŋeŋic râekicne fokac , i juku rauckeniŋte iŋuc hâcne eŋarewec .
60001005	Ehuc Anutu tâpiri-ticnezi bâwâzâŋ-ŋopame mamanasiŋhec juhapie juku dameŋ tarame bâbâpiaŋ kâdoc bâmockekicne i fua tâcneocmu .
60001006	Ŋoŋe irec šeri ehuc juŋgopieŋ , â Anutuzi muŋareme fific guguriŋ faio ferâ šâic busâqocko juhuc sifu dameŋ bembeŋne macte jamaŋ kirâ jueŋgopieŋ .
60001007	Manaŋgopieŋ , goì i wiac šašaŋkene fuŋne-ticne šocko taniŋkeekac , ŋoŋe ine mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic , wiac furi sâko jâmbâŋ , irec fârine fific guguriŋko fua taniŋkeme Jesu Kristo fifisi-ticnao ŋoŋere šeri bubiaŋ â mumuteŋ â eri qaraweŋ fuaocmu .
60001008	Ŋoŋe Jesu e hawari-ticne mi honembiŋzi sifu maŋŋeŋic qikiŋnecneeŋgopieŋ , erâ dameŋ šiŋucne wâc šâŋezi mi hohone sifu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ . Ehuc šeri bubiaŋ fuŋmoc , ŋicmiczi mi mumufuane , manacneeŋgopieŋ .
60001009	Mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte fârine maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicte bâbâpiaŋ hâcne , maic-ŋopakacte šeri eŋgopieŋ .
60001010	Bâbâpiaŋ i weniŋuc fuazokac , porofete jaŋe mârâc jaha iŋuc wiorâ gufu koparic ehuc jumbiŋ , ehuc ŋoŋerao aki anonoc fuaocte irec findaŋdâŋ muhuc jumbiŋ .
60001011	Kristo e šâic fâro manaku eri tatamac-ticne rorâ juocmu , irec dâŋ Mâro-ticnezi maŋjeŋicko râeme jaŋe dameŋ wezimucko â weniŋucnao Kristo iŋuc fuacnezokac muhuc wawariehuc jumbiŋ .
60001012	Jaŋe gie bambiŋ irec fârine jaŋacnao mâcne , ŋoŋerao fuaocte mukicne , i jaŋe mufua-jarekicne . Eme šâhec irec fârine fuame Tiri Mârozi sambâŋkonec waharâ mitiŋic neŋgoc ŋejareme Biŋebiaŋ muromackembiŋ jaŋe hâcne findaŋdâŋte fârine mujaŋgeŋke-ŋarembiŋ . Dâŋ irec šuhucne aŋelo jaŋe wâc mana šiguaniŋte buââkec jueŋgopieŋ .
60001013	Irec ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋicte umbika jomarâ maŋsowa junšepieŋ , ehuc Jesu Kristo fua tâcnerâ aki anonoc bâfua-ŋareocmu , irec mamanac junšepieŋ .
60001014	Anuture mume rereŋfâc ŋoŋe mârâc jaha qâpuc-ŋeŋicko sasechec jujumbieŋ , ju ju sâc ijaha šiŋuczia mi junšepieŋ .
60001015	Tiri runezi hefârec-ŋopawec ere sâcko tiri jaha jufârenšepieŋ .
60001016	Dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac : “ No tiri jukopacte ŋoŋe tiri jaha junšepieŋ . ”
60001017	Ŋoŋe Mamac mucnehuc wâsickeeŋgopieŋ e ra rowec ware rowec mi ehuc juju bapa-nâŋecte sâcko dâŋnâŋec mutaraocmu ” irec ŋoŋe mâreŋko jaba juhuc sâc e araŋ bacnehuc junšepieŋ .
60001018	Ŋoŋe šiŋuc sâcne manaeŋgopieŋ , kâcɋenefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere sindaŋ hata âtehuc juhapie wiac sisirowenezi , goì siliwa wiaczi mi kitâc-ŋopawec .
60001019	Ŋoŋe Kristore soc furi Sâko izi kitâc-ŋopawec . E hâcne lama sahac fâsâc â wânâŋ tâmiric iŋucne juwec .
60001020	E mârâc jaha , mâreŋte hobeteŋne mi fuahame gie i mucnekicne fufua ine šâhec dameŋ tarazo ehame ŋoŋere erâ fuawec .
60001021	Erâ ŋoŋe Anuturao šuhuc-ŋopawec , Anutu hâmockonec bâɋârerâ eri tatamac hec neme huwec erao hâcne ” eme irec mamanasiŋ â woworic-ŋeŋic Anuturao fokac .
60001022	Ŋoŋe dâŋfâri murâ rereŋ ekupie maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋic ɋaɋackewec i ââgo fârihec eniŋte iŋuc fuawec ” eme irec maŋzi jâmbâŋ šâšâfic ehuc junšepieŋ
60001023	Ŋoŋe fufua ɋâri i ukic sisirowenaonec mâcne , mi sisirowenaonec , Anuture dâŋ jujune â fofo sanaŋ , irecnec âkešurâ fuambiŋ .
60001024	Dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Sahachec jaŋe sopâc kecɋaŋ iŋucne , â šâŋe rarac biaŋ-jeŋic i šariŋ âri iŋucne . Sopâc kecɋaŋzi ɋaŋaekac â ârinezi mârâŋkeekac . Anuture dâŋzi ine fofo sanaŋ foocmu . ”
60001025	Biŋedâŋ biaŋne ŋazakicne ši hâcne .
60002001	Ŋoŋe sindaŋ â burec wiac â eeatuc â iiŋguuŋ â gupe micko âkec i hetara-fârenšepieŋ .
60002002	Hetararâ naru motec ɋiene susure ejareekac iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicte susu biaŋ irec eŋarezejec . I nâhuc mitio soka pupuŋ enšepieŋ .
60002003	Wofuŋ jauŋ-ticne moc mana aŋac embiŋko iŋuc enšepieŋ .
60002004	Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ , qânâ jujune hâcne , ŋiczi hone suŋgiŋkehapie Anutuzi maname fekicne eme bâwosâewec , erao âtesiŋkeniŋ .
60002005	Ehuc qânâ jujunea efârerâ šuhuckeme šuhuc doma doma fehuc Mârore ufuŋ enšepieŋ . Erâ wâc tiri taha bapa guru erâ maŋzi Anutu taha bâzi ecnenšepieŋ . I Jesu Kristore erâ maname biaŋkeocmu .
60002006	Miti papiao dâŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac : “ Manakic , no Zioŋko qânâ moc hekopac , qânâ wâtuŋ bâwosâekicne furi sâko . Ŋic moczi erao roweckeocmu e mi qurutuaocmu . ”
60002007	Irec erao roweckeeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋerao wiac furi sâko ekac . Á mamanasiŋ tâmiric jaŋere šiŋuc mukicne : “ Ficbapa jaŋe qânâ surehuc behembiŋ , izi hâcne qânâ wâtuŋ ewec domakac . ”
60002008	Erâ wâc “ Qânâ ira kike-jeŋic hepirickeniŋmu â buse ira heariweniŋmu . ” Ŋic miti qikiŋnehuc ira heariweniŋte mukicnere iŋuc hâcne eeŋgopieŋ .
60002009	Ŋoŋe ine bâwosâecfâc-ticne â taha bapa ŋicbomboŋfâc-ticne â tiri ŋicgurufâc-ticne â fuŋfuŋ gurufâc-ticne . Iŋucne ŋoŋe dapâckonec bawefuc-ŋoparâ tatamac jaŋgeŋ-ticnao râec-ŋopawec ere mâsi sâkore biŋedâŋ muropiepie haŋ bazejec .
60002010	Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha ruc hurâ jumbiŋ , ši ine Anuture ŋicfâc embiŋ juŋgopieŋ ” mârâc jaha qarâ suŋgiŋne jumbiŋ , ši ine uruc jauŋko juŋgopieŋ .
60002011	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , no ŋazape mananiŋ , ŋoŋe mâreŋko jaba â ŋicmanac jueŋgopieŋzi sasec , maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicte râsi hâcne , i getâckenšepieŋ .
60002012	Ehuc qâpuc jaŋere ŋondeŋko juju tiŋne junšepieŋ . Iŋuc jupie qâpuc jaŋe fuŋne-ŋeŋic hone mana tarac erâ , sâqocne bapa muŋareeŋgopieŋ , i beherâ juku Anuture iiqic dameŋko eehâmo gie-ŋeŋicte erâ Anutu muteŋkenšepieŋ .
60002013	Ŋiczi sâcmutâc fuŋne fuŋne râekicne i ŋoŋe Wofuŋte erâ reŋke-fârenšepieŋ . Ŋicwofuŋ , femicne juekac , ere mecne ,
60002014	â kia gawamaî râec-jopawec jaŋere mumupaŋ mecne , mâmâc reŋkenšepieŋ ” jaŋe hâcne sâqocne bapa okacne jareniŋte , â sâcne jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe mumbiaŋ-jopaniŋte mu jarekicne .
60002015	Ŋoŋe eehâmo gie bahuc ŋic mutucne , mumusifuc bâfuaeŋgopieŋ jaŋere dâŋ bâniniŋkeniŋte Anutuzi muŋareekac hâcne .
60002016	Ŋoŋe goroŋ-ŋopakicnere rambaŋ juŋgopieŋ , erâ juju izi sâqocnere tapa mi ezejec , rambaŋ juhuc Anuture kiŋaŋ qanšepieŋ .
60002017	Ŋoŋe ŋic šeŋgoma sâsec-jopanšepieŋ , âgofâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarenšepieŋ , Anutu araŋ bacnenšepieŋ , ŋicwofuŋ sâsenšepieŋ .
60002018	Kiŋaŋ qaqa ŋoŋe bomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic araŋ bajarehuc micjeŋic reŋkenšepieŋ , i bomboŋ urucne â mâteŋne jaŋe sawa mâcne , šâšâicne jaŋe mâmâc iŋuc ejarenšepieŋ .
60002019	Jaŋe maŋgâŋ bahac tâmiricko bâšâic-ŋopapie Anuture manasuhuc rârâŋgeŋ tâmiric jupie maname biaŋkeocmu .
60002020	Á bahac bâfuarâ šika kihuc rârâŋgeŋ tâmiric jupie mozi maname biaŋkeocmu ? Tiŋne juhuc šika kirâ rârâŋgeŋ tâmiric jupie ine Anutuzi maname biaŋkeocmu .
60002021	Ŋoŋe iŋuc eniŋte hâcne muŋarekicne . Kristo e iŋuc jaha ŋoŋere erâ šâic manahuc bânie-ŋarewec , eme ŋoŋe kike hata-ticne honehuc ijaha âte ranšepieŋ .
60002022	E bahac mi bâfuawec , â sioc micticnaonec mi fuawec .
60002023	E musâqorepie okacne mi musâqorec-jopawec , bâšâickepie okacnere dâŋ mi jazawec . E dâŋ mumutara gie fârine baekac ere biŋe qawec .
60002024	Nâŋâcne sâqocnezi ere sahacko feme maripoŋko bafewec , i sâqocne hâmocnehuc tiŋkerâ junaŋte ewec . Ere wiczi ŋoŋere wic bâsomiewec hâcne .
60002025	Ŋoŋe lama iŋucne qâsoc bâsoriehuc jumbiŋ . Ʒi ine maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicte rusoŋaŋzi hefârec-ŋopame erao fisimbiŋ .
60003001	Ŋokac ŋoŋere iŋuc jaha mupe , ŋoŋe ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere wahamicne junšepieŋ . Eme ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic gâcne miti qiqikiŋ jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe dâŋ mi jajaza mâc rume-jarehuc maŋɋaɋac jupie
60003002	ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic ŋoŋere juju bapa hone manac erâ maŋjeŋic bârisienšepieŋ .
60003003	Ŋoŋe sahacte eri , qizec ba ericko bapa , kubu wiac furi sâko qoqonaŋ , ŋaqi qâreŋ biaŋ rojuju , irec manapie jawane ezejec .
60003004	Ehame buuruc fârine , maŋwâmbuŋko soŋkerâ tiŋbenoŋ bâfuaekac , izi eri fofo sanaŋ-ŋeŋic eme Anutuzi maname furi sâko eocmu .
60003005	Miti ŋokac mârâc jujumbieŋ jaŋe eri i hâcne baju jumbieŋ , ehuc Anuturao roweckehuc ŋowefâc-jeŋic sâsec-jopa jumbieŋ .
60003006	Sara eki hâcne Abraham dâŋticne reŋke jujec , ehuc ŋicbomboŋ mucne jujec . Eme ŋoŋe wiac biaŋne bahuc mu hâhâwicte mana mezac mi eniŋmuo otâfâc-ticne embiŋ juŋgopieŋ muŋarezo .
60003007	Ŋic ŋoŋere iŋuc jaha mupe ” ŋokac e tâpirine wahakacte ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic wiac mana manahuc ejarenšepieŋ . Erâ juju sanaŋte biŋe mâmâc qajarekicnere sâsec-jopahuc junšepieŋ . Eme nunumu-ŋeŋiczi ququŋke tâmiric qâfâsâerâ fezejec .
60003008	Erâ qâhâckehuc mupe ” ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa maŋ mocjaha erâ miriŋhec junšepieŋ , ehuc âgofâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarehuc wama ruaine â maŋhuhuŋ junšepieŋ .
60003009	Wiac sâqocne eŋarepie okacne sâqocne jaha mi ejarenšepieŋ , sosopec dâŋ ŋazapie okacne sosopec dâŋ jaha mi jazanšepieŋ , aricne , ŋoŋe jambuŋ hotâckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopakicnere jaŋe wâc jambuŋdâŋ jazanšepieŋ .
60003010	“ Moc e jujure aŋackekac â dameŋ biaŋ bâfuazo ecnekac , e nameŋ-ticne soŋaŋkeha sâqocne mi bazejec , â micbipic-ticne qataracneme burecdâŋ mi ezejec .
60003011	Eme sâqocne râpeckerâ wiac biaŋne ezejec , erâ wamao juhuc irec giene fotarierâ bazejec .
60003012	Wofuŋ e ŋic tiŋne jaŋerao šâŋe fihuc mu wâwâsic-jeŋicte hazec râeekac , sâqocne bapa jaŋe ine Wofuŋzi hone qikiŋ ejareekac . ”
60003013	Ŋoŋe wiac biaŋnere henširiŋnehuc juhapie mozi wemo wiac eŋareocmu ?
60003014	Me juju bapa tiŋnere erâ fific guguriŋ faio feniŋmu , ine manapie bubiaŋnehec ezejec . Ʒika hâhâwic eŋarepie ɋarac ɋarac mi qanšepieŋ â hâbi gogoroŋ mi enšepieŋ .
60003015	Maŋŋeŋic ba emasaŋ epie Kristo e tiri Wofuŋ juŋarezejec . Erâ maŋzi wiac worickehuc jueŋgopieŋ irec mu indiŋ eŋarepie afeckerâ fuŋne mutaniŋkenšepieŋ .
60003016	Erâ dâŋ i urucko â acmeruŋ ehuc , maŋŋeŋiczi mumu hehec mi eŋareha munšepieŋ . Iŋuc epie , Kristohec juhuc wiac ebac eeŋgopieŋ irec qoric-ŋopaeŋgopieŋ , ŋic i jaŋe burec-jeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeme mimienšepieŋ .
60003017	Ŋoŋe wiac biaŋne ehuc juhapie Anutuzi maname sâckeha šika kâpâcwâru eŋareniŋmu irec manape fekac , â bahac bâfuapie eŋareniŋmu ine manape wahakac .
60003018	Kristo e iŋuc jaha tiŋnezi sâqocnere erâ arec moc hâmowec , e tiŋnezi hehesicne ŋoŋere erâ iŋuc ewec , Anuturao râec-ŋopaocte . E sahachec juwecte qapie hâmowec , â Mârohec juwecte ɋârewec .
60003019	Mârohec wâc juhuc qâqâtâc kâpâcwâruo fombiŋ jaŋerao rarâ miti jazawec .
60003020	Jaŋe mârâc jaha Noa e woke bahuc juhame Anutuzi maŋuruc-ticnere erâ woŋec-jeŋic juipiehame dâŋticne qâsuambiŋ . Eme ŋic ŋokac jahec mac , 8 sawa , jaŋe wokeo fepie opâzi akic-jopame Jumbiŋ .
60003021	Eme ŋifecne ši opâzi wâc Miti Opâo bâpiaŋ-ŋopaekac . Miti Opâ e sahac wânâŋ mi šureekac , e Anutu hefâreme ware maŋŋeŋic šureme mumu hehec mocwâc mi eŋareekac ” wiac i Jesu Kristozi hâmockonec ɋârehuc bâfuawec .
60003022	E jahacne sambâŋko Anutu fârenao fewec jukac ” ira juhame aŋelo fekicne jaŋe ere wahamicnao jueŋgopieŋ .
60004001	Kristo e sahac šâic manawecte ŋoŋe ijaha eniŋte hâbi-ŋeŋic hepie huzejec . Ehuc šiŋuc mananšepieŋ , moc e sahac šâic manaekaczi sâqocnere ninikec bâfuaekac .
60004002	Eme sahacko juju dameŋ-ticne fokac sâc sasecte gie mi bapa Anuture micdâŋ sawa reŋkehuc juzejec .
60004003	Juwicnao qâpuc wiac šiŋuc ehuc jumbiŋ : Wiac gapec tâmiric ee , sasec , opâ momori âmbâŋ nânâ , bec qowi âmbâŋ nânâ , tiwâ sisiricko nânâ , nemu burec kiŋaŋ qaqajare , wiac i hâcne ewarehuc jukupie micne qawec .
60004004	Eme ši ine qâpuc jaŋe sâqocnere šâkâŋko fohapie mi qâtec-jopaeŋgopieŋte manapie moc eme mu supaic eŋareeŋgopieŋ .
60004005	Erâ jaŋe juku jukicne hâmokicne fuŋne-nâŋec bataniŋkeocte šawierâ jukac erao dâŋgie baniŋmu .
60004006	Eme fuŋne šiŋucte hâmokicne wâc Biŋebiaŋ jazakicne : Jaŋe ŋifec ŋic hata fokac irec sâcko sahaczi okacne roniŋte , â ŋifec Anuture hata fokac irec sâcko mârozi juniŋte .
60004007	Wiac sasawa irec dameŋ bembeŋkekac . Irec ŋoŋe maŋsowa â pectâc juhuc nunumure afeckenšepieŋ .
60004008	Erâ maŋŋeŋiczi jauŋ babac ehuc junšepieŋ . Maŋjauŋhec juhuc kiŋ bebehec sâcne ezo .
60004009	Ŋoŋe mutakic tâmiric hezu hewâneŋ eec enšepieŋ .
60004010	Ŋoŋe Anutuzi miti mâriri fuŋne fuŋne tahac-ŋopawec , i ŋicne ŋicne foŋarekac sâc aimuŋ bajuhuc bâmec babac â dodopec ehuc junšepieŋ .
60004011	Moc e miti muocmu i Anuture dâŋ jâmbâŋ ezejec , moc e gie mucnekicko baocmu ine Anutuzi tâpiri râcneme sâc bazejec . Ŋoŋe iŋuc epie Anuture huriri qâreŋ i Jesu Kristore erâ ŋoŋerao fua tâcnezejec . Eri tatamac â tâpiri i erao foweczi fohuc juocmu sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
60004012	Jorocfâc-nane , ŋoŋerao hâbi qaqazure wiac micne momori fuawec fokac , eme ŋoŋe wiac šâŋe furu fua-nârekac muhuc bipic tatara mi enšepieŋ .
60004013	Ŋoŋe Kristore erâ šâic fâro manahuc sâc bubiaŋ bâfuanšepieŋ , eme juku eri tatamac-ticne fua tâcneme iŋuc jaha bubiaŋ sâko manahuc šeri bari eniŋmu .
60004014	Ŋoŋe Kristo šâŋe biŋe-ticnere musoc qâsoriŋ-ŋopapie manapie šerine ezejec . Wiac i eŋarepie tatamacte maqâreŋ , Anuture Mâro hâcne , ŋoŋerao waha juocmu .
60004015	Ŋoŋeraonec moczi šikare me fiucte me sindaŋte me penaroŋte šika kâpâcwâru faio mi fezejec .
60004016	Á moc e Kristoŋic jukacte šika kâpâcwâru ecnepie ine irec maname mimi busâqochec mi ezejec . E šâŋe i bajuhuc Anuture mumuteŋ bâfuazejec .
60004017	Manaŋgopieŋ , Anutu e fuŋne babataniŋ gie-ticne ŋicfâc-ticne nâŋâcnao fuŋkerâ baocte dameŋne maickekac hâcne . Nâŋâcnao qanaŋ fuŋkerâ baraku Biŋebiaŋ-ticne qikiŋneeŋgopieŋ jaŋerao batarame sâc weniŋucne fuaocmu ?
60004018	Â “ Ŋic tiŋne e okac dameŋko bipic tatara ecnehame miti qiqikiŋ â sâqocne bapa e wenac eocmu ! ”
60004019	Eme irec Anutuzi maname sâckeha fific guguriŋ faio feniŋmu jaŋe maŋ qâqâtâc-jeŋic i bâbâfua mume sasanaŋ erao râehuc eehâmo gie banšepieŋ .
60005001	Ŋoŋerao micne bapa juŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe no micne bapa âgo-ŋeŋiczi dâŋ ŋazape . No Kristo e šâic fâro maname šâŋe fâri-nanezi honepo , izi juku eri tatamac-ticne fua tâcneme i wâc rauckepemu . Irec no hâcne dâŋ mu qâmoc eŋarepe mananiŋ :
60005002	Anuture lama guru soŋaŋ-jopaniŋte muŋarekicne , i jâiŋko mâcne , buafec jaha hone maiŋ ejarenšepieŋ , erâ moneŋ mafa huhurere manasuhuc mâcne , giere buâkec eŋareha enšepieŋ .
60005003	Erâ wâc ŋicbomboŋ ejarehuc mâcne , lama micne bajarehuc miti hata bânie-jarenšepieŋ .
60005004	Eme juku soŋaŋ sâkozi fisirâ hendiŋ huririnehec fofo sanaŋ i heŋareme hume rojuniŋmu .
60005005	Ŋic socɋâri ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ŋazakopac , ŋoŋe ŋic kâcɋene jaŋere wahamicne junšepieŋ . Erâ mâmâc sasawa ine gie qoruc šâŋene maŋhuhuŋ i jomarâ kiŋaŋ qaqac enšepieŋ . Manaŋgopieŋ , Anutu e ŋic maŋfefe jaŋe dope qatara-jareekac â ŋic maŋhuhuŋ ine dope sicne-jareekac .
60005006	Anuture mesanaŋzi bâuruŋ-ŋopame dapenšepieŋ . Iŋuc epie juku dameŋ-ticne maickeme ekizia bafaharec-ŋopaocmu .
60005007	Wiac mezac-ŋopaekac sasawa Anutu qârâriecnenšepieŋ , eki sâcne hone jauŋ eŋareekac .
60005008	Ŋoŋe maŋsowa juhuc rucgereŋ-ŋeŋic banšepieŋ . Râsi sâko-ŋeŋic Sataŋ e oâ iŋucne erâ mic aŋkerâ e me e ɋâckepe muhuc ra fisi ware fisi ehuc juekac .
60005009	Eme ŋoŋe mamanasiŋhec qiŋ herâ domahuc e hetapaickenšepieŋ . Erâ šiŋuc mananšepieŋ , âgofâc-ŋeŋic mâreŋ sâc jaŋerao šâic fâro ijaha fua-fârewec fokac .
60005010	Erâ Anutu aki anonoc rune , e eri tatamac fofo sanaŋ focnekac , ira Kristore erâ fisiniŋte hefârec-ŋopaweczi šâic fâro dameŋ bembeŋne manahapie bâtiec-ŋopahuc âkesiŋ-ŋopaocmu , erâ basanaŋ-ŋopahuc keteŋ-ŋopaocmu .
60005011	Tâpiri i erao hâcne foweczi fohuc juocmu sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
60005012	No dâŋ i Siliwano âzâcnepe qâreŋke-ŋarekac . No ere hâcne manape âgo fârine ekac . No bapa fuŋfuŋ jaha manapozi Anutu uruc jauŋ-ticnere dâŋ bembeŋnea mutaniŋke-ŋarerâ faŋ qaŋarehuc mukopac , dâŋ i fârine , maŋnao qiŋ herâ domanšepieŋ .
60005013	Babe haeonec kikefuŋ , nâŋâcnehec mâmâc rowosâec-jopakicne , jaŋe manasu-ŋareŋgopieŋ , erâ motec-nane Mareko e mâmâc .
60005014	Ŋoŋe mitio ââgo ehuc meo babac efârenšepieŋ . Kristohec jueŋgopieŋ ŋoŋerao wama fofârezejec .
61001001	Simoŋ Petoro , Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa â aposolo noni , Anutu â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo tiŋne-ticnere erâ mamanasiŋ furi sâko tahac-nâpokicne ijaha ŋare tahac ekicne , ŋoŋe papia ši qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
61001002	Ŋoŋe Anutu â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu mana maŋ epie ŋoŋerao aki anonoc â wama ɋaŋɋaŋ ɋâriaŋ fuahuc fozejec .
61001003	Jesu e tatamac â tâpiri-ticnezi hefârec-nâpome hone šâŋitac ecnepene sahacte â maŋte dope sasawa i Anutu tâpiri-ticnezi bâfua-nârewec .
61001004	Iŋuc erâ dâŋ biŋe fekicne furi sâko nâre tahac ewec , i maŋkepene irec fârine nâŋâcnao fuame mâreŋko sasecte sisipiric fokac i râpeckerâ Anuture hawari qâreŋfâc enaŋmu .
61001005	Irec ŋoŋe mamanasiŋhec juŋgopieŋte šoɋac epie tiŋne ju ju-ŋeŋic fuazejec , tiŋne jujuzi mamana bâfuazejec ,
61001006	mamanazi maŋte sowa bâfuazejec , maŋte sowazi sasanaŋ bâfuazejec , sasanaŋzi miti nunumure aafec bâfuazejec ,
61001007	miti nunumure aafeczi ââgo juju bâfuazejec , ââgo jujuzi maŋjauŋ bâfuazejec .
61001008	Wiac i sasawa ŋoŋerao fohuc fua ɋârâŋkeme Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo mana maŋ eniŋte giene bapie fârimâc mi eocmu .
61001009	Moc e wiac i tâmiric juocmu , ere šiŋuc muzo : E šâŋe tiŋtuŋ â maŋmutuc , mârâc šure bâpiaŋ ecnekicne irec nikeckewec .
61001010	Âgofâc , ŋoŋe irec hâcne samarierâ , bâwosâec-ŋoparâ hefârec-ŋopakicne i fârinehec eocte sasanaŋ bâfuanšepieŋ . Ŋoŋe iŋuc erâ docke pârâc tâmiric sâcne juniŋmu .
61001011	Iŋuc epie juku Wofuŋ â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristozi eŋareme ere juju sanaŋte uucmaŋko ququŋke tâmiric hata aaŋko rašiniŋmu .
61001012	Ŋoŋe wiac i sasawa qazu-ŋarekicne â dâŋfârio keteŋ-ŋopakicne domaŋgopieŋ , i manahuc sifu dâŋ ijaha heɋâre-ŋarehuc jupemu .
61001013	Sahac boze-nanehec juhuc sâc dâŋ i manasu-ŋarehuc wiwic-ŋopape sâckeocmu .
61001014	No boze-nane biac hetarapemu i manakopac , dâŋ i Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristozi mufua-narewec .
61001015	Erâ behec-ŋopape ŋoŋe dâŋ i ɋâreme ɋâre mana rahuc juniŋte emoc bâmoc eŋarepemu .
61001016	Nâŋe Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo tâpiri-ticnere â fifisi-ticnere dâŋ ŋazambeŋ , i nemu binaŋ ŋic mamanao fuakicne mi ŋazambeŋ , nâŋe bapa fuŋfuŋ domahuc Wofuŋ tatamac-ticne fuame honembeŋ .
61001017	Ine Anutu Mamaczi eri mumuteŋ râcnehame sambâŋ tatamackonec erao dâŋ šiŋuc wahawec : “ Joroc Ŋokâ-nane keci hâcne , no hone aŋac ecneekopac . ”
61001018	Nâŋe ehec mâmâc tiri tikio juhapene dâŋ i sambâŋkonec wahame manambeŋ .
61001019	Eme nâŋe irec porofete jaŋere dâŋ manapene fârine jâmbâŋ eekac , izi šoclambe iŋucne erâ dapâcko tamaeekacte ŋoŋe ira šâŋe fihuc juhapie hae fure-fârezejec â maŋŋeŋicko bâpiŋ sâkozi wefuzejec .
61001020	Erâ qanaŋ moc šiŋuc mana-hâmonšepieŋ : Findaŋdâŋ miti papiao qâreŋkekicne fokac irec fuŋne i ŋic moczi e jahacne maŋte mi mumune .
61001021	Findaŋdâŋ i ŋiczi manasu biric erâ moc mi mukicne , ŋic jaŋe Tiri Mârozi fenšoŋ-jopame Anuturaonec dâŋ mu jumbieŋ .
61002001	Israe ŋic jaŋerao porofete burecne i wâc mâmâc fuarâ jumbiŋ , eme ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha qaqazu burecne fuaniŋmu . Jaŋe mitire mumusifuc bâfuapie ŋoŋerao fâfâuc fuaocmu , erâ Wofuŋ kiwiric-jeŋic rowec e mickeniŋmu . Iŋuc epie sisipiric ɋeŋfâfâc jaha fisi-jareocmu .
61002002	Ŋic i jaŋe sasec gie bapie bocjahazi honerâ bâjâpec-jopaniŋmu , eme jaŋere erâ miti hata susure fuaocmu .
61002003	Erâ wâc moneŋ mafare andac ehuc maŋko fuac dâŋzi eatuc-ŋopahuc wiac-ŋeŋicte kâŋgâc gie baniŋmu . Jaŋere okacne dâŋ esecne mukicne i mi pârâwewec , â sisipiric-jeŋic i micmâŋ mi ewec .
61002004	Anuture manaeŋgopeneŋ , e aŋelo sâqorekicne jaŋe mi akic-jopawec , aricne , e hârâcko tuŋjopame duŋdapâcko humbiŋ , ira okac dameŋte woŋec foeŋgopieŋ .
61002005	E mârâc sasac jaha ŋic â wiac sasawa mi akic-jopawec , mâc Noa , tiŋne jujure biŋe mumu , erâ ŋic ŋokac 7 jaŋe sawa ŋezic-jopame ɋâricne juhapie ŋic sâqocne jaŋerao rumi sâko fisiwec .
61002006	Erâ Sodom â Gomora hae iŋuc jaha sirowenicte mume šoczi šacjofawec , i ŋic sâqocne šâhec fuarâ juniŋmu jaŋere uŋ muhuc iŋuc ewec .
61002007	Erâ wâc mitiŋic Loti e sindaŋŋic jaŋe wiac mamakâcne mimi tâmiric ehuc jupie irec bušâic manahuc juhame ŋezickewec .
61002008	Loti e mitiheczi jaŋere ŋondeŋko juhame jaŋe sindaŋ hârindaŋ epie šoaŋne šoaŋne hone manac ehuc maŋne sisi hâhâŋ wemo afecne ewec .
61002009	Wofuŋ eki ine ŋic mitihec eesâic docko roroŋ sasapec ejareekac â miti tâmiric jaŋe okac dameŋko šâic gie mujareocte kâpâcwâru bacjopaekac .

61002011	Iŋuc ehapie aŋelo jaŋe ine sasanaŋ â tâpiri fuŋmoc fojarekaczi Wofuŋte maio mi mugâpâre-jareeŋgopieŋ .

61002013	ehuc hehesic-jeŋicte furine roniŋmu . Jaŋe šoaŋ ɋaɋacko tiwâ šepec â gae wowozi šeri-jeŋic eekac . Mamakâcne â maŋwânâŋ qâŋkerâ juju , šege hârocko hefârec-ŋopahuc bâbâsifucte eeatuc-ŋopa ,
61002014	šâŋe-jeŋiczi sasec šâŋe fifi , sâqocne gapecmâc ee , ŋic biric borocne wiac iŋucnere doc babac-jopa , moneŋ mafare harac eku maŋjeŋic ekicne , ŋic iŋucnezi hârâcte biŋe hâcne ¡

61002016	Wofuŋzi qaqatara-ticnere haneckewec . Eme doŋgi dâŋ tâmiriczi ŋicdâŋ dâŋehuc porofete bâbâsifucne e heckenewec .

61002018	Jaŋe pacgoroŋ dâŋ erâ , ŋic qâpuc hata ɋâri qaqa jaha râpeckembiŋ , jaŋe eatuc-jopaeŋgopieŋ , ehuc tiwâ šepeczi gisicbeŋ eme sicne-jarepie fisipie qâturerâ sasec gie baeŋgopieŋ .
61002019	Ehuc ŋic šiŋuc jazaeŋgopieŋ : “ Iŋuc erâ niŋgiŋ tâmiric sâcne juhâmozo ” , i jaŋacne sisipiricte niŋgiŋko fohuc iŋuc mueŋgopieŋ . Ŋic moczi wiac mocte kiŋaŋ qaocmu , e wiac irec niŋgiŋko juocmu hâcne . Hata raŋɋanao risierâ kiŋsâko hurezo

61002021	Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe tiŋne hata kâuc bahuc mi âtepie muzac boc mi sâqorezac ” â hata i âtekicnezi tiri sâcmutâc dâŋ qazu-jarekicne i mocwâc igockehuc hata raŋɋanao risiepie ine sâqoreekac .

61003001	Jorocfâc-nane , ŋoŋere papia ši qâreŋkehape jajahec ekac . No maŋŋeŋic wiwickepe mitidâŋ mi mana sifuckehuc sâcne mana taraniŋte qâreŋke-ŋareekopac hâcne .
61003002	Eme ŋoŋe tiri porofete mârâc jaha dâŋ mumbiŋ irec mecne â aposolofâc-ŋeŋic nâŋe Wofuŋ â bâbâpiaŋte sâcmutâc dâŋ ŋazambeŋ i mecne mâmâc manasuhuc junšepieŋ .
61003003	Ehuc qanaŋ šiŋuc mana sanaŋkenšepieŋ : Dameŋ bembeŋkezo eme ŋic âke sisicne fuarâ mufec muriŋ dâŋ muhuc sasec gie-jeŋicte hešâkiriŋkerâ juniŋmu .
61003004	Ehuc šiŋuc muniŋmu : “ Wofuŋ risieocte mukicne fârine weni ? Kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec hâmombiŋ , ehame wiac sasawa mâreŋ fuaweckonecteaŋ fowarehuc juwec iŋucnea fohuc jukac . ”
61003005	Jaŋe fuŋne šiŋuc mana-bipiehuc dâŋ i mueŋgopieŋ : Sambâŋ e mârâc jaha fuawec â mâreŋ e iŋuc jaha . I Anutu dâŋticnere opâonec fuarâ opâheckoaŋ fowec .
61003006	Eme šâhec opâzia ŋic â wiac sasawa qâuruc-jopahuc bâsirowec-jopawec .
61003007	Á sambâŋ â mâreŋ ši fokopirec ine Anuture dâŋzi sakarec-jofame šocte biŋe erâ fokopirec . Okac dameŋ maickeme ŋic sâqocne jaŋe sipirickeniŋte irec woŋec fokopirec hâcne .
61003008	Jorocfâc-nane , wiac moc ši kâuc mi banšepieŋ : Wofuŋ e šoaŋ gie bapa mocjahare maname jare I tauseŋ tinac eekac â jara I tauseŋ irec maname šoaŋ gie bapa mocjaha tinac eekac .
61003009	Wofuŋ e dâŋ muwec irec fârine bâfuaocte bititiehuc dameŋ mi bâšoraekac , ŋic gâcnezi manapie iŋuc tinac eekac . Aricne , e ŋic gâcnezi sipirickenšipiŋte ŋoŋere erâ woŋec juekac . E ŋic mâmâc sasawa maŋjeŋic bârisie-fâreniŋte muekac hâcne .
61003010	Wofuŋte dameŋ e râsi fisieŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha ututuŋ maickeocmu . Maickeme sambâŋ e fânâŋ sâko ehuc siroweocmu , â wiac hohonene sasawa i šoczi šafâreocmu , erâ wâc mâreŋ â fainao wiac bâfuakicne i šoczi šâseŋkeocmu .
61003011	Wiac sasawa sirowe-fâreocmu , irec ŋoŋe pectâc juhuc miti sisirombe faio bajunšepieŋ .
61003012	Iŋuc ehuc Anutu dameŋ-ticne hejâpehuc harac huacbuc enšepieŋ . Maickeme hâcne sambâŋ e šoczi šârârâŋneocmu , â wiac hohonene sasawa i šocbâruŋko šâtâmireocmu .
61003013	Nâŋâc ine sambâŋ ɋâricne â mâreŋ ɋâricne fuaocte biŋe qanârekicne , irec woŋec jueŋgopeneŋ , eme ira tiŋne jujuzi sâcke-fârerâ fozokac .
61003014	Jorocfâc-nane , ŋoŋe wiac iŋucnere woŋec juhuc ere maio maŋfuru â bahacmâc juniŋte wawariehuc wamao jupie honec-ŋopame sâckezejec .
61003015	Erâ Wofuŋ-nâŋeczi dameŋ-ticne bâšorame munšepieŋ , bâpiaŋ-nâpoocte ekac . Âgo biaŋ-nâŋec Paulo e maŋɋârâŋ-ticnere sâcko dâŋ irecteaŋ qâreŋke-ŋarewec .
61003016	E papia qâreŋkehuc sâc dâŋ i mufua rawec . Papia-ticnao dâŋ gâcne fokac irec fuŋne qame hukicne . Eme dâŋ iŋucne i ŋic mutucne â biric borocne jaŋe musifuckeeŋgopieŋ . Erâ i ere papiare sawa mâcne , miti papia gâcnere mâmâc ehuc sisipiric maickeeŋgopieŋ .
61003017	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , uŋdâŋ qanaŋ ŋazakicnere ŋic kosa jujune jaŋere mumusifuczi maŋŋeŋic bâŋgoroŋkeme dockenšipiŋte sawaŋ-ŋeŋic qahuc junšepieŋ .
61003018	Ehuc Wofuŋ â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonocko â fuŋne-ticne mana utuckehuc soka sanaŋ enšepieŋ . E eri tatamac i šiŋuczia focnekac erâ juju sanaŋ dameŋko iŋuc jaha focne rahuc juzokac .
62001001	Fuŋnaonecteaŋ fowarehuc juwec , eme hazeczi manambeŋ â šâŋe-nâŋeczi honembeŋ , erâ hone dendeŋnehuc mezi ba bâuac ecnembeŋ , i juju sanaŋte Micdâŋ hâcne .
62001002	Juju fârine fua tâcneme honembeŋte juju sanaŋte biŋedâŋ hâcne mufuarâ ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ . Juju sanaŋ i Mamactao fowarehuc juku nâŋerao fomârâŋkewec .
62001003	Ine hâcne wiac hone manac embeŋ ijaha ŋoŋe wâc ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ . Ŋazapene manapie miriŋ-nâŋec fuame mocjaha junaŋte hâcne mueŋgopeneŋ . Eme miriŋ babac-nâŋec i Mamac â Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu Kristo erao qâsiŋnerâ foekac .
62001004	Iŋuc fuame bubiaŋ-nâŋec fua ɋârâŋke taraocte papia ši hâcne qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
62001005	Dâŋ biŋe Jesuraonec kecšiŋuc manambeŋte ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ : Anutu e tatamac , dapâc i erao moc mi fohuŋgaŋkekac .
62001006	Nâŋâc dapâcko juhuc Anuturao qohotaŋgopeneŋ mupene burec eocmu â dâŋ fâri qizecne mi bajunaŋmu .
62001007	E jahacne tatamacko jukac iŋuc jaha wâc nâŋâc tatamacko junaŋmu , ine miriŋ babac sâcne enaŋmu , eme Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu Kristo ere soczi sâqocne-nâŋec šureme ɋaɋackenaŋmu .
62001008	Nâŋâc sâqocne-nâŋec mi fokac , iŋuc munaŋmuo maŋnâŋec eatuckenaŋmu â dâŋ fâri qizecne maŋnâŋecko mi foocmu .
62001009	Á sâqocne-nâŋec mufuanaŋmuo ine e mume sasanaŋ â tiŋne runezi sâqocne-nâŋec šurehuc bahac-nâŋec nâwoc rofâreocmu .
62001010	Nâŋâc sâqocne mi baeŋgopeneŋ , iŋuc mupene Anutu burecŋic mucneŋgopeneŋ eocmu â dâŋticne maŋnâŋecko mi foocmu .
62002001	Naru motecfâc-nane , ŋoŋe sâqocne banšipiŋte dâŋ i qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . Á moc e sâqocne baocmu , ine Mamactao sacfozic-nâŋec Jesu Kristo e tiŋne runezi jukac , irec manasuzejec .
62002002	Eki hâcne sâqocne-nâŋecte kiwiric rowec , erâ nâŋâcne sawa mâcne , mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere mâmâc rowec .
62002003	Anutu mana maŋ eeŋgopeneŋ , ine sâcmutâc dâŋticne mana rereŋ epene fuŋne jaŋgeŋkeme mananaŋmu .
62002004	Á ŋic moc e sâcmutâc dâŋticne mana rereŋ mi ehuc muocmu , “ No Anutu mana maŋ eekopac ” , ere burecŋic muzo , ŋic iŋucnere maŋko dâŋ fâri qizecne mi fokac .
62002005	Moc e ine Anuture dâŋ mana rereŋ eocmu , e jâmbomac Anutu maŋjauŋ fârine ecneocmu . Iŋuc ehuc ine Anuturao qohotaeŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne taniŋkeme mananaŋmu .
62002006	Moc e Anuturao qohotahuc jukopac muocmu , e Jesu juwec irec sâcko jaha juzejec .
62002007	Jorocfâc-nane , no sâcmutâc dâŋ ɋâricne moc mi qâreŋke-ŋarekopac , i raŋɋane , fuŋnaonec mana wefuhuc jueŋgopieŋ i hâcne . Dâŋ qazu-ŋarekicne irec hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋ raŋɋane mukopac .
62002008	Erâ dâŋ qâreŋkekopac i sâcmutâc dâŋ ɋâricne wâc ekac , i Jesurao â ŋoŋerao mâmâc fârine ekac . Ine fuŋne šiŋucte : Dapâc raruŋkehame tatamac fârinezi fua tâcnehuc fokac .
62002009	Eme ŋic moc e âgo-ticne qaisockeekaczi “ no tatamacko jukopac ” muocmu , ere dapâcko juweczi jukac muzo .
62002010	Á moc e âgo-ticne maŋzi jauŋkeocmu , e ine tatamacko sâcne juraocmu , ehuc sâqocne bâbâiŋ moc mi bâfuaocmu .
62002011	Á moc e âgo-ticne qaisockeocmu , e ine dapâcko juocmu â dapâcte hatao raocmu , e dapâcko šâŋe fime qiŋquŋkeme wemocko hata-ticne hone taraocmu .
62002012	Naru motec ŋoŋe Jesu šâŋe-ticnere erâ sâqocne bâtâmire-ŋarekicnere dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
62002013	Mamac ŋoŋe juwarehuc juwec sanaŋ e mana maŋ embiŋte dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . ŋicmotec ŋoŋe sâqocne rune sanaŋkecnembiŋte dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . Naru motec ŋoŋe Mamac mana maŋ embiŋte dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
62002014	Mamac ŋoŋe juwarehuc juwec sanaŋ e mana maŋ embiŋte dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . Ŋicmotec ŋoŋe sasanaŋ-ŋeŋic fokac â Anuture dâŋzi maŋŋeŋicko fokac â sâqocne rune sanaŋkecnembiŋte dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
62002015	Maŋŋeŋic mâreŋko me mâreŋte wiacko mi râepie fozejec . Moc e maŋticne mâreŋko râeme foocmu , e wemocko Mamac maŋjauŋ ecneocmu .
62002016	Manaŋgopieŋ , mâreŋkopec wiac sasawa : Sahaczi sasec , šâŋezi sasec â maŋzi fefe wiac , i Mamactaonec mâcne , i mâreŋkonec .
62002017	Eme mâreŋ e sasec wiac-ticnehec siroweocmu , Anuture micdâŋ mana rereŋ eocmu e ine juhuc juocmu sanaŋ .
62002018	Naru motecfâc-nane , dameŋ bembeŋke-jâmbâŋkekac ” eme ŋoŋe Kristore râsi qizec fuaocte mukicne i manaŋgopieŋ ” eme ši biac râsifâcne bocjaha fuambiŋ juraŋgopieŋ ” irec hâcne dameŋ bembeŋke-jâmbâŋkekac i manaŋgopeneŋ .
62002019	Jaŋe fufua i nâŋâcne ŋondeŋkonec fuambiŋ , â âgo fârifâc-nâŋec juju ine mi jumbiŋ . Jaŋe âgo fârifâc-nâŋec jurâ muzac mi behec-nâponšapiŋ . Behec-nâpombiŋ i fuŋne šiŋuc taniŋkeocte embiŋ : Nâŋâcnehec jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe âgo fârifâc-nâŋec sasawa aricne .
62002020	Ŋoŋe ine Tiri runezi Mâro rua-ŋarewecte mamanahec sasawa juŋgopieŋ .
62002021	Ŋoŋe dâŋ fâri qizecne kâuc baeŋgopieŋ muhuc papia mi qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . Aricne , ŋoŋe dâŋfâri manaeŋgopieŋte qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . Erâ wâc šiŋucte : Burec sasawa i ere maŋnaonec mi fuaekac .
62002022	Burecŋic i more muzo ? Jesu e Kristo aricne , ŋic moczi iŋuc mume ere burecŋic muzo . Mamac â Ŋokâ mic bacjofaocmu , ŋic ere muzo , e Kristore râsi qizec .
62002023	Moc e Ŋokâ mickeocmu , e Mamac mâmâc qikiŋneocmu , â moc e Ŋokâ muɋaɋackeocmu , e Mamac mâmâc sakareocmu .
62002024	Fuŋnaonecteaŋ mitidâŋ mana warehuc jumbiŋ i hâcne maŋke junšepieŋ . Mitidâŋ i maŋke jupie Ŋokâ â Mamac jahe iŋuc jaha maŋŋopahuc junicmu .
62002025	Wiac i Jesuzi biŋe qanârewec , juju sanaŋ hâcne .
62002026	Maŋ bâsifuc eŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋere dâŋ iŋuc qâreŋke-ŋarekopac .
62002027	Ŋoŋere ine šiŋuc mukopac , Mâro rua-ŋarewec i ŋoŋerao foocmu , irec wemocte ŋic moczi mu qazuc eŋareocmu , i aricne . Mâro ruambiŋ eki dâŋ sasawa ŋaza qazuc eekac . Eme dâŋ i burec mâcne , i jâmbomac . Eme qazu-ŋarewec iŋuc maŋnao junšepieŋ .
62002028	Naru motecfâc-nane , ŋoŋe Kristo maŋnao junšepieŋ . Eme juku fua tâcneme qacfiric domanšepeneŋ , ehuc fifisi-ticnao mimišu qâšušu ehuc wise ŋeŋe uruŋ mi enšepeneŋ .
62002029	Anutu e tiŋne juekac , ŋoŋe iŋuc manaeŋgopieŋko ine ŋic moc tiŋnea jume honerâ munšepieŋ , Anuturaonec fuawec .
62003001	Manaŋgopieŋ , Mamac-nâŋec e maŋjauŋ mo iŋucne enârehuc naru motecfâc-ticne munârewec . Eme i hâcne juŋgopeneŋ . Ŋic miti tâmiric jaŋe mi šâŋitac-nâpoeŋgopieŋ , i Anutu e jahacne mi šâŋitambiŋ irec .
62003002	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , nâŋâc šiŋuczia Anuture naru motecfâc juŋgopeneŋ , â juku sâc weniŋucne bâfuanaŋmu , ine biac mi fua taniŋkekac . šiŋuc ine manaŋgopeneŋ : Wofuŋ fua tâcneme juju hawari-ticne honehuc sâc ijaha enaŋmu .
62003003	Eme moc e irec erâ worickehuc juocmuzi Wofuŋ e ɋaɋacne jukac iŋucnea juocte maŋticne emasaŋkeocmu .
62003004	Moc e sâqocne baekac , e sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuaekac , sâcmutâc dâŋ qâqâsua izi hâcne sâqocne fârine .
62003005	Á Jesure ine manaeŋgopieŋ , e sâqocne bârireocte fisiwec , erâ e jahacne ine bahac fâsâc juwec .
62003006	Moc e Jesuo juekaczi sâqocne mi baekac . Á moc e sâqocne baekac , e ine Jesu hone manac mi ecnewec .
62003007	Naru motecfâc-nane , moczi moc maŋ bâsifuc eŋarezo mupie mi mananšepieŋ . Moc e tiŋne hata âteme ere ŋic tiŋne muzo , e Jesuzi juju tiŋne juekac , iŋuc jaha juocmu .
62003008	Moc e sâqocne baocmu , e Sataŋte ŋic . Sataŋ e sâqocne fuŋnaonecteaŋ bawec bahuc juekac . Anuture Ŋokâ eki Sataŋte gie imackeocte fisiwec hâcne .
62003009	Moc e Anuturaonec fuaweczi sâqocne mi baocmu . Anuturaonec jujure tâpiri focnehame e Anuturaonec fuakicnezi wemocko sâqocne baocmu .
62003010	Anuture naru motec â Sataŋte naru motecfâc jaŋere fuŋne šiŋucko hâcne taniŋkeme honezo : Moc e juju tiŋne mi juocmu , e Anuturaonec mi mucnezo , â moc e âgo-ticne maŋjauŋ mi ecneocmu , ere ijaha muzo .
62003011	Mitidâŋ mana wareeŋgopieŋ i šiŋuc hâcne : Maŋzi Jauŋ babac enšepeneŋ .
62003012	Kaiŋte hata mi âtenšepeneŋ , e sâqocne runere motec erâ ɋaticne qâhâmowec . Erâ wemocte qâhâmowec ? Ine kecšiŋucte : E Jahacne juju bapa sâqocne â ɋaticnere juju bapa biaŋne irec .
62003013	Âgofâc-nane , miti tâmiriczi qaisoc-ŋopapie manapie iŋuc me iŋuc mi ezejec .
62003014	Nâŋâcne šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ : Hâmockonec wiserâ jujuo rašimbeŋ . Iŋuc ekicnere hâcne âgofâc-nâŋec maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ . Moc e maŋjauŋ tâmiric juocmu e ine hâmocnea Juocmu .
62003015	Moc e âgo-ticne qaisockeocmu e šika qaqaŋic mucnezo . Eme ŋoŋe šika qaqaŋic jaŋere manaeŋgopieŋ , jaŋere maŋko juju sanaŋ mi fuarâ foocmu .
62003016	Jesu e nâŋâcnere erâ juju-ticne qikiŋnewecko maŋjauŋte fuŋne šâŋitambeŋ . Eme nâŋâc iŋuc jaha âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋere erâ juju-nâŋec qikiŋnenaŋte munârekicne .
62003017	Ŋic moc e nânâ mafa mâriri-ticne fohame âgo-ticne waha qaqane jume hone takirerâ bune bofackeocmu , ere muzo , maŋticnao Anuture maŋjauŋ mi fokac .
62003018	Naru motecfâc-mae , nâŋâc jauŋ i dâŋzi â micbipiczi sawa mâcne , mezi â maŋzi banšepeneŋ .
62003019	Iŋuc epene dâŋ fâri qizecnere kikefuŋ juŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne taniŋkeme mananaŋmu . Eme maŋnâŋeczi mumu hehec enâreme Anuture maio sâcne bâmiriŋkenaŋmu .
62003020	Ehuc šiŋuc munšepeneŋ : Anutu e maŋnâŋecte sâc mâcne , e sâc moc juhuc wiac mana-fâreekac .
62003021	Jorocfâc-nane , maŋnâŋeczi mumu hehec mi enârehame Anuture maio qacfiric sâcne junaŋmu .
62003022	Erâ micdâŋ-ticne reŋkehuc ere maio wiac ebac epene biaŋkeekacte irec me irec numucnepene nâreekac .
62003023	Sâcmutâc dâŋticne kecšiŋuc fokac : ŋokâ-ticne Jesu Kristo ere šâŋe manasiŋkehuc maŋzi jauŋ babac enšepeneŋ . Iŋuc hâcne enaŋte munârewec .
62003024	Moc e sâcmutâc dâŋticne reŋkeocmu e Anutuhec maŋmaŋ enicmu . Anutu maŋkeeŋgopeneŋ i Mâro nârewec eki mufua-nâreme manaeŋgopeneŋ .
62004001	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , mâro kosa jaŋere dâŋ mi mana šakienšepieŋ . Mâro moc e Anuturaonec me mâcne , i mana taraniŋte ruc banšepieŋ . Porofete burecne wemo afecne fuambiŋ juraŋgopieŋ .
62004002	Anuture Mâro e šiŋucko šâŋitazo : Mâro moc e Jesu Kristo ŋic fuawec i mutaniŋkeocmu , e Anuturaonec iŋuc mucnezo .
62004003	Á mâro moc e Jesu mi mutaniŋkeocmu e Anuturaonec mâcne . E Kristo râsi qizec-ticnere mâro iŋuc muzo . Ere manaeŋgopieŋ , e mâreŋko fuaocte mukicne , eme šine hâcne biac fuakac .
62004004	Naru motecfâc-mae , ŋoŋe Anuturaonec , irec porofete burecne sanaŋke-jarembiŋ . Ŋoŋere maŋko juekac ere tâpirizi mâreŋko juekac ere tâpiri sirickekac hâcne .
62004005	Porofete burecne jaŋe mâreŋkonec , irec mâreŋkonec ŋiczi dâŋ mumu i mueŋgopieŋ , mupie mâreŋkoneczi hazec-jeŋic râeeŋgopieŋ .
62004006	Nâŋâc ine Anuturaonec , eme moc e Anutu hone šâŋitac eekaczi dâŋnâŋec manaekac . Anuturaonec mi fuakicnezi ine dâŋnâŋec qikiŋneekac . Dâŋ fâri qizecnere mâro â bâbâsifuc mâro jahere fuŋne iŋucko hâcne šâŋitaeŋgopeneŋ .
62004007	Jorocfâc-nane , nâŋâc maŋjauŋ eec enšepeneŋ . Maŋjauŋ i Anuturaonec . Eme moc e maŋjauŋhec juomu , e Anuturaonec fuakicnezi Anutu mana maŋ eekac mucnezo .
62004008	Moc e maŋjauŋ tâmiric juocmuzi Anutu šâŋe ruruŋkeocmu . Anutu e maŋjauŋ irec fuŋqizecne hâcne .
62004009	Anutuzi Ŋokâ-ticne mocjaha e juju bâfua-nâreocte mâreŋko soreme wahawec ira hâcne maŋjauŋ-ticne nâŋâcnao fua taniŋkewec .
62004010	Maŋjauŋte fuŋne šiŋuc fokac : Nâŋâc Anutu maŋjauŋ mi ecnembeŋ , ekizia nâŋâc maŋjauŋ enârehuc Ŋokâ-ticne soreme waharâ sâqocne-nâŋecte erâ kiwiric nâwoc rowec .
62004011	Jorocfâc-nane , Anutu e maŋjauŋ iŋucne sâko enarewecte nâŋâc iŋuc jaha maŋzi jauŋ babac ehuc junšepeneŋ .
62004012	Ŋiczi Anutu hohone i moc mi ekicne , maŋzi jauŋ babac enaŋmuo ine Anutu maŋkenaŋmu , eme maŋjauŋ-ticne nâŋâcnao fua sarickeocmu .
62004013	Eki nâŋâc maŋnâpoekac â nâŋâc e maŋkeeŋgopeneŋ , irec fuŋne ine Mâro-ticne nârewec ira taniŋkewec .
62004014	Mamac e Ŋokâ-ticne mâreŋ sâc ŋic bâpiaŋ-nâpoocte soreme wahawec , eme nâŋe šâŋe fâri-nâŋeczi qame honembeŋte dâŋ i mutaniŋkeeŋgopeneŋ .
62004015	Eme ŋic moczi Jesu e Anuture Ŋokâ jâmbâŋ dâŋ i mutaniŋkeocmu , e Anutu maŋkeocmu â Anutuzi wâc e maŋkeocmu .
62004016	Anutu maŋjauŋ-ticne nâŋâcnao fuawec i hone šâŋitac erâ mana šakiembeŋ . Anutu e maŋjauŋte fuŋqizecne , eme moc e maŋjauŋhec juocmu e Anutuzi maŋkeocmu , â eki wâc Anutu maŋkeocmu .
62004017	Iŋucko nâŋâcnao maŋjauŋ fua tarawec , i okac dameŋko qacfiric domanaŋte . Jesuzi juekac iŋuc jaha nâŋâc wâc mâreŋko šira jueŋgopeneŋ hâcne .
62004018	Hâhâwic â maŋjauŋ jahe ââgo aricne , maŋjauŋ fârinezi hâhâwic guriŋkeocmu . Hâhâwic e šâic-ticnehec . Irec moc e hâhâwic bajuocmu , erao maŋjauŋ sâcne mi fua tarawec muzo .
62004019	Nâŋâc ine Anutuzi qanaŋ maŋjauŋ enarewecte maŋjauŋhec junšepeneŋ .
62004020	Ŋic moc e Anutu maŋjauŋ ecneekopac muhuc âgo-ticne qaisockeocmu , ere burecŋic muzo . Manaŋgopieŋ , moc e âgo-ticne šâŋezi hohonene e qaisockehuc wemocko Anutu mi hohonene maŋjauŋ ecneocmu .
62004021	Jesure sâcmutâc dâŋ šiŋuc fonârekac : Anutu maŋjauŋ ecneekaczi âgo-ticne mâmâc ecnezejec .
62005001	Ŋic moczi Jesu e Kristo muhuc mana šakieocmu , e Anuturaonec fuakicne muzo . Eme moc e mamac bâbâfua maŋjauŋ ecneocmuzi ɋâricfâcne mâmâc ejareocmu .
62005002	Nâŋâc Anuture naru motecfâc maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ me mâcne , ine Anutu maŋjauŋ ecnehuc sâcmutâc dâŋticne reŋkepene izi mufuaocmu .
62005003	Anutu maŋjauŋ mâc mi ecnezo , sâcmutâc dâŋticne reŋkehuc hâcne maŋjauŋ ecnezo . Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ i dâŋ ŋemâcne aricne .
62005004	Anuturaonec fuakicne sasawa jaŋe mâreŋkonec wiac qamaseeŋgopieŋ , â mâreŋkonec wiac qame wahaekac tâpiri i šâŋene mamanasiŋ-nâŋec .
62005005	Moczi sasanaŋhec erâ mâreŋkonec wiac sasawa qamaseocmu ? Ŋic moc e , Jesu e Anuture Ŋokâ , iŋuc muhuc mana šakieocmu eki hâcne iŋuc eocmu .
62005006	Jesu Kristo eki hâcne opâhec â sochec fisiwec , opâhec sawa mâcne , opâhec â sochec mâmâc .
62005007	Mârozi ine fuŋne mufuaekac , Mâro e dâŋ fâri qizecnere rune hâcne .
62005008	Irec jahec â moc jaŋe dodopec gie baeŋgopieŋ : Mâro â opâ â soc . Eme jaŋe jahec â moczi fuŋne-jeŋic mocjaha .
62005009	Ŋiczi dâŋ dodopec ehuc mupie manapene jâmbomac eekac , â Anutuzi dâŋ moc dopeckeme ine fâri rarau jâmbâŋ eekac . Anuture dodopec dâŋ ine Ŋokâ-ticnere dâŋ dopeckewec i hâcne .
62005010	Moc e Anutu Ŋokâ-ticne manasiŋkeocmu , e Anuture dâŋ fârine maŋkeocmu . Moc e Anuture dâŋ mi mana šakieocmu , i Anutu burecŋic mucnekac eocmu . Ŋic iŋucnezi Anutu e Ŋokâ-ticnere dâŋ dopeckewec i maname fâri tâmiric ekac hâcne .
62005011	Á dâŋ dopeckewec ine šiŋuc fuakac : Anutu e juju sanaŋ bâfua-nârewec , â juju sanaŋ irec jâcne ine Ŋokâ-ticne .
62005012	Moc e Ŋokâ rauckeocmu e juju rauckeocmu , moc e ŋokâ mi rauckeocmu e juju wâc mi rauckeocmu .
62005013	No dâŋ i ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mananiŋte qâreŋke-ŋarekopac : Anutu Ŋokâ-ticne manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe juju sanaŋ foŋarekac .
62005014	Nâŋâc šiŋuc muhuc Anutu bubiaŋ manacneeŋgopeneŋ : Wiac mocte , e jahac maname fokac irec sâcko râehuc numucnepene mana-nâreocmu .
62005015	Ine hâcne , wiac i me i numucnepene mana-nâreocmu , i manahuc šiŋuc wâc mananaŋmu : Wiac numucnekicne i biac rauckeŋgopeneŋ .
62005016	Ŋic moc e âgo-ticnezi sâqocne bame honeocmu , sâqocne hârâcte niŋgiŋ sanaŋ-ticnehec i mâcne , ine honerâ ere erâ numume Anutuzi juju hatao râeocmu , ine sâqocne hârâcte niŋgiŋ sanaŋ-ticnehec mi baniŋmu jaŋe iŋuc ejareocmu . Sâqocne hârâcte niŋgiŋ sanaŋ-ticnehec i fokac wâc . Iŋucnere nunumu gie baocte mi mukopac .
62005017	Juju bapa hehesicne i sâqocne sasawa . Erâ sâqocne gâcne ine hârâcte niŋgiŋ sanaŋ-ticnehec mi ekac .
62005018	Nâŋâc šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ : Anuturaonec fuakicnezi sâqocne mi baocmu . Anuture Ŋokâzi hone maiŋ ecnehame sâqocne runezi mi bâuaocmu .
62005019	Nâŋâc Anuturaonec fuakicne , â miti tâmiric sasawa jaŋe sâqocne rune ere rurumaŋko foŋgopieŋ , iŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ .
62005020	Erâ šiŋuc wâc manaŋgopeneŋ : Anutu Ŋokâ-ticne e waharâ maŋ mamanasu bâfua-nârewecte jâmbomac rune mana maŋ ecneeŋgopeneŋ . Eme jâmbomac rune , Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu Kristo , eki maŋnâpokac . Eki hâcne Anutu fârine â juju sanaŋ rune .
62005021	Naru motecfâc-mae , wofuŋ jawane jaŋere rucgereŋ-ŋeŋic banšepieŋ .
63001001	Ŋicraŋɋa no ŋokac bomboŋ bâwosâekicne go â naru motecfâcge ŋoŋere papia ši qâreŋke-ŋarekopac . No maŋjauŋ eŋareekopac , erâ noni sawa mâcne , dâŋ fâri qizecne mana maŋ eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe mâmâc eŋareeŋgopieŋ .
63001002	Miti maŋnâŋecko fokac erâ nâŋâcnehec fohuc juocmu sanaŋ , irec erâ ââgo jueŋgopeneŋ .
63001003	Anutu Mamac â Jesu Kristo , Mamacte Ŋokâ , eraonec aki anonoc , uruc jauŋ â wama i dâŋfâri â maŋjauŋhec juhapene nâŋâcnao fotâcnerâ fohuc juocmu .
63001004	Naru motecfâcge gâcne Mamaczi sâcmutâc dâŋticne nâzâwec reŋkehuc dâŋ fâri qizecne sâcne bajueŋgopieŋ , fuŋne-jeŋic iŋuc manarâ bunane boc biaŋkewec .
63001005	Eme ši ŋokac bomboŋ go sâcmutâc dâŋ moc gazape manac . Dâŋ furune aricne , raŋɋane fuŋnaonec mana warehuc jueŋgopeneŋ ijaha šiŋuc gazape : Maŋjauŋ eec ehuc junšepeneŋ .
63001006	Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋke izi hâcne maŋjauŋ ekac . Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ fuŋnaonec mana warehuc jueŋgopieŋ i hâcne bajuhuc sâseniŋte muŋareekac .
63001007	Manakomec , eeatuc ŋic bocjaha fuambiŋ juraŋgopieŋ , jaŋe Jesu Kristo e mâreŋ sahachec fuawec , dâŋ i mickeeŋgopieŋ . Ŋic iŋucne hâcne eeatuc ŋic â Kristore râsi ɋizec mucnezo .
63001008	Gie bapene ŋoŋerao fârine fuawec , i sifucke-ŋarezacte soŋaŋ babac ehuc junšepieŋ . Eme juku fârine ŋemâcne ronšepieŋ .
63001009	Moc e Kristore mu qaqazuc dâŋ mi bajuhuc âke sipuocmu e Anutu mi rauckeocmu . Moc e mu qaqazuc dâŋ bajuocmu e ine Mamac â Ŋokâ mâmâc rauc-jofaocmu .
63001010	Ŋic moc e mu qaqazuc dâŋ i mi bajuekaczi iqic-ŋopazo mume fic sakarecnehuc âgo mi ecnenšepieŋ .
63001011	Moc e ŋic iŋucne âgo ecneocmuzi bâbâsifuc-ticnere bafickeocmu .
63001012	Dâŋ gâcne bocjaha fokac , erâ tintezi papiao qâreŋkezo mi enarekac . No ŋoŋerao biac fâpe miczi muc manac enaŋte mukopac . Ehuc bubiaŋ kâcɋene bâfuanšepeneŋ .
63001013	Go qoge bâwosâekicne ere naru motecfâc jaŋe manasu-gareŋgopieŋ .
64001001	No ŋicraŋɋazi âgo-nane Gaio gore papia ši qâreŋkekopac . No gore jâmbomac enarekac .
64001002	Âgo-nane , maŋge mitio sâcne foekac , iŋuc jaha sahackopec huc šâic tâmiric sâcne juhâmocmurâ enarekac .
64001003	Go dâŋ fâri qizecne sâcne bajuhuc reŋkeekomec , irec âgo gâcne jaŋe ware dâŋ binaŋ epie manarâ bunane boc biaŋkekac .
64001004	Naru motecfâc-nane jaŋe dâŋ fâri qizecnere hata âteeŋgopieŋ , dâŋ i manarâ bubiaŋ fekicne jâmbâŋ manaekopac .
64001005	Âgo-nane , go ŋic âgo ehâmo-jareekomec , erâ bembeŋkonec sawa mâcne , šorickonec mâmâc ejareekic , i sâcnea eekic .
64001006	Ŋic jaŋe šira kikefuŋte maio jauŋgere mu warec embiŋ . Ŋic fâpie go Anutu šâŋe biŋe-ticnere erâ hone jauŋ ejarerâ râec-jopatec rapie biaŋkeocmu .
64001007	Jaŋe šâŋe-ticnere erâ miti kiŋaŋ rahuc mâreŋ-jeŋic beherâ qâpuc jaŋeraonec moneŋ mafa mi roeŋgopieŋte ehâmo-jarezo hâcne .
64001008	Ŋic iŋucne âgo ejarehuc bafic-jopapene dâŋ fâri qizecne haŋ baocte munârekicne hâcne .
64001009	No kikefuŋ dâŋ wirec-jeŋic qâreŋkepo . Eme Diotrefe e micne-jeŋic juocte muekaczi dâŋnâŋec qikiŋneekac .
64001010	Irec no fârâ juju bapa-ticnere fuŋne bataniŋkepemu . E nâŋere burec ehuc boc musâqorec-nâpoekac . Erâ i sawa mâcne , ŋic fâpie e jahac hezu hewâneŋ mi ejarehame gâcnezi ejarepie qatara-jarerâ kikefuŋ sahacnao râec-jopaekac .
64001011	Âgo-nane go ŋic jaŋe wiac sâqocne epie mi bâjâpec-jopazemec , wiac biaŋne epie ine bâjâpec-jopazemec . Moc e wiac biaŋne ehuc juocmu ere muzo , e Anuturaonec fuakicne . Moc e sâqocne ehuc juocmu , e Anutu mi šâŋitawec muzo .
64001012	Demetrio ere fuŋne ine ŋic sasawa mutaniŋke-fârembiŋ . Erâ mitio fuŋne-ticne taniŋkewec wâc . Nâŋe iŋuc jaha dâŋticne dopeckeŋgopeneŋ . Erâ dâŋ jâmbomac mueŋgopeneŋ i manaekic .
64001013	Dâŋ gâcne bocjaha fokac , erâ tinte â fedazi qâreŋkezo mi enarekac .
64001014	No gorao biac fâzore mukopac . Fâ fisipe miczi nazaŋ gazaŋ ezeperec .
64001015	Wama gorao fozejec . Âgo jaŋe manasu-gare-fâreŋgopieŋ . Go iŋuc jaha âgofâc-nâŋec šâŋe-jeŋic wosehuc manasu-jarezemec .
65001001	Juda no Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa â Jakobore ɋa . Mitio hefârec-ŋoparâ Anutu Mamacte jauŋko râec-ŋoparâ Jesu Kristore biŋe qacŋopakicne ŋoŋere papia ši qâreŋkekopac .
65001002	Ŋoŋerao uruc jauŋ , wama â maŋjauŋ fua bâbâriŋ fuahuc fozejec .
65001003	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , miti wirec-nâŋecte qâreŋke-ŋarepemurâ boc enareekac . Ehuc miti ŋic mamanasiŋte hata fosanaŋkeocte biricke-nârekicne i sifuckezacte sasanaŋ bâfuarâ juju gie baniŋte irec faŋdâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarepemurâ dameŋ-nane maickekac .
65001004	Ŋic gâcne guru-ŋeŋicko kamic kamic rašimbiŋ , jaŋe fuŋne-jeŋic qanaŋ šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne : ŋic miti tâmiric , nâ areŋ juhuc sasec gie baeŋgopieŋ , ehuc wiac-jeŋic Anuture jauŋdâŋzi foŋkehuc fekicne sâko-nâŋec mocjaha , Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo hâcne e mickeeŋgopieŋ .
65001005	Ŋoŋe dâŋ mana-fâreeŋgopieŋ ijaha manasu-ŋarepe . Wofuŋ e Israe ŋicguru Aigita mâreŋkonec batarac-joparâ šâhec dâŋticne qikiŋnembiŋ i jaŋe behec-jopame sipirickembiŋ .
65001006	Erâ aŋelo soŋaŋ gie-jeŋic hetararâ hae mâreŋ-jeŋic behembiŋ , jaŋe okac dameŋ sâkore woŋec foniŋte kâpâcwâru fofo sanaŋzi dapâczi ɋoroc-jopawec .
65001007	Erâ Sodom , Gomora â hae rârec rârec ŋerawec , irec ŋic jaŋe ŋic keci jaŋe iŋucne sasec kosa ehuc mamakâc fuŋmoc bâfuapie šocsanaŋko behec-jopame humbiŋ juŋgopieŋ , i hâhâwic râe-nâreocte iŋuc ewec .
65001008	Eme sifu ŋic keci jaŋe wâc iŋuc jaha , guŋko jujune tinac erâ sahaczi mamakâc eeŋgopieŋ , erâ fekicne ro waha âte ejarehuc tatamachec jaŋe wâc musuac-jopaeŋgopieŋ .
65001009	Mikae e aŋelo fekicnezi Mose qâŋɋâŋ-ticnere Sataŋhec iiriac erâ mu qaqatarac ehuc Sataŋ dâŋ sâqocne âzâcneocte maname quŋkeme šiŋuc sawa muwec : “ Wofuŋzi okacne bazu-garezejec . ”
65001010	Ŋic keci jaŋe ine wiac kâuc baeŋgopieŋ i kosa musua fâreeŋgopieŋ , â qowi jaŋere sâc tinac erâ mâc maŋjeŋiczi manaeŋgopieŋ ira ine sâqorerâ sipirickeeŋgopieŋ .
65001011	Jei , jaŋe juku wenac eniŋmu ? Jaŋe Kaiŋte hata âteeŋgopieŋ , â moneŋ mafare harac ehuc Bileamte bâbâsifuc bâfuaeŋgopieŋ , â Kora pepec-ticnere sipirickewec iŋuc jaha pepec-jeŋicte sipirickeeŋgopieŋ .
65001012	Ŋic i jaŋe hâcne nânâ qowire harac ehuc fisi tutumaŋ-ŋeŋic hehegâpârene , mimi tâmiric nâ areŋ eene , karorac hoe mi hehuc mâc mâŋâŋzi ficneme rame arictac eekac irec sâcko jujune , jâc garaŋ garaŋne , fâri tâmiric , hâsi fâri hâmokicne , qâqâfiene , ŋic iŋucne tinac hâcne ,
65001013	hâwec siri šocnehec bazu bâfeŋ eekac iŋucne , jaŋacne sâqocne miminehec qâqâtâtiene , bâpiŋ qâsoriekicne iŋucne , duŋdapâc fofo sanaŋ i jaŋere biŋe hâcne bâfuakicne .
65001014	Adamte oso gitecne fua warekupie 7 eha Enoko fuawec , eme eki hâcne ŋic iŋucne jaŋere findaŋdâŋ šiŋuc muwec : “ Wofuŋ e tiri ŋicfâc-ticne guru hâhâwicne jaŋehec fisizokac ,
65001015	erâ ŋic mâmâc sasawa fuŋne-jeŋic bataniŋkehuc ŋic sindaŋne jaŋe sindaŋ-jeŋicte okacne bazu-jareocmu . Ŋic sindaŋne miti tâmiric jaŋe wiac gâgâpâcne bocjaha mu bac eeŋgopieŋte katucne fisi-jareocmu hâcne . ”
65001016	Ŋic izi mu qâtimbucne , isoc qaisocne , sasec fuŋne fuŋnere hešâkiriŋkerâ jujune , pepecdâŋ mumune , ŋic moneŋ mafare mu bâmiriŋ eejarene , iŋuc hâcne jueŋgopieŋ .
65001017	Âgo biaŋfâc-nane , ŋoŋe ine Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo aposolofâc-ticne jaŋe qanaŋ dâŋ mumbiŋ , irec manasuhuc junšepieŋ .
65001018	Jaŋe kecšiŋuc ŋazahuc jumbiŋ : “ Dameŋ bembeŋkeme ŋic âke sisicne fuarâ miti imackehuc sasec gie-jeŋicte hešâkiriŋkerâ juniŋmu . ”
65001019	Ŋic iŋucnezi hâcne fâfâuc bâfuaeŋgopieŋ , erâ Mâro tâmiric maŋ qâŋɋâŋne jueŋgopieŋ .
65001020	Jorocfâc-nane , ŋoŋe ine tiri mamanasiŋ fârine izi ŋesiŋ ŋeŋarehame sanaŋkerâ junšepieŋ . Ehuc Tiri Mârorao roweckerâ numuhuc junšepieŋ .
65001021	Iŋuc ehuc Anuture maŋjauŋko aimuŋ junšepieŋ . Erâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo uruc jauŋ-ticne fua tâcneme juju sanaŋko fisiniŋte woŋec junšepieŋ .
65001022	Ŋic miti bape behepe bajueŋgopieŋ jaŋe dopec-jopanšepieŋ .
65001023	Á gâcne jaŋere busâqoc manarâ rucŋeŋic bahuc bafic-jopanšepieŋ , ehuc qoruc-jeŋic sâqocnezi hegâpârekicne i wâc bâec banšepieŋ .
65001024	Âkesiŋ-ŋopame docke pârâc tâmiric juhapie tatamac-ticnao bahacmâc â šerihec râec-ŋopaocte tâpiri focnekac ,
65001025	Anutu mocjaha hâcne , e Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec juekaczi tatamac â eri qaraweŋ â sasanaŋ â tâpiri mârâc dameŋ tâmiricko focnewec iŋuc jaha ši focnekac , erâ focne rahuc juocmu sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
66001001	Jesu Kristore mu bararuŋ dâŋ , dameŋ mi šoraha wiac fuaocte mukicne i kiŋaŋŋicfâcne jaza mutâc eocte Anutuzi Jesu mufuacnewec , eme eki aŋelo-ticne soreme kiŋaŋŋic-ticne Johane âzâcne jâutuc ewec .
66001002	Eme eki Anuture dâŋ â Jesu Kristore mumutaniŋ dâŋ hone manac eweczi manapaŋkehuc mufuawec .
66001003	Eme findaŋdâŋ i wose-jareocmu e jahacne mecne , â dâŋ mu qâreŋ ekicne manarâ maŋkeniŋmu jaŋe mecne , mâmâc juhâc qâhâmoniŋmu . Dameŋ bembeŋkekac hâcne .
66001004	Johane no Asia mâreŋko kikefuŋ 7 juŋgopieŋ ŋoŋere papia ši qâreŋkekopac . Juweczi jukac erâ wâc wareocmu eraonec mecne , â mâro 7 eri ŋeŋefuŋ-ticnao juŋgopieŋ jaŋeraonec mecne ,
66001005	â Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec . Eki hâcne mume sasanaŋ erâ wâc hâmockonec fafahare irec micne , â mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋere fekicne sâko jukac . E maŋjauŋ enârehuc socticnezi sâqocnaonec bâhoc-nâporâ
66001006	uucmaŋ-ticnere kikefuŋfâc bacnâporâ Anutu â Mamac-ticnere taha bapafâc junaŋte munârewec , erao hâcne eri qaraweŋ â tâpiri ɋuŋɋasaŋ fokaczi fohuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac .
66001007	Manaŋgopieŋ , e karorac faio warekac , eme ŋic sasawa šâŋe-jeŋiczi honeniŋmu , â âkeckembiŋ jaŋe mâmâc honeniŋmu . Erâ mâreŋ sâc ŋic gurune gurune jaŋe ere kio mamakuc eniŋmu . Dâŋ i jâmbomac jâmbâŋ .
66001008	“ Nonizia šâhec â bâbâni ” , Wofuŋ Anutu e iŋuc mukac , e juweczi jukac erâ wâc wareocmu , e bapafâre hâcne .
66001009	Johane no fific guguriŋte â uucmaŋte â Jesure woŋec jujure mâmâc qâtec-ŋopahuc âgo babafic-ŋeŋic juekopac . Eme no Anuture dâŋte â Jesu mutaniŋkepore Patimo nucko râecnupie ŋepo .
66001010	Ŋehuc Wofuŋte šoaŋko maŋ qâruru-nane ropieme râpefuŋ-naneo dâŋsâko qeŋfânâŋ iŋucne fuame
66001011	šiŋuc manapo : “ Wiac honekomec i papiao qâreŋkerâ kikefuŋ 7 kecšiŋuc jaŋerao râetec razejec : Efeso haeo â Simirna haeo â Peagamoŋ haeo â Tiatira haeo â Sarde haeo â Filadefia haeo â Laodikea haeo . ”
66001012	Eme no ŋic dâŋ nazawec e honepemurâ fotikiepo . Fotikierâ lambe 7 golzi bakicne honepo .
66001013	Lambe ŋondeŋko moc domame honepo , e hawarine ŋic hawari tinac . Ŋaqi-ticne šoricne waha domawec , â amecnao umbika golzi bakicne fowec .
66001014	Qizec-ticne â qizec susuc-ticne qaŋqaŋ jâmbâŋ , kota hâpokicne , faroqac iŋucne , â šâŋe jahecne šoc bâruŋkeekac iŋucne tinac .
66001015	Kike jahec-ticne ine aeŋ šocko šahuc bâruŋkeekac iŋucne tinac â dâŋ hawari-ticne opâ sâro fânâŋ tinac .
66001016	Mefâre-ticnezi bâpiŋ 7 badomawec , â michawec-ticnao sâqe momori moc bune râpene micnehec waha domawec , â šâŋemai-ticne ine šoaŋ gereŋ gereŋne eekac iŋuc tinac tamaewec .
66001017	No hawari-ticne iŋuc honerâ rândiŋkerâ kikefuŋnao hâmocne tinac fopo . Fohape mefâre-ticne fai-naneo râerâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Go mi hâwicguoc , šâhec bâbâni â juju rune no hâcne ši ”

66006008	Eme šâŋe firâ honehape mi becâsic moc sahacne gowaekicne warezejec i ¡ Ŋic fainao ŋewec šâŋene hâmoc . Erâ hârâckoneczi bâjâpembiŋ . Eme mâreŋko rukec jahec â moc mâc fohame moc ira mume šikazi â roroczi â huc mimicnezi â kâte qowi momorizi ŋic sipiric-jopaniŋte tâpiri râe-jarekicne .

66006010	Jaŋe dâŋ wiwic jaha wirahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Tiri â mume sasanaŋ Wofuŋ , go wemocte okac dameŋ bâšorahuc socnâŋecte kiŋ ŋic mâreŋko juŋgopieŋ jaŋerao mi batarakic ? ”
66006011	Iŋuc mupie ŋaqi qaŋqaŋ ru sâc jare-fârerâ šiŋuc jazambiŋ : “ Kiŋaŋ qaqa âgofâc-ŋeŋic gâcne iŋuc jaha jopa qâhâmoc ejarepie šare-jeŋic qosackeocte woŋec piticne junšepieŋ . ”
66006012	Eme wiac šiŋuc honepo : Lama e sâfâ namba 6 bâhockeme homeŋ sâko bawec . Ehame šoaŋ gâpârerâ kuši sahacne iŋucne ewec , â mosa e soc iŋucne ewec .
66006013	Á bâpiŋ jaŋe mâŋâŋzi nemuja qâmârâŋkeme wahaekac , iŋuc sambâŋkonec mârâŋkerâ wahambiŋ .
66006014	Á sambâŋ e ine papia bataforieeŋgopeneŋ iŋuc foforierâ sirowewec . Á tiki â nuc jaŋe . ŋeŋe-jeŋic behembiŋ .
66006015	Wiac iŋucne fuame mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ â ŋicbomboŋ , erâ momori micnefâc-jeŋic â mafa mâririhec â tâpirihec , ŋic fekicne â wahakicne mâmâc sasawa mâreŋ â qânâ hawecko soŋkerâ tiki â hârâc wâsic-jopahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ :
66006016	“ Waharâ ŋemac-nâporâ bârârâŋ-nâpopie eri ŋeŋeo ŋekac ere šâŋeo mi henšepeneŋ â Lamare kimbeŋ mi honenšepeneŋ .
66006017	Kimbeŋ-jeŋicte dameŋ sâko maickekacte ŋic mozi moc juocmu ? ”
66007001	Eme no šâŋe firâ aŋelo 4 honec-jopapo , jaŋe mâreŋ tuturuŋne 4 ira doma rahuc mâreŋte mâŋâŋ 4 badomambiŋ . Mâreŋko me hâwecko me jâcko mâŋâŋ moc mi qaocte iŋuc embiŋ .
66007002	Ehame šoaŋ wewefunaonec aŋelo moc wefume honepo . E Anutu jujune eraonec maqâreŋ bajuwec . Bajuhuc aŋelo 4 mâreŋko â hâwecko ima baniŋte mujarekicne jaŋe wiwic jaha wira-jarehuc šiŋuc muwec :
66007003	“ Ŋoŋe mâreŋko me hâwecko me jâcko ima biac mi banšepieŋ , nâŋe qanaŋ Anuture ŋicfâc mai-jeŋicko maqâreŋ râenaŋmu . ”
66007004	Iŋuc mume ŋic maqâreŋhec jaŋere šare kecšiŋuc mupie manapo : “ Israe guru sâc jaŋeraonec 144 tauseŋ maqâreŋ râe-jarekicne .
