66007009	Wiac i hone manac efârerâ moc honepo , mâreŋ sâc irec ŋic tucne , sahac hawari-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne â dâŋ marac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne , guru sokawec jâmbâŋ , ŋic moczi mi wowosene , jaŋe eri ŋeŋere â Lamare maŋfuŋko domapie honec-jopapo . Jaŋe ŋaqi qaŋqaŋhec sasawa ,
66007010	erâ mejeŋiczi šariŋ badomahuc dâŋ hahaŋne bahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Bâbâpiaŋ i Anutu-nâŋec eri ŋeŋeo ŋekac erao â Lamarao fokac . ”
66007011	Eme aŋelo sasawa eri ŋeŋe â ŋicqizec â wiac jujune 4 orâŋ-jopahuc domambiŋ , jaŋe eri ŋeŋe maŋfuŋnao fodaperâ Anutu nunumu mumuteŋ ecnehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ :
66007012	“ Jâmbomac ¡ Mumuteŋ â eri qaraweŋ â maŋɋârâŋ â daŋge mumu â šâŋe rara â tâpiri â sasanaŋ i Anutu-nâŋec focnekaczi focne rahuc juzejec sanaŋ . Jâmbomac . ”
66007013	Eme ŋicqizec jaŋeraonec moczi wio-narerâ muwec : “ Ŋaqi qaŋqaŋhec i mo jaŋe ? Wenirec warembiŋ ? ”
66007014	Wio-nareme dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnepo : “ Ŋicbomboŋ-nane , i goki manakic . ” Eme nazawec : “ Jaŋe šâic busâqoc maŋnaonec warembiŋ â ŋaqi-jeŋic Lamere soczi šure ɋaɋackembiŋ .
66007015	Irec ši Anutu eri ŋeŋe-ticnere maŋfuŋko juhuc ŋafe furec ufuŋ-ticnao kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopieŋ . Ehame eri ŋeŋeo ŋeekaczi qâtec-jopahuc sâoc-jopaocmu .
66007016	Eme nânâ opâre mocwâc mi hâmoniŋmu ; šoaŋzi mi rikec-jopaocmu â šâic fâro mi fua-jareocmu . Ŋeŋe šâšâŋiŋko Lama domakac eki hâcne soŋaŋ-jopaocmu , ehuc juju opâ šâkâŋnao amec-jopa rahuc juocmu ; erâ Anutuzi šâŋeuc-jeŋic bâkereŋke-fâreocmu . ”
66007017	Ŋeŋe ʒâʒâŋiŋko Lama domakac eki hâcne soŋaŋ-jopaocmu , ehuc juju opâ ʒâkâŋnao amec-jopa rahuc juocmu ; erâ Anutuzi ʒâŋeuc-jeŋic bâkereŋke-fâreocmu . ”
66008001	Eme Lama e sâfâ namba 7 bâhockeme sambâŋko niniŋ qiririŋ fuarâ fohame haæ aua qâririŋ ewec .
66008002	I tarame aŋelo 7 Anuture maŋfuŋko domambiŋ jaŋe honec-jopahape gâcnezi qeŋ 7 jarembiŋ .
66008003	Eme aŋelo moczi râqâc golzi bakicne ihec warerâ ra alata maŋfuŋko badomame gâcnezi ira hosâc âsu biaŋ bocjaha râepie huwec . Hume eri ŋeŋe mainao alata golzi bakicne ŋewec irec fainao râehuc mitiŋic jaŋere nunumuo šuhuckewec .
66008004	Ehame meticnaonec hosâc âsu biaŋ izi mitiŋic jaŋere nunumu bafickehuc Anuturao fewec .
66008005	Aŋelo e iŋuc erâ alataonec šoc kine rorâ râqâc-ticne bâfuserâ mâreŋko hoŋkeme huwec . Hume ɋuŋ parandaŋ â bâbâric â homeŋ fuawec .
66008006	Eme aŋelo 7 qeŋ jarekicne jaŋe qeŋ qaniŋte šawiembiŋ .
66008007	Ehuc aŋelo namba wâŋ eki qeŋ qame hoe sanaŋ â šoc sochec bâsifuckekicne izi mâreŋko hewec . Heme mâreŋ tucne šoczi šawec â jâc tucne â sopâc kecɋaŋ sasawa šoczi šafârewec .
66008008	Eme aŋelo namba 2 eki qeŋ qawec . Qeŋ qame wiac moc tiki sâko iŋucne šocbâruŋnehec hâwecko rucnewec .
66008009	Rucneme hâwec tucne soc efârewec . Eme hâwec qowi tucne hâmo-fârembiŋ â woke tucne šaŋke-fârewec .
66008010	Eme aŋelo namba 3 eki qeŋ qawec . Qeŋ qame bâpiŋ sâko moc sambâŋkonec tara waharâ ine waha iŋucne bâruŋkehuc opâ gâcnao huwec .
66008011	Bâpiŋ šâŋene Hâtâqiŋqiŋ . Eme irec opâ gâcne hâtâ qiŋqiŋne eme ŋic jaŋe nâpie hâtâc-jopame bocjaha hâmombiŋ .
66008012	Eme aŋelo namba 4 eki qeŋ qawec . Qeŋ qame šoaŋ mosa â bâpiŋ gâcne ira sâwec fuame tatamac-jeŋic pitiwawec . Tatamac-jeŋic gâkowawecte hae burec burec sawa furewec â ŋafeo iŋuc jaha mosa bâpiŋ buburecne tamaewec .
66008013	Eme no šâŋe firâ tucwipe sâko moc honepo . E sawao faic jâmbâŋ juhuc wiwic jaha šiŋuc wirawec : “ Jei , jei , jei , aŋelo jahec â moc jaŋere qeŋ fokac , i qapie mâreŋŋic jaŋe weniŋuc eniŋmu ! ”
66009001	Eme aŋelo namba 5 eki qeŋ qawec . Eme noni bâpiŋ moc sambâŋkonec tararâ mâreŋko wahame honepo . E hârâcte tapa roocte irec ki râcnekicne .
66009002	Eme hârâcte tapa rome hosâc sâko wefuwec , gie šame hosâc feekac , irec sâc hosâc wefu ferâ šoaŋ â sawa sâocke-fârewec .
66009003	Hosâc maŋkonec ine ɋirikiŋ wefurâ mâreŋko wahambiŋ . Micjeŋic ine omeqaqare Sâc .
66009004	Erâ jaŋe mâreŋko sopâc nânâ kise me jâcrehac wiac râsi ecneniŋte mi mukicne , ŋic Anuture maqâreŋ mai-jeŋicko mi fowec , jaŋe sawa râsi ejareniŋte mukicne .
66009005	Erâ jopapie hâmoniŋte mâcne , mâc mosa 5 kišâic-jopahuc juniŋte mukicne . Ʒâic ine omeqaqare micte sâc iŋuc manazo .
66009006	Eme dameŋ ira ŋic jaŋe hâmoniŋte biŋe muniŋmu erâ mi hâmoniŋmu , hâmoc hefâre-bipiepie sifu mi maic-jopaocmu .
66009007	Ɋirikiŋ jaŋe ine becâsic hawari , momori jaŋe šikao raniŋte becâsic wiac bâmocke-jareeŋgopieŋ hawari iŋucne hâcne . Qizec-jeŋicko du golzi bakicne tinac ŋewec , šâŋe mai-jeŋic ŋic šâŋe mai tinac .
66009008	Kanšaŋ-jeŋic šoricne , ŋokac qizec gere-jeŋicte sâc . Micjeŋic laioŋte mic iŋucne .
66009009	Amec-jeŋicko maro wapazi bakicne tinac fowec . Fakec fânâŋ-jeŋic ine keretac fânâŋ iŋucne , becâsic bocjaha jaŋe šikao raniŋte keretac gagasac jaha fâre rapie fânâŋkeekac , iŋucne tinac hâcne .
66009010	Gecjeŋic omeqaqare gec iŋucne Micjeŋic i gecjeŋicko hâcne fokac , izi ŋic mosa 5 kišâic-jopahuc juniŋmu .
66009011	Erâ hârâckonec aŋelo e ŋicwofuŋ jujarekac , šâŋene Judaŋic jaŋere dâŋko Abadoŋ â Grikŋic jaŋere dâŋko Apolioŋ . ª
66009012	Tucwipezi jei jahec â moc wirawec , moc omaekac , ši jajahec fokopirec . Aŋelo namba 6 eki qeŋ qame momori guru hâhâwicne fuambiŋ
66009013	Eme aŋelo namba 6 eki qeŋ qawec . Eme alata golzi bakicne , Anuture maio ŋekac , masune 4 ,
66009014	irecnec dâŋ wefurâ aŋelo namba 6 qeŋ badomawec e šiŋuc âzâcnewec : “ Eufrata opâ sâkoo aŋelo 4 niŋgiŋ-jopakicne jaŋe bâŋgoroŋ-jopac . ”
66009015	Eme aŋelo 4 jaŋe jara , mosa , šoaŋ , aua maickeme mâreŋ sâc ŋic tucne qâmiziec-jopaniŋte woŋec jumbiŋ , jaŋe hâcne firuec-jopawec .
66009016	Eme momorifâc-jeŋic becâsicko ŋeŋe jaŋere šare 200 million , iŋuc mupie manapo .
66009017	Ŋic â becâsic jaŋere hawari ine maŋ šâŋe-nanezi kecšiŋuc honepo : Ŋic jaŋe maruku bâbâroŋ â keda â bâbâŋeŋ iŋuc rojumbiŋ , â becâsic jaŋere qizec laioŋ qizecne iŋucne , micjeŋickonec ine šoc â hosâc â tepe šocne wahawec .
66009018	Eme wiac fârone jahec â moc izi ŋic gâcne sipiric-jopa-fârewec , becâsic mickonec šoc â hosâc â tepe šocne wahawec izi hâcne .
66009019	Becâsic tâpiri-jeŋic ine micjeŋicko â gecjeŋicko fowec . Gecjeŋic homa iŋucne , qizecnehec , izi hâcne ŋic sipiric-jopaeŋgopieŋ .
66009020	Eme ŋic tucne hâmo sipiric ehapie tucne akic-jopakicne jaŋe maŋjeŋic mi bârisiembiŋ â juju bapa-jeŋicte manapie mi sâqorewec . Aricne , jaŋe sifu demoŋ wiac bajumbiŋ . Á nemuɋâŋ golzi â siliwazi â aeŋzi â qânâzi â jâczi bakicne , hone manac eene tâmiric â rarac wawarecne tâmiric , i numu-jarehuc jumbiŋ .
66009021	Ehuc šika â qaŋgec â sasec â fiuc i mi behembiŋ .
66010001	Eme aŋelo sâko moc sambâŋkonec wahame honepo . E karoraczi rufacnekicne , qizec botâŋnao huriri somâckerâ domawec , šâŋe maine šoaŋ iŋucne , kike jahecne šocbâruŋhec .
66010002	Meticnezi papia piticne moc bâdâmârekicne i badomawec . Erâ kike fâre-ticnezi hâwec faio â kike qanazi mâreŋko âterâ domawec .
66010003	Domahuc dâŋ wiwira kâcɋene , laioŋte dâŋ sâcko ewec . Wirame ɋuŋ 7 jaŋe dâŋembiŋ .
66010004	Dâŋehuc mupie manarâ qâreŋke 20 ehape sambâŋkonec wiwira norao šiŋuc wahawec : “ Ɋuŋ 7 dâŋ mumbieŋ i mi qâreŋkec , mâc tapa batec fooc . ”
66010005	Eme aŋelo hâwecko â mâreŋko âterâ domawec , eki mefâre-ticne sambâŋkopec sicnehuc dâŋ mupaŋkewec .
66010006	Ehuc jurašihuc juocmu sanaŋzi wiac bâfua-fârewec , sambâŋ â irec wiac-ticne , mâreŋ 3 irec wiac-ticne , hâwec â irec wiac-ticne , erao hâcne ɋetickehuc šiŋuc mupaŋkewec : “ Dameŋ mocwâc mi fokac .
66010007	Aŋelo namba 7 qeŋticne qame fânâŋ fuaocmu , dameŋ ira Anuture dâŋsoŋ , ŋicfâc-ticne porofete biŋene jazawec , irec fârine fua taraocmu . ”
66010008	Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋ manapo ijaha mocwâc fuarâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Go rarâ aŋelo hâwecko â mâreŋko âterâ domahuc papia bâdâmârekicne badomakac i roc . ”
66010009	Mume no aŋelorao rarâ papia nareocte âzâcnepe šiŋuc nazawec : “ Rorâ nâc . Nâtecne bugao hâtâcguocmu â micgao baŋac iŋucne erâ aŋacguocmu . ”
66010010	Iŋuc murâ papia nareme nâpo . Nârâ micnaneo baŋac iŋucne erâ aŋacnuwec , izi nâkâcnepe ine bunaneo hâtâcnuwec .
66010011	Eme šiŋuc nazambiŋ : “ Go ŋicguru bocjaha , sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne erâ ŋicwofuŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋere findaŋdâŋ mocwâc muzemec . ” Kâtedâŋko : Sisipiric rune .
66011001	Eme moczi gunusâc narehuc šiŋuc nazawec : “ Go fahare Anuture ufuŋ â alata sâc barâ maŋnao numuhuc jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe wosec-jopazemec .
66011002	Ufuŋte hae šoŋa ine sâc mi bahuc mâc behetec fooc , i qâpuc jaŋere qikiŋnekicne . Jaŋe hâcne miti hae mosa 42 ima bahuc juniŋmu .
66011003	“ Eme no mumutaniŋ ŋicjahec-nane ejactepe mateŋ barâ ŋic findaŋdâŋ jazahuc juhapire šoaŋ gie bapa 1 tauseŋ â 260 tarazejec . ”
66011004	Jahe oliwa jâc â lambe iŋucne , jahe mâreŋte Wofuŋ ere maio domakopirec .
66011005	Ŋic moc e râsi ejactezo mume micjekickonec šoc waharâ šaocmu . Irec ŋic moczi râsi ejacterâ sipirickeocmu .
66011006	Ŋic jahe hoere motâc henicte tâpiri jactekicne , irec mupire hoe mi hehe mâc fohame findaŋdâŋ muhuc junicmu . Erâ mupire opâzi soc eocte irec tâpiri fojacteocmu , erâ mâreŋko wiac micne momori fuaocte mupire sâc fuaocmu .
66011007	Eme miti mumutaniŋ dameŋ-jekic tarame hârâckonec qowi mimicnezi wefurâ râsi ejacterâ jofame hâmonicmu .
66011008	Hâmopire ŋic jaŋe qâŋɋâŋ-jekic behec-jofapie hae sâkore hae šoŋao fonicmu . Hae irec šâŋe herâriehuc Sodom â Aigita mukicne , Wofuŋ-jekic hae ijaha maripoŋko qapie hâmowec .
66011009	Eme mâreŋ sâc ŋic gâcne , sahac hawari-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne , izi qâŋɋâŋ-jekic šoaŋ gie bapa jahec â moc â moc nâfocne honec-jofahuc juniŋmu , erâ gâcnezi ducjofazo mupie qatara-jareniŋmu .
66011010	Eme porofete jahe ŋic boc bâšâic-jopapicte mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic šeri bubiaŋ ehuc boreŋ nareŋ gareŋ eniŋmu .
66011011	Eme šoaŋ gie bapa jahec â moc â moc nâfocne tarame Anuturaonec juju bâbâfua mâro qâŋɋâŋ-jekicko rašime ɋârerâ faharepic . Faharepire ŋic jaŋe honerâ bipic-jeŋic tarawec .
66011012	Ehame sambâŋkonec wiwira kâcɋene jaherao šiŋuc wahawec : “ Ŋohe šira wefunic . ” Eme râsifâc-jekic honec-jofahapie karorac maŋko sambâŋko fepic .
66011013	Eme dameŋ ijaha sambâŋko fepire izia homeŋ sâko bawec . Bame hae sâkoo fic gâcne , teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc , herickehuc ŋic 7 tauseŋ jopame hâmombiŋ . Eme ɋâricne jumbiŋ jaŋe hâwic-jopame Anutu sambâŋ rune muteŋkembiŋ .
66011014	Tucwipezi jei jahec â moc wirawec , ine jajahecte fârine fuawec , mocjahare fokac ine biac fuaocmu .
66011015	Eme aŋelo namba 7 eki qeŋ qawec . Qeŋ qame sambâŋko micfânâŋ sâko embiŋ , ehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Ʒi mâreŋ sâko mâreŋ irec Wofuŋ jujure tâpiri i Wofuŋ-nâŋec â Kristo-ticne ere meo fekac , eme e guriŋ bapa gie barašihuc juocmu sanaŋ . ”
66011016	Eme ŋicqizec 24 Anuture maio eri ŋeŋe-jeŋicko ŋembiŋzi waha fodaperâ Anutu šiŋuc muhuc daŋge nunumu ecnembiŋ :
66011017	“ Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre , jumeŋzi juekic , nâŋe go daŋge mumuteŋ egareŋgopeneŋ . Go tâpiri sâkoge qaratietec fuakac , ehuc Wofuŋ giege fuŋkerâ bataniŋkekic .
66011018	Ŋicne ŋicne kimbeŋ qapie gore kimbeŋzi fuakac . Erâ hâmokicne jaŋere dâŋ mutaracmurâ dameŋ maickekac . Erâ kiŋaŋ qaqafâcge , porofete â mitiŋic , â araŋ bagareeŋgopieŋ fekicne wahakicne , jaŋe furine jarecmurâ dameŋne maickekac , â mâreŋ sipirickeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sipiric-jopacmurâ irec dameŋ mâmâc maickekac . ”
66011019	Jaŋe iŋuc epie sambâŋko Anuture ufuŋ aŋkeme qorac tapa katapa ufuŋmaŋko tâtâc fuawec . Eme izia bâbâric â micfânâŋ â ɋuŋ parandaŋ â homeŋ â hoe sanaŋ hâhâwicne fuawec .
66012001	Eme sambâŋko mâsi qâreŋ kecšiŋuc fuawec : Ŋokac moc domawec , e šoaŋzi rufacnekicne , kike jujuwicnao mosa ŋewec , qizecnao bâpiŋ 12 izi hendiŋ ecnembiŋ .
66012002	Erâ e kiwechec , eme motec roocte gozi kime kio owa ewec .
66012003	E iŋuc ehuc domahame mâsi qâreŋ moc sambâŋkoa fuawec . Ine oâ sâko moc fowec , hawarine bâbâroŋ jâmbâŋ , qizecne 7 â šuŋene 10 , â qizec-ticne sâc ŋicwofuŋ du jaha ŋerawec .
66012004	Eme gecnezi sambâŋko bâpiŋ gâcne qatarac-joparâ mâreŋko sâroc-jopame wahambiŋ . Oâ e iŋuc erâ , ŋokac motec rozo ehame šiŋuc manasuhuc ra maŋfuŋnao fowec : Motec rome ɋâckezepac .
66012005	Eme motec rowec , e mâreŋ sâc ŋicne ŋicne aeŋ gunuzi soŋaŋ-jopaocte mucnekicne . Erâ motec fuame ine Anuturao baferâ eri ŋeŋe-ticnere maŋfuŋko râekicne .
66012006	Á ŋokac e ine mâreŋ tuhuo wiserâ rawec , ira šoaŋ gie bapa 1 tauseŋ â 260 gume jauŋ ecneniŋte Anutuzi ŋeŋe hae moc bâfuacnewec .
66012007	Eme sambâŋko šika fuawec . Mikae â aŋelofâc-ticne jaŋe oâ qa jâpec ecneniŋte râsi roroc embiŋ , â ŋifec oâ â aŋelofâcne jaŋe iŋuc jaha râsi roroc embiŋ .
66012008	Erâ mi sanaŋkembiŋ . Dockepie sambâŋ sakare-jarembiŋ .
66012009	Ehuc oâ sâko , homa raŋɋa , demoŋ micne sâko Sataŋ hâcne , mâreŋ sâc ŋic maŋ bâsifuc ejareekac , e hâcne tuŋkepie mâreŋko wahawec . E jahacne tuŋkehuc aŋelofâcne mâmâc tuŋjopapie wahambiŋ .
66012010	Eme sambâŋko dâŋ wiwira šiŋuc fuame manapo : “ Anutu-nâŋecte bâbâpiaŋ â tâpiri â guriŋ bapa gie â Kristo-ticnere Wofuŋ qâreŋ ši fua taniŋkekac . Âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋere râsi , Anuturao ŋafe furec qoric-jopaekac , e tuŋkeŋgopieŋ hâcne .
66012011	Jaŋe Lamare socko ŋesiŋnehuc miti hâwicmâc mutaniŋkembiŋte sanaŋkembiŋ , ehuc juju-jeŋic mi sakarehuc hâmocte qikiŋnembiŋ .
66012012	Irec sambâŋ maŋne maŋne â ira juŋgopieŋzi šeri enšepieŋ . Á mâreŋ â hâwec , jei , ŋohe weniŋuc enicmu ¡ Ʒi Sataŋzi ŋoŋerao hufakac , erâ dameŋ-ticne biac taraocmu , i manahuc aaric sâkohec jukac hâcne . ”
66012013	Eme oâ e mâreŋko behepie waharâ , ŋokac motec rowec e râsi ecnewec .
66012014	Eme ŋokac e tucwipe sâkore fakec jahecne râcnepie mâreŋ tuhuo ŋeŋe hae-ticnao wiserâ homare hâhâwic soŋkewec , ira gume jauŋ ecnehuc juhapie jara jahec â moc â moc nâfocne taraocmu .
66012015	Eme ŋokac wisehame homa e râpefuŋnao opâ maŋume micticnaonec waharâ rumi sâko ewec , i ŋokac jowaocte iŋuc ewec .
66012016	Eme mâreŋzi ŋokac ŋezickehuc micne aŋkeme oâzi opâ maŋuwec i ira hufârewec .
66012017	Eme oâ e ŋokacte mana gâpârerâ kikefuŋfâc-ticne jopaocte rawec . Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc Jesu mutaniŋkeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne jopaocte rawec .
66013001	Ehuc hâwec moŋgeŋko hurâ domawec . Eme no honehape hâwecmaŋkonec qowi mimicne moczi wefuwec . E šuŋene 10 â qizecne 7 , erâ šuŋene sâc ira ŋicwofuŋ du 10 ŋerawec . Erâ qizec-ticnao šâŋe qâreŋ simbiŋne forawec .
66013002	Qowi mimicne honepo e hawarine qâto iŋucne , menezi pusime iŋucne , â micnezi laioŋ mic iŋucne . Eme oâ e šoɋac sasanaŋ-ticne â ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋe-ticne â tâpiri sâko qikiŋnecnewec .
66013003	Qowi qizecne moc qâhâmokicne tinac honepo . Eme izi wicticne somieme biaŋkewec . Eme irec mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋe qowi hone warec boc ecnehuc râpefuŋnao jumbiŋ .
66013004	Erâ oâ e qowi tâpiri râcnewecte muteŋ bâteŋ ecnembiŋ . Ehuc qowi iŋuc jaha fenšoŋkehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ : “ Qowi e iŋucne mozi jukac ? Erâ mozi moc wemo ecneocmu ? ”
66013005	Eme sahac mumuteŋ dâŋ â dâŋ gâgâpâcne muocte irec micne heteckekicne . Erâ gie-ticne i mosa 42 bahuc juocte dameŋ bacnekicne .
66013006	Eme irec Anutu e jahacne mecne â šâŋe biŋe-ticne mecne â sambâŋko ŋeŋe juju eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe mecne musoc qâsoriŋ ejarehuc juwec .
66013007	Erâ Anuture tiriŋicfâc râsi ejarehuc jopa sipiric ejareocte mana fâsâecnekicne , erâ wâc mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne jaŋe ŋicbomboŋ ejare-fâreocte tâpiri râcnekicne .
66013008	Eme mâreŋŋic sasawa jaŋe mu šeri ecneniŋmu , ŋic šâŋe-jeŋic Lama qa hezuc ekicne ere juju papiao mârâc jaha mâreŋ fufuaonecteaŋ mi qâreŋkekicne jaŋe hâcne qowi iŋuc ecne-fâreniŋmu .
66013009	Hazecneheczi dâŋ kecši manazejec :
66013010	“ Moc e kâpâcwârure biŋe eweczi kâpâcwâru ficko fezejec . Moc e šikare biŋe eweczi šika kizejec . ” Tiriŋic jaŋe dameŋ ira hâcne sasanaŋhec â mamanasiŋhec junšepieŋ .
66013011	Eme mâreŋmaŋkonec qowi mimicne moc wefume honepo , e lama iŋucne šuŋene jajahec sawa fowec . Dâŋticnezi ine oâdâŋ .
66013012	Eme qowi izi qowi mârâc wefuwec ere maio ere tâpiri gie jaha bahuc jukac . Ehuc mâreŋŋic ejareme mârâc qowi , hâmocne tinac erâ ɋârewec , e dieŋzi hecneeŋgopieŋ .
66013013	Erâ mâsi kâcɋene baekac , ehuc mume mâreŋŋic honehapie sambâŋkonec šoc wahaekac .
66013014	Mâsi iŋucne hâcne baocte manacnekicnere mârâc qowi ere maio bahuc mâreŋŋic maŋ bâsifuc ejareekac . Ehuc mume qowi hâmokicne tinac erâ ɋârewec ere hawari baeŋgopieŋ .
66013015	Hawari i barâ râepie domaha šâhec qowi e manacnekicnere bâɋâreme dâŋ dâŋ eekac . Dâŋ dâŋ ehuc mume ŋic , e dieŋzi mi hecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe qâhâmoc-jopaeŋgopieŋ .
66013016	Erâ wâc fekicne â wahakicne , mafahec â hapetac , ŋicbomboŋ â kiŋaŋ qaqa , ŋic i mâmâc sasawa ejareme mefâre-jeŋicko â mai-jeŋicko maqâreŋ bafâreeŋgopieŋ .
66013017	Eme qowire šâŋe qâreŋ â šare mi bajueŋgopieŋ , jaŋe wiac furi bapare aka hejareeŋgopieŋ .
66013018	Maŋɋârâŋ šira fokac : Ŋic moc e mamana focnekacko qowi šare-ticnere fuŋne bâfuazejec . Ʒare i ŋic mocte šâŋe . Ʒare hâcne i 666 .
66014001	Eme no šâŋe firâ mi Lama Zioŋ tikio domame honezepac i ¡ Erâ ehec ŋic 144 tauseŋ mâmâc domambiŋ . Mai-jeŋicko e jahacne šâŋe qâreŋ â Mamac-ticnere šâŋe qâreŋ fowec .
66014002	Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋfânâŋ manapo , i opâ sâro fânâŋ iŋucne â ɋuŋ fânâŋ sâko iŋucne . Erâ dâŋfânâŋ i manape musi tinac ewec , ŋic bocjaha musi bapie fânâŋkeekac iŋuc tinac manapo .
66014003	Jaŋe eri ŋeŋere maŋfuŋko â wiac jujune 4 â ŋicqizec jaŋere maio gae ɋâricne moc heeŋgopieŋ . Gae i ŋic gâcnezi he manac eene mi ewec , ŋic 144 tauseŋ , mâreŋŋic gâcne jaŋeraonec furi bacjopakicne , jaŋe sawa mamanane .
66014004	Jaŋe hâcne ŋokacko mi sâqorehuc maŋɋaɋac jaha jumbiŋ ” jaŋe hâcne Lama jume ju ecneeŋgopieŋ ” jaŋe hâcne mâreŋŋic gâcne jaŋeraonec Anuture â Lamare qaqasune bâbâni rocjopakicne .
66014005	Erâ micjeŋickonec burecdâŋ moc mi wahawec , jaŋe bahacmâc .
66014006	Eme no aŋelo moc honepo , e faic sawao fotâcnehuc rawec . E mâreŋŋic jaŋere Biŋebiaŋ fofo sanaŋ , mâreŋ sâc ŋic sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne , jaŋere bajuwec .
66014007	Eki wiwic jaha wirahuc šiŋuc muwec : “ Ŋoŋe Anutu araŋ bacnehuc sâsenšepieŋ , okac dameŋ-ticne maickekac hâcne . Sambaŋ â mâreŋ , hâwec â opâ šâŋe bâfuawec e mu wâwâsic ecnenšepieŋ . ”
66014008	Iŋuc murâ rame râpefuŋnao aŋelo moczi warerâ šiŋuc wirawec : “ Babe hae sâko tâtiekac , tâtie-jâmbâŋkekac , hae irec rune mâreŋ sâc ŋicne sasecte waiŋ opâ momori gumec-jopahuc jumbiŋ hâcne . ”
66014009	Eme râpefuŋnao aŋelo âgo-ticne moczi warerâ dâŋ hahaŋne bahuc šiŋuc muwec : “ Moc e qowi mimicne e jahacne me hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecneocmu â mai-ticnao me meticnao maqâreŋ roocmu ,
66014010	e Anutuzi kimbeŋ-ticnere waiŋ opâ momori jâmbâŋ , opâ jâmbâŋhec mi bâsifuckekicne , i râqâc-ticnaonec gumeme tiri aŋelo â Lama jaŋere maio šocbâruŋko hurâ šâic serereŋ mana rahuc juocmu .
66014011	Eme šoczi ŋic iŋucne šâfitac-jopame irec hosâcne ŋezume ŋezu fehuc foocmu sanaŋ . Irec ŋic qowi mimicne â hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecnembiŋ jaŋe mecne , â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne bajumbiŋ jaŋe mâmâc šâiczi mi behec-jopame ŋeŋe mana tâmiric ŋafe furec šušuhuc jaha mana rahuc juniŋmu . ”
66014012	Dameŋ ira hâcne Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc Jesure miti hâwicmâc bajueŋgopieŋ tiriŋic i jaŋe sasanaŋ bâfuanšepieŋ .
66014013	Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋ moc šiŋuc wahame manapo : “ Go dâŋ ši qâreŋkec : Dameŋ ši fuŋkerâ , Wofuŋtao qohotahuc hâmoniŋmu jaŋere bubiaŋ manazo . Mârozi mukac , jâmbomac , jaŋe neneŋ gie-jeŋic hetararâ ŋemanahuc biaŋ-jopaocmu . Erâ juju bapa-jeŋicte fârinezi rapie raocmu . ”
66014014	Eme no fipe feme karorac qaŋqaŋ ututuŋ fuame honepo . Erâ karorac faio moc ŋewec , e hawari-ticne ŋic iŋucne . Qizec-ticnao ŋicwofuŋ du golzi bakicne roŋewec â meticnezi sâqe mictara baŋewec .
66014015	Ehame ufuŋkonec aŋelo moczi waharâ karorac faio ŋewec , e šiŋuc wiracnewec : “ Go sâqegezi gie fârine qa roro ec , mâreŋko giere fârine woze-fârewecte qa roro ezore dameŋne maickekac hâcne . ”
66014016	Iŋuc mume karorac faio ŋeweczi sâqe-ticne wickeme mâreŋko fârine qafârewec .
66014017	Eme aŋelo moczi sambâŋko ufuŋkonec wahawec , e iŋuc jaha sâqe mictara bajuwec .
66014018	Warehame âgo-ticne moczi alata ŋeweckonec warewec . E šocte soŋaŋzi âgo-ticne sâqe mictara bajuwec e šiŋuc wiracnewec : “ Go sâqege mictara mâreŋko waiŋ fârine qâtâcne-fârec , hândâŋne qeue-fârekac hâcne ”

66014020	Erâ hae râpeo âte pisickepie katapa maŋkonec socsâko wahahuc fowec . Wahaku šâkâŋne fuarâ becâsic mecqaŋeŋ-jeŋicko qawec . Á šâkâŋ rereŋ šoric-ticnere sâc ine 300 kilometa iŋuc ŋerawec .
66015001	Eme sambâŋko mâsi qâreŋ sâko bipinehec moc honepo . Aŋelo 7 jaŋe wiac micne momori 7 badomambiŋ . Wiac i mimic fuahame Anuturaonec okacne fisi taraocte mukicne .
66015002	Erâ hâwec moc honepo , i kiruŋzi barâ šocbâruŋhec bâbâsifuc ekicne tinac fome honepo . Erâ qowi mimicne ere dâŋ â hawari â šare qâreŋ i sanaŋkerâ qikiŋnembiŋ ŋic i jaŋe kiruŋzi hâwec irec mecnao Anuturaonec musi badomapie honec-jopapo .
66015003	Jaŋe Anuture kiŋaŋŋic Mose â Lamare gae kecšiŋuc muhuc heeŋgopieŋ : “ O Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre , go gie fekicne â bipinehec baekic . Ŋicne ŋicne jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko , go hatage tiŋne â fâri fideteŋ .
66015004	Wofuŋ go mozi araŋ mi bagareocmu â mozi šâŋege mi mumbiaŋkeocmu ? Go mocjahazi tiri hâcne . Irec ŋicne ŋicne gorao warerâ dieŋzi hegareniŋmu . Go bâbâtiŋ gie fârine batec fuŋne taniŋkekac hâcne . ”
66015005	Eme no šâŋe firâ honehape sambâŋko ufuŋ qoruc boze-ticnehec irec motâc aŋkewec .
66015006	Aŋkeme aŋelo 7 wiac micne momori 7 bajumbiŋ , jaŋe ufuŋkonec wahambiŋ . Jaŋe ŋaqi ɋaɋacne qaŋqaŋ rojumbiŋ , â amec-jeŋicko umbika golzi bakicne fowec .
66015007	Eme wiac jujune 4 domambiŋ jaŋeraonec moczi aŋelo 7 râqâc 7 golzi bakicne jare-fârewec . Râqâcmaŋko ine Anutu juju sanaŋ runere kimbeŋ fusucmarâ fowec .

66016001	Eme ufuŋmaŋkonec dâŋ wiwira sâko wahame manapo . I aŋelo 7 šiŋuc jazawec : “ Ŋoŋe rarâ râqâc 7 hoŋkepie Anuture kimbeŋzi mâreŋko huzejec . ”
66016002	Eme aŋelo namba 1 eki rarâ râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme mâreŋko huwec . Hume ŋic qowi mimicnere šâŋe qâreŋ bajumbiŋ â hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecnembiŋ jaŋe wicšâhâc šâic sisiac-ticnehec mâretec fua-jarewec .
66016003	Eme aŋelo namba 2 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hâwecko hoŋkeme huwec . Hume hâweczi soc tânipu tinac ewec . Eme irec hâwecko qowi hâmo-fârembiŋ .

66016007	Eme alatazi dâŋ šiŋuc mume manapo : “ Jâmbomac , Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre , okac babazuge tiŋne â fâri fideteŋ . ”
66016008	Eme aŋelo namba 4 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme šoaŋko huwec . Ira hume šoaŋ šocne bâruŋke-jâmbâŋkerâ ŋic mâretec šacjopawec .
66016009	Eme ŋic jaŋe šoaŋ fâroroc-ticnezi boc rikec-jopame Anutu , micticnere wiac micne momori iŋuc fuawec , e šâŋe biŋe-ticne musâqorembiŋ . Erâ maŋjeŋic sifu mi bârisierâ Anutu mi sâsembiŋ .
66016010	Eme aŋelo namba 5 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac qowi mimicnere ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋeo hoŋkeme wahawec . Wahame hae mâreŋ-ticne dapâc efârewec . Eme ŋic jaŋe šâic serereŋ manahuc nameŋ-jeŋic kitâcnembiŋ .
66016011	Eme šâic-jeŋicte â wicšâhâc-jeŋicte Anutu sambâŋ rune musoriŋkembiŋ . Ehuc maŋjeŋic mi bârisierâ juju bapa-jeŋic mi qikiŋnembiŋ .
66016012	Eme aŋelo namba 6 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme Eufrata opâ sâkoo huwec . Hume opâ šickewec . I hata fuame šoaŋ wewefunaonec ŋicwofuŋ fisiniŋte iŋuc fuawec .
66016013	Eme no honehape oâre mickonec â qowi mimicnere mickonec â porofete burecne ere mickonec demoŋ repicne jahec â moc qaqec hawari tinac wefumbiŋ .
66016014	I jaŋe demoŋ fârine , mâsi wiac baniŋte tâpiri fojarekac . Jaŋe hâcne mâreŋ sâc irec ŋicwofuŋ qafeŋ-jopapie Anutu bapafâre ere dameŋ sâkoo râsi roroc erâ fisirâ qaqac eniŋmu .
66016015	“ Manaŋgopieŋ , no šika qaqa jaŋe iŋucne ututuŋ fisipemu . Irec moc e biuctac jume mimi-ticne fuazacte maŋɋâri juhuc ŋaqi-ticne soŋaŋkezejec . Iŋuc eocmu ere manape šerine ekac . ”
66016016	Eme demoŋ jaŋe mâreŋ moc šâŋene Judadâŋko Hamagedoŋ mukicne , ira ŋicwofuŋ hetumaŋ-jopa-fârembiŋ .
66016017	Eme aŋelo namba 7 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac sawao hoŋkeme huwec . Eme ufuŋko eri ŋeŋe ŋeweckonec dâŋ wiwira moc šiŋuc wahawec : “ Efârekicne . ”
66016018	Eme bâbâric â ɋuŋ parandaŋ â micfânâŋ fuawec â homeŋ kâcɋene sâko jâmbâŋ bawec , sâc iŋucne moc ŋic fuarâ juwarembiŋko mi bawec .
66016019	Eme hae sâko fâuckeme jahec â moc ewec . Erâ mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere hae tâtie-fârewec , â Babe hae sâkore rufâc jaŋere Anutuzi iŋuc jaha manasurâ kimbeŋ-ticnere waiŋ opâ gumec-jopawec .
66016020	Erâ wâc nuc â tiki mâmâc sirowe-fârembiŋ .
66016021	Á sambâŋkonec hoe sanaŋ hewec , hândâŋne buse iŋucne , izi ŋic hecjopame Anutu musoriŋkembiŋ . Hoe i hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ , ima-ticnehec .
66017001	Eme aŋelo 7 râqâc 7 bajumbiŋ jaŋeraonec moczi norao warerâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Sasec ŋokac sâko opâ kâcɋenao ŋeekac e okacne fisicneocmu , i waretec gowatupe .
66017002	Mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic jaŋe ehec sasec eec eeŋgopieŋ â mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe eraonec hâcne sasec-ticnere waiŋ opâ nârâ maŋsifuc ejareekac . ”
66017003	Iŋuc nazame maŋnane ŋerisieme mâreŋ tuhuo jowacnu rawec . Eme ira ŋokac moc honepo , e qowi mimicne bâbâroŋ moc ere faio ŋewec . Qowi sahac-ticnao šâŋe qâreŋ simbiŋne fuŋne fuŋne sâcke-fârerâ fowec . Erâ qowi hâcne e qizec-ticne 7 â šuŋene 10 .
66017004	Á ŋokac e ŋaqi bâbâroŋ â âmuc âmucne rojuwec , erâ erizi kiseŋ qâseŋ kiwec . Meticnezi râqâc moc golzi bakicne badomawec , i sasec-ticnere sohoŋ mamakâczi fusewec .
66017005	Mai-ticnao šâŋesoŋ-ticne kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne fowec : “ Babe hae sâko , mâreŋ sâc sasec mamakâc wiac irec neŋgocne no hâcne . ”
66017006	Eme ŋokac e tiriŋic â Jesure mumutaniŋfâc jaŋere soc nâku maŋne bibiriwame honepo . Honerâ bipic tatara enarewec .
66017007	Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc muhuc wio-narewec : “ Wemocte bipic tatara egarekac ? No ŋokacte fuŋne â qowizi âsickekac ere fuŋne â qowi qizecne 7 â šuŋene 10 irec fuŋne mâmâc gazape manac .
66017008	Go qowi mimicne honemec i mârâc jaha juwec , ši mi jukac , šâhec ine hârâckonec risie wefurâ sisipiric sanaŋko huocmu . Eme qowi mârâc juwec , ši mi jukac , juku ine risieocmu , i mâreŋko ŋic jaŋe honerâ mu warec ecneniŋmu . Ʒâŋe-jeŋic mâreŋ fufuaonecteaŋ juju sanaŋte papiao mi qâreŋkekicne , ŋic i jaŋe hâcne iŋuc eniŋmu .
66017009	Ʒi maŋɋârâŋheczi mamanane fokac : Qizecne 7 i tiki 7 , ŋokaczi ŋefackekac hâcne .
66017010	Eme tiki 7 izi ŋicwofuŋ 7 . Ŋicwofuŋ 5 arictac embiŋ , moc ši jukac â moc juku fuaocmu . Fuarâ dameŋ bembeŋne mac juocte mucnekicne .
66017011	Qowi mârâc juwec , ši ine mi jukac , izi ŋicwofuŋ 7 jaŋere birio zuhuckehuc namba 8 eocmu , erâ sisipiricko huocmu .
66017012	“ Ʒuŋene 10 honemec i ŋicwofuŋ 10 jaha wâc , erâ jaŋe gie-jeŋic dameŋ šiŋuczia mi fuŋkembiŋ . Ŋicwofuŋ gie-jeŋic fuŋkerâ qowi mimicnehec dameŋ bembeŋne mac baniŋmu .
66017013	Jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic mocjaha fome qowi mimicnere kiŋaŋ šoɋachec qaniŋmu .
66017014	Ehuc Lamahec šika gie baniŋmu . Eme Lama eki ine sanaŋkerâ jopaocmu . Eki hâcne fekicne jaŋere Fekicne â ŋicwofuŋ jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko . Á jume jujufâc-ticne rowosâec-joparâ rocjoparâ bufuŋfâc-ticne bacjopakicne hâcne . ”
66017015	Iŋuc murâ šiŋuc šuhuckerâ nazawec : “ Sasec ŋokac e opâ sâko irec mecnao ŋeme honemec , opâ izi ŋicne ŋicne , sahac hawari â dâŋmarac fuŋne fuŋnehec .
66017016	Erâ šuŋene 10 honemec , jaŋe mecne â qowi e mâmâc qaisockerâ ŋaqi wiac jâoc rofârerâ biucne nârâ siec sahacne šocko rikeniŋmu .
66017017	Erâ i mâc mi eniŋmu , Anutuzi maŋ jeŋicko mu qafeŋ râeme jaŋe dâŋticne reŋkehuc maŋ mocjaha efârerâ qowi kiŋaŋ qacneniŋmu . Qacnehuc juhapie Anuture dâŋ hâcne sanaŋke-fâreocmu .
66017018	Erâ go ŋokac honemec i hae sâko , e hâcne mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ ejareme kiŋaŋ qacneniŋte tâpiri focnekac . ”
66020001	Eme no sambâŋkonec aŋelo moczi wahame honepo . E hârâcte ki â kâpâcwâru sâko moc bajuwec .
66020002	Erâ e oâ , homa raŋɋa , demoŋ micne Sataŋ hâcne , e rorâ kâpâcwâruzi bândeŋnerâ jara 1 tauseŋ niŋgiŋhec foocte mucnerâ
66020003	hârâcko tuŋkeme huwec . Hume motâcne kizi basanaŋkerâ sâfâzi bâbâzickewec . Eme ŋicne ŋicne maŋ bâsifuc mocwâc mi ejarehuc mâc fohame jara 1 tauseŋ taraocte mukicne . Tarame firuepie wefurâ dameŋ bembeŋne mac juocmu .
66020004	Eme no eri ŋeŋe ŋerame honepo . Honehape ŋic fisirâ fainao ŋembiŋ jaŋe mumutara gie baniŋte mujarekicne . Eme Jesu mutaniŋkehuc Anuture dâŋ hâwicmâc bajuhapie upe-jeŋic qâtâcnekicne jaŋere maŋ qâqâtâc honec-jopapo , erâ qowi mimicne e jahacne â hawari-ticne dieŋzi mi hecnembiŋ â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne mai-jeŋicko â mejeŋicko mi bajumbiŋ , jaŋere maŋ qâqâtâc mâmâc honec-jopapo . Eme ŋic i jaŋe sahac-jeŋic ɋâreme honec-jopapo . Eme jaŋe Kristohec ŋicwofuŋ gie bahapie jara 1 tauseŋ tarawec .
66020005	Hâmokicne gâcne sâko jaŋe ine mi ɋârehuc jara 1 tauseŋ taraocte irec woŋec fombiŋ . Fafahare honepo i fafahare namba wâŋ .
66020006	Fafahare namba wâŋko šuhuckeŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeri bubiaŋ faio tiri juŋgopieŋ . Ŋic iŋucne hâmoc namba tuzi bâsowariec-jopaocmu . Jaŋe Anuture â Kristore taha bapafâc erâ juniŋmu , ehuc ehec ŋicwofuŋ gie bahuc juhapie jara 1 tauseŋ taraocmu .
66020007	Eme jara 1 tauseŋ tarame Sataŋ firuepie kâpâcwâru fickonec mocwâc wefuocmu .
66020008	Wefurâ ŋicne ŋicne mâreŋ ŋifec â ŋifec , faic â juwic juŋgopieŋ maŋjeŋic bâsifuckerâ Gogo â Magogo ŋic qafeŋ-jopame râsi roroc erâ fisiniŋmu , jaŋe šare-jeŋic hâwec moŋgeŋ iŋucne , wowosene tâmiric .
66020009	Fisirâ mâreŋ wâneŋ sâko ira raferâ tiriŋic toma âterâ fohapie somâc-jopambiŋ . Somâc-jopahuc hae biaŋ i mâmâc orâŋkembiŋ . Iŋuc ehapie sambâŋkonec šoc waharâ šâhâmoc-jopa-fârewec .
66020010	Á Sataŋ , maŋ bâsifuc ejarehuc juwec , e lambe opâre riqiczi šoc šahuc foekac ira behepie huwec . Qowi mimicne â porofete-ticne burecne jahe ijaha mâmâc jupic . Eme jahe ira ŋafe šoaŋ qâqâtiri šâic fâro mana rahuc junicmu sanaŋ .
66020011	Eme no eri ŋeŋe kâcɋene qaŋqaŋ moc honepo . Fainao ŋewec ere maionec sambâŋ â mâreŋ wise tâmirepic .
66020012	Ehame hâmokicne fekicne wahakicne jaŋe mâmâc sasawa eri ŋeŋe fuŋnao domapie honec-jopapo . Domahapie papiane papiane qaratiembiŋ . Erâ moc qaratiembiŋ i juju sanaŋte papia . Eme hâmokicne jaŋe juju bapa-jeŋicte dâŋ papiao qâreŋkekicne i honehuc dâŋjeŋic mutarambiŋ .
66020013	Eme dameŋ ira hâweczi maŋnao hâmokicne fombiŋ jaŋe bârisiec-jopawec â hâmoczi ŋic hâmocne bârisiec-jopawec â hârâczi ŋic hâmocne bârisiec-jopawec wâc . Eme hâmokicne sasawa jaŋe ju ju bapa-jeŋicte fuŋne rituhuc tofa bazu-jarekicne .
66020014	Eme hâmoc â hârâc i šocriqicko behepie huwec . Izi hâmoc namba tu ekac , šocriqic hâcne .
66020015	Eme ŋic moc e šâŋene juju sanaŋte papiao basarâ šocriqicko behepie huwec .
66021001	Eme no sambâŋ ɋâricne â mâreŋ ɋâricne honec-jofapo . Sambâŋ raŋɋane â mâreŋ raŋɋane jahe ine sirowepic . Erâ hâwec iŋuc jaha arictac ewec .
66021002	Eme tiri hae , Jerusalem ɋâricne hâcne , sambâŋkonec Anuturaonec wahame honepo , ŋokac biŋe moc ŋicko râeniŋte erickeeŋgopieŋ iŋuc tinac ericke emasaŋ ekicne honepo .
66021003	Eme eri ŋeŋeonec dâŋ kâcɋene šiŋuc wareme manapo : “ Honekic , Anuture ŋeŋe hae ŋic jaŋerao fuakac hâcne . Eki ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ehame jaŋe ŋicfâc-ticne erâ juniŋmu .
66021004	Anutu e jahac jaŋerao juhuc šâŋeuc-jeŋic bâkereŋke-fâreocmu . Hâmoc me busâqoc me ki oowa me huc šâic ira mi fuaocmu . Wiac raŋɋanezi omae-fârewec hâcne . ”
66021005	Eme eri ŋeŋeo ŋeweczi šiŋuc nazawec : “ Manakic , no wiac sasawa ɋâricne bâfuakopac . ” Iŋuc murâ muwec : “ Go qâreŋkec , dâŋ i fâri hândâŋne jâmbâŋ . ”
66021006	Erâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Wiac efârekicne , no bâbâni â šâhec , wiac fufuŋke â babatara . Moc e opâre hâmome no juju opâ šâkâŋkonec fiarâ katucmâc gumepemu .
66021007	Moc e sasanaŋte gie baku batararâ wiac ši raucke-fâreocmu , eme noni Anutu-ticne erâ juhape eki motec-nane erâ juocmu .
66021008	Hâwic bâroŋ â miti qiqikiŋ â wâwânâŋhec â šika qaqa â sasecŋic â hafec qaŋgec ŋic â nemuɋâî babaju â siocdâŋ babaju sasawa , ŋic i jaŋere ŋeŋe lambe opâre riqiczi šoc šahuc foekac ira mukicne . Izi hâmoc namba tu . ”
66021009	Eme aŋelo 7 râqâc-jeŋic sâc wiac micne momorizi fuseme badomambiŋ , jaŋeraonec moczi norao warerâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Waretec Lamare ŋokac biŋe gowatupe . ”
66021010	Iŋuc murâ enareme maŋnane ŋerisieme tiki sâko šoricne moc ŋewec ira jowacnu ferâ tiri hae Jerusalem i sambâŋkonec Anuturaonec wahame nowatume kecšiŋuc honepo :
66021011	Anuture eri tatamaczi geroŋke-fârekicne . Hae irec tatamacnezi qânâ furi sâko jawa ririŋ kikicne iŋucne erâ bâric bâricneekac .
66021012	Qânâsac sâko šoricnezi hae râreckekac . Sac i motâc-ticne 12 , erâ motâc botâŋnao aŋelo moc moc doma rapie 12 jaha ekac , erâ wâc motâc sâc Israe ŋicguru 12 jaŋere šâŋe qâreŋ forakac .
66021013	Ʒoaŋ wewefunaopec motâc jahec â moc domakac , mâreŋ juwicpec motâc jahec â moc domakac , mâreŋ faicpec motâc jahec â moc domakac , â šoaŋ huhunaopec iŋuc jaha motâc jahec â moc domakac .
66021014	Haesac irec qânâ wâtuŋ 12 doma rakac , eme wâtuŋ 12 irec ombâŋnao Lamare aposolofâc 12 jaŋere šâŋe qâreŋ 12 jaha forakac .
66021015	Aŋelo dâŋ nazawec eki gunusâc moc golzi bakicne badomawec , izi hae â motâc-ticne â sâcticne sâc bawec .
66021016	Hae i tuturuŋne jahec â jahec , hâŋne otecne sâckoa . Eme aŋelozi hae rârec rârec gunusâc-ticnezi sâc bame kilometa 2 tauseŋ ewec . Hâŋne otecne â šoricne sâckoa sasawa .
66021017	Eme haesac ɋâfoŋ-ticnere sâc bame 70 meta ewec , ŋiczi sâc bajueŋgopeneŋ ijaha aŋelozi bajuhuc hae sâc bawec .
66021018	Haesac i qânâ ɋaɋacne , huririnehec izi bakicne , â hae ine goì fifimârâŋne kiruŋ ɋaɋacne iŋucne izi bakicne .
66021019	Haesac irec qânâ wâtuŋ i qânâ furi sâko fuŋne fuŋne findowakicne sasawa izi bakicne . Wâtuŋ namba 1 i qânâ ɋaɋacne kiruŋ tinac izi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 2 i qânâ keŋkeŋne izi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 3 i qânâ kedazi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 4 i qânâ ârâŋ ɋâri izi bakicne ,
66021020	wâtuŋ namba 5 i qânâ birâ birâ izi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 6 i qânâ bâbâroŋzi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 7 i qânâ âmuc âmucnezi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 8 i qânâ buge tinac weweaŋne izi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 9 i qânâ bâbâŋeŋzi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 10 i qânâ râweckekicnezi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 11 i qânâ soc tinac gogowacne izi bakicne , wâtuŋ namba 12 i qânâ qondaŋ horiki tinac izi bakicne .
66021021	Sacmotâc 12 i kubu furi sâko 12 izi bakicne , motâc moc i kubi moczi bakicne , motâc moc i kubu moczi , iŋuc sasawa . Hae hata i goì ɋaɋacnezi bakicne , kiruŋ iŋucne fifimârâŋne .
66021022	Ufuŋ ine haeo moc mi ŋeme honepo , Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre eki ufuŋ ejareekac â Lamazi mâmâc .
66021023	Erâ hae i mosa šoaŋzi mi âke tamaeekac , Anuture eri tatamaczi batamaeekac â Lamazi šoc tatamac-ticne eekac .
66021024	Mâreŋ sâc ŋicne ŋicne jaŋe hae irec tatamackoa jufâreniŋmu , â mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe eri boreŋ wiac-jeŋic hae ira bara-fâreniŋmu .

66022001	Eme aŋelozi juju opâ sâko moc nowatume honepo , ɋaɋacne , jawa ririŋ kikicne . I Anutu â Lama ere eri ŋeŋe fuŋkonec wahakac .
66022002	Waharâ hae hata šâšâŋiŋnao rakac . Opâ mecnao ŋifec â ŋifec jujujâc doma rakac . Jâc irec fârine hawarine fuŋne fuŋne 12 izi mosa sâc fua qeuc eekac . Eme mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋe jâc irec rehacne nâhuc biaŋkeniŋmu .
66022003	Hae ira wiac sâwechec mi foocmu . Anutu â Lama ere ŋeŋe hae ira hâcne fuame ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋe kiŋaŋ qacnehuc juniŋmu .
66022004	Erâ hawari-ticne honehuc juniŋmu , â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne mai-jeŋicko fuarâ foocmu .
66022005	Hae i mi ŋafeocmu , erâ lambe me šoaŋ tatamacnere mi muniŋmu , Wofuŋ Anutu e jahac šoaŋ ejareocmu . Eme hae rune jaŋe ŋicwofuŋ gie barahuc juniŋmu sanaŋ .
66022006	Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc nazawec : “ Dâŋ i fâri hândâŋne jâmbâŋ . Wofuŋ Anutu porofete ejareme maŋjeŋic ŋerisieekac , eki hâcne aŋelo-ticne soreme kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ticne ŋoŋe wiac , mi šoraha fuaocte mukicne i ŋaza ŋowatuc ewec .
66022007	Manakic , no biac fâpemu , eme moc e papia kecšira findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkekicne i sisirombe faio bajuocmu e šeri bubiaŋ manacnezo . ”
66022008	Eme Johane no hâcne wiac i hone manac efârepo . Hone manac efârerâ aŋelo wiac nowatuwec ere maŋfuŋko fodaperâ numucnezo ehape
66022009	qatara-narerâ muwec : “ Misac mac , no kiŋaŋ qaqa âgoge , erâ porofete qomâfâcge jaŋere âgo , â papia širec dâŋ aimuŋ bajuniŋmu jaŋere âgo jaha . Go Anutu e jahacne sawa daŋge nunumu ecnec . ”
66022010	Iŋuc murâ šiŋuc nazawec : “ Go papia širec findaŋdâŋ fâzâ mi bazemec . Dâŋ i fârinehec eocte dameŋne bembeŋkekac hâcne .
66022011	Irec sâqocne bapa e sâqocne bazo murâ bazejec , â maŋwânâŋheczi maŋwânâŋhec juzo murâ juzejec , â mitio juekaczi ine mitioa juzejec , â maŋfuru juekaczi maŋfuru jaha juzejec . ”

66022015	Hae râpenao juniŋmu ine qâto â hafec qaŋgec bapa â sasecŋic â šika qaqa â nemuɋâŋ babaju erâ burec bajuhuc irec aŋac-jopaekac .
66022016	“ Jesu no hâcne aŋelo-nane sorepe eki kikefuŋ gurufâc-nane ŋoŋe mumutaniŋ dâŋ i mufua-ŋarewec . No hâcne Dawidire fuŋqizecne â oso gitecne , erâ bâpiŋ sâko tatamachec . ”
66022017	Mâro â Jesure biŋefâc jaŋe šiŋuc mueŋgop ieŋ : “ Go warezemec . ” Á moc e dâŋ ši manarâ iŋuc jaha muzejec : “ Go warezemec . ” Moc e opâre hâmorâ šira fisizejec . Á moc e irec ecnekacko ware juju opâ furimâc nâzejec .
66022018	Papia kecšira findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkekicne i wose manac eniŋmu ŋoŋe uŋ ŋazape mananiŋ : Moc e maŋticnere dâŋ moc šuhuckeocmu , ŋic e Anutuzi wiac micne momori papia kecšira qâreŋkekicne i šuhuckecneocmu wâc ,
66022019	â moc e findaŋdâŋ ši âke sipuocmu , ŋic erao Anutuzi jujujâcte dâŋ â tiri haere dâŋ ši qâreŋkekicne iŋuc jaha âke sipuocmu .
66022020	Dâŋ mufuakicne ši dopeckekaczi šiŋuc mukac : “ Jâmbomac , no biac fâpemu . ” Jâmbomac , Wofuŋ Jesu go warezemec .
66022021	Wofuŋ Jesure aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fofârezejec . Jâmbomac .
